
// 游戏版本号
const GAME_VERSION = '1.0.0';

// 全局错误日志捕获
const ERROR_LOG_KEY = 'farm_game_error_log';
window.addEventListener('error', function(e) {
    try {
        const logs = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(ERROR_LOG_KEY) || '[]');
        logs.push({
            time: new Date().toLocaleString(),
            message: e.message,
            file: e.filename,
            line: e.lineno,
            col: e.colno
        });
        // 最多保留50条
        if (logs.length > 50) logs.shift();
        localStorage.setItem(ERROR_LOG_KEY, JSON.stringify(logs));
    } catch(err) {}
});

// 初始化音频（必须用户交互后调用）
function initAudio() {
    if (!audioCtx) {
        audioCtx = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
        musicGainNode = audioCtx.createGain();
        musicGainNode.gain.value = musicVolume;
        musicGainNode.connect(audioCtx.destination);
        
        sfxGainNode = audioCtx.createGain();
        sfxGainNode.gain.value = sfxVolume;
        sfxGainNode.connect(audioCtx.destination);
    }
    if (audioCtx.state === 'suspended') {
        audioCtx.resume();
    }
}

// 播放单个音符
function playNote(frequency, duration, wave = 'sine', volume = 0.06, targetNode = null) {
    if (!audioCtx) return;
    const target = targetNode || musicGainNode;
    
    const osc = audioCtx.createOscillator();
    const gain = audioCtx.createGain();
    osc.connect(gain);
    gain.connect(target);
    
    osc.type = wave;
    osc.frequency.value = frequency;
    
    // 更柔和的ADSR包络
    const now = audioCtx.currentTime;
    const attack = duration * 0.15;
    const decay = duration * 0.1;
    const sustain = duration * 0.6;
    const release = duration * 0.15;
    
    gain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, now);
    gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(volume, now + attack); // Attack
    gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(volume * 0.8, now + attack + decay); // Decay
    gain.gain.setValueAtTime(volume * 0.8, now + attack + decay + sustain); // Sustain
    gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, now + duration); // Release
    
    osc.start(now);
    osc.stop(now + duration + 0.05);
}

// 播放白噪声
function playNoise(duration, volume = 0.03, filterFreq = 1000) {
    if (!audioCtx) return;
    
    const bufferSize = audioCtx.sampleRate * duration;
    const buffer = audioCtx.createBuffer(1, bufferSize, audioCtx.sampleRate);
    const data = buffer.getChannelData(0);
    for (let i = 0; i < bufferSize; i++) {
        data[i] = (Math.random() * 2 - 1) * (1 - i / bufferSize);
    }
    
    const source = audioCtx.createBufferSource();
    source.buffer = buffer;
    
    const filter = audioCtx.createBiquadFilter();
    filter.type = 'lowpass';
    filter.frequency.value = filterFreq;
    
    const gain = audioCtx.createGain();
    gain.gain.value = volume;
    
    source.connect(filter);
    filter.connect(gain);
    gain.connect(sfxGainNode);
    
    source.start();
}

// ========== 各种音效 ==========

// 点击音效（木头轻响）
function playClickSound() {
    if (!sfxEnabled) return;
    initAudio();
    
    const osc = audioCtx.createOscillator();
    const gain = audioCtx.createGain();
    osc.connect(gain);
    gain.connect(sfxGainNode);
    
    osc.type = 'triangle';
    osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(800, audioCtx.currentTime);
    osc.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(400, audioCtx.currentTime + 0.08);
    
    gain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, audioCtx.currentTime);
    gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.04, audioCtx.currentTime + 0.01);
    gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, audioCtx.currentTime + 0.1);
    
    osc.start();
    osc.stop(audioCtx.currentTime + 0.12);
}

// ==================== NPC呢喃音效系统 ====================
// 每个NPC独特的声音配置，参考动森/小黄人风格
const NPC_VOICE_CONFIG = {
    'wangcunzhang': { baseFreq: 140, speed: 0.9, wave: 'triangle', variation: 25, name: '村长' },
    'lilaonong': { baseFreq: 160, speed: 0.85, wave: 'sawtooth', variation: 20, name: '李老农' },
    'zhangshen': { baseFreq: 340, speed: 1.3, wave: 'sine', variation: 50, name: '张婶' },
    'wangerdan': { baseFreq: 500, speed: 1.7, wave: 'square', variation: 70, name: '王二蛋' },
    'zhaolaoban': { baseFreq: 210, speed: 1.1, wave: 'triangle', variation: 30, name: '赵老板' },
    'linxiaoyu': { baseFreq: 400, speed: 1.0, wave: 'sine', variation: 35, name: '林小雨' },
    'chenyang': { baseFreq: 190, speed: 1.4, wave: 'triangle', variation: 45, name: '陈阳' },
    'suxiao': { baseFreq: 370, speed: 1.5, wave: 'sine', variation: 55, name: '孙妙青' },
    'zhouming': { baseFreq: 175, speed: 0.75, wave: 'sine', variation: 15, name: '周明' },
    'wangmengmeng': { baseFreq: 520, speed: 1.8, wave: 'square', variation: 80, name: '王萌萌' },
};

// 播放NPC呢喃声（类似动森那种叽叽喳喳的感觉）
function playNpcChatter(npcKey, duration = 1.2) {
    if (!sfxEnabled) return;
    initAudio();
    
    const config = NPC_VOICE_CONFIG[npcKey] || NPC_VOICE_CONFIG['wangcunzhang'];
    const startTime = audioCtx.currentTime;
    // 根据语速计算音节数量
    const syllableCount = Math.floor(duration * config.speed * 3.5);
    
    for (let i = 0; i < syllableCount; i++) {
        const syllableStart = startTime + i * (1 / config.speed / 3.5);
        const syllableDuration = 0.12 + Math.random() * 0.12;
        
        // 随机音高变化，模拟说话的抑扬顿挫
        const freqVariation = (Math.random() - 0.3) * config.variation;
        const freq = config.baseFreq + freqVariation;
        
        const osc = audioCtx.createOscillator();
        const gain = audioCtx.createGain();
        
        osc.connect(gain);
        gain.connect(sfxGainNode);
        
        osc.type = config.wave;
        osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(freq, syllableStart);
        // 每个音节内有一点点音高滑动，更自然
        osc.frequency.linearRampToValueAtTime(
            freq + (Math.random() - 0.5) * 25, 
            syllableStart + syllableDuration
        );
        
        // 音量包络：快速起音，中间平稳，快速收尾
        gain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, syllableStart);
        gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.07, syllableStart + 0.015);
        gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.05, syllableStart + syllableDuration * 0.6);
        gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, syllableStart + syllableDuration);
        
        osc.start(syllableStart);
        osc.stop(syllableStart + syllableDuration + 0.02);
    }
}

// ==================== 剧情演唱音效系统 ====================
// 不同情绪的旋律配置
const SING_MELODIES = {
    'normal': [262, 294, 330, 294],      // C D E D 平缓叙述
    'happy': [330, 392, 440, 523],       // E G A C 欢快上升
    'sad': [294, 262, 220, 196],         // D C A G 悲伤下降
    'surprised': [262, 440, 392, 330],   // C A G E 惊讶跳跃
    'tired': [247, 233, 220, 207],       // B Bb A G# 疲惫缓慢
    'angry': [330, 311, 330, 349],       // E Eb E F 生气短促
    'funny': [330, 294, 330, 392, 330],  // E D E G E 搞笑跳跃
};

// 播放剧情演唱音效（每句话"唱出来"的感觉）
function playStorySinging(emotion = 'normal', speed = 1.0) {
    if (!sfxEnabled) return;
    initAudio();
    
    const melody = SING_MELODIES[emotion] || SING_MELODIES['normal'];
    const startTime = audioCtx.currentTime;
    const noteDuration = (0.18 / speed);
    
    melody.forEach((freq, i) => {
        const noteStart = startTime + i * noteDuration;
        
        const osc = audioCtx.createOscillator();
        const gain = audioCtx.createGain();
        
        osc.connect(gain);
        gain.connect(sfxGainNode);
        
        osc.type = 'triangle';
        osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(freq, noteStart);
        
        // 每个音之间有滑音，更像唱歌
        if (i < melody.length - 1) {
            osc.frequency.linearRampToValueAtTime(
                melody[i + 1], 
                noteStart + noteDuration * 0.85
            );
        }
        
        // 音量包络
        gain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, noteStart);
        gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.09, noteStart + 0.03);
        gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.07, noteStart + noteDuration * 0.5);
        gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, noteStart + noteDuration);
        
        osc.start(noteStart);
        osc.stop(noteStart + noteDuration + 0.02);
    });
}

// 翻页音效（唰唰声）
function playPageFlipSound() {
    if (!sfxEnabled) return;
    initAudio();
    playNoise(0.15, 0.025, 2000);
}

// 收获音效（欢快上升音阶）
function playHarvestSound() {
    if (!sfxEnabled) return;
    initAudio();
    
    const notes = [523, 659, 784, 1047];
    notes.forEach((note, i) => {
        setTimeout(() => {
            playNote(note, 0.15, 'square', 0.15, sfxGainNode);
        }, i * 80);
    });
}

function playCoinSound() {
    if (!sfxEnabled) return;
    initAudio();
    
    playNote(1319, 0.1, 'square', 0.04, sfxGainNode);
    setTimeout(() => {
        playNote(1568, 0.15, 'square', 0.04, sfxGainNode);
    }, 60);
    setTimeout(() => {
        playNote(2093, 0.2, 'square', 0.03, sfxGainNode);
    }, 120);
}

    setTimeout(() => {
        playNote(1109, 0.2, 'triangle', 0.06, sfxGainNode);
    }, 100);
}

// 灾害音效（打雷轰隆隆）
function playDisasterSound() {
    if (!sfxEnabled) return;
    initAudio();
    
    playNoise(0.5, 0.15, 300);
    playNote(80, 0.4, 'sawtooth', 0.1, sfxGainNode);
}

// 增益音效（欢快叮叮）
function playBonusSound() {
    if (!sfxEnabled) return;
    initAudio();
    
    const notes = [523, 659, 784, 880, 1047];
    notes.forEach((note, i) => {
        setTimeout(() => {
            playNote(note, 0.12, 'sine', 0.075, sfxGainNode);
        }, i * 60);
    });
}

// 错误音效（低沉嗡声）
function playErrorSound() {
    if (!sfxEnabled) return;
    initAudio();
    
    const osc = audioCtx.createOscillator();
    const gain = audioCtx.createGain();
    osc.connect(gain);
    gain.connect(sfxGainNode);
    
    osc.type = 'sawtooth';
    osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(200, audioCtx.currentTime);
    osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(150, audioCtx.currentTime + 0.1);
    osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(200, audioCtx.currentTime + 0.2);
    
    gain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, audioCtx.currentTime);
    gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.075, audioCtx.currentTime + 0.02);
    gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, audioCtx.currentTime + 0.3);
    
    osc.start();
    osc.stop(audioCtx.currentTime + 0.3);
}

// 通用音效分发函数
function playSound(type) {
    switch(type) {
        case 'coin': return playCoinSound();
        case 'build': return playBonusSound();
        case 'levelup': return playBonusSound();
        default: return playClickSound();
    }
}

// 浇水音效（水流声）
function playWaterSound() {
    if (!sfxEnabled) return;
    initAudio();
    
    const bufferSize = audioCtx.sampleRate * 0.4;
    const buffer = audioCtx.createBuffer(1, bufferSize, audioCtx.sampleRate);
    const data = buffer.getChannelData(0);
    for (let i = 0; i < bufferSize; i++) {
        data[i] = (Math.random() * 2 - 1) * (1 - Math.abs(i / bufferSize * 2 - 1));
    }
    
    const source = audioCtx.createBufferSource();
    source.buffer = buffer;
    
    const filter = audioCtx.createBiquadFilter();
    filter.type = 'bandpass';
    filter.frequency.value = 1500;
    filter.Q.value = 0.5;
    
    const gain = audioCtx.createGain();
    gain.gain.value = 0.06;
    
    source.connect(filter);
    filter.connect(gain);
    gain.connect(sfxGainNode);
    
    source.start();
}

// 除草音效（沙沙声）
function playWeedSound() {
    if (!sfxEnabled) return;
    initAudio();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
        setTimeout(() => {
            const bufferSize = audioCtx.sampleRate * 0.1;
            const buffer = audioCtx.createBuffer(1, bufferSize, audioCtx.sampleRate);
            const data = buffer.getChannelData(0);
            for (let j = 0; j < bufferSize; j++) {
                data[j] = (Math.random() * 2 - 1) * (1 - j / bufferSize);
            }
            
            const source = audioCtx.createBufferSource();
            source.buffer = buffer;
            
            const filter = audioCtx.createBiquadFilter();
            filter.type = 'highpass';
            filter.frequency.value = 2000;
            
            const gain = audioCtx.createGain();
            gain.gain.value = 0.08;
            
            source.connect(filter);
            filter.connect(gain);
            gain.connect(sfxGainNode);
            
            source.start();
        }, i * 60);
    }
}

// 种植/翻土音效（泥土声）
function playDirtSound() {
    if (!sfxEnabled) return;
    initAudio();
    
    const osc = audioCtx.createOscillator();
    const gain = audioCtx.createGain();
    osc.connect(gain);
    gain.connect(sfxGainNode);
    
    osc.type = 'sine';
    osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(150, audioCtx.currentTime);
    osc.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(80, audioCtx.currentTime + 0.15);
    
    gain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, audioCtx.currentTime);
    gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.15, audioCtx.currentTime + 0.02);
    gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, audioCtx.currentTime + 0.2);
    
    osc.start();
    osc.stop(audioCtx.currentTime + 0.22);
    
    playNoise(0.1, 0.05, 300);
}

// 施肥音效（轻微哗啦声）
function playFertilizerSound() {
    if (!sfxEnabled) return;
    initAudio();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
        setTimeout(() => {
            playNote(2000 + Math.random() * 1000, 0.03, 'square', 0.03, sfxGainNode);
        }, i * 40);
    }
}

// 标签切换音效（轻微嗒声）
function playTabSound() {
    if (!sfxEnabled) return;
    initAudio();
    
    const osc = audioCtx.createOscillator();
    const gain = audioCtx.createGain();
    osc.connect(gain);
    gain.connect(sfxGainNode);
    
    osc.type = 'sine';
    osc.frequency.value = 1200;
    
    gain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, audioCtx.currentTime);
    gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.08, audioCtx.currentTime + 0.005);
    gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, audioCtx.currentTime + 0.06);
    
    osc.start();
    osc.stop(audioCtx.currentTime + 0.08);
}

// ========== 背景音乐系统 ==========

let bgmFadeTimer = null;
let rainNoiseNode = null;
let rainGainNode = null;

// 开始播放指定BGM
function startBgm(bgmName, fadeIn = true) {
    if (!musicEnabled) return;
    if (currentBgm === bgmName && musicIsPlaying) return;
    
    stopMusic();
    initAudio();
    
    const bgm = BGM_DATA[bgmName];
    if (!bgm) return;
    
    currentBgm = bgmName;
    musicIsPlaying = true;
    bgmNoteIndex = 0;
    
    // 淡入效果
    if (fadeIn && musicGainNode) {
        musicGainNode.gain.setValueAtTime(0, audioCtx.currentTime);
        musicGainNode.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(musicVolume, audioCtx.currentTime + 1.5);
    } else if (musicGainNode) {
        musicGainNode.gain.value = musicVolume;
    }
    
    // 雨天BGM加雨声
    if (bgm.hasRain) {
        startRainSound();
    }
    
    function playNextNote() {
        if (!musicIsPlaying || currentBgm !== bgmName) return;
        
        const note = bgm.notes[bgmNoteIndex % bgm.notes.length];
        const noteDur = (bgm.tempo / 1000) * (bgm.noteLength || 0.8);
        playNote(note, noteDur, bgm.wave, bgm.volume);
        
        // 添加和声（三度音程），使旋律更丰富
        if (bgm.harmony) {
            const harmonyFreq = note * 1.25; // 大三度音程
            playNote(harmonyFreq, noteDur * 0.7, 'sine', bgm.volume * 0.3);
        }
        
        // 游戏BGM加低音
        if (bgm.bassNotes) {
            const bassNote = bgm.bassNotes[Math.floor(bgmNoteIndex / 2) % bgm.bassNotes.length];
            const bassDur = (bgm.tempo / 1000) * 1.8;
            playNote(bassNote, bassDur, 'triangle', bgm.volume * 0.6);
        }
        
        bgmNoteIndex++;
        musicTimer = setTimeout(playNextNote, bgm.tempo);
    }
    
    playNextNote();
}

// 停止音乐
function stopMusic() {
    musicIsPlaying = false;
    currentBgm = null;
    if (musicTimer) {
        clearTimeout(musicTimer);
        musicTimer = null;
    }
    if (bgmFadeTimer) {
        clearTimeout(bgmFadeTimer);
        bgmFadeTimer = null;
    }
    stopRainSound();
}

// 平滑切换BGM
function switchBgm(bgmName) {
    if (currentBgm === bgmName) return;
    if (!musicEnabled) {
        currentBgm = bgmName;
        return;
    }
    
    initAudio();
    
    // 渐出当前音乐
    if (musicGainNode && musicIsPlaying) {
        musicGainNode.gain.setValueAtTime(musicGainNode.gain.value, audioCtx.currentTime);
        musicGainNode.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.001, audioCtx.currentTime + 1);
        
        bgmFadeTimer = setTimeout(() => {
            stopMusic();
            musicGainNode.gain.value = musicVolume;
            startBgm(bgmName, true);
        }, 1000);
    } else {
        startBgm(bgmName, true);
    }
}

// 雨声效果
function startRainSound() {
    if (!audioCtx || rainNoiseNode) return;
    
    const bufferSize = audioCtx.sampleRate * 2;
    const buffer = audioCtx.createBuffer(1, bufferSize, audioCtx.sampleRate);
    const data = buffer.getChannelData(0);
    for (let i = 0; i < bufferSize; i++) {
        data[i] = (Math.random() * 2 - 1) * 0.5;
    }
    
    rainNoiseNode = audioCtx.createBufferSource();
    rainNoiseNode.buffer = buffer;
    rainNoiseNode.loop = true;
    
    const filter = audioCtx.createBiquadFilter();
    filter.type = 'lowpass';
    filter.frequency.value = 1500;
    
    rainGainNode = audioCtx.createGain();
    rainGainNode.gain.value = 0.03;
    
    rainNoiseNode.connect(filter);
    filter.connect(rainGainNode);
    rainGainNode.connect(musicGainNode);
    
    rainNoiseNode.start();
}

function stopRainSound() {
    if (rainNoiseNode) {
        rainNoiseNode.stop();
        rainNoiseNode = null;
    }
    rainGainNode = null;
}

// 开始播放音乐（兼容旧函数）
function startMusic() {
    if (!musicEnabled || musicIsPlaying) return;
    initAudio();
    // 默认播放游戏BGM
    startBgm('game');
}

// ========== 音量控制 ==========

function setMusicVolume(value) {
    musicVolume = parseFloat(value);
    if (musicGainNode) {
        musicGainNode.gain.value = musicVolume;
    }
    localStorage.setItem('farm_music_volume', musicVolume);
}

function setSfxVolume(value) {
    sfxVolume = parseFloat(value);
    if (sfxGainNode) {
        sfxGainNode.gain.value = sfxVolume;
    }
    localStorage.setItem('farm_sfx_volume', sfxVolume);
}

function toggleMusic(enabled) {
    playClickSound();
    musicEnabled = enabled;
    localStorage.setItem('farm_music_enabled', musicEnabled);
    if (enabled) {
        if (game && game.started) {
            startBgm('game');
        }
    } else {
        stopMusic();
    }
}

function toggleSfx(enabled) {
    playClickSound();
    sfxEnabled = enabled;
    localStorage.setItem('farm_sfx_enabled', sfxEnabled);
}

// ========== 设置面板 ==========

// 切换BGM风格
function selectBgmStyle(styleName, clickedBtn) {
    playClickSound();
    if (currentBgm === styleName) return;
    
    // 更新按钮状态
    document.querySelectorAll('.bgm-btn').forEach(btn => {
        btn.classList.remove('active');
    });
    if (clickedBtn) clickedBtn.classList.add('active');
    
    // 保存选择
    localStorage.setItem('farm_bgm_style', styleName);
    
    // 切换音乐
    if (musicEnabled && musicIsPlaying) {
        switchBgm(styleName);
    } else {
        currentBgm = styleName;
    }
}

function toggleSettings() {
    playClickSound();
    const overlay = document.getElementById('settings-overlay');
    if (overlay.style.display === 'flex') {
        closeSettings();
    } else {
        document.getElementById('music-toggle').checked = musicEnabled;
        document.getElementById('sfx-toggle').checked = sfxEnabled;
        document.getElementById('music-volume').value = musicVolume;
        document.getElementById('sfx-volume').value = sfxVolume;
        
        // 同步BGM风格选中状态
        const savedStyle = localStorage.getItem('farm_bgm_style') || currentBgm || 'game';
        document.querySelectorAll('.bgm-btn').forEach(btn => {
            btn.classList.remove('active');
            if (btn.getAttribute('onclick').includes(savedStyle)) {
                btn.classList.add('active');
            }
        });
        
        overlay.style.display = 'flex';
    }
}

function closeSettings() {
    document.getElementById('settings-overlay').style.display = 'none';
}

// 加载音频设置
function loadAudioSettings() {
    const savedMusicVol = localStorage.getItem('farm_music_volume');
    if (savedMusicVol !== null) {
        musicVolume = parseFloat(savedMusicVol);
    }
    
    const savedSfxVol = localStorage.getItem('farm_sfx_volume');
    if (savedSfxVol !== null) {
        sfxVolume = parseFloat(savedSfxVol);
    }
    
    const savedMusicEnabled = localStorage.getItem('farm_music_enabled');
    if (savedMusicEnabled !== null) {
        musicEnabled = savedMusicEnabled === 'true';
    }
    
    const savedSfxEnabled = localStorage.getItem('farm_sfx_enabled');
    if (savedSfxEnabled !== null) {
        sfxEnabled = savedSfxEnabled === 'true';
    }
    
    // 加载保存的BGM风格
    const savedBgmStyle = localStorage.getItem('farm_bgm_style');
    if (savedBgmStyle) {
        currentBgm = savedBgmStyle;
    }
}

// 页面加载时监听第一次点击，自动初始化音频
document.addEventListener('click', function initAudioOnFirstClick() {
    initAudio();
    document.removeEventListener('click', initAudioOnFirstClick);
}, { once: true });

// 获取随机文案
function getRandomFlavor(type) {
    const flavors = LOG_FLAVORS[type];
    if (!flavors || flavors.length === 0) return '';
    return flavors[Math.floor(Math.random() * flavors.length)];
}

// ==================== 游戏状态 ====================
let game = null;
let storyPage = 0;
let modalCallback = null;
let currentMainTab = 'fields'; // 当前主标签
let currentShopTab = 'seeds'; // 当前商店子标签：默认显示种子（玩家刚进来买种子最重要）

// ==================== 初始化 ====================
window.onload = function() {
    loadAudioSettings();
    loadGameSpeed();
    
    // 检测是否通过 file:// 协议打开（会导致 localStorage 不稳定，存档丢失）
    if (window.location.protocol === 'file:') {
        console.warn('【警告】通过 file:// 打开HTML文件，localStorage 可能无法正常工作，导致存档刷新后丢失。');
        console.warn('请通过 http://localhost:8082/farm_game.html 访问游戏，存档才能正常保存。');
    }
    
    // 检查localStorage是否可用
    if (!isLocalStorageAvailable()) {
        console.warn('localStorage不可用，存档功能受限。请使用设置中的导出/导入功能备份存档。');
    }
    
    // 检查存档
    const saved = localStorage.getItem(SAVE_KEY);
    if (saved) {
        try {
            game = JSON.parse(saved);
            fixSaveData(); // 存档兼容处理
            showGame();
            startGameLoop();
            
            // 计算并显示离线收益
            setTimeout(() => {
                try {
                    const reward = calculateOfflineReward();
                    if (reward) {
                        showOfflineReward(reward);
                        saveGame(); // 保存更新后的状态
                    }
                } catch(e) {
                    console.error('离线收益计算失败', e);
                }
            }, 500);
            
            showToast('📂 已加载存档，第' + (game.totalDay || game.day) + '天', 'good');
            return;
        } catch(e) {
            console.error('存档读取失败', e);
            // 存档读取失败，尝试修复
            try {
                if (game) {
                    fixSaveData();
                    showGame();
                    startGameLoop();
                    showToast('⚠️ 存档已修复，继续游戏', 'warn');
                    saveGame();
                    return;
                }
            } catch(e2) {
                console.error('存档修复失败', e2);
            }
            showToast('⚠️ 存档读取失败，开始新游戏', 'bad');
            game = null;
        }
    }
    // 新玩家，显示故事
    showStory();
};

// ==================== 开头故事 ====================
function showStory() {
    document.getElementById('story-container').style.display = 'flex';
    storyPage = 0;
    updateStoryPage();
    
    // 检测是否通过 file:// 打开，显示警告
    if (window.location.protocol === 'file:') {
        const warning = document.getElementById('file-warning');
        if (warning) warning.style.display = 'block';
    }
}

function updateStoryPage() {
    const page = STORY_PAGES[storyPage];
    document.getElementById('story-emoji').textContent = page.emoji;
    document.getElementById('story-title').textContent = page.title;
    
    let html = '';
    page.texts.forEach(t => {
        html += `<div class="story-text">${t}</div>`;
    });
    document.getElementById('story-text').innerHTML = html;

    // 背景色
    const container = document.getElementById('story-container');
    if (page.warm) {
        container.classList.add('warm');
    } else {
        container.classList.remove('warm');
    }

    // 动画
    const pageEl = document.getElementById('story-page');
    pageEl.classList.remove('active');
    setTimeout(() => {
        pageEl.classList.add('active');
    }, 50);
}

function nextStoryPage() {
    playPageFlipSound();
    initAudio();
    
    storyPage++;
    if (storyPage >= STORY_PAGES.length) {
        skipStory();
        return;
    }
    
    // 根据故事进度切换BGM
    if (storyPage < 6) {
        // 前半段城市回忆部分，灰暗低沉
        startBgm('gloomy');
        // 疲惫的演唱
        playStorySinging('tired', 0.8);
    } else if (storyPage === 6) {
        // 第6页决定离职，开始转折
        switchBgm('warm');
        // 惊讶/开心的演唱
        playStorySinging('surprised', 1.0);
    } else {
        // 后半段乡村部分，欢快
        playStorySinging('happy', 1.2);
    }
    
    updateStoryPage();
}

function skipStory() {
    playClickSound();
    document.getElementById('story-container').style.display = 'none';
    
    // 检查是否有存档，有存档直接加载，不进入模式选择
    const save = localStorage.getItem('farm_game_save_v1');
    if (save) {
        loadGame();
        showGame();
        startGameLoop();
        showToast('📂 已加载存档，第' + (game.totalDay || game.day) + '天', 'good');
    } else {
        showSelectMode();
    }
}

// ==================== 开局选择 ====================
function showSelectMode() {
    document.getElementById('select-container').style.display = 'flex';
    document.body.classList.add('select-open');
}

function selectMode(mode) {
    playClickSound();
    showModal(
        '确认选择',
        `确定选择【${getModeName(mode)}】吗？选择后无法更改。`,
        () => {
            initGame(mode);
            closeModal();
            document.getElementById('select-container').style.display = 'none';
            document.body.classList.remove('select-open');
            showGame();
            startGameLoop();
        }
    );
}

function getModeName(mode) {
    const names = { easy: '归隐田园', normal: '耕读传家', hard: '富甲一方' };
    return names[mode] || mode;
}
