// ==================== 离线收益 ====================
function calculateOfflineReward() {
    if (!game || !game.lastSaveTimestamp) return null;
    
    const now = Date.now();
    const offlineMs = now - game.lastSaveTimestamp;
    const offlineSeconds = Math.max(0, offlineMs / 1000);
    
    // 离线太短（小于30秒）不显示
    if (offlineSeconds < 30) return null;
    
    // 获取游戏速度
    const speed = gameSpeed || 1;
    
    // 计算游戏内过去了多少小时 (1秒=2游戏小时，与在线一致)
    const gameHours = offlineSeconds * 2 * speed;
    
    // 最多离线7天游戏时间（无论离线多久，最多推进7天）
    // 避免玩家离线太久导致游戏内时间跳跃过大
    const MAX_OFFLINE_DAYS = 7; // 最多7天
    const maxGameHours = MAX_OFFLINE_DAYS * 24; // 168游戏小时
    const actualGameHours = Math.min(gameHours, maxGameHours);
    
    // 是否达到上限
    const capped = gameHours > maxGameHours;
    
    // 计算游戏天数
    const gameDays = Math.floor(actualGameHours / 24);
    const remainingHours = Math.floor(actualGameHours % 24);
    
    // 记录离线前的状态
    const beforeFields = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(game.fields));
    const beforeStamina = game.stamina;
    const beforeMoney = game.money;
    const beforeSeason = game.season;
    
    // 推进游戏时间
    // 确保totalDay有初始值，避免fallback时因game.day已改变而计算错误
    if (!game.totalDay) game.totalDay = game.day;
    game.time += remainingHours;
    game.day += gameDays;
    game.totalDay += gameDays;
    
    // 处理跨天
    let daysPassed = 0;
    while (game.time >= 24) {
        game.time -= 24;
        game.day += 1;
        game.totalDay += 1;
        daysPassed++;
        // 重置每日操作
        game.dailyActions = {exercise: 0, chat: 0, fish: 0, read: 0, foraging: 0, sideHustle: 0};
        game.dailyProcessed = {};
        // 村民每天帮你干活（浇水除草）
        if (game.hiredWorker && NPC_DATA[game.hiredWorker]) {
            const npc = NPC_DATA[game.hiredWorker];
            const workerDays = game.day - (game.lastWorkerWaterDay || game.day - 1);
            if (npc.skills && npc.skills.includes('water') && workerDays >= 1) {
                game.fields.forEach(field => {
                    if (field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle' && field.stage !== 'mature') {
                        field.lastWaterDay = game.day;
                    }
                });
                game.lastWorkerWaterDay = game.day;
            }
            const weedDays = game.day - (game.lastWorkerWeedDay || game.day - 3);
            if (npc.skills && npc.skills.includes('weed') && weedDays >= 3) {
                game.fields.forEach(field => {
                    if (field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle' && field.stage !== 'mature') {
                        field.lastWeedDay = game.day;
                    }
                });
                game.lastWorkerWeedDay = game.day;
            }
        }
        // 每天吃饭扣钱
        const mealCost = 15; // 与在线一致
        if (game.money >= mealCost) {
            game.money -= mealCost;
        } else {
            game.money = 0;
            game.stamina = Math.max(0, game.stamina - 10);
            game.health = Math.max(0, game.health - 2);
        }
        // 自动化设备离线运行
        if (game.automation) {
            for (const [deviceId, level] of Object.entries(game.automation)) {
                if (level <= 0) continue;
                const device = AUTOMATION_DATA[deviceId];
                if (!device) continue;
                
                if (deviceId === 'sprinkler') {
                    const maxFields = level;
                    game.fields.forEach((field, idx) => {
                        if (idx < maxFields && field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle' && field.stage !== 'mature') {
                            field.lastWaterDay = game.day;
                        }
                    });
                }
                if (deviceId === 'weeder') {
                    game.fields.forEach(field => {
                        if (field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle' && field.stage !== 'mature') {
                            field.lastWeedDay = game.day;
                        }
                    });
                }
                if (deviceId === 'autoFeeder' && game.animals) {
                    for (const animals of Object.values(game.animals)) {
                        animals.forEach(animal => {
                            animal.weight = Math.min(100, (animal.weight || 50) + 1);
                        });
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        // 检查季节变化（28天/季）
        if (game.day > 28) {
            advanceSeason();
        }
        // 推进加工任务
        if (game.processingJobs && game.processingJobs.length > 0) {
            updateProcessingJobs();
        }
        // 作物生长
        if (typeof growCrops === 'function') {
            growCrops();
        }
        
        // ===== 离线自动收获成熟作物 =====
        game.fields.forEach((field) => {
            if (field.crop && field.stage === 'mature') {
                const cropData = CROP_DATA[field.crop];
                let yield_ = cropData.baseYield;
                const levelBonus = { '新手档': 1.0, '进阶档': 1.15, '精英档': 1.35, '终极档': 1.6 };
                yield_ *= levelBonus[field.level] || 1.0;
                const cropSkillLevel =(game.skills.cropFamiliarity && game.skills.cropFamiliarity.level) || 0;
                if (cropSkillLevel > 0) yield_ *= (1 + cropSkillLevel * 0.03);
                if (field.fertilized) {
                    yield_ *= (field.fertilizerType === 'organic' ? 1.08 : 1.05);
                }
                const daysSinceWeed = game.day - field.lastWeedDay;
                if (daysSinceWeed < 7) yield_ *= 1.08;
                const daysSinceWater = game.day - field.lastWaterDay;
                if (daysSinceWater < 3) yield_ *= 1.05;
                if (cropData.type === 'sweet') {
                    if (field.turnedVine1) yield_ *= 1.05;
                    if (field.turnedVine2) yield_ *= 1.05;
                }
                if (field.yieldBonus) yield_ *= (1 + field.yieldBonus);
                if (field.yieldLoss) yield_ *= Math.max(0.1, 1 - field.yieldLoss);
                if (game.currentSeasonBonus) yield_ *= (1 + game.currentSeasonBonus);
                yield_ *= (0.9 + Math.random() * 0.2);
                yield_ = Math.max(0, Math.floor(yield_));
                
                const storageCap = game.storageCapacity || 2000;
                const currentStorage = Object.values(game.crops || {}).reduce((sum, v) => sum + (v || 0), 0);
                let actualYield = yield_;
                if (currentStorage + yield_ > storageCap) {
                    actualYield = Math.max(0, storageCap - currentStorage);
                }
                if (cropData.type === 'rice') game.crops.rice = (game.crops.rice || 0) + actualYield;
                else if (cropData.type === 'sweet') game.crops.sweet = (game.crops.sweet || 0) + actualYield;
                else if (cropData.type === 'wheat') game.crops.wheat = (game.crops.wheat || 0) + actualYield;
                else if (cropData.type === 'corn') game.crops.corn = (game.crops.corn || 0) + actualYield;
                else if (cropData.type === 'soybean') game.crops.soybean = (game.crops.soybean || 0) + actualYield;
                else if (cropData.type === 'potato') game.crops.potato = (game.crops.potato || 0) + actualYield;
                else if (cropData.type === 'peanut') game.crops.peanut = (game.crops.peanut || 0) + actualYield;
                else if (cropData.type === 'pepper') game.crops.pepper = (game.crops.pepper || 0) + actualYield;
                else if (cropData.type === 'cabbage') game.crops.cabbage = (game.crops.cabbage || 0) + actualYield;
                else if (cropData.type === 'radish') game.crops.radish = (game.crops.radish || 0) + actualYield;
                else if (cropData.type === 'eggplant') game.crops.eggplant = (game.crops.eggplant || 0) + actualYield;
                else if (cropData.type === 'garlic') game.crops.garlic = (game.crops.garlic || 0) + actualYield;
                
                if (!game.stats) game.stats = {};
                game.stats.totalHarvest = (game.stats.totalHarvest || 0) + actualYield;
                
                let cropExp = 6;
                const npcCropExpBonus = (typeof getNpcBonus === 'function') ? getNpcBonus('cropExpGain') : 0;
                if (npcCropExpBonus > 0) cropExp = Math.floor(cropExp * (1 + npcCropExpBonus));
                if (typeof addSkillExp === 'function') addSkillExp('cropFamiliarity', cropExp);
                
                const rpGain = Math.floor(actualYield / 100);
                if (rpGain > 0) game.researchPoints += rpGain;
                
                field.crop = null;
                field.stage = 'idle';
                field.step = 0;
                field.growProgress = 0;
                field.plantedDay = 0;
                field.prepared = true;
                field.fertilized = false;
                field.fertilizerType = null;
                field.yieldLoss = 0;
                field.yieldBonus = 0;
                field.turnedVine1 = false;
                field.turnedVine2 = false;
            }
        });
        
        // ===== 离线自动种植 =====
        game.fields.forEach((field) => {
            if (field.stage === 'idle' && field.prepared) {
                const seasonCrops = Object.keys(CROP_DATA).filter(key => CROP_DATA[key].season === game.season);
                for (const cropKey of seasonCrops) {
                    if (game.seeds[cropKey] > 0) {
                        game.seeds[cropKey]--;
                        field.crop = cropKey;
                        field.stage = 'seedling';
                        field.step = 1;
                        field.growProgress = 0;
                        field.plantedDay = game.day;
                        field.lastWaterDay = game.day;
                        field.lastWeedDay = game.day;
                        field.fertilized = false;
                        field.fertilizerType = null;
                        field.yieldLoss = 0;
                        field.yieldBonus = 0;
                        field.turnedVine1 = false;
                        field.turnedVine2 = false;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
        });
        
        // 触发新的一天逻辑（但不触发事件，避免离线时事件爆炸）
        // 只处理：天气变化、雇佣的村民、宠物等
        if (typeof changeWeather === 'function') {
            changeWeather();
        }
    }
    
    // 处理季节变化（28天/季）
    while (game.day > 28) {
        advanceSeason();
    }
    
    // 作物生长（剩余小时）
    if (typeof growCrops === 'function') {
        growCrops();
    }
    
    // 推进加工任务（剩余小时）
    if (game.processingJobs && game.processingJobs.length > 0) {
        updateProcessingJobs();
    }
    
    // 体力恢复
    const regenRate = getStaminaRegenRate();
    const totalRegen = actualGameHours * regenRate;
    game.stamina = Math.min(game.maxStamina, game.stamina + totalRegen);
    
    // 计算成熟的作物
    const maturedCrops = [];
    game.fields.forEach((field, idx) => {
        if (field.crop && field.stage === 'mature' && beforeFields[idx].stage !== 'mature') {
            maturedCrops.push({
                fieldIdx: idx,
                crop: field.crop,
                cropName:(CROP_DATA[field.crop] && CROP_DATA[field.crop].name) || '作物'
            });
        }
    });
    
    // 计算已雇佣村民帮你干的活
    const workerActions = [];
    if (game.hiredWorker && NPC_DATA[game.hiredWorker]) {
        const npc = NPC_DATA[game.hiredWorker];
        const npcName = npc.name;
        let wateredCount = 0;
        let weededCount = 0;
        game.fields.forEach(field => {
            if (field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle' && field.stage !== 'mature') {
                if (field.lastWaterDay > ((beforeFields[game.fields.indexOf(field)] && beforeFields[game.fields.indexOf(field)].lastWaterDay) || 0)) {
                    wateredCount++;
                }
                if (field.lastWeedDay > ((beforeFields[game.fields.indexOf(field)] && beforeFields[game.fields.indexOf(field)].lastWeedDay) || 0)) {
                    weededCount++;
                }
            }
        });
        if (wateredCount > 0) {
            workerActions.push(`${npcName}帮你浇了${wateredCount}块地`);
        }
        if (weededCount > 0) {
            workerActions.push(`${npcName}帮你除了${weededCount}块地的草`);
        }
    }
    
    // 计算房租扣除（季节变化时）
    let rentDeducted = 0;
    if (beforeSeason !== game.season) {
        const houseData = HOUSE_DATA[game.house];
        if (houseData && houseData.rent > 0) {
            rentDeducted = houseData.rent;
        }
    }
    
    // 计算加工坊离线产出
    const processingOutput = [];
    if (game.processedItems) {
        const beforeProcessed = beforeFields._processedItems || {};
        // 这个不太准确，跳过详细对比，只显示当前加工状态
    }
    
    // 格式化离线时间
    let offlineText = '';
    const offlineMinutes = Math.floor(offlineSeconds / 60);
    if (offlineMinutes < 60) {
        offlineText = `${offlineMinutes}分钟`;
    } else {
        const hours = Math.floor(offlineMinutes / 60);
        const mins = offlineMinutes % 60;
        offlineText = `${hours}小时${mins}分钟`;
    }
    
    // 游戏内时间文本
    let gameTimeText = '';
    if (gameDays > 0) {
        gameTimeText = `${gameDays}天${remainingHours}小时`;
    } else {
        gameTimeText = `${remainingHours}小时`;
    }
    
    // 离线自动销售所有库存作物
    let totalOfflineSell = 0;
    Object.keys(game.crops || {}).forEach(cropType => {
        const amount = game.crops[cropType] || 0;
        if (amount > 0) {
            const price = getSeasonPrice(cropType);
            let sellBonusTotal = game.sellBonus || 0;
            const npcSellBonus = (typeof getNpcBonus === 'function') ? getNpcBonus('sellPrice') : 0;
            if (npcSellBonus > 0) sellBonusTotal += npcSellBonus;
            const finalPrice = price * (1 + sellBonusTotal);
            const money = Math.floor(amount * finalPrice);
            game.crops[cropType] = 0;
            game.money += money;
            totalOfflineSell += money;
            if (!game.stats) game.stats = {};
            game.stats.totalSell = (game.stats.totalSell || 0) + money;
            game.stats.totalEarned = (game.stats.totalEarned || 0) + money;
        }
    });
    
    return {
        offlineText,
        gameTimeText,
        maturedCrops,
        staminaGained: Math.floor(game.stamina - beforeStamina),
        moneyChange: game.money - beforeMoney,
        workerActions,
        rentDeducted,
        seasonChanged: beforeSeason !== game.season,
        capped: gameHours > maxGameHours,
        totalOfflineSell
    };
}

function showOfflineReward(reward) {
    if (!reward) return;
    
    let content = `<div style="text-align: center; padding: 10px 0;">`;
    content += `<div style="font-size: 48px; margin-bottom: 16px;">🌙</div>`;
    content += `<div style="font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 12px; color: #2c3e50;">回来了？村里一切挺好</div>`;
    content += `<div style="color: #7f8c8d; margin-bottom: 20px;">你走了大概 ${reward.offlineText}</div>`;
    content += `<div style="background: #f8f9fa; border-radius: 12px; padding: 16px; margin-bottom: 16px;">`;
    content += `<div style="font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 12px; color: #2c3e50;">⏰ 村里已经过了 ${reward.gameTimeText}</div>`;
    
    // 成熟的作物
    if (reward.maturedCrops.length > 0) {
        content += `<div style="margin-top: 12px; padding-top: 12px; border-top: 1px solid #e9ecef;">`;
        content += `<div style="font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 8px; color: #27ae60;">🌾 地里成熟的作物</div>`;
        reward.maturedCrops.forEach(crop => {
            content += `<div style="color: #27ae60;">第${crop.fieldIdx + 1}块田 - ${crop.cropName}</div>`;
        });
        content += `</div>`;
    }
    
    // 体力恢复
    if (reward.staminaGained > 0) {
        content += `<div style="margin-top: 12px; padding-top: 12px; border-top: 1px solid #e9ecef;">`;
        content += `<div style="color: #3498db;">💪 歇了这么久，体力回满了 +${reward.staminaGained}</div>`;
        content += `</div>`;
    }
    
    // 村民帮忙
    if (reward.workerActions && reward.workerActions.length > 0) {
        content += `<div style="margin-top: 12px; padding-top: 12px; border-top: 1px solid #e9ecef;">`;
        content += `<div style="font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 8px; color: #9b59b6;">🧑‍🌾 雇的村民帮你干了点活</div>`;
        reward.workerActions.forEach(action => {
            content += `<div style="color: #9b59b6;">${action}</div>`;
        });
        content += `</div>`;
    }
    
    // 金钱变化
    if (reward.moneyChange !== 0) {
        const moneyColor = reward.moneyChange >= 0 ? '#27ae60' : '#e74c3c';
        const moneyIcon = reward.moneyChange >= 0 ? '💰' : '💸';
        content += `<div style="margin-top: 12px; padding-top: 12px; border-top: 1px solid #e9ecef;">`;
        content += `<div style="color: ${moneyColor};">${moneyIcon} 兜里钱变了：${reward.moneyChange >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${reward.moneyChange}元</div>`;
        if (reward.rentDeducted > 0) {
            content += `<div style="color: #e67e22; font-size: 13px;">（换季交了${reward.rentDeducted}块房租）</div>`;
        }
        if (reward.totalOfflineSell > 0) {
            content += `<div style="color: #27ae60; font-size: 13px;">💹 顺手卖了点作物，多赚了${reward.totalOfflineSell}块</div>`;
        }
        content += `</div>`;
    }
    
    // 季节变化
    if (reward.seasonChanged) {
        content += `<div style="margin-top: 12px; padding-top: 12px; border-top: 1px solid #e9ecef;">`;
        content += `<div style="color: #e67e22; font-weight: bold;">🍂 换季了！${SEASON_NAMES[game.season]}来了</div>`;
        content += `</div>`;
    }
    
    if (reward.capped) {
        content += `<div style="margin-top: 12px; padding-top: 12px; border-top: 1px solid #e9ecef; color: #e67e22; font-size: 13px;">`;
        content += `💡 离线最多推进7天，记得常回村看看~`;
        content += `</div>`;
    }
    
    content += `</div>`;
    content += `</div>`;
    
    // 显示弹窗
    showModal('离线收益', content, null);
}


// ==================== 存档系统 ====================


function doExercise() {
    // 统一使用 exerciseToday 计数器（与UI和按钮状态一致）
    if (!game.exerciseToday) game.exerciseToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (game.exerciseToday.day !== game.day) game.exerciseToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    if (game.exerciseToday.count >= 3) { addLog('今天已经锻炼过了，胳膊都酸了，明天再练吧', 'warn'); return; }
    if (game.stamina < 20) { addLog('累得不行了，先吃点东西或睡一觉恢复体力再来吧', 'warn'); return; }
    game.stamina -= 20;
    game.health = Math.min(game.maxHealth, game.health + 2);
    game.exerciseToday.count++;
    game.dailyActions.exercise++;
    addLog('你锻炼了一会，身体更结实了，健康+2', 'action');
    // 任务检查：第一次锻炼
    if (!game.quests.q18) {
        game.quests.q18 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q18', 80, '✅ 任务完成：强身健体，奖励80元');
    }
    updateDailyButtons();
    updateUI();
}

function doChat() {
    // 统一使用 visitToday 计数器（与UI和按钮状态一致）
    if (!game.visitToday) game.visitToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (game.visitToday.day !== game.day) game.visitToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    if (game.visitToday.count >= 3) { addLog('今天串了太多门了，人家都烦了', 'warn'); return; }
    if (game.stamina < 10) { addLog('累得不行了，先吃点东西或睡一觉恢复体力再来吧', 'warn'); return; }
    game.stamina -= 10;
    // 只从已认识的NPC中随机选择
    const npcKeys = Object.keys(NPC_DATA).filter(k => isNpcKnown(k));
    if (npcKeys.length === 0) {
        addLog('👋 去村里转了转，但还不认识什么人...', 'action');
        updateDailyButtons();
        updateUI();
        return;
    }
    const npcKey = npcKeys[Math.floor(Math.random() * npcKeys.length)];
    const npcData = NPC_DATA[npcKey];
    const npcName = npcData ? npcData.name : npcKey;
    const add = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
    const oldFriendship = game.npcs[npcKey] || 0;
    game.npcs[npcKey] = Math.min(100, oldFriendship + add);
    if (!game.friendship[npcKey]) game.friendship[npcKey] = 0;
    game.friendship[npcKey] = Math.min(100, game.friendship[npcKey] + add);
    game.visitToday.count++;
    game.dailyActions.chat++;
    addLog(`你去${npcName}家串了个门，好感+${add}`, 'action');
    // 任务检查：第一次和村民聊天（通过串门也触发）
    if (!game.quests.q9) {
        game.quests.q9 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q9', 50, '✅ 任务完成：初次交流，奖励50元');
    }
    // 检查是否达到友好
    const friendship = game.npcs[npcKey] || 0;
    if (!game.quests.q15 && friendship >= 40) {
        game.quests.q15 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q15', 300, '✅ 任务完成：打成一片，奖励300元');
    }
    updateDailyButtons();
    updateUI();
}

function doFish() {
    // 统一使用 fishToday 计数器（与UI和按钮状态一致）
    if (!game.fishToday) game.fishToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (game.fishToday.day !== game.day) game.fishToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    if (game.fishToday.count >= 2) { addLog('今天钓过鱼了，明天再钓吧', 'warn'); return; }
    if (game.stamina < 15) { addLog('累得不行了，先吃点东西或睡一觉恢复体力再来吧', 'warn'); return; }
    game.stamina -= 15;
    const fishCount = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3);
    game.fishToday.count++;
    game.dailyActions.fish++;
    if (fishCount > 0) {
        game.items.fish = (game.items.fish || 0) + fishCount;
        addLog(`你钓了${fishCount}条鱼，晚上可以炖鱼吃了`, 'action');
    } else {
        addLog('你钓了半天，鱼都跑了，什么都没钓到', 'action');
    }
    // 任务检查：第一次钓鱼
    if (!game.quests.q19) {
        game.quests.q19 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q19', 80, '✅ 任务完成：垂钓之乐，奖励80元');
    }
    updateDailyButtons();
    updateUI();
    renderBackpack();
}

function doRead() {
    // 统一使用 studyToday 计数器（与UI和按钮状态一致）
    if (!game.studyToday) game.studyToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (game.studyToday.day !== game.day) game.studyToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    if (game.studyToday.count >= 2) { addLog('今天看过书了，明天再看吧', 'warn'); return; }
    if (game.stamina < 10) { addLog('累得不行了，先吃点东西或睡一觉恢复体力再来吧', 'warn'); return; }
    game.stamina -= 10;
    const skills = Object.keys(game.skills);
    const skillId = skills[Math.floor(Math.random() * skills.length)];
    let add = Math.floor(Math.random() * 4) + 5;
    
    // 林晓雨NPC好感度增加读书经验
    const npcReadBonus = (typeof getNpcBonus === 'function') ? getNpcBonus('readExpBonus') : 0;
    if (npcReadBonus > 0) {
        add = Math.floor(add * (1 + npcReadBonus));
    }
    
    game.skills[skillId].exp += add;
    game.studyToday.count++;
    game.dailyActions.read++;
    addLog(`你看了会书，${game.skills[skillId].name}经验+${add}`, 'action');
    // 检查升级
    while (game.skills[skillId].exp >= game.skills[skillId].expNeeded && game.skills[skillId].level < 15) {
        game.skills[skillId].exp -= game.skills[skillId].expNeeded;
        game.skills[skillId].level++;
        game.skills[skillId].expNeeded = Math.floor(game.skills[skillId].expNeeded * 1.3);
        addLog('🎉 你的' + game.skills[skillId].name + '升级到了Lv' + game.skills[skillId].level + '！', 'milestone');
    }
    updateDailyButtons();
    updateUI();
}

function updateDailyButtons() {
    // 统一使用 xxxToday 计数器，与 renderPlayerPanel 和 doXxx 函数一致
    if (!game.exerciseToday) game.exerciseToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (game.exerciseToday.day !== game.day) game.exerciseToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    if (!game.visitToday) game.visitToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (game.visitToday.day !== game.day) game.visitToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    if (!game.fishToday) game.fishToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (game.fishToday.day !== game.day) game.fishToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    
    document.getElementById('btn-exercise').disabled = (game.exerciseToday.count >= 3) || game.stamina < 20;
    document.getElementById('btn-chat').disabled = (game.visitToday.count >= 3) || game.stamina < 10;
    document.getElementById('btn-fish').disabled = (game.fishToday.count >= 2) || game.stamina < 15;
    document.getElementById('btn-foraging').disabled = game.dailyActions.foraging >= 1 || game.stamina < 15;
}

function renderBackpack() {
    const list = document.getElementById('backpack-list');
    if (!list) return;
    list.innerHTML = '';
    let hasItem = false;
    for (const itemId in game.items) {
        if (game.items[itemId] > 0 && ITEM_EFFECTS[itemId]) {
            hasItem = true;
            const item = ITEM_EFFECTS[itemId];
            const div = document.createElement('div');
            div.style.cssText = 'padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #d4b896; border-radius: 8px; background: #fff9f0; text-align: center;';
            div.innerHTML = `
                <div style="font-size: 24px;">${item.icon}</div>
                <div style="margin: 5px 0; font-size: 14px;">${item.name} ×${game.items[itemId]}</div>
                <button onclick="useItem('${itemId}')" style="padding: 4px 8px; font-size: 12px; background: #8b5a2b; color: white; border: none; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer;">使用</button>
            `;
            list.appendChild(div);
        }
    }
    if (!hasItem) {
        list.innerHTML = '<div style="color: #888; text-align: center; grid-column: 1/-1; padding: 20px;">背包空空的，什么都没有</div>';
    }
}

function useItem(itemId) {
    if (!game.items[itemId] || game.items[itemId] <= 0) return;
    const item = ITEM_EFFECTS[itemId];
    game.items[itemId]--;
    // 加效果
    if (item.use.stamina) game.stamina = Math.min(game.maxStamina, game.stamina + item.use.stamina);
    if (item.use.health) game.health = Math.min(game.maxHealth, game.health + item.use.health);
    if (item.use.mood) game.mood = Math.min(100, game.mood + item.use.mood);
    addLog(`使用了${item.icon}${item.name}`, 'item');
    renderBackpack();
    updateDailyButtons();
    updateUI();
}

function saveGame() {
    if (!game) return;
    try {
        // 自动备份：轮转保存最近3个存档
        try {
            const b2 = localStorage.getItem(SAVE_KEY + '_backup_2');
            if (b2) localStorage.setItem(SAVE_KEY + '_backup_3', b2);
            const b1 = localStorage.getItem(SAVE_KEY + '_backup_1');
            if (b1) localStorage.setItem(SAVE_KEY + '_backup_2', b1);
            const current = localStorage.getItem(SAVE_KEY);
            if (current) localStorage.setItem(SAVE_KEY + '_backup_1', current);
        } catch(e) {}
        
        game.lastSaveTimestamp = Date.now();
        const saveData = JSON.stringify(game);
        localStorage.setItem(SAVE_KEY, saveData);
    } catch(e) {
        console.error('存档保存失败', e);
    }
    
    if (typeof checkMilestones === 'function' && game.day > 0) {
        try { checkMilestones(); } catch(e) {}
    }
    
    if (typeof renderSidebarQuests === 'function') {
        try { renderSidebarQuests(); } catch(e) {}
    }
}

// 导出存档为文件（支持file://协议）
function exportSaveFile() {
    if (!game) {
        showToast('没有游戏进度可导出', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    try {
        const saveData = JSON.stringify(game, null, 2);
        const blob = new Blob([saveData], { type: 'application/json' });
        const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = url;
        a.download = `farm_save_${game.totalDay || game.day}day_${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.json`;
        document.body.appendChild(a);
        a.click();
        document.body.removeChild(a);
        URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
        showToast('✅ 存档已导出！', 'good');
    } catch(e) {
        console.error('导出失败', e);
        showToast('导出失败', 'bad');
    }
}

// 从文件导入存档
function importSaveFile(input) {
    const file = input.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = function(e) {
        try {
            const data = JSON.parse(e.target.result);
            if (!data || !data.day) {
                showToast('无效的存档文件', 'bad');
                return;
            }
            if (confirm('导入存档将覆盖当前进度，确定继续？')) {
                game = data;
                fixSaveData();
                saveGame();
                updateUI();
                showToast('✅ 存档导入成功！', 'good');
                addLog('📂 导入了存档文件', 'info');
            }
        } catch(err) {
            showToast('存档文件解析失败', 'bad');
            console.error('导入失败', err);
        }
        input.value = '';
    };
    reader.readAsText(file);
}
function manualSave() {
    saveGame();
    playClickSound();
    showToast('存档已保存！', 'good');
}

function manualLoad() {
    if (confirm('确定要读取存档吗？当前进度将丢失。')) {
        loadGame();
        playClickSound();
        showToast('存档已读取！', 'info');
    }
}


// 手动保存
function saveGameManual() {
    if (!game) {
        showToast('没有游戏进度可保存', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    saveGame();
    if (typeof playClickSound === 'function') {
        playClickSound();
    }
    showToast('✅ 存档已保存！', 'good');
}

// 手动读取
function loadGameManual() {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem(SAVE_KEY);
    if (!saved) {
        showToast('没有找到存档', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    try {
        game = JSON.parse(saved);
        fixSaveData();
        if (game && typeof updateUI === 'function') {
            updateUI();
            if (typeof playClickSound === 'function') {
                playClickSound();
            }
            showToast('✅ 存档已读取！', 'good');
            if (typeof addLog === 'function') {
                addLog('📂 读取了存档', 'info');
            }
            
            // 更新页签解锁状态
            if (typeof updateTabLockStatus === 'function') {
                updateTabLockStatus();
            }
            
            // 计算并显示离线收益
            setTimeout(() => {
                const reward = calculateOfflineReward();
                if (reward) {
                    showOfflineReward(reward);
                    saveGame();
                }
            }, 500);
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('读取失败:', e);
        showToast('存档读取失败', 'bad');
    }
}

// 存档兼容处理：给旧存档补上缺失的字段
function fixSaveData() {
    if (!game) return;
    
    // 补全核心游戏状态（极旧存档可能缺少这些基础字段）
    if (game.mode === undefined) game.mode = 'normal';
    if (game.money === undefined) game.money = 1500;
    if (game.maxHealth === undefined) game.maxHealth = 100;
    if (game.health === undefined) game.health = Math.floor(game.maxHealth * 0.6);
    if (game.maxStamina === undefined) game.maxStamina = 100;
    if (game.stamina === undefined) game.stamina = Math.floor(game.maxStamina * 0.5);
    if (game.day === undefined) game.day = 1;
    if (game.totalDay === undefined) game.totalDay = game.day || 1;
    if (game.season === undefined) game.season = 'spring';
    if (game.time === undefined) game.time = 6;
    if (game.disasterRate === undefined) game.disasterRate = 1.0;
    
    // 补全items和dailyActions（只补全缺失字段，不覆盖当天数据）
    if (!game.items) game.items = {};
    if (!game.dailyActions) game.dailyActions = {};
    if (game.dailyActions.exercise === undefined) game.dailyActions.exercise = 0;
    if (game.dailyActions.chat === undefined) game.dailyActions.chat = 0;
    if (game.dailyActions.fish === undefined) game.dailyActions.fish = 0;
    if (game.dailyActions.read === undefined) game.dailyActions.read = 0;
    if (game.dailyActions.foraging === undefined) game.dailyActions.foraging = 0;
    if (game.dailyActions.sideHustle === undefined) game.dailyActions.sideHustle = 0;
    if (game.items.organicFertilizer === undefined) game.items.organicFertilizer = 0;
    if (game.items.fertilizer === undefined) game.items.fertilizer = 0;
    if (game.items.pesticide === undefined) game.items.pesticide = 0;
    if (game.items.bun === undefined) game.items.bun = 0;
    if (game.items.medicine === undefined) game.items.medicine = 0;
    
    // 补全堆肥相关
    if (game.composting === undefined) game.composting = false;
    if (game.compostStartDay === undefined) game.compostStartDay = 0;
    if (game.bankDeposit === undefined) game.bankDeposit = 0;
    if (game.agriTechLevel === undefined) game.agriTechLevel = 0;
    if (game.agriTechEffects === undefined) game.agriTechEffects = {};
    
    // 补全技能
    if (!game.skills) {
        game.skills = {
            cropFamiliarity: { level: 0, exp: 0 },
            fieldManagement: { level: 0, exp: 0 },
            toolMastery: { level: 0, exp: 0 },
            composting: { level: 0, exp: 0 },
            fishingMastery: { level: 0, exp: 0 }
        };
    } else {
        if (!game.skills.cropFamiliarity) game.skills.cropFamiliarity = { level: 0, exp: 0 };
        if (!game.skills.fieldManagement) game.skills.fieldManagement = { level: 0, exp: 0 };
        if (!game.skills.toolMastery) game.skills.toolMastery = { level: 0, exp: 0 };
        if (!game.skills.composting) game.skills.composting = { level: 0, exp: 0 };
        if (!game.skills.fishingMastery) game.skills.fishingMastery = { level: 0, exp: 0 };
    }
    
    // 补全科技相关
    if (game.researchPoints === undefined) game.researchPoints = 0;
    if (!game.unlockedTechs) game.unlockedTechs = {};
    
    // 补全NPC里程碑
    if (!game.npcMilestones) game.npcMilestones = {};
    
    // 补全加工相关
    if (!game.processedItems) game.processedItems = { riceGrain: 0, driedSweetPotato: 0, driedFish: 0, fishBall: 0, fishSoup: 0, polishedRice: 0, riceWine: 0, riceCake: 0, sweetPotatoStarch: 0, sweetPotatoNoodles: 0, flour: 0, noodles: 0, tofu: 0, soyMilk: 0, cornOil: 0, potatoChips: 0, potatoStarch: 0, peanutOil: 0, peanutCandy: 0, chiliSauce: 0, chiliOil: 0, honey: 0, mushroom: 0, pickle: 0 };
    if (!game.builtProcessing) game.builtProcessing = {};
    if (!game.dailyProcessed) game.dailyProcessed = {};
    if (!game.cookedFoods) game.cookedFoods = {};
    if (!game.communityProjects) game.communityProjects = {};
    if (!game.collection) game.collection = {};
    
    // 补全新存档字段（新增加工品、页签解锁、任务弹窗等）
    if (!game.unlockedTabs) game.unlockedTabs = {};
    if (!game.pendingQuestRewards) game.pendingQuestRewards = [];
    if (game.metSunmiaoqing === undefined) game.metSunmiaoqing = false;
    if (game.metChenyang === undefined) game.metChenyang = false;
    if (game.metLinxiaoyu === undefined) game.metLinxiaoyu = false;
    if (game.hasBookBonus === undefined) game.hasBookBonus = false;
    if (game.hasMedicineKit === undefined) game.hasMedicineKit = false;
    if (game.zhaoBonusNoticed === undefined) game.zhaoBonusNoticed = false;
    if (game.storageCapacity === undefined) game.storageCapacity = 2000;
    if (game.totalDay === undefined) game.totalDay = game.day || 1;
    
    // 修复：如果村小学已扩建完成但林老师未解锁，自动解锁
    if (game.communityProjects && game.communityProjects.village_school && game.communityProjects.village_school.completed && !game.metLinxiaoyu) {
        game.metLinxiaoyu = true;
        if (!game.npcs.linxiaoyu) game.npcs.linxiaoyu = 0;
        if (!game.friendship.linxiaoyu) game.friendship.linxiaoyu = 0;
        game.npcs.linxiaoyu = Math.max(game.npcs.linxiaoyu, 10);
        game.friendship.linxiaoyu = Math.max(game.friendship.linxiaoyu, 10);
    }
    
    // 补全采集相关
    if (!game.foragingItems) game.foragingItems = {};
    if (!game.mineInventory) game.mineInventory = { stone: 0, coal: 0, iron: 0, copper: 0, crystal: 0 };
    
    // 补全畜牧
    if (!game.animals) game.animals = {};
    if (!game.animalProducts) game.animalProducts = {};
    
    // 补全果园
    if (!game.orchard) game.orchard = [];
    if (!game.fruits) game.fruits = {};
    if (!game.mineStats) game.mineStats = { totalDigs: 0, deepestLayer: 0 };
    
    // 补全NPC相关（迁移旧的对象格式）
    if (!game.npcs) game.npcs = {};
    // 如果旧存档的game.npcs是对象格式 { favor: 5, met: true }，需要迁移为数字格式
    for (const npcKey in game.npcs) {
        const val = game.npcs[npcKey];
        if (val && typeof val === 'object' && val.favor !== undefined) {
            game.npcs[npcKey] = val.favor;
        }
    }
    if (!game.friendship) game.friendship = {};
    // 将game.npcs中的好感度同步到game.friendship（确保里程碑和加成效果正确）
    for (const npcKey in game.npcs) {
        if (typeof game.npcs[npcKey] === 'number' && game.npcs[npcKey] > 0) {
            game.friendship[npcKey] = game.npcs[npcKey];
        }
    }
    if (!game.lastChatDay) game.lastChatDay = {};
    if (!game.lastGiftDay) game.lastGiftDay = {};
    if (!game.lastDialogue) game.lastDialogue = {};
    
    // 补全日常活动记录（visit/fish/study）
    if (!game.visitToday) game.visitToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (!game.fishToday) game.fishToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (!game.studyToday) game.studyToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    
    // 补全出售加成
    if (game.sellBonus === undefined) game.sellBonus = 0;
    
    // 补全雇佣村民相关
    if (game.hiredWorker === undefined) game.hiredWorker = null;
    if (game.hireStartDay === undefined) game.hireStartDay = 0;
    if (game.lastWorkerWaterDay === undefined) game.lastWorkerWaterDay = 0;
    if (game.lastWorkerWeedDay === undefined) game.lastWorkerWeedDay = 0;
    if (game.pestReduction === undefined) game.pestReduction = 0;
    
    if (!game.neighborHelp) game.neighborHelp = {};
    if (game.marketVisited === undefined) game.marketVisited = false;
    
    if (game.automation === undefined) game.automation = {};
    
    // 补全里程碑和统计相关
    if (!game.milestones) game.milestones = {};
    
    // 补全加工相关（第2处，确保所有加工品字段存在）
    if (!game.processedItems) {
        game.processedItems = {
            riceGrain: 0, driedSweetPotato: 0, driedFish: 0, fishBall: 0, fishSoup: 0,
            polishedRice: 0, riceWine: 0, riceCake: 0, sweetPotatoStarch: 0, sweetPotatoNoodles: 0,
            flour: 0, noodles: 0, tofu: 0, soyMilk: 0, cornOil: 0,
            potatoChips: 0, potatoStarch: 0, peanutOil: 0, peanutCandy: 0,
            chiliSauce: 0, chiliOil: 0, honey: 0, mushroom: 0, pickle: 0
        };
    } else {
        // 确保新加工品字段存在
        const processedDefaults = {
            flour: 0, noodles: 0, tofu: 0, soyMilk: 0, cornOil: 0,
            potatoChips: 0, potatoStarch: 0, peanutOil: 0, peanutCandy: 0,
            chiliSauce: 0, chiliOil: 0, honey: 0, mushroom: 0, pickle: 0
        };
        for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(processedDefaults)) {
            if (game.processedItems[k] === undefined) game.processedItems[k] = v;
        }
    }
    if (!game.builtProcessing) game.builtProcessing = {};
    
    // 将旧版 builtProcessing（true/false）转换为等级
    if (game.builtProcessing) {
        for (const key of Object.keys(game.builtProcessing)) {
            if (game.builtProcessing[key] === true) {
                game.builtProcessing[key] = 1;
            }
        }
    }
    if (!game.dailyProcessed) game.dailyProcessed = {};
    
    // 补全科技相关
    if (game.researchPoints === undefined) game.researchPoints = 0;
    if (!game.unlockedTechs) game.unlockedTechs = {};
    if (!game.stats) {
        game.stats = {
            totalHarvest: 0,
            totalSell: 0,
            totalEarned: 0,
            totalFish: 0,
            totalForage: 0,
            totalProcessed: 0,
            totalCooked: 0,
            totalDigs: 0,
            daysPlayed: 0
        };
    } else {
        if (game.stats.totalHarvest === undefined) game.stats.totalHarvest = 0;
        if (game.stats.totalSell === undefined) game.stats.totalSell = 0;
        if (game.stats.totalEarned === undefined) game.stats.totalEarned = 0;
        if (game.stats.totalFish === undefined) game.stats.totalFish = 0;
        if (game.stats.totalForage === undefined) game.stats.totalForage = 0;
        if (game.stats.totalProcessed === undefined) game.stats.totalProcessed = 0;
        if (game.stats.totalCooked === undefined) game.stats.totalCooked = 0;
        if (game.stats.totalDigs === undefined) game.stats.totalDigs = 0;
        if (game.stats.daysPlayed === undefined) game.stats.daysPlayed = 0;
    }
    
    // 补全成就
    if (!game.achievements) game.achievements = {};
    
    // 补全宠物相关（新格式：宠物未领养时为空对象）
    if (!game.pets) game.pets = {};
    if (!game.petEvents) {
        game.petEvents = {
            strayCatVisits: 0,
            dogUnlocked: false,
            catUnlocked: false
        };
    }
    if (game.petPoop === undefined) game.petPoop = 0;
    
    // 迁移旧版 pets 格式（旧版 {have: false} 对象需要清理）
    if (game.pets) {
        for (const key in game.pets) {
            const pet = game.pets[key];
            if (pet && typeof pet === 'object' && pet.have === false) {
                // 旧版未领养格式，删除该键
                delete game.pets[key];
            } else if (pet && typeof pet === 'object' && pet.have === true) {
                // 旧版已领养格式，确保新字段存在
                if (pet.affection === undefined) pet.affection = pet.friendship || 10;
                if (pet.lastFedDay === undefined) pet.lastFedDay = 0;
                if (pet.lastPettedDay === undefined) pet.lastPettedDay = 0;
                if (pet.lastPlayedDay === undefined) pet.lastPlayedDay = 0;
            }
        }
        
        // 迁移旧版 dog/cat 键名到 dahuang/ahua
        if (game.pets.dog && !game.pets.dahuang) {
            game.pets.dahuang = game.pets.dog;
            delete game.pets.dog;
        }
        if (game.pets.cat && !game.pets.ahua) {
            game.pets.ahua = game.pets.cat;
            delete game.pets.cat;
        }
        
        // 确保所有已领养宠物数据完整
        for (const petKey of ['dahuang', 'ahua']) {
            if (game.pets[petKey]) {
                const pet = game.pets[petKey];
                if (pet.affection === undefined) pet.affection = pet.friendship || 10;
                if (pet.friendship === undefined) pet.friendship = pet.affection || 10;
                if (pet.lastFedDay === undefined) pet.lastFedDay = 0;
                if (pet.lastPettedDay === undefined) pet.lastPettedDay = 0;
                if (pet.lastPlayedDay === undefined) pet.lastPlayedDay = 0;
            }
        }
    }
    
    // 补全田地字段
    if (!game.fields || !Array.isArray(game.fields)) {
        game.fields = [{
            id: 1, level: '新手档', type: 'paddy', crop: null, stage: 'idle',
            step: 0, growProgress: 0, plantedDay: 0, lastWaterDay: 0, lastWeedDay: 0,
            fertilized: false, fertilizerType: null, turnedVine1: false, turnedVine2: false,
            prepared: false, yieldLoss: 0, yieldBonus: 0
        }];
    }
    if (game.fields) {
        game.fields.forEach(field => {
            if (field.id === undefined) field.id = 1;
            if (field.level === undefined) field.level = '新手档';
            if (field.type === undefined) field.type = 'paddy';
            if (field.crop === undefined) field.crop = null;
            if (field.stage === undefined) field.stage = 'idle';
            if (field.step === undefined) field.step = 0;
            if (field.growProgress === undefined) field.growProgress = 0;
            if (field.plantedDay === undefined) field.plantedDay = 0;
            if (field.lastWaterDay === undefined) field.lastWaterDay = 0;
            if (field.lastWeedDay === undefined) field.lastWeedDay = 0;
            if (field.fertilized === undefined) field.fertilized = false;
            if (field.fertilizerType === undefined) field.fertilizerType = null;
            if (field.prepared === undefined) field.prepared = false;
            if (field.turnedVine1 === undefined) field.turnedVine1 = false;
            if (field.turnedVine2 === undefined) field.turnedVine2 = false;
            if (field.yieldLoss === undefined) field.yieldLoss = 0;
            if (field.yieldBonus === undefined) field.yieldBonus = 0;
            
            // 迁移旧版作物ID（不带季节后缀）为新版格式
            if (field.crop && !field.crop.includes('_')) {
                const cropType = field.crop; // rice, sweet, wheat, corn, soybean
                const season = field.season || game.season || 'spring';
                const newCropId = cropType + '_' + season;
                // 检查新ID是否存在，若不存在则尝试其他季节
                if (CROP_DATA[newCropId]) {
                    field.crop = newCropId;
                } else {
                    // 尝试找到该作物类型的第一个可用季节
                    const availableKeys = Object.keys(CROP_DATA).filter(k => k.startsWith(cropType + '_'));
                    if (availableKeys.length > 0) {
                        field.crop = availableKeys[0];
                    } else {
                        // 无法匹配，清空作物
                        field.crop = null;
                        field.stage = 'idle';
                        field.growProgress = 0;
                        field.step = 0;
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }
    
    // 补全天气
    if (!game.weather) game.weather = 'sunny';
    if (game.weatherDuration === undefined) game.weatherDuration = 0;
    
    // 补全技能字段（name和expNeeded）
    const SKILL_DEFAULTS = {
        cropFamiliarity: { name: '作物熟悉度', expNeeded: 3 },
        fieldManagement: { name: '田间管理', expNeeded: 3 },
        toolMastery: { name: '工具精通', expNeeded: 3 },
        composting: { name: '堆肥技巧', expNeeded: 3 },
        fishingMastery: { name: '钓鱼精通', expNeeded: 3 }
    };
    if (!game.skills) game.skills = {};
    for (const [key, defaults] of Object.entries(SKILL_DEFAULTS)) {
        if (!game.skills[key]) game.skills[key] = { level: 0, exp: 0 };
        if (game.skills[key].name === undefined) game.skills[key].name = defaults.name;
        if (game.skills[key].expNeeded === undefined) game.skills[key].expNeeded = defaults.expNeeded;
    }
    
    // 补全事件
    if (game.currentEvent === undefined) game.currentEvent = null;
    if (!game.eventHistory) game.eventHistory = [];
    if (game.nextSeasonBonus === undefined) game.nextSeasonBonus = 0;
    if (game.currentSeasonBonus === undefined) game.currentSeasonBonus = 0;
    
    // 补全加工任务队列
    if (!game.processingJobs) game.processingJobs = [];
    
    // 补全新手教程进度
    if (game.tutorialStep === undefined) game.tutorialStep = 0;
    
    // 补全心情值
    if (game.mood === undefined) game.mood = 50;

    // 补全任务：基于 QUEST_DATA 动态补全所有缺失键，确保存档与 UI 一致
    if (game.quests) {
        Object.keys(QUEST_DATA || {}).forEach(key => {
            if (game.quests[key] === undefined) game.quests[key] = false;
        });
    } else {
        game.quests = {};
        Object.keys(QUEST_DATA || {}).forEach(key => { game.quests[key] = false; });
    }
    
    // 补全声望
    if (game.reputation === undefined) game.reputation = 0;
    
    // 补全库存
    if (!game.crops) game.crops = { rice: 0, sweet: 0, wheat: 0, corn: 0, soybean: 0, potato: 0, peanut: 0, pepper: 0, cabbage: 0, radish: 0, eggplant: 0, garlic: 0 };
    if (!game.seeds) game.seeds = { rice_spring: 0, rice_summer: 0, sweet_spring: 0, sweet_autumn: 0, wheat_spring: 0, wheat_autumn: 0, corn_summer: 0, soybean_spring: 0, soybean_summer: 0, potato_spring: 0, potato_autumn: 0, peanut_summer: 0, pepper_summer: 0, pepper_autumn: 0, cabbage_autumn: 0, cabbage_winter: 0, radish_autumn: 0, radish_winter: 0, eggplant_summer: 0, eggplant_autumn: 0, garlic_autumn: 0, garlic_spring: 0 };
    if (!game.items) game.items = { fertilizer: 0, pesticide: 0, bun: 0, medicine: 0, organicFertilizer: 0 };
    
    // 补全锻炼相关
    if (!game.exerciseToday) game.exerciseToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    
    // 补全建筑
    if (!game.buildings) game.buildings = {};
    
    // 补全日常活动
    if (!game.dailyActivities) game.dailyActivities = {};
    
    // 补全房屋
    if (!game.house) game.house = '新手房';
    
    // 补全农具
    if (!game.tools) game.tools = [];
    
    // 补全justStarted（加载旧存档时跳过第一次事件）
    if (game.justStarted === undefined) game.justStarted = true;
    
    // 补全鱼塘库存
    if (!game.fishInventory) game.fishInventory = {};
    
    // 补全堆肥总天数（跨季节用）
    if (game.compostStartTotalDay === undefined) game.compostStartTotalDay = 0;
    
    // 补全社区建设加成字段
    if (game.staminaRegenBonus === undefined) game.staminaRegenBonus = 0;
    if (game.foragingBonus === undefined) game.foragingBonus = 0;
    if (game.researchPointBonus === undefined) game.researchPointBonus = 0;
    if (game.reputationBonus === undefined) game.reputationBonus = 0;
    if (game.healthRegenBonus === undefined) game.healthRegenBonus = 0;
    if (game.medicineDiscount === undefined) game.medicineDiscount = 0;
    if (game.tickCount === undefined) game.tickCount = 0;
    
    // 补全日常活动记录
    if (!game.visitToday) game.visitToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (!game.fishToday) game.fishToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (!game.studyToday) game.studyToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (!game.exerciseToday) game.exerciseToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    
    // 补全最后保存时间戳（离线收益用）
    if (game.lastSaveTimestamp === undefined) game.lastSaveTimestamp = Date.now();
    
    // 补全started（音乐切换用）
    if (game.started === undefined) game.started = true;
    
    // 补全村长合作项目
    if (!game.villageProjects) game.villageProjects = {};
    
    // 补全农家乐
    if (!game.farmStay) game.farmStay = { level: 0, guests: 0, reputation: 0 };
    if (!game.farmStayDishes) game.farmStayDishes = {};
}

function loadGame() {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem(SAVE_KEY);
    if (saved) {
        game = JSON.parse(saved);
        return true;
    }
    // 尝试从备份恢复
    for (let i = 1; i <= 3; i++) {
        const backup = localStorage.getItem(SAVE_KEY + '_backup_' + i);
        if (backup) {
            try {
                game = JSON.parse(backup);
                localStorage.setItem(SAVE_KEY, backup);
                if (typeof showToast === 'function') {
                    showToast('📂 已从备份' + i + '恢复存档', 'warn');
                }
                return true;
            } catch(e) {}
        }
    }
    return false;
}

function restartGame() {
    playClickSound();
    showModal(
        '重新开始',
        '确定要重新开始吗？所有进度将丢失，无法恢复。',
        () => {
            localStorage.removeItem(SAVE_KEY);
            game = null;
            closeModal();
            location.reload();
        }
    );
}

// ==================== 存档导出/导入 ====================
function exportSave() {
    if (!game) {
        showToast('当前没有游戏存档！', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    const saveData = localStorage.getItem(SAVE_KEY);
    if (!saveData) {
        showToast('存档不存在！', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    // 尝试多种方式复制到剪贴板
    function tryCopy(text) {
        // 方式1: navigator.clipboard（需要HTTPS）
        if (navigator.clipboard && navigator.clipboard.writeText) {
            return navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(() => true).catch(() => false);
        }
        return Promise.resolve(false);
    }
    
    function fallbackCopy(text) {
        // 方式2: document.execCommand('copy')
        const textarea = document.createElement('textarea');
        textarea.value = text;
        textarea.style.position = 'fixed';
        textarea.style.left = '-9999px';
        document.body.appendChild(textarea);
        textarea.select();
        try {
            const success = document.execCommand('copy');
            document.body.removeChild(textarea);
            return success;
        } catch (e) {
            document.body.removeChild(textarea);
            return false;
        }
    }
    
    tryCopy(saveData).then(success => {
        if (success) {
            showToast('📋 存档已复制到剪贴板！请到另一台设备粘贴导入', 'good');
        } else if (fallbackCopy(saveData)) {
            showToast('📋 存档已复制到剪贴板！请到另一台设备粘贴导入', 'good');
        } else {
            // 最终降级：显示弹窗让用户手动复制
            showModal(
                '导出存档',
                '<div style="text-align:left;"><p>请长按复制以下存档代码，保存到备忘录或微信收藏：</p><textarea readonly style="width:100%;height:120px;margin-top:10px;padding:8px;border:1px solid #d4b896;border-radius:6px;font-size:12px;resize:none;" onclick="this.select()">' + saveData.substring(0, 500) + '...</textarea><p style="font-size:11px;color:#999;margin-top:8px;">💡 提示：点击文本框即可全选，然后复制</p></div>',
                null
            );
        }
    });
}

function importSavePrompt() {
    document.getElementById('save-import-area').style.display = 'block';
    document.getElementById('save-import-text').value = '';
    document.getElementById('save-import-text').focus();
}

function cancelImportSave() {
    document.getElementById('save-import-area').style.display = 'none';
}

function doImportSave() {
    const text = document.getElementById('save-import-text').value.trim();
    if (!text) {
        showToast('请输入存档代码！', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    try {
        const data = JSON.parse(text);
        // 验证基本结构（修复了原来的逻辑bug：!data.money === undefined 永远为false）
        if (!data || data.day === undefined || data.money === undefined) {
            showToast('存档格式不正确！缺少关键字段', 'bad');
            return;
        }
        game = data;
        fixSaveData();
        localStorage.setItem(SAVE_KEY, JSON.stringify(game));
        document.getElementById('save-import-area').style.display = 'none';
        showToast('✅ 存档导入成功！即将刷新...', 'good');
        // 刷新页面以应用新存档
        setTimeout(() => {
            location.reload();
        }, 1500);
    } catch (e) {
        showToast('存档解析失败，请检查粘贴的内容是否完整！', 'bad');
        console.error('Import save error:', e);
    }
}

// 检查localStorage是否可用
function isLocalStorageAvailable() {
    try {
        const test = '__test__';
        localStorage.setItem(test, test);
        localStorage.removeItem(test);
        return true;
    } catch (e) {
        return false;
    }
}

// ==================== 游戏主循环 ====================
let gameLoopInterval = null;
let gamePaused = false; // 暂停状态
let gameSpeed = 1; // 游戏速度倍率

function setGameSpeed(speed) {
    gameSpeed = speed;
    localStorage.setItem('farm_game_speed', speed);
    
    // 更新按钮选中状态（设置弹窗内的按钮）
    document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(btn => {
        btn.classList.remove('active');
        if (parseInt(btn.textContent) === speed) {
            btn.classList.add('active');
        }
    });
    // 更新顶部的时间流速按钮
    document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn-top').forEach(btn => {
        btn.classList.remove('active');
        if (parseInt(btn.textContent) === speed) {
            btn.classList.add('active');
        }
    });
    
    // 重启游戏循环（如果未暂停）
    if (game && !gamePaused) {
        if (gameLoopInterval) {
            startGameLoop();
        }
    }
    
    if (typeof playClickSound === 'function') {
        playClickSound();
    }
    if (typeof showToast === 'function') {
        showToast(`⏱️ 游戏速度已切换为 ${speed}x`, 'good');
    }
    
    // 确保游戏循环在运行
    if (game && !gameLoopInterval) {
        startGameLoop();
    }
}

function loadGameSpeed() {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem('farm_game_speed');
    if (saved) {
        gameSpeed = parseInt(saved) || 1;
    }
    // 更新所有时间流速按钮的选中状态
    setTimeout(() => {
        // 设置弹窗内的按钮
        document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(btn => {
            if (parseInt(btn.textContent) === gameSpeed) {
                btn.classList.add('active');
            } else {
                btn.classList.remove('active');
            }
        });
        // 顶部的时间流速按钮
        document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn-top').forEach(btn => {
            if (parseInt(btn.textContent) === gameSpeed) {
                btn.classList.add('active');
            } else {
                btn.classList.remove('active');
            }
        });
    }, 100);
}

function togglePause() {
    if (!game) return;
    gamePaused = !gamePaused;
    
    const pauseBtn = document.getElementById('pause-btn');
    const clockEl = document.querySelector('.game-clock');
    const speedBtns = document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn-top');
    
    if (gamePaused) {
        // 暂停：停止循环，更新UI
        if (gameLoopInterval) {
            clearInterval(gameLoopInterval);
            gameLoopInterval = null;
        }
        if (pauseBtn) {
            pauseBtn.innerHTML = '▶️ 继续';
            pauseBtn.classList.add('paused');
            pauseBtn.title = '游戏已暂停，点击继续';
        }
        if (clockEl) clockEl.classList.add('paused');
        // 禁用速度按钮
        speedBtns.forEach(btn => btn.disabled = true);
        showToast('⏸️ 游戏已暂停', 'good');
    } else {
        // 继续：重启循环
        startGameLoop();
        if (pauseBtn) {
            pauseBtn.innerHTML = '⏸️ 暂停';
            pauseBtn.classList.remove('paused');
            pauseBtn.title = '点击暂停游戏时间';
        }
        if (clockEl) clockEl.classList.remove('paused');
        // 启用速度按钮
        speedBtns.forEach(btn => btn.disabled = false);
        showToast('▶️ 游戏继续', 'good');
    }
}

function startGameLoop() {
    // 自动种田模式已完全禁用，所有操作由玩家手动进行
    if (gameLoopInterval) clearInterval(gameLoopInterval);
    // 如果暂停则不启动循环
    if (gamePaused) {
        gameLoopInterval = null;
        return;
    }
    // 2秒 = 2游戏小时，24秒 = 1游戏天（比原来120秒/天快5倍）
    const baseInterval = 2000;
    const interval = baseInterval / gameSpeed;
    gameLoopInterval = setInterval(gameTick, interval);
    updateUI();
}

function advanceSeason() {
    if (game.day <= 28) return;
    
    const oldDay = game.day;
    game.day -= 28;
    const dayOffset = 28;
    
    const seasons = ['spring', 'summer', 'autumn', 'winter'];
    const idx = seasons.indexOf(game.season);
    game.season = seasons[(idx + 1) % 4];
    
    game.fields.forEach(field => {
        if (field.plantedDay > 0) field.plantedDay -= dayOffset;
    });
    
    let removedCount = 0;
    game.fields.forEach(field => {
        if (field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle') {
            const cropData = CROP_DATA[field.crop];
            if (cropData && cropData.season !== game.season) {
                field.crop = null;
                field.stage = 'idle';
                field.growProgress = 0;
                field.step = 0;
                field.prepared = false;
                field.fertilized = false;
                field.fertilizerType = null;
                field.yieldLoss = 0;
                field.yieldBonus = 0;
                removedCount++;
            }
        }
    });
    
    if (removedCount > 0) {
        addLog(`🍂 季节更替，${removedCount}块田里的作物因不适应新季节而枯萎了。`, 'bad');
    }
    
    game.currentSeasonBonus = game.nextSeasonBonus || 0;
    game.nextSeasonBonus = 0;
    if (game.currentSeasonBonus > 0) {
        addLog(`🌟 本季产量加成+${Math.floor(game.currentSeasonBonus * 100)}%！`, 'good');
    }
    addLog(`${SEASON_ICONS[game.season]} ${SEASON_NAMES[game.season]}来了。${getRandomFlavor('season')}`, 'info');
    
    // 租金扣除（改为按天扣除，降低前期压力）
    const houseData = HOUSE_DATA[game.house];
    if (houseData && houseData.rent > 0) {
        const dailyRent = Math.ceil(houseData.rent / 7); // 按周折算为日租
        if (game.money >= dailyRent) {
            game.money -= dailyRent;
            addLog(`🏠 今日房租${dailyRent}元已扣除。`, 'info');
        } else {
            game.money = 0;
            game.stamina = Math.max(0, game.stamina - 15);
            game.health = Math.max(0, game.health - 3);
            addLog(`🏠 拖欠房租！房东来催了，体力-15，健康-3。`, 'bad');
        }
    }
}

function gameTick() {
    // 游戏未正式开始时不执行
    if (!game || !gameLoopInterval) return;

    game.time += 2;
    
    // 体力恢复（每2小时恢复一次）
    const regenRate = getStaminaRegenRate();
    if (game.stamina < game.maxStamina) {
        game.stamina = Math.min(game.maxStamina, game.stamina + regenRate);
    }

    // 夜间（20:00~6:00）恢复加倍
    if (game.time >= 20 || game.time < 6) {
        if (game.stamina < game.maxStamina) {
            game.stamina = Math.min(game.maxStamina, game.stamina + regenRate);
        }
    }

    // 过了一天
    if (game.time >= 24) {
        game.time = 6;
        game.day++;
        game.totalDay = (game.totalDay || game.day) + 1;
        onNewDay();
    }

    // 季节变化
    advanceSeason();

    // 作物生长
    growCrops();
    
    // 推进加工任务进度
    updateProcessingJobs();
    
    // 防止浮点数累积
    roundGameState();
    
    // tickCount 初始化（确保判断前存在）
    if (!game.tickCount) game.tickCount = 0;
    game.tickCount++;
    
    // 每30秒保存一次，或新的一天立即保存
    const shouldSave = game.time === 6 || (game.tickCount % 6 === 0);
    if (shouldSave) {
        saveGame();
    }
    updateUI();
}

function getStaminaRegenRate() {
    const house = HOUSE_DATA[game.house];
    let rate = house ? house.staminaRegen : 15;
    // 每游戏小时恢复的体力值（除以4是为了平衡，避免恢复太快）
    let finalRate = rate / 4;
    
    // 科技体力恢复加成
    const techStaminaRegen = getTechBonus('staminaRegen');
    if (techStaminaRegen > 0) {
        finalRate *= (1 + techStaminaRegen);
    }
    
    // NPC好感度体力恢复加成（张婶）
    const npcStaminaRegen = getNpcBonus('staminaRegen');
    if (npcStaminaRegen > 0) {
        finalRate *= (1 + npcStaminaRegen);
    }
    
    // 社区建设加成（村口老井）
    if (game.staminaRegenBonus) {
        finalRate += game.staminaRegenBonus;
    }
    
    return Math.floor(finalRate);
}

function onNewDay() {
    // 刚进入游戏时不触发事件（避免加载存档后立刻弹出事件）
    if (game.justStarted) {
        game.justStarted = false;
    } else {
        // 触发夜间事件（前一天晚上发生的）
        if (typeof triggerNightEvent === 'function') {
            triggerNightEvent();
        }
    }
    // 游戏天数统计
    if (!game.stats) game.stats = {};
    game.stats.daysPlayed = (game.stats.daysPlayed || 0) + 1;
    
    // 检查成就
    checkAchievements();
    
    addLog(`🌅 第${game.totalDay || game.day}天 - ${getRandomFlavor('newDay')}`, 'info');
    
    // 每天早上检查是否有待领取的任务奖励
    if (game.pendingQuestRewards && game.pendingQuestRewards.length > 0) {
        setTimeout(() => {
            const overlay = document.getElementById('modal-overlay');
            if (!overlay || overlay.style.display !== 'flex') {
                showQuestRewardModal();
            }
        }, 500);
    }
    
    // 自动化设备每日运行
    if (game.automation) {
        for (const [deviceId, level] of Object.entries(game.automation)) {
            if (level <= 0) continue;
            const device = AUTOMATION_DATA[deviceId];
            if (!device) continue;
            
            if (deviceId === 'sprinkler') {
                // 自动灌溉：给所有田地浇水
                const maxFields = level; // Lv1=1块, Lv2=2块...
                let watered = 0;
                game.fields.forEach((field, idx) => {
                    if (idx < maxFields && field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle' && field.stage !== 'mature') {
                        field.lastWaterDay = game.day;
                        watered++;
                    }
                });
                if (watered > 0) {
                    addLog(`💧 ${device.name}自动浇了${watered}块地`, 'info');
                }
            }
            
            if (deviceId === 'weeder') {
                // 自动除草
                const weedInterval = Math.max(1, 4 - level); // Lv1=3天, Lv2=2天, Lv3=1天
                const daysSinceWeed = game.day - (game.lastAutoWeedDay || 0);
                if (daysSinceWeed >= weedInterval) {
                    let weeded = 0;
                    game.fields.forEach(field => {
                        if (field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle' && field.stage !== 'mature') {
                            field.lastWeedDay = game.day;
                            weeded++;
                        }
                    });
                    if (weeded > 0) {
                        game.lastAutoWeedDay = game.day;
                        addLog(`🌿 ${device.name}除了${weeded}块地的草`, 'info');
                    }
                }
            }
            
            if (deviceId === 'autoFeeder') {
                // 自动喂养：畜牧自动喂食，不消耗玩家手动操作
                if (game.animals) {
                    for (const [animalKey, animals] of Object.entries(game.animals)) {
                        if (animals.length === 0) continue;
                        const data = ANIMAL_DATA[animalKey];
                        if (!data) continue;
                        animals.forEach(animal => {
                            animal.weight = Math.min(100, (animal.weight || 50) + 1);
                        });
                    }
                    addLog(`🤖 ${device.name}自动喂养了所有牲口`, 'info');
                }
            }
            
            if (deviceId === 'harvester') {
                // 自动收割：收割成熟作物
                const maxHarvest = level * 2; // Lv1=2块, Lv2=4块, Lv3=全部
                let harvested = 0;
                game.fields.forEach((field, idx) => {
                    if (harvested >= maxHarvest && level < 3) return;
                    if (field.crop && field.stage === 'mature') {
                        // 执行收割逻辑
                        const cropData = CROP_DATA[field.crop];
                        if (cropData) {
                            let yield_ = cropData.baseYield;
                            const levelBonus = { '新手档': 1.0, '进阶档': 1.15, '精英档': 1.35, '终极档': 1.6 };
                            yield_ *= levelBonus[field.level] || 1.0;
                            yield_ = Math.max(0, Math.floor(yield_ * (0.9 + Math.random() * 0.2)));
                            
                            if (cropData.type === 'rice') game.crops.rice = (game.crops.rice || 0) + yield_;
                            else if (cropData.type === 'sweet') game.crops.sweet = (game.crops.sweet || 0) + yield_;
                            else if (cropData.type === 'wheat') game.crops.wheat = (game.crops.wheat || 0) + yield_;
                            else if (cropData.type === 'corn') game.crops.corn = (game.crops.corn || 0) + yield_;
                            else if (cropData.type === 'soybean') game.crops.soybean = (game.crops.soybean || 0) + yield_;
                            else if (cropData.type === 'potato') game.crops.potato = (game.crops.potato || 0) + yield_;
                            else if (cropData.type === 'peanut') game.crops.peanut = (game.crops.peanut || 0) + yield_;
                            else if (cropData.type === 'pepper') game.crops.pepper = (game.crops.pepper || 0) + yield_;
                            else if (cropData.type === 'cabbage') game.crops.cabbage = (game.crops.cabbage || 0) + yield_;
                            else if (cropData.type === 'radish') game.crops.radish = (game.crops.radish || 0) + yield_;
                            else if (cropData.type === 'eggplant') game.crops.eggplant = (game.crops.eggplant || 0) + yield_;
                            else if (cropData.type === 'garlic') game.crops.garlic = (game.crops.garlic || 0) + yield_;
                            
                            field.crop = null;
                            field.stage = 'idle';
                            field.step = 0;
                            field.growProgress = 0;
                            field.plantedDay = 0;
                            field.prepared = true;
                            harvested++;
                        }
                    }
                });
                if (harvested > 0) {
                    addLog(`🚜 ${device.name}自动收割了${harvested}块地的庄稼`, 'good');
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    // 每日吃饭消耗（现代社会农民也要吃饭）
    const mealCost = 15; // 一日三餐约15元
    if (game.money >= mealCost) {
        game.money -= mealCost;
        addLog(`🍚 吃饭花了${mealCost}元，体力恢复了一些`, 'info');
    } else {
        game.money = 0;
        game.stamina = Math.max(0, game.stamina - 10);
        game.health = Math.max(0, game.health - 2);
        addLog('😰 没钱吃饭了，今天饿了一整天，体力-10，健康-2', 'bad');
    }
    
    // 宠物每日饲料消耗
    if (game.pets) {
        for (const [petId, pet] of Object.entries(game.pets)) {
            if (!pet || !pet.owned) continue;
            const petData = PET_DATA[petId];
            if (!petData) continue;
            const foodCost = petData.dailyFoodCost || 0;
            if (foodCost > 0) {
                if (game.money >= foodCost) {
                    game.money -= foodCost;
                    addLog(`🐕 ${petData.name}的饲料费-${foodCost}元`, 'info');
                } else {
                    game.money = 0;
                    pet.affection = Math.max(0, (pet.affection || 0) - 2);
                    addLog(`🐕 ${petData.name}没饲料吃了，好感度-2`, 'bad');
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    // 房屋租金每日扣除（已租房）
    if (game.house && game.house.rent > 0) {
        const rent = game.house.rent;
        if (game.money >= rent) {
            game.money -= rent;
            addLog(`🏠 房屋租金-${rent}元`, 'info');
        } else {
            game.money = 0;
            addLog(`🏠 没钱交房租了！房东很不高兴...`, 'bad');
        }
    }
    
    // 农业科技效果应用
    if (game.agriTechEffects && game.agriTechEffects.autoGrowth) {
        // 所有田地自动生长
        game.fields.forEach(field => {
            if (field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle' && field.stage !== 'mature') {
                field.growProgress += game.agriTechEffects.autoGrowth * 0.1;
            }
        });
    }
    
    // 银行利息（每日结算）
    if (game.bankDeposit > 0) {
        const interest = Math.floor(game.bankDeposit * BANK_DATA.interestRate);
        game.bankDeposit += interest;
        addLog(`🏦 银行利息结算：存入${interest}元，当前存款${game.bankDeposit}元`, 'good');
    }
    
    // 社区建设加成 + 孙妙青NPC好感度（健康恢复）
    let totalHealthRegen = game.healthRegenBonus || 0;
    const npcHealthRegen = (typeof getNpcBonus === 'function') ? getNpcBonus('healthRegen') : 0;
    if (npcHealthRegen > 0) {
        totalHealthRegen += Math.floor(npcHealthRegen);
    }
    if (totalHealthRegen > 0 && game.health < game.maxHealth) {
        game.health = Math.min(game.maxHealth, game.health + totalHealthRegen);
    }
    
    // 重置每日加工上限
    game.dailyProcessed = {};
    
    // 重置每日活动记录
    game.visitToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    game.fishToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    game.studyToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    game.exerciseToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    
    // 天气变化
    changeWeather();
    
    // 雇佣的村民干活
    if (typeof processWorkerDaily === 'function') {
        processWorkerDaily();
    }
    
    // 邻里互助效果
    if (game.neighborHelp) {
        const totalFriendship = Object.values(game.friendship || {}).reduce((sum, v) => sum + (v || 0), 0);
        
        for (const [helpId, active] of Object.entries(game.neighborHelp)) {
            if (!active) continue;
            const help = NEIGHBOR_HELP_DATA[helpId];
            if (!help) continue;
            
            if (helpId === 'waterHelp' && game.day % 3 === 0) {
                let watered = 0;
                game.fields.forEach(field => {
                    if (field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle' && field.stage !== 'mature') {
                        field.lastWaterDay = game.day;
                        watered++;
                    }
                });
                if (watered > 0) addLog(`💧 邻居帮你浇了${watered}块地`, 'good');
            }
            
            if (helpId === 'weedHelp' && game.day % 5 === 0) {
                let weeded = 0;
                game.fields.forEach(field => {
                    if (field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle' && field.stage !== 'mature') {
                        field.lastWeedDay = game.day;
                        weeded++;
                    }
                });
                if (weeded > 0) addLog(`🌿 邻居帮你除了${weeded}块地的草`, 'good');
            }
            
            if (helpId === 'feedHelp' && game.animals) {
                for (const animals of Object.values(game.animals)) {
                    animals.forEach(animal => {
                        animal.weight = Math.min(100, (animal.weight || 50) + 2);
                    });
                }
                addLog(`🐷 邻居帮你喂了牲口，体重增长更快`, 'good');
            }
        }
    }
    
    // 重置集市访问状态
    game.marketVisited = false;
    
    // 加工坊自动加工（已改为手动，玩家需点击加工按钮）
    // if (typeof processDailyProcessing === 'function') {
    //     processDailyProcessing();
    // }
    
    // 随机事件（85%概率触发——对标某某宗女修修炼手札的高密度事件体验）
    if (!game.currentEvent && Math.random() < 0.85) {
        triggerRandomEvent();
    }
    
    // 检查任务
    checkQuests();
    
    // 检查里程碑（状态类里程碑）
    if (typeof checkMilestones === 'function') {
        checkMilestones();
    }
    
    // 宠物过天：重置互动次数
    if (game.pets) {
        Object.keys(game.pets).forEach(k => {
            if (!game.pets[k]) return; // 跳过空条目
            game.pets[k].petToday = 0;
            game.pets[k].fedToday = false;
        });
    }

    // 宠物好感度高了有概率带小礼物
    if (game.pets && Math.random() < 0.1) {
        const petGifts = [
            { name: '野果', icon: '🍎', text: '叼回来几个野果，也不知道从哪摘的。' },
            { name: '小田鼠', icon: '🐭', text: '抓了一只小田鼠放在门口，得意地冲你叫。' },
            { name: '漂亮石头', icon: '🪨', text: '叼回来一块亮晶晶的石头，放在你脚边。' },
            { name: '羽毛', icon: '🪶', text: '叼回来一根漂亮的鸟羽毛，炫耀似的在你面前晃。' },
            { name: '干树枝', icon: '🌿', text: '叼回来一根奇形怪状的树枝，一脸期待地看着你。' }
        ];
        const candidates = [];
        // 使用正确的键名 dahuang 和 ahua
        if (game.pets.dahuang && (game.pets.dahuang.affection || game.pets.dahuang.friendship || 0) >= 5) candidates.push('dahuang');
        if (game.pets.ahua && (game.pets.ahua.affection || game.pets.ahua.friendship || 0) >= 5) candidates.push('ahua');
        // 兼容旧版存档的 dog/cat 键名
        if (game.pets.dog && (game.pets.dog.affection || game.pets.dog.friendship || 0) >= 5) candidates.push('dahuang');
        if (game.pets.cat && (game.pets.cat.affection || game.pets.cat.friendship || 0) >= 5) candidates.push('ahua');
        if (candidates.length > 0) {
            const petId = candidates[Math.floor(Math.random() * candidates.length)];
            const gift = petGifts[Math.floor(Math.random() * petGifts.length)];
            const names = { dahuang: '大黄', ahua: '阿花' };
            game.mood = Math.min(100, (game.mood === undefined ? 50 : game.mood) + 3);
            addLog(`🎁 ${names[petId]}${gift.icon} ${gift.text} 心情+3`, 'pet');
        }
    }

    // 畜牧每日更新
    if (game.animals) {
        for (const [animalKey, animals] of Object.entries(game.animals)) {
            if (!animals || animals.length === 0) continue;
            const data = ANIMAL_DATA[animalKey];
            if (!data) continue;
            
            animals.forEach(animal => {
                animal.age++;
                animal.daysSinceProduct++;
                
                // 自动喂养（消耗作物）
                let canFeed = true;
                for (const [crop, amount] of Object.entries(data.dailyFeed)) {
                    if ((game.crops[crop] || 0) < amount) {
                        canFeed = false;
                        break;
                    }
                }
                
                if (canFeed) {
                    for (const [crop, amount] of Object.entries(data.dailyFeed)) {
                        game.crops[crop] -= amount;
                    }
                    animal.weight = Math.min(100, (animal.weight || 50) + 2);
                    
                    // 产出产品
                    if (data.product && animal.age >= data.growthDays && animal.daysSinceProduct >= data.productDays) {
                        animal.daysSinceProduct = 0;
                        const productAmount = Math.floor(data.productPrice / 5) + 1;
                        game.animalProducts[data.product] = (game.animalProducts[data.product] || 0) + productAmount;
                        addLog(`${data.emoji} ${animal.name} 产出了${data.productName} ${productAmount}个`, 'good');
                    }
                } else {
                    animal.weight = Math.max(10, (animal.weight || 50) - 1);
                    addLog(`${data.emoji} ${animal.name} 没吃饱，体重下降了`, 'bad');
                }
            });
        }
    }
    
    // 果园每日更新
    if (game.orchard) {
        game.orchard.forEach(tree => {
            if (tree.mature) {
                tree.daysSinceHarvest++;
                const data = ORCHARD_DATA[tree.type];
                if (data && tree.daysSinceHarvest >= 7) {
                    tree.ready = true;
                }
            } else {
                tree.growDays++;
                const data = ORCHARD_DATA[tree.type];
                if (data && tree.growDays >= data.growDays) {
                    tree.mature = true;
                    addLog(`${data.emoji} ${data.name} 成熟了，可以收获了！`, 'good');
                }
            }
        });
    }
    
    // 村长合作项目收益
    if (game.villageProjects) {
        for (const [key, level] of Object.entries(game.villageProjects)) {
            if (level <= 0) continue;
            const project = VILLAGE_PROJECTS[key];
            if (!project) continue;
            
            if (project.effect === 'dailyIncome') {
                const incomes = [50, 100, 200];
                const income = incomes[level - 1] || 0;
                game.money += income;
                addLog(`🏪 ${project.name} 今日收入 ${income} 元`, 'good');
            }
            if (project.effect === 'waterBonus') {
                // 灌溉水渠：所有田地自动浇水
                game.fields.forEach(field => {
                    if (field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle') {
                        field.lastWaterDay = game.day;
                    }
                });
            }
        }
    }
    
    // 农家乐每日收益
    if (game.farmStay && game.farmStay.level > 0) {
        const levelData = FARM_STAY_DATA.level[game.farmStay.level - 1];
        if (levelData) {
            // 随机客人数量
            const guests = Math.floor(Math.random() * levelData.maxGuests) + 1;
            const income = levelData.dailyIncome * guests;
            game.money += income;
            game.farmStay.guests = guests;
            addLog(`🏡 农家乐今日接待 ${guests} 位客人，收入 ${income} 元`, 'good');
        }
    }

    // 检查页签解锁
    if (typeof updateTabLockStatus === 'function') {
        updateTabLockStatus();
    }
    
    // 重置每日活动次数
    game.dailyActions = { exercise: 0, chat: 0, fish: 0, read: 0, foraging: 0, sideHustle: 0 };
    
    // 检查健康值是否归零
    if (typeof checkHealthDeath === 'function') {
        checkHealthDeath();
    }
}

function checkHealthDeath() {
    if (game.health <= 0) {
        // 健康归零——累倒了，不是死亡
        game.health = 1; // 健康值不会低于1
        game.stamina = Math.min(game.maxStamina, game.stamina + 30); // 强制休息恢复体力
        
        // 扣除医药费
        const medicalCost = 50;
        if (game.money >= medicalCost) {
            game.money -= medicalCost;
        } else {
            game.money = 0;
        }
        
        addLog('🏥 你累倒了！乡亲们把你送到村卫生所，休息了一天。医药费' + medicalCost + '元，体力恢复了一些。', 'warn');
        showToast('🏥 累倒了！注意休息，健康值已恢复。', 'warn');
        
        // 显示休息弹窗
        const restHtml = `
            <div style="text-align:center;padding:20px;">
                <div style="font-size:48px;margin-bottom:10px;">😵</div>
                <div style="font-size:18px;font-weight:bold;color:#e67e22;margin-bottom:15px;">累倒了...</div>
                <div style="font-size:14px;line-height:1.8;color:#555;margin-bottom:20px;text-align:left;">
                    你太拼了，身体发出了警报。乡亲们发现你昏倒在田里，赶紧把你送到村卫生所。<br><br>
                    王大夫给你输了液，叮嘱你注意劳逸结合。健康值已恢复，但记得多休息！
                </div>
                <div style="font-size:12px;color:#999;margin-bottom:10px;">医药费：${medicalCost}元 | 体力恢复：+30</div>
            </div>
        `;
        showModal('注意身体', restHtml, () => {
            closeModal();
        });
    }
}

function changeWeather() {
    if (!game.weather) game.weather = 'sunny';
    
    // 天气持续时间递减
    if (game.weatherDuration === undefined) game.weatherDuration = 0;
    game.weatherDuration--;
    
    // 天气到期或每天20%概率改变
    if (game.weatherDuration <= 0 || Math.random() < 0.2) {
        const available = SEASON_WEATHER[game.season] || ['sunny'];
        const nextWeather = available[Math.floor(Math.random() * available.length)];
        if (nextWeather !== game.weather) {
            game.weather = nextWeather;
            const w = WEATHER_DATA[nextWeather];
            addLog(`${w.emoji} 天气变为：${w.name}`, 'info');
        }
        const wData = WEATHER_DATA[game.weather];
        const minD = wData.duration[0];
        const maxD = wData.duration[1];
        game.weatherDuration = minD + Math.floor(Math.random() * (maxD - minD + 1));
    }
}
