// 检查是否有正在生长的作物
function hasGrowingCrops() {
    if (!game || !game.fields) return false;
    return game.fields.some(field => field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle' && field.stage !== 'mature');
}

// 触发随机事件
function triggerRandomEvent() {
    // 确保游戏已正式开始（不在模式选择或故事界面）
    const selectContainer = document.getElementById('select-container');
    const storyContainer = document.getElementById('story-container');
    if ((selectContainer && selectContainer.style.display !== 'none') ||
        (storyContainer && storyContainer.style.display !== 'none')) {
        return;
    }
    
    // 1. 先尝试触发故事事件
    const availableStoryEvents = STORY_EVENTS.filter(e => {
        // 天数检查（使用totalDay累计天数，避免季节切换重置）
        if (e.minDay !== undefined && e.minDay !== null && game.totalDay <= e.minDay) return false;
        if (e.maxDay !== undefined && e.maxDay !== null && game.totalDay >= e.maxDay) return false;
        
        // 季节检查
        if (e.seasons && e.seasons.length > 0 && !e.seasons.includes(game.season)) return false;
        
        // NPC好感检查
        if (e.requiresNpc) {
            if (!game.npcs[e.requiresNpc.id] || game.npcs[e.requiresNpc.id] < e.requiresNpc.minFavor) return false;
        }
        
        // 相遇标记检查
        if (e.requiresMet && !game[e.requiresMet]) return false;
        if (e.requiresNotMet && game[e.requiresNotMet]) return false;
        
        // 作物检查
        if (e.requiresCrop && !hasGrowingCrops()) return false;
        
        // 宠物检查
        if (e.requiresPet) {
            if (e.requiresPet === 'both') {
                if (!game.pets || !game.pets.ahua || !game.pets.dahuang) return false;
            } else if (!game.pets || !game.pets[e.requiresPet]) {
                return false;
            }
        }
        
        return true;
    });
    
    if (availableStoryEvents.length > 0) {
        // 按概率加权选择
        let totalWeight = 0;
        availableStoryEvents.forEach(e => {
            totalWeight += e.probability || 0;
        });
        
        if (totalWeight > 0 && Math.random() < totalWeight) {
            let random = Math.random() * totalWeight;
            for (const event of availableStoryEvents) {
                random -= event.probability || 0;
                if (random <= 0) {
                    showEventPopup(event);
                    return;
                }
            }
            // Fallback to last event
            showEventPopup(availableStoryEvents[availableStoryEvents.length - 1]);
            return;
        }
    }
    
    // 2. 如果没有故事事件触发，再尝试 EVENTS 对象中的系统事件（自然灾害等）
    if (!game || !gameLoopInterval) return;
    
    const hasCrops = hasGrowingCrops();
    
    // 需要作物才能触发的事件ID
    const cropRequiredEvents = [
        'drought', 'rainstorm', 'pest', 'heatwave', 'coldDew', 
        'continuousRain', 'hail', 'lateSpringCold',
        'timelyRain', 'morningDew',
        'theft', 'kidTrample'
    ];
    
    // 筛选当前季节可用、且满足前置条件的事件
    const availableEvents = Object.values(EVENTS).filter(e => {
        // 季节检查
        if (!e.seasons.includes(game.season)) return false;
        
        // 日期检查（使用totalDay累计天数，避免季节切换重置）
        if (e.minDay !== undefined && game.totalDay < e.minDay) return false;
        if (e.maxDay !== undefined && game.totalDay > e.maxDay) return false;
        
        // 作物前置条件检查
        if (cropRequiredEvents.includes(e.id) && !hasCrops) return false;
        
        // NPC前置条件检查
        if (e.npcRequired) {
            const npcKnown = isNpcKnown(e.npcRequired);
            if (!npcKnown) return false;
        }
        
        // 燕子归来：需要至少过了一年
        if (e.id === 'swallow' && game.totalDay <= 240) return false;
        
        return true;
    });
    
    if (availableEvents.length === 0) return;
    
    // 30%概率无事发生，增加"平静的一天"体验
    if (Math.random() < 0.3) return;
    
    // 按概率加权选择
    let totalWeight = 0;
    const petTheftReduction = getPetEffect('theftReduction');
    
    availableEvents.forEach(e => {
        let weight = e.probability;
        // 应用灾难率系数（只对灾难和人为破坏事件）
        if (game.disasterRate && (e.type === 'disaster' || e.type === 'human')) {
            weight *= game.disasterRate;
        }
        if (e.id === 'theft' && petTheftReduction > 0) {
            weight *= (1 - petTheftReduction);
        }
        if (e.id === 'pest' && game.pestReduction > 0) {
            weight *= (1 - game.pestReduction);
        }
        totalWeight += weight;
    });
    
    let random = Math.random() * totalWeight;
    let selectedEvent = null;
    
    for (const event of availableEvents) {
        let weight = event.probability;
        // 应用灾难率系数（只对灾难和人为破坏事件）
        if (game.disasterRate && (event.type === 'disaster' || event.type === 'human')) {
            weight *= game.disasterRate;
        }
        if (event.id === 'theft' && petTheftReduction > 0) {
            weight *= (1 - petTheftReduction);
        }
        if (event.id === 'pest' && game.pestReduction > 0) {
            weight *= (1 - game.pestReduction);
        }
        random -= weight;
        if (random <= 0) {
            selectedEvent = event;
            break;
        }
    }
    
    if (!selectedEvent) return;
    
    // 新手期保护（使用totalDay累计天数）
    if (game.totalDay <= 3) {
        return;
    }
    if (game.totalDay <= 5 && selectedEvent.type === 'human') {
        return;
    }
    if (game.totalDay <= 10 && selectedEvent.type === 'disaster' && Math.random() > 0.3) {
        return;
    }
    
    // 如果已有弹窗打开（如反馈弹窗），不触发事件，避免覆盖
    const overlay = document.getElementById('modal-overlay');
    if (overlay && overlay.style.display === 'flex') {
        return;
    }
    
    // 触发事件
    game.currentEvent = selectedEvent.id;
    showEventModal(selectedEvent);
}

// 触发夜间事件
function triggerNightEvent() {
    // 新手期保护：前3天不触发（使用totalDay累计天数）
    if (game.totalDay <= 3) return;
    
    // 如果已有弹窗打开，不触发夜间事件
    const overlay = document.getElementById('modal-overlay');
    if (overlay && overlay.style.display === 'flex') {
        return;
    }
    
    // 30%概率触发夜间事件
    if (Math.random() > 0.3) return;
    
    // 筛选可触发的事件
    const availableEvents = NIGHT_EVENTS.filter(event => {
        // 检查天气要求
        if (event.weatherRequired && game.weather !== event.weatherRequired) {
            return false;
        }
        // 检查季节要求
        if (event.seasonRequired && game.season !== event.seasonRequired) {
            return false;
        }
        // 检查NPC要求（需要认识对应NPC）
        if (event.npcRequired) {
            const friendship = Math.max((game.friendship && game.friendship[event.npcRequired]) || 0,(game.npcs && game.npcs[event.npcRequired]) || 0);
            if (friendship < 10) return false;
        }
        return true;
    });
    
    if (availableEvents.length === 0) return;
    
    // 按概率权重选择事件
    const totalWeight = availableEvents.reduce((sum, e) => sum + e.probability, 0);
    let rand = Math.random() * totalWeight;
    let selectedEvent = null;
    
    for (const event of availableEvents) {
        rand -= event.probability;
        if (rand <= 0) {
            selectedEvent = event;
            break;
        }
    }
    
    if (!selectedEvent) return;
    
    // 应用事件效果
    const effect = selectedEvent.effect;
    let logText = selectedEvent.desc;
    
    if (effect.staminaRecover) {
        // 体力恢复（直接加减体力）
        game.stamina = Math.min(game.maxStamina, game.stamina + effect.staminaRecover);
        if (effect.staminaRecover < 0) {
            logText += `（体力${effect.staminaRecover}）`;
        } else {
            logText += `（体力+${effect.staminaRecover}）`;
        }
    }
    
    if (effect.healthRecover || effect.health) {
        const healthChange = effect.healthRecover || effect.health;
        game.health = Math.max(0, Math.min(game.maxHealth, game.health + healthChange));
        if (healthChange < 0) {
            logText += `（健康${healthChange}）`;
        } else {
            logText += `（健康+${healthChange}）`;
        }
    }
    
    if (effect.reputation) {
        let repGain = effect.reputation;
        // 社区建设加成（村祠堂翻修：声望获取+30%）
        if (game.reputationBonus) {
            repGain = Math.floor(repGain * (1 + game.reputationBonus));
        }
        game.reputation += repGain;
        logText += `（声望+${repGain}）`;
    }
    
    if (effect.riceLoss) {
        const loss = effect.riceLoss;
        if (game.crops && game.crops.rice) {
            game.crops.rice = Math.max(0, game.crops.rice - loss);
            logText += `（稻谷-${loss}斤）`;
        }
    }
    
    if (effect.skillExp) {
        // 随机增加技能经验
        const skillKeys = ['cropFamiliarity', 'fieldManagement', 'toolMastery', 'composting'];
        const randomSkill = skillKeys[Math.floor(Math.random() * skillKeys.length)];
        addSkillExp(randomSkill, effect.skillExp);
        logText += `（技能经验+${effect.skillExp}）`;
    }
    
    // 添加日志
    addLog(`🌙 ${selectedEvent.name}：${selectedEvent.desc}`, selectedEvent.type === 'good' ? 'good' : (selectedEvent.type === 'bad' ? 'bad' : 'info'));
    
    // 显示弹窗
    showModal(selectedEvent.name, selectedEvent.desc + '<br><br>' + 
        '<span style="color: ' + (selectedEvent.type === 'good' ? '#27ae60' : '#e74c3c') + ';">' +
        selectedEvent.effectText + '</span>');
    
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
}

// 显示故事事件弹窗（用于 STORY_EVENTS 数组中的事件）
function showEventPopup(event) {
    const eventId = 'story_' + event.name.replace(/[\s\u{1F300}-\u{1F9FF}]/gu, '_');
    // 创建副本，避免修改原事件对象
    const eventCopy = { ...event, id: eventId };
    if (!window.STORY_EVENTS_MAP) window.STORY_EVENTS_MAP = {};
    window.STORY_EVENTS_MAP[eventId] = eventCopy;
    game.currentEvent = eventId;
    showEventModal(eventCopy);
}

function showEventModal(event) {
    let html = `<div style="text-align: center; margin-bottom: 20px;">`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 60px; margin-bottom: 10px;">${event.emoji}</div>`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 15px; color: ${event.type === 'disaster' ? '#e74c3c' : event.type === 'gain' ? '#27ae60' : '#f39c12'};">${event.name}</div>`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.8; color: #666; margin-bottom: 20px;">${event.description}</div>`;
    html += `</div>`;
    
    html += '<div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 10px;">';
    
    // 有选项的事件：必须选择
    if (event.options && event.options.length > 0) {
        event.options.forEach((opt, idx) => {
            html += `<button class="modal-btn" onclick="handleEventChoice(${idx})">${opt.text}</button>`;
        });
    } else {
        // 被动事件（无选项）：显示"知道了"按钮
        html += `<button class="modal-btn" onclick="closeEventModal()">知道了</button>`;
    }
    html += '</div>';
    
    // 显示弹窗
    document.getElementById('modal-title').textContent = '突发事件';
    document.getElementById('modal-content').innerHTML = html;
    document.querySelector('.modal-buttons').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('modal-overlay').style.display = 'flex';
}

function getSkillName(skillKey) {
    const names = {
        cropFamiliarity: '作物熟悉',
        fieldManagement: '田间管理',
        toolMastery: '农具掌握',
        composting: '堆肥技术',
        fishingMastery: '钓鱼技巧'
    };
    return names[skillKey] || skillKey;
}

function checkSkillLevelUp(skillKey) {
    // 统一使用addSkillExp处理升级，避免双系统不一致
    // 此函数保留兼容旧代码调用，但逻辑统一
    if (!game.skills[skillKey]) return;
    const skill = game.skills[skillKey];
    const currentLevel = getSkillLevel(skill.exp || 0);
    if (currentLevel > (skill.level || 0)) {
        skill.level = currentLevel;
        addLog(`🎉 ${getSkillName(skillKey)}升级到Lv.${skill.level}！`, 'good');
    }
}

// 处理事件选择
// 事件选项分支概率处理
function applyEventBranches(event, option) {
    if (!option.branches) return { effect: option.effect, result: option.result };
    const rand = Math.random();
    let cumulative = 0;
    for (const branch of option.branches) {
        cumulative += branch.probability;
        if (rand <= cumulative) {
            return { effect: branch.effect, result: branch.result };
        }
    }
    return { effect: option.effect, result: option.result };
}

function handleEventChoice(optionIdx) {
    const eventId = game.currentEvent;
    let event = EVENTS[eventId];
    // 支持故事事件
    if (!event && window.STORY_EVENTS_MAP && window.STORY_EVENTS_MAP[eventId]) {
        event = window.STORY_EVENTS_MAP[eventId];
    }
    if (!event || !event.options || !event.options[optionIdx]) {
        console.error('事件或选项不存在:', eventId, optionIdx);
        closeModal();
        return;
    }
    const option = event.options[optionIdx];
    
    // 检查物品消耗（如农药、化肥等）
    const checkEffect = option.branches ? option.branches[0].effect : option.effect;
    if (checkEffect.item_pesticide !== undefined && checkEffect.item_pesticide < 0) {
        const hasPesticide = (game.items.pesticide || 0) >= Math.abs(checkEffect.item_pesticide);
        if (!hasPesticide) {
            showToast('农药不足！去商店购买后再来吧', 'bad');
            playErrorSound();
            return;
        }
    }
    if (checkEffect.items) {
        for (const [itemId, val] of Object.entries(checkEffect.items)) {
            if (val < 0) {
                const current = (game.items[itemId] || 0);
                if (current < Math.abs(val)) {
                    showToast(`${(typeof ITEM_DATA !== 'undefined' &&(ITEM_DATA[itemId] && ITEM_DATA[itemId].name)) || itemId}不足！`, 'bad');
                    playErrorSound();
                    return;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    // 检查金钱消耗
    if (checkEffect.money !== undefined && checkEffect.money < 0) {
        if (game.money < Math.abs(checkEffect.money)) {
            showToast(`手头紧，还差${Math.abs(checkEffect.money)}块钱`, 'bad');
            playErrorSound();
            return;
        }
    }
    // 检查体力消耗
    if (checkEffect.stamina !== undefined && checkEffect.stamina < 0) {
        if (game.stamina < Math.abs(checkEffect.stamina)) {
            showToast(`累得不行了，需要${Math.abs(checkEffect.stamina)}点体力...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西再来吧`, 'bad');
            playErrorSound();
            return;
        }
    }
    
    // 应用事件分支概率（不同选择有不同概率产生不同结果）
    const branchResult = applyEventBranches(event, option);
    const effect = {...branchResult.effect};
    const resultText = branchResult.result;
    
    // 事件强度系数（强化事件影响）
    const EVENT_STRENGTH = 1.5;
    const STAMINA_STRENGTH = 1.2;
    
    // 应用强度系数
    if (effect.yieldLoss) effect.yieldLoss *= EVENT_STRENGTH;
    if (effect.yieldBonus) effect.yieldBonus *= EVENT_STRENGTH;
    if (effect.money) effect.money = Math.floor(effect.money * EVENT_STRENGTH);
    
    // 宠物虫害减少（阿花）- 只对病虫害事件生效
    const petPestReduction = getPetEffect('pestReduction');
    if (petPestReduction > 0 && effect.yieldLoss && event.id === 'pest') {
        effect.yieldLoss *= (1 - petPestReduction);
    }
    
    // 科技灾害减少
    const techDisasterReduction = getTechBonus('disasterReduction');
    if (techDisasterReduction > 0 && effect.yieldLoss) {
        effect.yieldLoss *= (1 - techDisasterReduction);
    }
    
    // 田间管理技能减少灾害损失
    const fieldSkillLevel =(game.skills.fieldManagement && game.skills.fieldManagement.level) || 0;
    if (fieldSkillLevel > 0 && effect.yieldLoss) {
        effect.yieldLoss *= (1 - fieldSkillLevel * 0.05);
    }
    if (effect.stamina) effect.stamina = Math.floor(effect.stamina * STAMINA_STRENGTH);
    if (effect.reputation) effect.reputation = Math.floor(effect.reputation * EVENT_STRENGTH);
    if (effect.health) effect.health = Math.floor(effect.health * EVENT_STRENGTH);
    
    // 应用效果
    if (effect.stamina) {
        game.stamina = Math.max(0, Math.min(game.maxStamina, game.stamina + effect.stamina));
    }
    if (effect.money) {
        game.money += effect.money;
        if (game.money < 0) game.money = 0;
    }
    if (effect.reputation) {
        // NPC好感度声望加成（王村长）
        let repGain = effect.reputation;
        const npcRepBonus = getNpcBonus('reputationGain');
        if (npcRepBonus > 0) {
            repGain = Math.floor(repGain * (1 + npcRepBonus));
        }
        // 社区建设加成（村祠堂翻修：声望获取+30%）
        if (game.reputationBonus) {
            repGain = Math.floor(repGain * (1 + game.reputationBonus));
        }
        game.reputation += repGain;
    }
    if (effect.item_pesticide) {
        game.items.pesticide = Math.max(0, (game.items.pesticide || 0) + effect.item_pesticide);
    }
    if (effect.yieldLoss) {
        // 田间管理减少灾害损失（每级-5%）
        let reducedLoss = effect.yieldLoss * (1 - fieldSkillLevel * 0.05);
        
        // 科技减少灾害损失
        const techDisasterReduction = getTechBonus('disasterReduction');
        if (techDisasterReduction > 0) {
            reducedLoss *= (1 - techDisasterReduction);
        }
        
        // 所有正在生长的作物减产
        game.fields.forEach(field => {
            if (field.crop && field.stage !== 'mature' && field.stage !== 'idle') {
                field.yieldLoss = (field.yieldLoss || 0) + reducedLoss;
            }
        });
    }
    if (effect.yieldBonus) {
        // 所有正在生长的作物增产
        game.fields.forEach(field => {
            if (field.crop && field.stage !== 'mature' && field.stage !== 'idle') {
                field.yieldBonus = (field.yieldBonus || 0) + effect.yieldBonus;
            }
        });
    }
    if (effect.nextSeasonBonus) {
        game.nextSeasonBonus = (game.nextSeasonBonus || 0) + effect.nextSeasonBonus;
    }
    if (effect.health) {
        game.health = Math.max(0, Math.min(game.maxHealth || 100, game.health + effect.health));
    }
    if (effect.mood) {
        game.mood = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (game.mood === undefined ? 50 : game.mood) + effect.mood));
    }
    if (effect.items) {
        if (!game.items) game.items = {};
        for (const [itemId, val] of Object.entries(effect.items)) {
            game.items[itemId] = (game.items[itemId] || 0) + val;
            if (game.items[itemId] < 0) game.items[itemId] = 0;
        }
    }
    if (effect.npcs) {
        for (const [npcId, val] of Object.entries(effect.npcs)) {
            addNpcFavor(npcId, val);
        }
    }
    if (effect.pets) {
        for (const [petId, petEffect] of Object.entries(effect.pets)) {
            if (game.pets && game.pets[petId]) {
                if (petEffect.favor) {
                    game.pets[petId].affection = Math.max(0, (game.pets[petId].affection || game.pets[petId].friendship || 0) + petEffect.favor);
                }
            }
        }
    }
    if (effect.metSunmiaoqing) { game.metSunmiaoqing = true; }
    if (effect.metChenyang) { game.metChenyang = true; }
    if (effect.metLinxiaoyu) { game.metLinxiaoyu = true; }
    if (effect.hasBookBonus) { game.hasBookBonus = true; }
    if (effect.hasMedicineKit) { game.hasMedicineKit = true; }
    if (effect.zhaoBonusNoticed) { game.zhaoBonusNoticed = true; }
    if (effect.skills) {
        const skillMap = { fieldManage: 'fieldManagement', cropFamiliar: 'cropFamiliarity' };
        for (const [key, val] of Object.entries(effect.skills)) {
            const mappedKey = skillMap[key] || key;
            if (typeof addSkillExp === 'function') {
                addSkillExp(mappedKey, val);
            }
        }
    }
    if (effect.skillExp_cropFamiliarity) {
        if (typeof addSkillExp === 'function') {
            addSkillExp('cropFamiliarity', effect.skillExp_cropFamiliarity);
        }
    }
    if (effect.skillExp_fieldManagement) {
        if (typeof addSkillExp === 'function') {
            addSkillExp('fieldManagement', effect.skillExp_fieldManagement);
        }
    }
    if (effect.skillExp_toolMastery) {
        if (typeof addSkillExp === 'function') {
            addSkillExp('toolMastery', effect.skillExp_toolMastery);
        }
    }
    if (effect.skillExp_composting) {
        if (typeof addSkillExp === 'function') {
            addSkillExp('composting', effect.skillExp_composting);
        }
    }
    if (effect.skillExp_fishingMastery) {
        if (typeof addSkillExp === 'function') {
            addSkillExp('fishingMastery', effect.skillExp_fishingMastery);
        }
    }
    if (effect.sellBonus) {
        game.sellBonus = (game.sellBonus || 0) + effect.sellBonus;
    }
    if (effect.time) {
        // 时间快进/倒退
        game.time += effect.time;
        // 处理跨天
        while (game.time >= 24) {
            game.time -= 24;
            game.day += 1;
            game.totalDay = (game.totalDay || game.day) + 1;
            // 触发完整的新的一天逻辑
            onNewDay();
        }
        while (game.time < 0) {
            game.time += 24;
            game.day -= 1;
            game.totalDay -= 1;
            if (game.day < 1) game.day = 1;
            if (game.totalDay < 1) game.totalDay = 1;
        }
    }
    
    if (effect.pestReduce) {
        game.pestReduction = (game.pestReduction || 0) + effect.pestReduce;
        addLog(`🐦 虫害减少效果已生效（当前减少${Math.floor(game.pestReduction * 100)}%）`, 'good');
    }
    
    // 特殊事件处理
    if (eventId === 'strayCat') {
        if (optionIdx === 0) {
            // 选择了给它点吃的，增加流浪猫来访次数
            game.petEvents.strayCatVisits = (game.petEvents.strayCatVisits || 0) + 1;
        }
    }
    
    // 记录事件（限制历史长度防止存档膨胀）
    game.eventHistory.push({
        day: game.day,
        season: game.season,
        eventId: eventId,
        choice: optionIdx,
        result: resultText
    });
    if (game.eventHistory.length > 100) {
        game.eventHistory = game.eventHistory.slice(-100);
    }
    
    addLog(`⚡ ${event.name}：${resultText}`, event.type === 'disaster' ? 'bad' : event.type === 'gain' ? 'good' : 'info');
    
    // 清除当前事件
    game.currentEvent = null;
    
    // 防止浮点数累积
    roundGameState();
    
    // 关闭弹窗
    closeModal();
    
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
}

function updateProcessingJobs() {
    if (!game.processingJobs || game.processingJobs.length === 0) return;
    
    const currentTotalTime = (game.totalDay || game.day) * 24 + game.time;
    
    game.processingJobs.forEach(job => {
        if (job.completed) return;
        
        const jobTotalTime = (job.startTotalDay || job.startDay) * 24 + job.startTime;
        const elapsed = currentTotalTime - jobTotalTime;
        job.progress = Math.min(100, Math.floor((elapsed / job.duration) * 100));
        
        if (elapsed >= job.duration) {
            // 加工完成
            job.completed = true;
            
            // 产出加工品
            if (!game.processedItems) game.processedItems = {};
            game.processedItems[job.outputItem] = (game.processedItems[job.outputItem] || 0) + job.outputAmount;
            
            // 记录今日加工（按输入量计算，而非产出量）
            if (!game.dailyProcessed) game.dailyProcessed = {};
            game.dailyProcessed[job.buildingKey] = (game.dailyProcessed[job.buildingKey] || 0) + job.inputAmount;
            
            addLog(`🏡 ${job.buildingName}加工完成！产出${job.outputAmount}斤${(PROCESSED_ITEMS[job.outputItem] && PROCESSED_ITEMS[job.outputItem].name) || ''}`, 'good');
            
            // 统计
            if (!game.stats) game.stats = {};
            game.stats.totalProcessed = (game.stats.totalProcessed || 0) + job.outputAmount;
            
            // 解锁图鉴
            unlockCollectionItem('processed', job.outputItem);
            
            // 任务检查：累积加工产出100斤
            const totalProcessed = Object.values(game.processedItems || {}).reduce((sum, v) => sum + (v || 0), 0);
            if (totalProcessed >= 100 && !game.quests.q24) {
                game.quests.q24 = true;
                queueQuestReward('q24', 300, '✅ 任务完成：米香四溢，奖励300元');
            }
            
            // 刷新面板
            if (currentMainTab === 'processing') {
                renderProcessingPanel();
            }
            updateTopBar();
        }
    });
    
    // 清理已完成的任务
    game.processingJobs = game.processingJobs.filter(j => !j.completed || j.progress < 100);
}

function growCrops() {
    let growRate = 1.0;
    if (game.neighborHelp && game.neighborHelp.seedShare) {
        growRate += 0.05;
    }
    game.fields.forEach(field => {
        if (!field.crop) return;
        
        const cropData = CROP_DATA[field.crop];
        if (!cropData) return;
        
        const growDays = Math.max(0, game.day - field.plantedDay);
        const TRANSPLANT_NEED_DAYS = 2; // 移栽期固定2天
        
        // 育苗期
        if (field.stage === 'seedling') {
            const seedlingDays = cropData.seedlingDays || 5;
            field.growProgress = Math.min(20, (growDays * growRate / seedlingDays) * 20);
            return;
        }
        
        // 移栽后（返青期/幼苗期）
        if (field.stage === 'transplanting') {
            const transplantDays = growDays - (cropData.seedlingDays || 5);
            if (transplantDays * growRate >= TRANSPLANT_NEED_DAYS) {
                field.stage = 'growing';
                field.step = 3;
            }
            const progress = Math.min(20, Math.max(0, (transplantDays * growRate / TRANSPLANT_NEED_DAYS) * 20));
            field.growProgress = 20 + progress;
            return;
        }
        
        // 生长期
        if (field.stage === 'growing') {
            const growingDays = growDays - (cropData.seedlingDays || 5) - TRANSPLANT_NEED_DAYS;
            const totalGrowingDays = (cropData.growDays || 50) - (cropData.seedlingDays || 5) - TRANSPLANT_NEED_DAYS;
            
            // 安全边界：生长期天数不足或为零时直接成熟
            if (totalGrowingDays <= 0) {
                field.stage = 'mature';
                field.growProgress = 100;
                return;
            }
            
            field.growProgress = 40 + Math.min(50, Math.max(0, (growingDays * growRate / totalGrowingDays) * 50));
            
            // 生长期结束，成熟
            if (growingDays * growRate >= totalGrowingDays) {
                field.stage = 'mature';
                field.growProgress = 100;
            }
            return;
        }
        
        // 成熟期，保持100%
        if (field.stage === 'mature') {
            field.growProgress = 100;
        }
    });
}

// ==================== UI更新 ====================
function updateUI() {
    if (!game) return;

    // 边界值保护：防止负数
    game.money = Math.max(0, game.money);
    game.stamina = Math.max(0, Math.min(game.maxStamina, game.stamina));
    game.health = Math.max(0, Math.min(game.maxHealth, game.health));

    // 顶部状态栏
    document.getElementById('stat-money').textContent = Math.floor(game.money);
    document.getElementById('stat-stamina').textContent = Math.floor(game.stamina);
    document.getElementById('stat-max-stamina').textContent = game.maxStamina;
    document.getElementById('stat-health').textContent = Math.floor(game.health);
    document.getElementById('stat-max-health').textContent = game.maxHealth;
    document.getElementById('stat-rice').textContent = Math.floor(game.crops.rice);
    document.getElementById('stat-sweet').textContent = Math.floor(game.crops.sweet);
    document.getElementById('stat-wheat').textContent = Math.floor(game.crops.wheat || 0);
    document.getElementById('stat-corn').textContent = Math.floor(game.crops.corn || 0);
    document.getElementById('stat-soybean').textContent = Math.floor(game.crops.soybean || 0);
    document.getElementById('stat-day').textContent = game.totalDay || game.day;
    document.getElementById('stat-season').textContent = SEASON_NAMES[game.season];
    document.getElementById('season-icon').textContent = SEASON_ICONS[game.season];
    
    // 天气显示
    const wData = WEATHER_DATA[game.weather] || WEATHER_DATA.sunny;
    document.getElementById('stat-weather').textContent = wData.name;
    document.getElementById('weather-icon').textContent = wData.emoji;
    
    // 游戏时钟
    const hour = game.time || 6;
    const timeStr = (hour < 10 ? '0' : '') + hour + ':00';
    const clockEl = document.getElementById('game-clock-time');
    if (clockEl) clockEl.textContent = timeStr;
    const ampmEl = document.getElementById('game-clock-ampm');
    if (ampmEl) {
        if (hour >= 6 && hour < 12) ampmEl.textContent = '上午';
        else if (hour >= 12 && hour < 14) ampmEl.textContent = '中午';
        else if (hour >= 14 && hour < 18) ampmEl.textContent = '下午';
        else if (hour >= 18 && hour < 20) ampmEl.textContent = '傍晚';
        else ampmEl.textContent = '深夜';
    }
    
    // 更新浮动倒计时按钮角标
    updateCountdownBadge();

    // 更新当前面板（只更新内容，不切换标签）
    if (currentMainTab) {
        renderPanel(currentMainTab);
    }
    
    // 更新页签解锁状态
    if (typeof updateTabLockStatus === 'function') {
        updateTabLockStatus();
    }
    
    // 更新暂停按钮状态
    const pauseBtn = document.getElementById('pause-btn');
    const gameClockEl = document.querySelector('.game-clock');
    const speedBtns = document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn-top');
    if (pauseBtn) {
        if (gamePaused) {
            pauseBtn.innerHTML = '▶️ 继续';
            pauseBtn.classList.add('paused');
            pauseBtn.title = '游戏已暂停，点击继续';
            if (gameClockEl) gameClockEl.classList.add('paused');
            speedBtns.forEach(btn => btn.disabled = true);
        } else {
            pauseBtn.innerHTML = '⏸️ 暂停';
            pauseBtn.classList.remove('paused');
            pauseBtn.title = '点击暂停游戏时间';
            if (gameClockEl) gameClockEl.classList.remove('paused');
            speedBtns.forEach(btn => btn.disabled = false);
        }
    }
}

function showGame() {
    const savedStyle = localStorage.getItem('farm_bgm_style') || 'game';
    switchBgm(savedStyle);
    document.getElementById('game-container').style.display = 'flex';
    
    // 检测是否是localhost，提示手机访问方式
    if (location.hostname === 'localhost' || location.hostname === '127.0.0.1') {
        setTimeout(() => {
            showToast('📱 手机和电脑连同一个WiFi，在手机浏览器输入 http://' + location.host + location.pathname + ' 即可同步游玩', 'info', 8000);
        }, 2000);
    }
    
    // 绑定标签点击（只绑定一次，防止重复）
    if (!window._sidebarTabBound) {
        window._sidebarTabBound = true;
        document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-tab').forEach(tab => {
            tab.addEventListener('click', function() {
                if (this.classList.contains('locked')) return;
                if (!this.dataset.tab) return;
                playTabSound();
                document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
                this.classList.add('active');
                currentMainTab = this.dataset.tab;
                renderPanel(currentMainTab);
            });
        });
    }
    // 默认选中第一个（只在未激活时设置）
    const firstTab = document.querySelector('.sidebar-tab[data-tab]');
    const activeTab = document.querySelector('.sidebar-tab.active');
    if (firstTab && !activeTab) {
        firstTab.classList.add('active');
        currentMainTab = firstTab.dataset.tab;
    }
    if (currentMainTab) {
        renderPanel(currentMainTab);
    }
    
    // 更新页签锁定状态
    if (typeof updateTabLockStatus === 'function') {
        updateTabLockStatus();
    }
    
    // 初始化左侧任务追踪器
    if (typeof renderSidebarQuests === 'function') {
        renderSidebarQuests();
    }
    
    // 确保UI正确显示初始数值
    if (typeof updateUI === 'function') {
        updateUI();
    }
}

// ==================== 面板渲染 ====================
function renderPanel(tab) {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    
    switch(tab) {
        case 'fields':
            renderFieldsPanel();
            break;
        case 'shop':
            renderShopPanel();
            break;
        case 'house':
            renderHousePanel();
            break;
        case 'tools':
            renderToolsPanel();
            break;
        case 'compost':
            renderCompostPanel();
            break;
        case 'processing':
            renderProcessingPanel();
            break;
        case 'foraging':
            renderForagingPanel();
            break;
        case 'fishing':
            renderFishingPanel();
            break;
        case 'buildings':
            renderBuildingPanel();
            break;

        case 'player':
            renderPlayerPanel();
            break;
        case 'skills':
            renderSkillsPanel();
            break;
        case 'tech':
            renderTechPanel();
            break;
        case 'npcs':
            renderNpcsPanel();
            renderBackpack();
            updateDailyButtons();
            break;
        case 'pets':
            renderPetsPanel();
            break;
        case 'animals':
            renderAnimalsPanel();
            break;
        case 'orchard':
            renderOrchardPanel();
            break;
        case 'village':
            renderVillagePanel();
            break;
        case 'farmstay':
            renderFarmStayPanel();
            break;
        case 'automation':
            renderAutomationPanel();
            break;
        case 'bank':
            renderBankPanel();
            break;
        case 'agritech':
            renderAgriTechPanel();
            break;
        case 'neighbor':
            renderNeighborPanel();
            break;
        case 'market':
            renderMarketPanel();
            break;
        case 'explore':
            renderExplorePanel();
            break;
        case 'cooking':
            renderCookingPanel();
            break;
        case 'community':
            renderCommunityPanel();
            break;
        case 'collection':
            renderCollectionPanel();
            break;
        case 'achievements':
            renderAchievementsPanel();
            break;
        case 'log':
            renderLogPanel();
            break;
        default:
            panel.innerHTML = '<div class="panel-title">敬请期待</div><p>该功能正在开发中...</p>';
    }
}

// ===== 田地管理面板 =====
function renderFieldsPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🌾 田地管理</div>';
    
    // 新手任务
    html += renderQuestBox();
    
    html += '<div class="field-grid">';
    
    game.fields.forEach((field, idx) => {
        html += renderFieldCard(field, idx);
    });
    
    html += '</div>';
    
    // 扩田按钮（如果够条件）
    if (game.fields.length < 4) {
        const nextRent = getNextFieldRent();
        html += `<div style="margin-top: 20px; text-align: center;">`;
        html += `<button class="action-btn" onclick="rentNewField()" ${game.money < nextRent ? 'disabled' : ''}>`;
        html += `🔓 租用新田地（${nextRent}元/季）</button></div>`;
    }
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

const MILESTONE_DATA = {

            const cropTypes = ['rice', 'sweet', 'wheat', 'corn', 'soybean', 'potato', 'peanut', 'pepper', 'cabbage', 'radish', 'eggplant', 'garlic'];

                const amount = (game.crops && game.crops[type]) || 0;

// 计算任务进度（0-100）
function getQuestProgress(questId) {
    const q = game.quests;
    if (q[questId]) return 100;
    
    // 根据任务类型估算进度
    const progressMap = {
        q0: game.fields[0] && game.fields[0].prepared ? 100 : 0,
        q1: game.seeds.rice_spring > 0 ? 100 : (game.money > 30 ? 50 : 20),
        q2: game.fields[0] && game.fields[0].stage === 'seedling' ? 100 : (game.seeds.rice_spring > 0 ? 50 : 0),
        q3: game.fields[0] && game.fields[0].stage === 'growing' ? 100 : (game.fields[0] && game.fields[0].stage === 'seedling' ? 70 : 0),
        q4: game.fields[0] && game.fields[0].stage === 'mature' ? 100 : (game.fields[0] && game.fields[0].growProgress > 0 ? Math.min(95, game.fields[0].growProgress) : 0),
        q5: game.crops.rice > 0 ? 60 : 0,
    };
    
    return progressMap[questId] || 0;
}

// 获取进度条颜色等级
function getProgressClass(progress) {
    if (progress >= 70) return 'high';
    if (progress >= 30) return 'medium';
    return 'low';
}

        { id: 'q31', name: '仓廪充实', desc: '将仓库扩建到5000斤以上', reward: '300元', icon: '📦', type: 'build', order: 31 },
        { id: 'q32', name: '阡陌纵横', desc: '租下第3块田', reward: '400元', icon: '🗺️', type: 'build', order: 32 },
        { id: 'q33', name: '阡陌四野', desc: '租下第4块田', reward: '500元', icon: '🗺️', type: 'build', order: 33 },
    ];
    
    // 成长任务
    const growthQuests = [
        { id: 'q13', name: '扩土开疆', desc: '租下第二块田', reward: '300元', icon: '🗺️', type: 'growth', order: 13 },
        { id: 'q14', name: '田间能手', desc: '田间管理达到3级', reward: '300元', icon: '🌾', type: 'growth', order: 14 },

    ];
    
    // 社交任务
    const socialQuests = [
        { id: 'q34', name: '村中知己', desc: '和2个村民达到友好关系', reward: '300元', icon: '🤝', type: 'social', order: 34 },

    ];
    
    // 技能与成长任务
    const skillQuests = [
        { id: 'q37', name: '农学专家', desc: '作物熟悉度达到5级', reward: '500元', icon: '📚', type: 'skill', order: 37 },

        { id: 'q40', name: '堆肥专家', desc: '堆肥技能达到5级', reward: '500元', icon: '💩', type: 'skill', order: 40 },
    ];
    
    // 财富任务
    const wealthQuests = [
        { id: 'q41', name: '万元户', desc: '总资产达到10000元', reward: '1000元', icon: '💰', type: 'wealth', order: 41 },
        { id: 'q42', name: '腰缠万贯', desc: '总资产达到20000元', reward: '2000元', icon: '💎', type: 'wealth', order: 42 },
        { id: 'q43', name: '富甲一方', desc: '总资产达到50000元', reward: '5000元', icon: '👑', type: 'wealth', order: 43 },
    ];
    
    // 后期综合任务
    const lateQuests = [
        { id: 'q44', name: '双宠之家', desc: '领养第二只宠物', reward: '300元', icon: '🐾', type: 'late', order: 44 },
        { id: 'q45', name: '科技兴农', desc: '研究任意一项科技', reward: '200元', icon: '🔬', type: 'late', order: 45 },
        { id: 'q46', name: '全面丰收', desc: '同时拥有早稻和红薯的成熟作物', reward: '200元', icon: '🌾', type: 'late', order: 46 },
        { id: 'q47', name: '声名远播', desc: '声望达到200点', reward: '800元', icon: '🌟', type: 'late', order: 47 },
        { id: 'q48', name: '世家大族', desc: '和4个村民达到友好关系', reward: '600元', icon: '👨‍👩‍👧‍👦', type: 'late', order: 48 },
        { id: 'q49', name: '农商一体', desc: '同时拥有3种置办好的副业作坊', reward: '400元', icon: '🏭', type: 'late', order: 49 },
        { id: 'q50', name: '年过半百', desc: '游戏时间超过50天', reward: '500元', icon: '📅', type: 'late', order: 50 },
    ];
    
    // 按优先级收集未完成任务（只统计存档中实际定义的任务）
    const allQuests = [...newbieQuests, ...devQuests, ...dailyQuests, ...sideQuests, ...fishQuests, ...buildQuests, ...growthQuests, ...socialQuests, ...skillQuests, ...wealthQuests, ...lateQuests];
    allQuests.forEach(quest => {
        // 只统计存档中已定义的任务（q21+在旧存档中可能不存在）
        if (q.hasOwnProperty(quest.id) && !q[quest.id]) {
            pendingQuests.push(quest);
        }
    });
    
    // 只取前3个（按顺序）
    const displayQuests = pendingQuests.slice(0, 3);
    
    let html = '<div class="quest-tracker">';
    html += '<div class="quest-tracker-header">';
    html += '<div class="quest-tracker-title">📋 任务追踪</div>';
    html += `<div class="quest-tracker-count">${pendingQuests.length} 个待完成</div>`;
    html += '</div>';
    
    if (displayQuests.length === 0) {
        html += '<div class="quest-all-done">🎉 所有任务都完成啦！继续探索吧~</div>';
    } else {
        displayQuests.forEach((quest, idx) => {
            // 计算任务进度
            let progress = 0;
            let progressText = '';
            
            // 根据任务类型计算进度
            if (quest.id === 'q0') {
                // 整地任务
                progress = game.fields[0].prepared ? 100 : 0;
                progressText = game.fields[0].prepared ? '已完成' : '未开始';
            } else if (quest.id === 'q1') {
                // 买种子任务
                const hasSeeds = Object.values(game.seeds).some(s => s > 0);
                progress = hasSeeds ? 100 : 0;
                progressText = hasSeeds ? '已完成' : '未开始';
            } else if (quest.id === 'q6') {
                // 买农具任务
                const hasTools = game.tools && game.tools.length > 0;
                progress = hasTools ? 100 : 0;
                progressText = hasTools ? '已完成' : '未开始';
            } else if (quest.id === 'q8') {
                // 堆肥任务
                const hasCompost = game.composting || (game.items && game.items.organicFertilizer > 0);
                progress = hasCompost ? 100 : 0;
                progressText = hasCompost ? '已完成' : '未开始';
            } else if (quest.id === 'q2') {
                // 育苗任务
                const isSeedling = game.fields.some(f => f.stage === 'seedling');
                progress = isSeedling ? 100 : 0;
                progressText = isSeedling ? '已完成' : '未开始';
            } else if (quest.id === 'q3') {
                // 移栽任务
                const isTransplanting = game.fields.some(f => f.stage === 'transplanting' || f.stage === 'growing');
                progress = isTransplanting ? 100 : 0;
                progressText = isTransplanting ? '已完成' : '未开始';
            } else if (quest.id === 'q4') {
                // 收割任务
                const hasCrop = game.crops.rice > 0 || game.crops.sweet > 0;
                progress = hasCrop ? 100 : 0;
                progressText = hasCrop ? '已完成' : '未开始';
            } else if (quest.id === 'q5') {
                // 售卖任务
                progress = q.q4 ? 50 : 0; // 完成收割后算50%
                progressText = q.q4 ? '进行中' : '未开始';
            } else {
                // 其他任务简单估算
                const questNum = parseInt(quest.id.slice(1));
                const completedBefore = Object.keys(q).filter(k => k.startsWith('q') && parseInt(k.slice(1)) < questNum && q[k]).length;
                const totalBefore = questNum;
                progress = Math.min(95, (completedBefore / totalBefore) * 100);
                progressText = '进行中';
            }
            
            // 进度条颜色
            let progressColor = 'linear-gradient(90deg, #e74c3c, #c0392b)';
            if (progress >= 30) progressColor = 'linear-gradient(90deg, #f39c12, #e67e22)';
            if (progress >= 70) progressColor = 'linear-gradient(90deg, #27ae60, #2ecc71)';
            
            // 第一个任务高亮
            const isFirst = idx === 0;
            
            html += `
                <div class="quest-item ${isFirst ? 'quest-item-active' : ''}">
                    <div class="quest-item-icon">${quest.icon}</div>
                    <div class="quest-item-content">
                        <div class="quest-item-header">
                            <span class="quest-item-name">${quest.name}</span>
                            <span class="quest-item-badge">${isFirst ? '当前' : '待办'}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="quest-item-desc">${quest.desc}</div>
                        <div class="quest-item-progress">
                            <div class="quest-item-progress-bar" style="width: ${Math.min(100, progress)}%; background: ${progressColor};"></div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="quest-item-footer">
                            <span class="quest-item-reward">🎁 ${quest.reward}</span>
                            <span class="quest-item-progress-text">${progressText}</span>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        });
    }
    
    // 显示剩余任务数量
    if (pendingQuests.length > 3) {
        html += `<div class="quest-more">还有 ${pendingQuests.length - 3} 个任务待完成 →</div>`;
    }
    
    // 里程碑进度
    if (typeof MILESTONE_DATA !== 'undefined' && game.milestones) {
        const totalMilestones = Object.keys(MILESTONE_DATA).length;
        const completedMilestones = Object.keys(game.milestones).filter(k => game.milestones[k]).length;
        
        html += `
            <div style="margin-top: 12px; padding-top: 12px; border-top: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1);">
                <div style="font-size: 13px; color: #f1c40f; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 6px;">
                    🏆 里程碑成就
                </div>
                <div style="font-size: 12px; color: #bbb; margin-bottom: 4px;">
                    已达成 ${completedMilestones} / ${totalMilestones} 个
                </div>
                <div style="height: 6px; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.1); border-radius: 3px; overflow: hidden;">
                    <div style="height: 100%; width: ${(completedMilestones / totalMilestones * 100)}%; background: linear-gradient(90deg, #f1c40f, #e67e22); border-radius: 3px;"></div>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }
    
    html += '</div>';
    return html;
}


// 渲染左侧任务追踪器
function renderSidebarQuests() {
    const listEl = document.getElementById('sidebar-quests-list');
    if (!listEl || !game) return;
    
    const q = game.quests;
    const pendingQuests = [];
    
    // 新手任务
    const newbieQuests = [
        { id: 'q0', name: '整地开荒', icon: '⛏️', order: 0 },
        { id: 'q1', name: '购买种子', icon: '🌾', order: 1 },
        { id: 'q2', name: '播种育苗', icon: '🌱', order: 2 },
        { id: 'q3', name: '移栽插秧', icon: '🌿', order: 3 },
        { id: 'q6', name: '添置农具', icon: '🔧', order: 4 },
        { id: 'q8', name: '堆肥入门', icon: '💩', order: 5 },
        { id: 'q4', name: '丰收时节', icon: '🌾', order: 6 },
        { id: 'q5', name: '开市售卖', icon: '💰', order: 7 },
    ];
    
    // 发展任务
    const devQuests = [
        { id: 'q7', name: '乔迁之喜', icon: '🏠', order: 8 },
        { id: 'q9', name: '邻里初识', icon: '👋', order: 9 },
        { id: 'q10', name: '礼尚往来', icon: '🎁', order: 10 },
        { id: 'q11', name: '萌宠相伴', icon: '🐱', order: 11 },
        { id: 'q12', name: '熟能生巧', icon: '📚', order: 12 },
    ];
    
    // 成长任务
    const growQuests = [
        { id: 'q13', name: '扩土开疆', icon: '🌾', order: 13 },
        { id: 'q14', name: '田间能手', icon: '🌿', order: 14 },
        { id: 'q15', name: '村民挚友', icon: '🤝', order: 15 },
        { id: 'q16', name: '小有积蓄', icon: '💎', order: 16 },
        { id: 'q17', name: '德高望重', icon: '⭐', order: 17 },
    ];
    
    // 收集未完成任务
    const allQuests = [...newbieQuests, ...devQuests, ...growQuests];
    allQuests.forEach(quest => {
        if (!q[quest.id]) {
            pendingQuests.push(quest);
        }
    });
    
    // 只取前2个（避免拥挤）
    const displayQuests = pendingQuests.slice(0, 2);
    
    if (displayQuests.length === 0) {
        listEl.innerHTML = '<div style="color: #27ae60; font-size: 11px; text-align: center; padding: 10px 0;">🎉 全部完成！</div>';
        return;
    }
    
    let html = '';
    displayQuests.forEach(quest => {
        if (!quest || !quest.id) return;
        // 计算任务进度
        let progress = 0;
        
        if (quest.id === 'q0') {
            const hasPlowed = game.fields.some(f => f.step >= 1);
            progress = hasPlowed ? 100 : 0;
        } else if (quest.id === 'q1') {
            const hasSeeds = (game.seeds && (game.seeds.rice_spring > 0 || game.seeds.rice_summer > 0)) || (game.crops && game.crops.rice > 0);
            progress = hasSeeds ? 100 : 0;
        } else if (quest.id === 'q2') {
            const isSeedling = game.fields.some(f => f.stage === 'seedling');
            progress = isSeedling ? 100 : 0;
        } else if (quest.id === 'q3') {
            const isTransplanting = game.fields.some(f => f.stage === 'transplanting' || f.stage === 'growing');
            progress = isTransplanting ? 100 : 0;
        } else if (quest.id === 'q4') {
            const hasCrop = (game.crops && game.crops.rice > 0) || (game.crops && game.crops.sweet > 0);
            progress = hasCrop ? 100 : 0;
        } else if (quest.id === 'q5') {
            progress = q.q4 ? 50 : 0;
        } else if (quest.id === 'q6') {
            const hasTools = game.tools && game.tools.length > 0;
            progress = hasTools ? 100 : 0;
        } else if (quest.id === 'q8') {
            const hasCompost = game.composting || (game.items && game.items.organicFertilizer > 0);
            progress = hasCompost ? 100 : 0;
        } else if (quest.id === 'q12') {
            const level = game.skills && game.skills.cropFamiliarity ? game.skills.cropFamiliarity.level : 0;
            progress = Math.min(100, Math.floor(level / 2 * 100));
        } else if (quest.id === 'q14') {
            const level = game.skills && game.skills.fieldManagement ? game.skills.fieldManagement.level : 0;
            progress = Math.min(100, Math.floor(level / 3 * 100));
        } else if (quest.id === 'q16') {
            const totalAssets = game.money + 
                ((game.crops && game.crops.rice) || 0) * 2 + 
                ((game.crops && game.crops.sweet) || 0) * 1;
            progress = Math.min(100, Math.floor(totalAssets / 5000 * 100));
        } else if (quest.id === 'q17') {
            progress = Math.min(100, Math.floor((game.reputation || 0) / 100 * 100));
        }
        
        html += `
            <div class="sidebar-quest-item">
                <div class="sidebar-quest-item-name">
                    <span>${quest.icon || '✨'}</span>
                    <span>${quest.name || '未知任务'}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="sidebar-quest-progress">
                    <div class="sidebar-quest-progress-bar" style="width: ${Math.min(100, progress)}%"></div>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    });
    
    listEl.innerHTML = html;
}


// 页签解锁配置
const TAB_UNLOCK_CONFIG = {
    fields: { day: 1, name: '田地管理' },
    shop: { day: 1, name: '商店' },
    player: { day: 1, name: '角色属性' },
    tools: { day: 2, name: '农具商店' },
    npcs: { day: 2, name: '村民' },
    house: { day: 1, name: '房屋租赁' },
    skills: { day: 3, name: '技能树' },
    compost: { day: 1, name: '堆肥工坊' },
    foraging: { day: 5, name: '后山采集' },
    pets: { day: 5, name: '宠物' },
    buildings: { day: 7, name: '农家设施' },
    processing: { day: 10, money: 500, name: '农家副业' },
    tech: { day: 15, name: '农技研究' },
};

// 更新页签锁定状态
function updateTabLockStatus() {
    if (!game) return;
    if (!game.unlockedTabs) game.unlockedTabs = {};
    
    const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-tab[data-tab]');
    let newlyUnlocked = [];
    
    tabs.forEach(tab => {
        const tabKey = tab.dataset.tab;
        const config = TAB_UNLOCK_CONFIG[tabKey];
        
        if (!config) return;
        
        // 已永久解锁的不再检查
        if (game.unlockedTabs[tabKey]) {
            if (tab.classList.contains('locked')) {
                tab.classList.remove('locked');
            }
            return;
        }
        
        const isUnlocked = game.totalDay >= config.day && (!config.money || game.money >= config.money);
        const wasLocked = tab.classList.contains('locked');
        
        if (isUnlocked) {
            if (wasLocked) {
                tab.classList.remove('locked');
                game.unlockedTabs[tabKey] = true; // 永久解锁
                newlyUnlocked.push(config.name);
            }
        } else {
            if (!wasLocked) {
                tab.classList.add('locked');
            }
        }
    });
    
    // 显示解锁提示
    if (newlyUnlocked.length > 0 && typeof addLog === 'function') {
        newlyUnlocked.forEach(name => {
            addLog(`🔓 解锁了新功能：${name}`, 'info');
        });
        if (typeof showToast === 'function') {
            showToast(`解锁了${newlyUnlocked.length}个新功能！`, 'good');
        }
    }
}


function toggleQuestList() {
    const list = document.getElementById('quest-full-list');
    const btn = document.querySelector('.quest-more-btn');
    if (list) {
        list.classList.toggle('show');
        if (btn) {
            if (list.classList.contains('show')) {
                btn.innerHTML = '▲ 收起任务列表';
            } else {
                const totalPending = Object.keys(QUEST_DATA).filter(id => !game.quests[id]).length;
                btn.innerHTML = `▼ 查看全部任务 (${totalPending})`;
            }
        }
    }
}

function renderFieldCard(field, idx) {
    let html = '<div class="field-card">';
    html += `<div class="field-header">
                <span class="field-name">第${field.id}块田</span>
                <span class="field-level">${field.level}</span>
             </div>`;

    if (field.stage === 'idle' || !field.crop) {
        // 空闲状态
        if (!field.prepared) {
            // 未整地
            html += `<div style="text-align: center; margin: 0 0 12px; padding: 25px 0; background: linear-gradient(135deg, #fafafa 0%, #f5f5f5 100%); border-radius: 12px; margin-left: -5px; margin-right: -5px;">
                        <span style="font-size: 64px; opacity: 0.7;">🏜️</span>
                    </div>`;
            html += `<div class="field-status" style="text-align: center; color: #999; margin-bottom: 12px;">荒地，需要先整地</div>`;
            html += `<div class="field-progress"><div class="field-progress-bar" style="width: 0%"></div></div>`;
            html += '<div class="field-actions" style="justify-content: center; margin-top: 12px;">';
            const prepCost = Math.floor(15 * (game.tools.includes('hoe') ? 0.9 : 1));
            html += `<button class="action-btn" onclick="prepareField(${idx})" ${game.stamina < prepCost ? 'disabled' : ''}>⛏️ 整地 (-${prepCost}体力)</button>`;
            html += '</div>';
        } else {
            // 已整地，可以种植
            html += `<div style="text-align: center; margin: 0 0 12px; padding: 25px 0; background: linear-gradient(135deg, #e8f5e9 0%, #c8e6c9 100%); border-radius: 12px; margin-left: -5px; margin-right: -5px;">
                        <span style="font-size: 64px; opacity: 0.9;">🌱</span>
                    </div>`;
            html += `<div class="field-status" style="text-align: center; color: #27ae60; font-weight: 500; margin-bottom: 8px;">已整地，等待播种</div>`;
            html += `<div class="field-progress"><div class="field-progress-bar" style="width: 5%"></div></div>`;
            html += `<div style="margin: 10px 0 8px; font-size: 13px; color: #666; text-align: center;">选择作物种植：</div>`;
            html += '<div class="field-actions" style="justify-content: center;">';
            
            // 显示当前季节可种的作物
            const availableCrops = Object.entries(CROP_DATA).filter(([key, data]) => {
                return data.season === game.season;
            });
            
            // 计算当前季节剩余天数（每季28天）
            const daysLeftInSeason = 28 - game.day;
            
            if (availableCrops.length === 0) {
                html += '<div style="text-align: center; padding: 15px;">';
                html += '<div style="font-size: 36px; margin-bottom: 10px;">❄️</div>';
                html += '<div style="color: #999; font-size: 13px; margin-bottom: 8px;">当前季节无可种植作物</div>';
                html += '<div style="color: #bbb; font-size: 11px;">距离下一季还有 ' + daysLeftInSeason + ' 天</div>';
                html += '</div>';
            } else {
                html += '<div style="font-size: 11px; color: #999; text-align: center; margin-bottom: 8px;">本季剩余 ' + daysLeftInSeason + ' 天</div>';
                availableCrops.forEach(([key, data]) => {
                    const hasSeed = game.seeds[key] > 0;
                    const canHarvestInTime = data.growDays <= daysLeftInSeason + 10; // 留10天缓冲
                    
                    html += `<div style="width: 100%; margin-bottom: 6px;">`;
                    html += `<button class="action-btn" onclick="plantCrop(${idx}, '${key}')" ${!hasSeed ? 'disabled' : ''} style="width: 100%; justify-content: space-between;">`;
                    html += `<span>${data.emoji} ${data.name}</span>`;
                    html += `<span style="font-size: 11px; opacity: 0.7;">${data.growDays}天 | -12体力</span>`;
                    html += `</button>`;
                    if (!canHarvestInTime) {
                        html += `<div style="font-size: 10px; color: #e67e22; text-align: center; margin-top: 2px;">⚠️ 本季内可能来不及成熟</div>`;
                    }
                    html += `</div>`;
                });
            }
            
            html += '</div>';
        }
    } else {
        const cropData = CROP_DATA[field.crop];
        const progress = Math.min(100, field.growProgress);
        const isMature = field.stage === 'mature';
        const stageDesc = getStageDesc(field.stage, cropData.type);
        
        // 大图标作为视觉焦点
        const iconSize = isMature ? '72px' : '64px';
        const iconOpacity = isMature ? '1' : '0.9';
        // 根据生长阶段选择背景色
        const bgColor = isMature ? 'linear-gradient(135deg, #fff9e6 0%, #ffe082 100%)' 
                      : field.stage === 'seedling' ? 'linear-gradient(135deg, #e8f5e9 0%, #c8e6c9 100%)'
                      : 'linear-gradient(135deg, #f1f8e9 0%, #dcedc8 100%)';
        html += `<div style="text-align: center; margin: 0 0 12px; padding: 20px 0; background: ${bgColor}; border-radius: 12px; margin-left: -5px; margin-right: -5px;">
                    <span style="font-size: ${iconSize}; opacity: ${iconOpacity}; display: inline-block; filter: drop-shadow(0 4px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.15)); animation: float 3s ease-in-out infinite;">${cropData.emoji}</span>
                </div>`;
        
        html += `<div class="field-status" style="text-align: center; font-size: 15px; font-weight: 500; margin-bottom: 4px;">${cropData.name}</div>`;
        html += `<div class="field-status" style="text-align: center; color: #27ae60; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px;">${stageDesc}</div>`;
        html += `<div class="field-progress"><div class="field-progress-bar" style="width: ${progress}%"></div></div>`;
        html += `<div style="font-size: 12px; color: #999; margin-bottom: 12px; text-align: center;">生长进度：${Math.floor(progress)}%</div>`;
        
        // 状态标签
        const statusTags = [];
        const daysSinceWater = game.day - field.lastWaterDay;
        if (daysSinceWater < 5) {
            statusTags.push('<span style="background: #e8f5e9; color: #2e7d32; padding: 2px 8px; border-radius: 10px; font-size: 11px;">💧 水分充足</span>');
        }
        if (field.fertilized) {
            const fertText = field.fertilizerType === 'organic' ? '🌱 已施有机肥' : '🧪 已施化肥';
            statusTags.push(`<span style="background: #fff3e0; color: #e65100; padding: 2px 8px; border-radius: 10px; font-size: 11px;">${fertText}</span>`);
        }
        if (statusTags.length > 0) {
            html += `<div style="display: flex; gap: 6px; flex-wrap: wrap; justify-content: center; margin-bottom: 12px;">${statusTags.join('')}</div>`;
        }
        
        // 生长阶段文案
        html += `<div style="font-size: 12px; color: #666; margin-bottom: 12px; font-style: italic; line-height: 1.6; text-align: center; padding: 0 8px;">${getStageFlavorText(field.stage, cropData.type)}</div>`;
        
        html += '<div class="field-actions">';
        
        if (isMature) {
            // 成熟了，可以收割
            const harvestCost = Math.floor(20 * (game.tools.includes('sickle') ? 0.9 : 1) * (1 - ((game.skills.toolMastery && game.skills.toolMastery.level) || 0) * 0.03));
            html += `<button class="action-btn highlight" onclick="harvestCrop(${idx})" ${game.stamina < harvestCost ? 'disabled' : ''}>🌾 收割 (-${harvestCost}体力)</button>`;
        } else {
            // 育苗阶段
            if (field.stage === 'seedling') {
                const daysLeft = Math.ceil((cropData.seedlingDays || 5) - (game.day - field.plantedDay));
                if (daysLeft <= 0) {
                    const transplantCost = game.tools.includes('seedlingRider') ? 7 : 18;
                    html += `<button class="action-btn highlight" onclick="transplantCrop(${idx})" ${game.stamina < transplantCost ? 'disabled' : ''}>🌱 移栽 (-${transplantCost}体力)</button>`;
                } else {
                    html += `<span style="font-size: 12px; color: #999;">育苗中，还需${daysLeft}天</span>`;
                }
            }
            
            // 生长阶段的日常操作
            if (field.stage === 'growing' || field.stage === 'transplanting') {
                // 浇水
                const needWater = game.day - field.lastWaterDay >= 1;
                if (needWater) {
                    const waterCost = Math.floor(8 * (1 - ((game.skills.toolMastery && game.skills.toolMastery.level) || 0) * 0.03));
                    html += `<div><button class="action-btn" onclick="waterField(${idx})" ${game.stamina < waterCost ? 'disabled' : ''}>💧 浇水 (-${waterCost}体力)</button></div>`;
                } else {
                    html += `<div><span style="font-size: 12px; color: #27ae60;">✓ 水分充足</span></div>`;
                }
                
                // 除草
                const needWeed = game.day - field.lastWeedDay >= 3;
                if (needWeed && field.step >= 2) {
                    const weedCost = Math.floor(15 * (1 - ((game.skills.toolMastery && game.skills.toolMastery.level) || 0) * 0.03));
                    html += `<div><button class="action-btn" onclick="weedField(${idx})" ${game.stamina < weedCost ? 'disabled' : ''}>🌿 除草 (-${weedCost}体力)</button></div>`;
                } else if (field.step >= 2) {
                    html += `<div><span style="font-size: 12px; color: #27ae60;">✓ 无杂草</span></div>`;
                }
                
                // 施肥
                if (!field.fertilized && field.step >= 2) {
                    const fertCost = game.tools.includes('fertilizerCart') ? 6 : 10;
                    html += `<div style="display: flex; gap: 8px; flex-wrap: wrap;">`;
                    html += `<button class="action-btn" style="font-size: 12px; padding: 6px 10px;" onclick="fertilizeField(${idx}, 'normal')" ${game.stamina < fertCost ? 'disabled' : ''}>🧪 化肥(+5%) -${fertCost}体力</button>`;
                    html += `<button class="action-btn" style="font-size: 12px; padding: 6px 10px; background: #4a7c59;" onclick="fertilizeField(${idx}, 'organic')" ${game.stamina < fertCost ? 'disabled' : ''}>💩 有机肥(+8%) -${fertCost}体力</button>`;
                    html += `</div>`;
                } else if (field.fertilized) {
                    const fertType = field.fertilizerType === 'organic' ? '有机肥(+8%)' : '化肥(+5%)';
                    html += `<div><span style="font-size: 12px; color: #27ae60;">✓ 已施${fertType}</span></div>`;
                }
                
                // 红薯翻藤
                if (cropData.type === 'sweet') {
                    const growDays = game.day - field.plantedDay;
                    if (growDays >= 30 && !field.turnedVine1) {
                        const vineCost = Math.floor(13 * (game.tools.includes('hoe') ? 0.9 : 1));
                        html += `<button class="action-btn" onclick="turnVine(${idx}, 1)" ${game.stamina < vineCost ? 'disabled' : ''}>🍃 翻藤1 (-${vineCost}体力)</button>`;
                    }
                    if (growDays >= 60 && !field.turnedVine2 && field.turnedVine1) {
                        const vineCost2 = Math.floor(13 * (game.tools.includes('hoe') ? 0.9 : 1));
                        html += `<button class="action-btn" onclick="turnVine(${idx}, 2)" ${game.stamina < vineCost2 ? 'disabled' : ''}>🍃 翻藤2 (-${vineCost2}体力)</button>`;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        html += '</div>';
    }

    html += '</div>';
    return html;
}

// 获取生长阶段描述
function getStageDesc(stage, type) {
    const descs = {
        idle: '空闲',
        preparing: '整地中',
        seedling: type === 'rice' ? '育苗期' : '发芽期',
        transplanting: type === 'rice' ? '返青期' : '幼苗期',
        growing: {
            rice: '分蘖期',
            sweet: '藤蔓期',
            wheat: '拔节期',
            corn: '抽穗期',
            soybean: '开花期'
        }[type] || '生长期',
        mature: '成熟'
    };
    return descs[stage] || stage;
}

// 获取生长阶段风味文案
function getStageFlavorText(stage, type) {
    const texts = {
        idle: '土地荒着，长满了杂草。得先翻翻地才能种。',
        preparing: '你一锄头一锄头地翻着地，泥土的腥气扑面而来。',
        seedling: type === 'rice' 
            ? '嫩绿的秧苗从土里钻出来，细细的，弱不禁风的样子。再过几天就能移栽了。'
            : '小芽破土而出，顶着两片嫩绿色的小叶子，可爱极了。',
        transplanting: type === 'rice'
            ? '秧苗插下去了，看着有点蔫。别担心，过两天就缓过来了。'
            : '小苗已经站稳了脚跟，开始长出新的叶子。',
        growing: {
            rice: '稻苗长得很快，一天一个样。风一吹，沙沙地响，像在唱歌。',
            sweet: '红薯藤开始蔓延，绿油油的一片，爬得满地都是。',
            wheat: '麦苗蹭蹭往上长，远看像一片绿色的波浪，风一吹就起伏。',
            corn: '玉米秆子拔节抽穗，顶端冒出了毛茸茸的雄花，叶子绿得发亮。',
            soybean: '大豆开花了，白色和淡紫色的小花藏在叶腋间，像星星点点。'
        }[type] || '作物一天天长高，叶片越来越茂盛。',
        mature: {
            rice: '金黄的稻穗沉甸甸地弯下了腰，空气中弥漫着稻香。丰收的季节到了！',
            sweet: '红薯叶变得深绿，藤蔓下面藏着大大的红薯。可以挖啦！',
            wheat: '麦穗变得金黄饱满，麦芒一根根竖着，像一片金色的海洋。',
            corn: '玉米棒子鼓囊囊的，剥开外皮，金黄的籽粒排列整齐，甜香扑鼻。',
            soybean: '豆荚鼓了起来，摸上去硬硬的，里面的豆子已经饱满了。'
        }[type] || '作物已经成熟了，可以收获了！'
    };
    return texts[stage] || '';
}

// ===== 商店面板 =====
function renderShopPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🏪 商店</div>';
    
    html += '<div class="shop-tabs">';
    html += `<div class="shop-tab ${currentShopTab === 'seeds' ? 'active' : ''}" data-shop="seeds">🌱 购买种子</div>`;
    html += `<div class="shop-tab ${currentShopTab === 'items' ? 'active' : ''}" data-shop="items">🎒 购买道具</div>`;
    html += `<div class="shop-tab ${currentShopTab === 'sell' ? 'active' : ''}" data-shop="sell">💰 出售作物</div>`;
    html += `<div class="shop-tab ${currentShopTab === 'processed' ? 'active' : ''}" data-shop="processed">🍚 出售农副产品</div>`;
    html += `<div class="shop-tab ${currentShopTab === 'gifts' ? 'active' : ''}" data-shop="gifts">🎁 送礼道具</div>`;
    html += '</div>';
    
    html += '<div id="shop-content">';
    switch(currentShopTab) {
        case 'seeds': html += renderSeedsTab(); break;
        case 'items': html += renderItemsTab(); break;
        case 'sell': html += renderSellTab(); break;
        case 'processed': html += renderProcessedSellTab(); break;
        case 'gifts': html += renderGiftsTab(); break;
    }
    html += '</div>';
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
    
    // 绑定页签点击
    document.querySelectorAll('.shop-tab').forEach(tab => {
        tab.addEventListener('click', function() {
            playTabSound();
            document.querySelectorAll('.shop-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
            this.classList.add('active');
            currentShopTab = this.dataset.shop;
            refreshShopContent();
        });
    });
}

// 只刷新商店内容，不重新渲染整个面板
function refreshShopContent() {
    let content = '';
    switch(currentShopTab) {
        case 'seeds': content = renderSeedsTab(); break;
        case 'items': content = renderItemsTab(); break;
        case 'sell': content = renderSellTab(); break;
        case 'processed': content = renderProcessedSellTab(); break;
        case 'gifts': content = renderGiftsTab(); break;
    }
    const shopContent = document.getElementById('shop-content');
    if (shopContent) {
        shopContent.innerHTML = content;
    }
}

function renderSellTab() {
    let html = '';
    
    const cropTypes = ['rice', 'sweet', 'wheat', 'corn', 'soybean', 'potato', 'peanut', 'pepper', 'cabbage', 'radish', 'eggplant', 'garlic'];
    const cropNames = { rice: '水稻', sweet: '红薯', wheat: '小麦', corn: '玉米', soybean: '大豆', potato: '土豆', peanut: '花生', pepper: '辣椒', cabbage: '白菜', radish: '萝卜', eggplant: '茄子', garlic: '大蒜' };
    const cropEmojis = { rice: '🌾', sweet: '🍠', wheat: '🌾', corn: '🌽', soybean: '🫘', potato: '🥔', peanut: '🥜', pepper: '🌶️', cabbage: '🥬', radish: '🥕', eggplant: '🍆', garlic: '🧄' };
    
    cropTypes.forEach(cropKey => {
        const amount = game.crops[cropKey] || 0;
        if (amount < 1) return; // 只显示有库存的作物
        const price = getSeasonPrice(cropKey);
        html += `<div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${cropEmojis[cropKey] || '🌱'}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${cropNames[cropKey] || cropKey}</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">库存：${Math.floor(amount)} kg</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 10px;">
                        <span class="shop-item-price">${price}元/kg</span>
                        <button class="buy-btn" onclick="sellCrop('${cropKey}', 10)" ${amount < 10 ? 'disabled' : ''}>卖10kg</button>
                        <button class="buy-btn" onclick="sellCrop('${cropKey}', 'all')" ${amount < 1 ? 'disabled' : ''}>全部出售</button>
                    </div>
                 </div>`;
    });
    
    if (html === '') {
        html = '<p style="color: #999; text-align: center; padding: 40px;">暂无可出售的作物</p>';
    }
    
    return html;
}

function renderProcessedSellTab() {
    let html = '';
    
    const processedItems = [
        { key: 'riceGrain', name: '糙米', emoji: '🍚' },
        { key: 'driedSweetPotato', name: '红薯干', emoji: '🍠' },
        { key: 'driedFish', name: '鱼干', emoji: '🐟' },
        { key: 'fishBall', name: '鱼丸', emoji: '🍡' },
        { key: 'fishSoup', name: '鲜鱼汤', emoji: '🍲' },
        { key: 'polishedRice', name: '精米', emoji: '✨' },
        { key: 'riceWine', name: '米酒', emoji: '🍶' },
        { key: 'riceCake', name: '米糕', emoji: '🥮' },
        { key: 'sweetPotatoStarch', name: '红薯粉', emoji: '💨' },
        { key: 'sweetPotatoNoodles', name: '红薯粉条', emoji: '🍜' },
        { key: 'flour', name: '面粉', emoji: '🥖' },
        { key: 'noodles', name: '手工面条', emoji: '🍜' },
        { key: 'tofu', name: '豆腐', emoji: '🧊' },
        { key: 'soyMilk', name: '豆浆', emoji: '🥛' },
        { key: 'cornOil', name: '玉米油', emoji: '🌽' },
        { key: 'potatoChips', name: '薯片', emoji: '🥔' },
        { key: 'potatoStarch', name: '土豆淀粉', emoji: '💨' },
        { key: 'peanutOil', name: '花生油', emoji: '🥜' },
        { key: 'peanutCandy', name: '花生糖', emoji: '🍬' },
        { key: 'chiliSauce', name: '辣椒酱', emoji: '🌶️' },
        { key: 'chiliOil', name: '辣椒油', emoji: '🌶️' },
        { key: 'honey', name: '蜂蜜', emoji: '🍯' },
        { key: 'mushroom', name: '栽培蘑菇', emoji: '🍄' },
        { key: 'pickle', name: '腌咸菜', emoji: '🥒' }
    ];
    
    let hasAny = false;
    processedItems.forEach(item => {
        const have =(game.processedItems && game.processedItems[item.key]) || 0;
        if (have < 1) return;
        hasAny = true;
        
        const product = PROCESSED_ITEMS[item.key];
        if (!product) return;
        
        let price = getProcessedItemPrice(item.key);
        
        html += `<div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${item.emoji}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${item.name}</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">库存：${Math.floor(have)} 斤</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 10px;">
                        <span class="shop-item-price">${price.toFixed(1)}元/斤</span>
                        <button class="buy-btn" onclick="sellProcessedItem('${item.key}', 5)" ${have < 5 ? 'disabled' : ''}>卖5斤</button>
                        <button class="buy-btn" onclick="sellProcessedItem('${item.key}', ${have})" ${have < 1 ? 'disabled' : ''}>全部出售</button>
                    </div>
                 </div>`;
    });
    
    if (!hasAny) {
        html = '<p style="color: #999; text-align: center; padding: 40px;">暂无可出售的农副产品</p>';
    }
    
    return html;
}

function renderSeedsTab() {
    let html = '';
    
    // 按季节分组排序：当前季节优先，然后春夏秋冬顺序
    const seasonOrder = { spring: 1, summer: 2, autumn: 3, winter: 4 };
    const currentSeason = game.season || 'spring';
    const seasonPriority = { [currentSeason]: 0, spring: 1, summer: 2, autumn: 3, winter: 4 };
    
    const sortedCrops = Object.entries(CROP_DATA).sort((a, b) => {
        const sa = a[1].season;
        const sb = b[1].season;
        // 先按季节优先级排
        if (seasonPriority[sa] !== seasonPriority[sb]) {
            return seasonPriority[sa] - seasonPriority[sb];
        }
        // 同季节按类型顺序（rice, sweet, wheat, corn, soybean）
        const typeOrder = { rice: 1, sweet: 2, wheat: 3, corn: 4, soybean: 5, potato: 6, peanut: 7, pepper: 8, cabbage: 9, radish: 10, eggplant: 11, garlic: 12 };
        return (typeOrder[a[1].type] || 99) - (typeOrder[b[1].type] || 99);
    });
    
    let lastSeason = null;
    sortedCrops.forEach(([key, data]) => {
        const inSeason = data.season === game.season;
        const owned = game.seeds[key] || 0;
        
        // 季节分隔线
        if (data.season !== lastSeason) {
            const seasonLabels = { spring: '🌸 春季', summer: '☀️ 夏季', autumn: '🍂 秋季', winter: '❄️ 冬季' };
            html += `<div style="padding: 8px 0; margin: 8px 0; border-bottom: 1px solid #e0e0e0; font-size: 13px; color: #888; font-weight: bold;">${seasonLabels[data.season] || data.season}作物</div>`;
            lastSeason = data.season;
        }
        
        html += `<div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${data.emoji}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${data.name}种子 ${!inSeason ? '（非种植季节）' : ''}</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">生长周期：${data.growDays}天 | 基础亩产：${data.baseYield}kg | 已拥有：${owned}亩</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 10px;">
                        <span class="shop-item-price">${getSeedPrice(data.seedPrice)}元/亩</span>
                        <button class="buy-btn" onclick="buySeed('${key}')" ${game.money < data.seedPrice ? 'disabled' : ''}>购买1亩</button>
                    </div>
                 </div>`;
    });
    
    return html;
}

function renderItemsTab() {
    const items = [
        { key: 'fertilizer', name: '化肥', emoji: '🧪', price: 50, desc: '作物产量+5%' },
        { key: 'pesticide', name: '农药', emoji: '💊', price: 80, desc: '治疗病虫害' },
        { key: 'bun', name: '肉包子', emoji: '🥟', price: 20, desc: '体力+20，健康+5' },
        { key: 'medicine', name: '感冒药', emoji: '💊', price: 100, desc: '健康+30' }
    ];
    
    let html = '';
    items.forEach(item => {
        const owned = game.items[item.key] || 0;
        html += `<div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${item.emoji}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${item.name}</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">${item.desc} | 已拥有：${owned}个</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 10px;">
                        <span class="shop-item-price">${item.price}元</span>
                        <button class="buy-btn" onclick="buyItem('${item.key}')" ${game.money < item.price ? 'disabled' : ''}>购买</button>
                    </div>
                 </div>`;
    });
    
    return html;
}
