// ===== 其他面板（占位） =====
function renderHousePanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🏠 房屋租赁</div>';
    
    // 当前房屋信息 + 睡觉按钮
    const currentHouse = HOUSE_DATA[game.house];
    html += `
        <div class="shop-item current" style="background: #e8f5e9; border: 2px solid #4a7c59;">
            <div class="shop-item-info">
                <div class="shop-item-icon">${currentHouse.emoji}</div>
                <div>
                    <div class="shop-item-name">当前住所：${currentHouse.name}</div>
                    <div class="shop-item-desc">${currentHouse.desc}</div>
                    <div class="shop-item-desc" style="color: #4a7c59; margin-top: 4px;">
                        ⚡ 每小时恢复体力：${currentHouse.staminaRegen}点 &nbsp;|&nbsp; 
                        ❤️ 夜间恢复健康：+${currentHouse.healthRegen}
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div>
                <button class="shop-btn" onclick="goSleep()">💤 睡觉恢复</button>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div style="margin: 15px 0; color: #666; font-size: 0.9em;">
            💡 睡觉将跳过当天剩余时间，直接到第二天早上，并恢复体力和健康。
        </div>
    `;
    
    const houseOrder = ['新手房', '进阶房', '精英房', '终极房'];
    
    houseOrder.forEach(houseName => {
        const house = HOUSE_DATA[houseName];
        const isCurrent = game.house === houseName;
        const currentIndex = houseOrder.indexOf(game.house);
        const houseIndex = houseOrder.indexOf(houseName);
        const canUpgrade = houseIndex === currentIndex + 1; // 只能升级下一级
        const canAfford = game.money >= house.upgradeCost;
        
        html += `
            <div class="shop-item ${isCurrent ? 'current' : ''}">
                <div class="shop-item-info">
                    <div class="shop-item-icon">${house.emoji}</div>
                    <div>
                        <div class="shop-item-name">${house.name} ${isCurrent ? '（当前）' : ''}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${house.desc}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc" style="color: #666; margin-top: 4px;">
                            ⚡ 体力恢复：${house.staminaRegen}点/小时 &nbsp;|&nbsp; 
                            ❤️ 健康恢复：+${house.healthRegen}/夜间 &nbsp;|&nbsp;
                            💰 租金：${house.rent}元/季
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div>
                    ${isCurrent ? '' : 
                      canUpgrade ? 
                        `<button class="shop-btn ${canAfford ? '' : 'disabled'}" onclick="upgradeHouse('${houseName}')">
                            升级 (${house.upgradeCost}元)
                        </button>` :
                        `<button class="shop-btn disabled" disabled>未解锁</button>`
                    }
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    });
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

// 睡觉恢复功能
function goSleep() {
    if (!game) return;
    
    const houseData = HOUSE_DATA[game.house];
    if (!houseData) return;
    
    // 计算恢复量：从当前时间到24小时的剩余小时数 * 每小时恢复量
    const hoursRemaining = 24 - game.time;
    const staminaRecovery = houseData.staminaRegen * hoursRemaining;
    const healthRecovery = houseData.healthRegen;
    
    // 恢复体力，溢出部分转健康
    const oldStamina = game.stamina;
    game.stamina = Math.min(game.maxStamina, game.stamina + staminaRecovery);
    const staminaOverflow = oldStamina + staminaRecovery - game.stamina; // 溢出的体力恢复
    
    // 恢复健康（基础恢复 + 溢出体力转健康，每3点溢出体力转1点健康）
    const healthFromOverflow = Math.floor(staminaOverflow / 3);
    const totalHealthRecovery = healthRecovery + healthFromOverflow;
    game.health = Math.min(game.maxHealth, game.health + totalHealthRecovery);
    
    // 重置时间到早上6点
    game.time = 6;
    
    // 增加天数（跳过当天）
    game.day++;
    game.totalDay = (game.totalDay || game.day) + 1;
    
    // 检查季节切换
    advanceSeason();
    
    // 触发新的一天逻辑
    if (typeof onNewDay === 'function') {
        onNewDay();
    }
    
    addLog(`💤 你睡了一觉。体力恢复+${staminaRecovery}，健康恢复+${totalHealthRecovery}${healthFromOverflow > 0 ? '（含' + healthFromOverflow + '点溢出体力转健康）' : ''}。新的一天开始了！`, 'good');
    
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    showToast('睡了一觉，精神饱满！', 'good');
}

function renderToolsPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🔧 农具商店</div>';
    
    const toolTypes = [
        { type: 'basic', name: '基础农具' },
        { type: 'advanced', name: '进阶农具' },
        { type: '高级', name: '高级农具' }
    ];
    
    toolTypes.forEach(typeInfo => {
        const toolsOfType = Object.entries(TOOL_DATA).filter(([key, tool]) => tool.type === typeInfo.type);
        if (toolsOfType.length === 0) return;
        
        html += `<div class="shop-category">${typeInfo.name}</div>`;
        
        toolsOfType.forEach(([toolKey, tool]) => {
            const owned = game.tools.includes(toolKey);
            const canAfford = game.money >= tool.price;
            // 暂时所有农具都可以买，解锁条件后面再加
            const unlocked = true;
            
            html += `
                <div class="shop-item ${owned ? 'owned' : ''}">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${tool.emoji}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${tool.name} ${owned ? '（已拥有）' : ''}</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">${tool.desc}</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc" style="color: #4a7c59; margin-top: 4px;">
                                ✨ 效果：${tool.effect}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        ${owned ? '' : 
                          unlocked ? 
                            `<button class="shop-btn ${canAfford ? '' : 'disabled'}" onclick="buyTool('${toolKey}')">
                                购买 (${tool.price}元)
                            </button>` :
                            `<button class="shop-btn disabled" disabled>未解锁</button>`
                        }
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        });
    });
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

// 角色属性面板

// ===== 采集面板 =====
function goForaging() {
    // 检查是否是白天（6:00-20:00）
    if (game.time < 6 || game.time >= 20) {
        showToast('天黑了，山路不好走，等明天天亮再去吧', 'warn');
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.dailyActions.foraging >= 1) {
        showToast('今天已经去过后山转了一圈，篮子都装满了，明天再去吧', 'warn');
        return;
    }
    if (game.stamina < 15) {
        showToast('感觉累得不行了，歇会儿再来吧', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    game.dailyActions.foraging++;
    const seasonData = FORAGING_DATA[game.season];
    if (!seasonData) {
        showToast('这个季节没什么可采集的', 'warn');
        return;
    }
    
    // 随机选择一个采集物
    const item = seasonData.items[Math.floor(Math.random() * seasonData.items.length)];
    let amount = Math.floor(Math.random() * (item.maxAmount - item.minAmount + 1)) + item.minAmount;
    
    // 社区建设加成（小河石桥：采集物产量+50%）
    if (game.foragingBonus) {
        amount = Math.floor(amount * game.foragingBonus);
    }
    
    // 检查体力
    if (game.stamina < item.staminaCost) {
        showToast('感觉累得不行了，先吃点东西或睡一觉恢复体力再来吧', 'warn');
        return;
    }
    
    game.stamina -= item.staminaCost;
    if (!game.foragingItems) game.foragingItems = {};
    game.foragingItems[item.id] = (game.foragingItems[item.id] || 0) + amount;
    
    // 统计
    if (!game.stats) game.stats = {};
    game.stats.totalForage = (game.stats.totalForage || 0) + 1;
    
    // 解锁图鉴
    unlockCollectionItem('foraging', item.id);
    
    // 消耗2小时游戏时间
    game.time += 2;
    
    addLog(`🌿 去后山转了一圈，花了两个钟头，采了${amount}斤${item.name}，累坏了。体力-${item.staminaCost}`, 'good');
    
    // 任务检查：第一次采集
    if (!game.quests.q20) {
        game.quests.q20 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q20', 80, '✅ 任务完成：山野采集，奖励80元');
    }
    
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    checkAchievements();
    showToast(`采了${amount}斤${item.name}！`, 'good');
}

function renderForagingPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🌿 后山采集</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">后山四季都有好东西，带上篮子去转转，说不定能采到宝贝。</p>';
    
    // 采集按钮
    const canForage = game.dailyActions.foraging < 1 && game.stamina >= 15;
    html += `<div style="margin-bottom: 20px;">`;
    html += `<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="goForaging()" ${canForage ? '' : 'disabled'} style="width: 100%; padding: 15px; font-size: 16px;">`;
    html += `🧺 去后山采集 ${canForage ? '' : '(今天已去或体力不足)'}`;
    html += `</button>`;
    html += `</div>`;
    
    // 当前季节可采集物品
    const seasonData = FORAGING_DATA[game.season];
    if (seasonData) {
        html += '<div class="section-title">🌱 这个季节能采到</div>';
        html += '<div class="processing-list">';
        seasonData.items.forEach(item => {
            html += `
                <div class="processing-card">
                    <div class="processing-header">
                        <span class="processing-emoji">${item.emoji}</span>
                        <span class="processing-name">${item.name}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="processing-stats">
                        <div>一次能采 ${item.minAmount}~${item.maxAmount} 斤</div>
                        <div>消耗 ${item.staminaCost} 点体力</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        });
        html += '</div>';
    }
    
    // 已采集物品
    html += '<div class="section-title">🎒 采集成果</div>';
    html += '<div class="processing-list">';
    let hasItems = false;
    if (game.foragingItems) {
        for (const [id, amount] of Object.entries(game.foragingItems)) {
            if (amount > 0) {
                hasItems = true;
                // 查找物品信息
                let itemInfo = null;
                for (const season of Object.values(FORAGING_DATA)) {
                    const found = season.items.find(i => i.id === id);
                    if (found) { itemInfo = found; break; }
                }
                const price = itemInfo ? itemInfo.basePrice : 5;
                html += `
                    <div class="processing-card">
                        <div class="processing-header">
                            <span class="processing-emoji">${itemInfo ? itemInfo.emoji : '🌿'}</span>
                            <span class="processing-name">${itemInfo ? itemInfo.name : id}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="processing-output">
                            <span>库存: ${amount} 斤</span>
                            <span class="output-price">${price}元/斤</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="processing-actions">
                            <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="sellForagingItem('${id}', 5)" ${amount < 5 ? 'disabled' : ''}>卖5斤</button>
                            <button class="btn btn-success" onclick="sellForagingItem('${id}', ${amount})" ${amount < 1 ? 'disabled' : ''}>全卖了</button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
            }
        }
    }
    if (!hasItems) {
        html += '<div class="empty-state">还没有采集到任何东西，去后山转转吧</div>';
    }
    html += '</div>';
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

// ===== 钓鱼面板 =====
function renderFishingPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🎣 河边钓鱼</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">村头小河边鱼虾不少，带上钓竿去碰碰运气。钓到的鱼会存入自家鱼塘，可以烹饪或出售。注意：晚上太黑没法钓鱼。</p>';
    
    // 钓鱼状态
    if (!game.fishToday) game.fishToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (game.fishToday.day !== game.day) {
        game.fishToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    }
    const canFish = game.fishToday.count < 5 && game.stamina >= 15;
    const isDaytime = game.time >= 6 && game.time < 20;
    
    html += `<div style="margin-bottom: 20px;">`;
    html += `<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="goFishing()" ${canFish && isDaytime ? '' : 'disabled'} style="width: 100%; padding: 15px; font-size: 16px;">`;
    if (!isDaytime) {
        html += `🌙 天黑了，等明天天亮再来吧`;
    } else if (game.fishToday.count >= 5) {
        html += `🎣 今天已经钓了5次了，明天再来吧`;
    } else if (game.stamina < 15) {
        html += `🎣 太累了，歇会儿再来吧`;
    } else {
        html += `🎣 去河边钓鱼 (-15体力)`;
    }
    html += `</button>`;
    html += `</div>`;
    
    // 鱼塘库存
    html += '<div class="section-title">🐟 鱼塘</div>';
    html += '<div class="processing-list">';
    
    if (game.fishInventory) {
        const fishTypes = {
            'carp': { name: '鲤鱼', emoji: '🐟' },
            'catfish': { name: '鲶鱼', emoji: '🐡' },
            'crucian': { name: '鲫鱼', emoji: '🐠' },
            'grass_carp': { name: '草鱼', emoji: '🐟' }
        };
        
        let hasFish = false;
        for (const [fishKey, count] of Object.entries(game.fishInventory)) {
            if (count > 0) {
                hasFish = true;
                const fishInfo = fishTypes[fishKey] || { name: fishKey, emoji: '🐟' };
                html += `
                    <div class="processing-card">
                        <div class="processing-header">
                            <span class="processing-emoji">${fishInfo.emoji}</span>
                            <span class="processing-name">${fishInfo.name}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="processing-output">
                            <span>库存: ${count} 斤</span>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
            }
        }
        if (!hasFish) {
            html += '<div class="empty-state">鱼塘里还没有鱼，快去钓几条吧</div>';
        } else {
            html += `<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="sellAllFish()" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 10px; padding: 12px; font-size: 15px;">💰 全部卖掉</button>`;
        }
    } else {
        html += '<div class="empty-state">鱼塘里还没有鱼，快去钓几条吧</div>';
    }
    
    html += '</div>';
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

function sellAllFish() {
    if (!game.fishInventory) {
        showToast('鱼塘里空空如也', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    const fishPrices = {
        'carp': 15,
        'catfish': 20,
        'crucian': 12,
        'grass_carp': 14
    };
    
    let totalMoney = 0;
    let totalWeight = 0;
    let soldLog = [];
    
    for (const [fishKey, count] of Object.entries(game.fishInventory)) {
        if (count > 0) {
            const price = fishPrices[fishKey] || 10;
            const money = Math.floor(count * price);
            totalMoney += money;
            totalWeight += count;
            soldLog.push(`${getFishName(fishKey)} ${count}斤`);
            delete game.fishInventory[fishKey];
        }
    }
    
    if (totalMoney <= 0) {
        showToast('鱼塘里空空如也', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    game.money += totalMoney;
    addLog(`💰 卖掉了${soldLog.join('、')}，共${totalWeight}斤鱼，获得${totalMoney}元`, 'success');
    playSound('coin');
    showToast(`卖掉${totalWeight}斤鱼，获得${totalMoney}元`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    updateTopBar();
    renderFishingPanel();
}

function sellForagingItem(itemId, amount) {
    if (!game.foragingItems || !game.foragingItems[itemId] || game.foragingItems[itemId] < amount) {
        showToast('库存不足', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    // 查找价格
    let price = 5;
    for (const season of Object.values(FORAGING_DATA)) {
        const item = season.items.find(i => i.id === itemId);
        if (item) { price = item.basePrice; break; }
    }
    
    const money = Math.floor(price * amount);
    game.foragingItems[itemId] -= amount;
    if (game.foragingItems[itemId] <= 0) {
        delete game.foragingItems[itemId];
    }
    game.money += money;
    
    addLog(`💰 卖了${amount}斤${itemId}，获得${money}元`, 'success');
    playSound('coin');
    
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    showToast(`卖了${amount}斤，获得${money}元`, 'good');
}

// ===== 加工坊面板 =====
// ===== 农家副业面板 =====
// 获取加工产品售价（与sellProcessedItem统一逻辑）
function getProcessedItemPrice(itemKey) {
    const item = PROCESSED_ITEMS[itemKey];
    if (!item) return 0;
    
    const basePrice = item.basePrice || 0;
    
    // 应用季节波动（基于原材料类型）
    const seasonalMultipliers = {
        rice: { spring: 1.1, summer: 1.0, autumn: 0.85, winter: 1.05 },
        sweet: { spring: 1.0, summer: 1.0, autumn: 0.9, winter: 1.25 },
        fish: { spring: 1.15, summer: 1.1, autumn: 0.9, winter: 0.7 },
        wheat: { spring: 1.05, summer: 0.9, autumn: 1.15, winter: 1.0 },
        soybean: { spring: 1.1, summer: 1.05, autumn: 0.95, winter: 1.15 },
        corn: { spring: 1.0, summer: 1.1, autumn: 1.2, winter: 0.85 },
        potato: { spring: 1.1, summer: 1.0, autumn: 1.0, winter: 1.0 },
        peanut: { spring: 1.0, summer: 1.1, autumn: 1.2, winter: 0.9 },
        pepper: { spring: 1.0, summer: 1.2, autumn: 1.1, winter: 0.8 },
        honey: { spring: 1.2, summer: 1.1, autumn: 1.0, winter: 0.9 },
        mushroom: { spring: 1.1, summer: 1.0, autumn: 1.2, winter: 0.9 },
        cabbage: { spring: 1.0, summer: 0.9, autumn: 1.1, winter: 1.2 }
    };
    
    // 判断属于哪一类
    let cropType = null;
    if (['riceGrain', 'polishedRice', 'riceWine', 'riceCake'].includes(itemKey)) {
        cropType = 'rice';
    } else if (['driedSweetPotato', 'sweetPotatoStarch', 'sweetPotatoNoodles'].includes(itemKey)) {
        cropType = 'sweet';
    } else if (['driedFish', 'fishBall', 'fishSoup'].includes(itemKey)) {
        cropType = 'fish';
    } else if (['flour', 'noodles'].includes(itemKey)) {
        cropType = 'wheat';
    } else if (['tofu', 'soyMilk'].includes(itemKey)) {
        cropType = 'soybean';
    } else if (['cornOil'].includes(itemKey)) {
        cropType = 'corn';
    } else if (['potatoChips', 'potatoStarch'].includes(itemKey)) {
        cropType = 'potato';
    } else if (['peanutOil', 'peanutCandy'].includes(itemKey)) {
        cropType = 'peanut';
    } else if (['chiliSauce', 'chiliOil'].includes(itemKey)) {
        cropType = 'pepper';
    } else if (['honey'].includes(itemKey)) {
        cropType = 'honey';
    } else if (['mushroom'].includes(itemKey)) {
        cropType = 'mushroom';
    } else if (['pickle'].includes(itemKey)) {
        cropType = 'cabbage';
    }
    
    let multiplier = 1.0;
    if (cropType && seasonalMultipliers[cropType] && seasonalMultipliers[cropType][game.season]) {
        multiplier = seasonalMultipliers[cropType][game.season];
    }
    
    // 每日小幅波动（模拟市场行情，±5%）
    const dailyFluctuation = 1 + Math.sin((game.day / 7) * Math.PI * 2) * 0.05;
    
    return Math.round(basePrice * multiplier * dailyFluctuation * 100) / 100;
}

// 获取副业原料描述
function getInputDesc(item) {
    let inputName = '';
    let inputAmount = item.inputAmount || 10;
    
    if (item.inputCrop === 'rice') {
        inputName = '稻谷';
    } else if (item.inputCrop === 'sweet') {
        inputName = '红薯';
    } else if (item.inputCrop === 'wheat') {
        inputName = '小麦';
    } else if (item.inputCrop === 'corn') {
        inputName = '玉米';
    } else if (item.inputCrop === 'soybean') {
        inputName = '大豆';
    } else if (item.inputCrop === 'potato') {
        inputName = '土豆';
    } else if (item.inputCrop === 'peanut') {
        inputName = '花生';
    } else if (item.inputCrop === 'pepper') {
        inputName = '辣椒';
    } else if (item.inputCrop === 'cabbage') {
        inputName = '白菜';
    } else if (item.inputCrop === 'radish') {
        inputName = '萝卜';
    } else if (item.inputCrop === 'eggplant') {
        inputName = '茄子';
    } else if (item.inputCrop === 'garlic') {
        inputName = '大蒜';
    } else if (item.inputType === 'fish') {
        inputName = '鲜鱼';
    } else if (item.inputType === 'processed' && item.inputItem) {
        const inputItem = PROCESSED_ITEMS[item.inputItem];
        inputName = inputItem ? inputItem.name : '原料';
    } else {
        inputName = '原料';
    }
    
    const outputName =(PROCESSED_ITEMS[item.outputItem] && PROCESSED_ITEMS[item.outputItem].name) || '产品';
    return `${inputAmount}斤${inputName}出${item.outputAmount}斤${outputName}`;
}

function renderProcessingPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🏡 农家副业</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">农闲的时候做点副业，换点零花钱。都是农家自己的手艺，产量不高，但都是实打实的好东西。</p>';
    
    // 进行中的加工任务
    const activeJobs = game.processingJobs && game.processingJobs.filter(j => !j.completed) || [];
    if (activeJobs.length > 0) {
        html += '<div class="section-title">⏳ 加工中</div>';
        html += '<div class="processing-list">';
        activeJobs.forEach(job => {
            const product = PROCESSED_ITEMS[job.outputItem];
            html += `
                <div class="processing-card">
                    <div class="processing-header">
                        <span class="processing-emoji">⏳</span>
                        <span class="processing-name">${job.buildingName}加工中</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="processing-desc">${(product && product.name) || ''}制作中，还需约${Math.max(0, job.duration - Math.floor(job.progress * job.duration / 100))}小时</div>
                    <div class="processing-stats">
                        <div style="width:100%;background:#e0e0e0;border-radius:4px;height:12px;margin-top:8px;">
                            <div style="width:${job.progress}%;background:#27ae60;height:12px;border-radius:4px;transition:width 0.5s;"></div>
                        </div>
                        <div style="text-align:center;font-size:11px;color:#666;margin-top:2px;">${job.progress}%</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        });
        html += '</div>';
    }
    
    // 已经会的副业
    html += '<div class="section-title">🌾 已置办的副业</div>';
    html += '<div class="processing-list">';
    
    let hasUnlocked = false;
    for (const [key, item] of Object.entries(PROCESSING_DATA)) {
        if (game.builtProcessing && game.builtProcessing[key] > 0) {
            hasUnlocked = true;
            
            const product = PROCESSED_ITEMS[item.outputItem];
            const have =(game.processedItems && game.processedItems[item.outputItem]) || 0;
            const dailyDone =(game.dailyProcessed && game.dailyProcessed[key]) || 0;
            
            // 计算价格
            let price = getProcessedItemPrice(item.outputItem);
            
            // 获取加工坊等级
            const buildingLevel = game.builtProcessing[key] || 1;
            const dailyCapacity = item.levelCapacity ? item.levelCapacity[buildingLevel - 1] : item.dailyCapacity;
            const levelStaminaCost = item.levelStaminaCost ? item.levelStaminaCost[buildingLevel - 1] : item.staminaCost;
            const canUpgrade = buildingLevel < 3 && item.upgradeCost;
            const upgradeBtn = canUpgrade ? 
                `<button class="buy-btn" onclick="upgradeProcessing('${key}')" ${game.money < item.upgradeCost[buildingLevel-1] ? 'disabled' : ''}>⬆️ Lv${buildingLevel+1}（${item.upgradeCost[buildingLevel-1]}元）</button>` : 
                '<span style="color:#27ae60;">✅ 已满级</span>';
            
            html += `
                <div class="processing-card">
                    <div class="processing-header">
                        <span class="processing-emoji">${item.emoji}</span>
                        <span class="processing-name">${item.name} <span style="color:#f39c12;font-size:14px;">Lv${buildingLevel}</span></span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="processing-desc">${item.desc}</div>
                    <div class="processing-stats">
                        <div>一天最多做${dailyCapacity}斤的量</div>
                        <div>今天已经做了${dailyDone}斤</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="processing-output">
                        <span class="output-item">${product.emoji} ${product.name}: ${have}斤</span>
                        <span class="output-price">能卖 ${price.toFixed(1)}元/斤</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="processing-actions">
                        ${(() => {
                            const dailyDone =(game.dailyProcessed && game.dailyProcessed[key]) || 0;
                            const remaining = dailyCapacity - dailyDone;
                            const canProcess = remaining >= item.inputAmount && game.stamina >= levelStaminaCost;
                            return `<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="manualProcess('${key}')" ${canProcess ? '' : 'disabled'}>⚡ 开始加工（耗${levelStaminaCost}体力）${!canProcess && remaining < item.inputAmount ? '(今日已达上限)' : ''}</button>`;
                        })()}
                        ${upgradeBtn}
                        <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="sellProcessedItem('${item.outputItem}', 5)" ${have < 5 ? 'disabled' : ''}>卖5斤</button>
                        <button class="btn btn-success" onclick="sellProcessedItem('${item.outputItem}', ${have})" ${have < 1 ? 'disabled' : ''}>全卖了</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        }
    }
    
    if (!hasUnlocked) {
        html += '<div class="empty-state">还没开始做副业呢</div>';
    }
    
    html += '</div>';
    
    // 可以学的副业
    html += '<div class="section-title">🔧 可置办的手艺</div>';
    html += '<div class="processing-list">';
    
    let hasAvailable = false;
    for (const [key, item] of Object.entries(PROCESSING_DATA)) {
        if (game.builtProcessing && game.builtProcessing[key] > 0) continue;
        
        const unlocked = isProcessingUnlocked(key);
        hasAvailable = true;
        
        html += `
            <div class="processing-card ${unlocked ? '' : 'locked'}">
                <div class="processing-header">
                    <span class="processing-emoji">${item.emoji}</span>
                    <span class="processing-name">${item.name}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="processing-desc">${item.desc}</div>
                <div class="processing-stats">
                    <div>${getInputDesc(item)}</div>
                    <div>一天最多做${item.dailyCapacity}斤的量</div>
                </div>
                <div class="processing-cost">
                    <span>置办成本：${item.buildCost}块钱</span>
                </div>
                ${unlocked ? `
                    <div class="processing-actions">
                        <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="buildProcessing('${key}')" ${game.money >= item.buildCost ? '' : 'disabled'}>置办起来</button>
                    </div>
                ` : `
                    <div class="lock-hint">🔒 得先${item.unlockCondition}</div>
                `}
            </div>
        `;
    }
    
    if (!hasAvailable) {
        html += '<div class="empty-state">该会的都会了</div>';
    }
    
    html += '</div>';
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}
function rerenderProcessing() {
    if (currentMainTab === 'processing') {
        renderProcessingPanel();
    }
}

                    <div class="field-progress" style="margin-top: 6px;">
                        <div class="field-progress-bar" style="width: ${(game.stamina / game.maxStamina) * 100}%;"></div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;

        <div class="shop-item">

    html += `

                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="shop-item-price">
                <button class="buy-btn" onclick="goFishing()" ${!canFish || game.stamina < 25 ? 'disabled' : ''}>

            </div>
        </div>

    if (!game.studyToday) game.studyToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (game.studyToday.day !== game.day) {
        game.studyToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    }
    const canStudy = game.studyToday.count < 2;
    
    html += `
        <div class="shop-item">
            <div class="shop-item-info">
                <div class="shop-item-icon">📚</div>
                <div>
                    <div class="shop-item-name">看书学习</div>
                    <div class="shop-item-desc">消耗15体力，随机增加技能经验</div>
                    <div class="shop-item-desc" style="color: #666; margin-top: 4px;">
                        今天已学习 ${game.studyToday.count}/2 次
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="shop-item-price">
                <button class="buy-btn" onclick="studySkill()" ${!canStudy || game.stamina < 15 ? 'disabled' : ''}>
                    学习
                </button>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;

    // 宠物互动

    const petList = [
        { id: 'dahuang', name: '大黄', icon: '🐕', desc: '一条忠诚的黄狗，摇着尾巴等你回家' },
        { id: 'ahua', name: '阿花', icon: '🐈', desc: '一只三花猫，懒洋洋地趴在窗台上' }
    ];
    petList.forEach(pet => {
        const p = game.pets[pet.id];
        if (!p) {
            // 宠物未领养
            html += `
                <div class="shop-item" style="opacity: 0.6;">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${pet.icon}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${pet.name}（未领养）</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">${pet.desc}</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            return;
        }
        const today = game.day;
        const fedToday = p.lastFedDay === today;
        const pettedToday = p.lastPettedDay === today;
        const playedToday = p.lastPlayedDay === today;
        const friendship = p.affection || p.friendship || 0;
        html += `
            <div class="shop-item">
                <div class="shop-item-info">
                    <div class="shop-item-icon">${pet.icon}</div>
                    <div>
                        <div class="shop-item-name">${pet.name}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">好感度 ${friendship}/100</div>
                        <div style="margin-top: 6px; display: flex; gap: 6px;">
                            <button class="action-btn" onclick="feedPet('${pet.id}')" ${fedToday ? 'disabled' : ''}>🍖 喂食${fedToday ? '（已喂）' : ''}</button>
                            <button class="action-btn" onclick="petPet('${pet.id}')" ${pettedToday ? 'disabled' : ''}>🤚 抚摸${pettedToday ? '（已摸）' : ''}</button>
                            <button class="action-btn" onclick="playWithPet('${pet.id}')" ${playedToday ? 'disabled' : ''}>🎾 玩耍${playedToday ? '（已玩）' : ''}</button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    });
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

// 检查背包里有没有可以喂宠物的食物
const PET_FOOD_KEYS = ['fish', 'egg', 'vegetable', 'meat', 'pickled_veg', 'shepherds_purse', 'candy', 'pickle', 'bun', 'pork', 'snack'];
function checkHasPetFood() {
    if (!game || !game.items) return false;
    return PET_FOOD_KEYS.some(k => (game.items[k] || 0) > 0);
}

// 消耗一个任意食物喂宠物
function consumeOnePetFood() {
    for (const k of PET_FOOD_KEYS) {
        if ((game.items[k] || 0) > 0) {
            game.items[k]--;
            return ITEM_EFFECTS[k] ? ITEM_EFFECTS[k].name : k;
        }
    }
    return null;
}

// 撸宠物
function petThePet(petId) {
    const p = game.pets[petId];
    if (!p) return;
    if (!p.petToday) p.petToday = 0;
    if (p.petToday >= 2) {
        showToast('今天已经撸够啦，明天再来吧~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    if (game.stamina < 5) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    game.stamina -= 5;
    game.mood = Math.min(100, (game.mood === undefined ? 50 : game.mood) + 5);
    p.petToday++;
    p.affection = (p.affection || 0) + 1;
    const names = { dog: '大黄', cat: '阿花' };
    const flavors = petId === 'dog'
        ? ['大黄舒服地眯起眼睛，尾巴摇得像风车一样。', '大黄翻过身来露出肚皮，让你多摸几下。', '大黄舔了舔你的手，眼神里满是信任。']
        : ['阿花发出咕噜咕噜的声音，用脑袋蹭你的手心。', '阿花伸了个懒腰，在你腿上踩起了奶。', '阿花眯着眼，尾巴尖轻轻晃了晃，看起来很享受。'];
    addLog(`🐾 你撸了撸${names[petId]}。${flavors[Math.floor(Math.random() * flavors.length)]}`, 'pet');
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    showToast('心情+5', 'good');
}

// 喂宠物
function feedThePet(petId) {
    const p = game.pets[petId];
    if (!p) return;
    if (p.fedToday) {
        showToast('今天已经喂过了！', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    if (!checkHasPetFood()) {
        showToast('背包里没有可以喂的食物！', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    const foodName = consumeOnePetFood();
    if (!foodName) return;
    p.fedToday = true;
    p.affection = (p.affection || 0) + 2;
    game.mood = Math.min(100, (game.mood === undefined ? 50 : game.mood) + 10);
    const names = { dog: '大黄', cat: '阿花' };
    const flavors = petId === 'dog'
        ? ['大黄狼吞虎咽地吃完，满足地打了个饱嗝。', '大黄吃完后叼着碗跑到你脚边，还想再来一份。', '大黄吃得尾巴直摇，吃完还用鼻子拱了拱你的手。']
        : ['阿花优雅地吃完，舔了舔爪子开始洗脸。', '阿花吃完后跳到你腿上，蜷成一团打起了呼噜。', '阿花细嚼慢咽地吃完，冲你喵了一声，像是在说谢谢。'];
    addLog(`🍖 你喂了${names[petId]}一个${foodName}。${flavors[Math.floor(Math.random() * flavors.length)]}`, 'pet');
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    showToast('心情+10', 'good');
}

// 锻炼
function exercise() {
    if (!game.exerciseToday) game.exerciseToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (game.exerciseToday.day !== game.day) {
        game.exerciseToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    }
    
    if (game.exerciseToday.count >= 3) {
        showToast('今天已经锻炼够啦，明天再来吧~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.stamina < 25) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.health >= game.maxHealth) {
        showToast('已经很健康啦，不用再锻炼了~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playClickSound();
    game.stamina -= 25;
    game.health = Math.min(game.maxHealth, game.health + 1);
    game.exerciseToday.count++;
    
    // 任务检查：第一次锻炼（兼容副业面板和旧版按钮）
    if (!game.quests.q18) {
        game.quests.q18 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q18', 80, '✅ 任务完成：强身健体，奖励80元');
    }
    
    // 健康值影响体力上限
    game.maxStamina = game.health;
    if (game.stamina > game.maxStamina) {
        game.stamina = game.maxStamina;
    }
    
    addLog('🏃 锻炼了一会儿，感觉身体更结实了，健康值+1', 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderPlayerPanel();
    updateTopBar();
    showToast('健康值+1！', 'good');
}

// 串门聊天
function visitNeighbor() {
    if (!game.visitToday) game.visitToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (game.visitToday.day !== game.day) {
        game.visitToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    }
    
    if (game.visitToday.count >= 3) {
        showToast('今天已经串够门啦，明天再来吧~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.stamina < 15) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playClickSound();
    game.stamina -= 15;
    game.visitToday.count++;
    
    // 只从已认识的NPC中随机选一个增加好感度
    const knownNpcKeys = Object.keys(NPC_DATA).filter(k => {
        return ((game.npcs && game.npcs[k]) || 0) > 0 || ((game.friendship && game.friendship[k]) || 0) > 0 || ['wangcunzhang', 'lilaonong', 'zhangshen', 'wangerdan', 'zhaolaoban'].includes(k);
    });
    
    if (knownNpcKeys.length === 0) {
        addLog('👋 去村里转了转，但还不认识什么人...', 'info');
        saveGame();
        renderPlayerPanel();
        updateTopBar();
        return;
    }
    
    const randomNpc = knownNpcKeys[Math.floor(Math.random() * knownNpcKeys.length)];
    const npc = NPC_DATA[randomNpc];
    
    if (!game.friendship[randomNpc]) {
        game.friendship[randomNpc] = 0;
    }
    if (!game.npcs[randomNpc]) {
        game.npcs[randomNpc] = 0;
    }
    
    const gain = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1; // 1~3点好感度
    game.friendship[randomNpc] += gain;
    game.npcs[randomNpc] += gain;
    
    // 检查NPC里程碑
    if (typeof checkNpcMilestones === 'function') {
        checkNpcMilestones(randomNpc);
    }
    
    addLog(`👋 去${npc.name}家串了个门，聊得挺开心，好感度+${gain}`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderPlayerPanel();
    updateTopBar();
    showToast(`${npc.name}好感度+${gain}！`, 'good');
}

// 河边钓鱼
function goFishing() {
    if (!game.fishToday) game.fishToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (game.fishToday.day !== game.day) {
        game.fishToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    }
    
    if (game.fishToday.count >= 5) {
        showToast('今天已经钓了5次了，鱼竿都累坏了，明天再来吧~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.stamina < 15) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playClickSound();
    game.stamina -= 15;
    game.fishToday.count++;
    
    // 增加钓鱼熟练度经验
    addSkillExp('fishingMastery', 5);
    
    // 随机钓鱼结果（收益随熟练度提升）
    const fishingLevel = (game.skills && game.skills.fishingMastery && game.skills.fishingMastery.level) || 0;
    let levelBonus = 1 + fishingLevel * 0.05; // 每级+5%收益
    
    // 老渔夫NPC好感度增加钓鱼产量
    const npcFishBonus = (typeof getNpcBonus === 'function') ? getNpcBonus('fishYield') : 0;
    if (npcFishBonus > 0) {
        levelBonus *= (1 + npcFishBonus);
    }
    
    const rand = Math.random();
    let result = '';
    let moneyGain = 0;
    const fishTypes = ['carp', 'crucian', 'grass_carp', 'catfish'];
    
    if (rand < 0.15) {
        // 15%概率空军（随等级降低）
        const missChance = Math.max(0.05, 0.15 - fishingLevel * 0.01);
        if (Math.random() < missChance / 0.15) {
            result = '钓了半天，啥也没钓着...';
            addLog('🎣 钓了半天鱼，啥也没钓着，空军了...', 'bad');
            showToast('空军了...', 'bad');
        } else {
            // 高等级时，部分空军转为小鱼
            moneyGain = Math.floor((Math.random() * 10 + 5) * levelBonus);
            const fishType = fishTypes[Math.floor(Math.random() * 2)];
            const fishAmount = Math.floor(Math.random() * 2 + 1);
            if (!game.fishInventory) game.fishInventory = {};
            game.fishInventory[fishType] = (game.fishInventory[fishType] || 0) + fishAmount;
            unlockCollectionItem('fish', fishType);
            game.money += moneyGain;
            result = `钓着了${fishAmount}斤${getFishName(fishType)}，卖了${moneyGain}块钱`;
            addLog(`🎣 ${result}`, 'good');
            showToast(`钓到${getFishName(fishType)}！+${moneyGain}元`, 'good');
            if (!game.stats) game.stats = {};
            game.stats.totalFish = (game.stats.totalFish || 0) + fishAmount;
        }
    } else if (rand < 0.55) {
        // 40%概率小鱼
        moneyGain = Math.floor((Math.random() * 15 + 10) * levelBonus);
        const fishType = fishTypes[Math.floor(Math.random() * 2)];
        const fishAmount = Math.floor(Math.random() * 2 + 1);
        if (!game.fishInventory) game.fishInventory = {};
        game.fishInventory[fishType] = (game.fishInventory[fishType] || 0) + fishAmount;
        unlockCollectionItem('fish', fishType);
        game.money += moneyGain;
        result = `钓着了${fishAmount}斤${getFishName(fishType)}，卖了${moneyGain}块钱`;
        addLog(`🎣 ${result}`, 'good');
        showToast(`钓到${getFishName(fishType)}！+${moneyGain}元`, 'good');
        if (!game.stats) game.stats = {};
        game.stats.totalFish = (game.stats.totalFish || 0) + fishAmount;
    } else if (rand < 0.85) {
        // 30%概率中鱼
        moneyGain = Math.floor((Math.random() * 25 + 30) * levelBonus);
        const fishType = fishTypes[Math.floor(Math.random() * 3)];
        const fishAmount = Math.floor(Math.random() * 2 + 2);
        if (!game.fishInventory) game.fishInventory = {};
        game.fishInventory[fishType] = (game.fishInventory[fishType] || 0) + fishAmount;
        unlockCollectionItem('fish', fishType);
        game.money += moneyGain;
        result = `钓着了${fishAmount}斤${getFishName(fishType)}，卖了${moneyGain}块钱`;
        addLog(`🎣 ${result}`, 'good');
        showToast(`钓到${getFishName(fishType)}！+${moneyGain}元`, 'good');
        if (!game.stats) game.stats = {};
        game.stats.totalFish = (game.stats.totalFish || 0) + fishAmount;
    } else {
        // 15%概率大鱼（随等级提升）
        moneyGain = Math.floor((Math.random() * 40 + 70) * levelBonus);
        const fishType = fishTypes[Math.floor(Math.random() * 4)];
        const fishAmount = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3 + 3);
        if (!game.fishInventory) game.fishInventory = {};
        game.fishInventory[fishType] = (game.fishInventory[fishType] || 0) + fishAmount;
        unlockCollectionItem('fish', fishType);
        game.money += moneyGain;
        result = `哇！钓着了${fishAmount}斤大${getFishName(fishType)}！卖了${moneyGain}块钱`;
        addLog(`🎣 ${result}`, 'good');
        showToast(`🎉 钓到大${getFishName(fishType)}！+${moneyGain}元`, 'good');
        if (!game.stats) game.stats = {};
        game.stats.totalFish = (game.stats.totalFish || 0) + fishAmount;
    }
    
    // 任务检查：累积钓到50条鱼
    if (game.stats.totalFish >= 50 && !game.quests.q27) {
        game.quests.q27 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q27', 300, '✅ 任务完成：鲜鱼上岸，奖励300元');
    }
    // 任务检查：第一次钓鱼
    if (!game.quests.q19) {
        game.quests.q19 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q19', 80, '✅ 任务完成：垂钓之乐，奖励80元');
    }
    
    saveGame();
    updateTopBar();
    checkAchievements();
    if (currentMainTab === 'fishing') {
        renderFishingPanel();
    }
}

// 看书学习
function studySkill() {
    if (!game.studyToday) game.studyToday = { day: 0, count: 0 };
    if (game.studyToday.day !== game.day) {
        game.studyToday = { day: game.day, count: 0 };
    }
    
    if (game.studyToday.count >= 2) {
        showToast('今天已经看够书啦，眼睛都花了~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.stamina < 15) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playClickSound();
    game.stamina -= 15;
    game.studyToday.count++;
    
    // 随机选一个技能增加经验
    const skillKeys = ['cropFamiliarity', 'fieldManagement', 'toolMastery', 'composting'];
    const randomSkill = skillKeys[Math.floor(Math.random() * skillKeys.length)];
    const skillInfo = SKILL_EFFECTS[randomSkill];
    
    const gain = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1; // 1~3点经验
    let bonusGain = gain;
    if (game.hasBookBonus) {
        bonusGain += 1; // 有林老师借的书，经验+1
    }
    // 社区建设加成（村小学扩建：每日研究点+2）
    if (game.researchPointBonus) {
        bonusGain += game.researchPointBonus;
    }
    addSkillExp(randomSkill, bonusGain);
    
    let bonusText = '';
    if (game.hasBookBonus) {
        bonusText = '（林老师借的书帮了大忙，额外+1）';
    }
    addLog(`📚 看了会儿${skillInfo.name}相关的书，学到了不少，经验+${bonusGain}${bonusText}`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderPlayerPanel();
    updateTopBar();
    showToast(`${skillInfo.name}经验+${gain}！`, 'good');
}

function renderSkillsPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">📚 技能树</div>';
    
    const skillKeys = ['cropFamiliarity', 'fieldManagement', 'toolMastery', 'composting'];
    
    skillKeys.forEach(skillKey => {
        const skillInfo = SKILL_EFFECTS[skillKey];
        const skill = game.skills[skillKey];
        const level = skill.level;
        const exp = skill.exp;
        
        // 计算当前技能效果
        let currentEffect = '';
        if (skillKey === 'cropFamiliarity') {
            currentEffect = `当前产量 +${level * 3}%`;
        } else if (skillKey === 'toolMastery') {
            currentEffect = `当前体力消耗 -${level * 3}%`;
        } else if (skillKey === 'fieldManagement') {
            currentEffect = `当前灾害损失 -${level * 5}%`;
        } else if (skillKey === 'composting') {
            currentEffect = `当前堆肥效果 +${level * 5}%`;
        }
        
        // 计算当前等级和下一级所需经验
        const nextLevelExp = SKILL_EXP_TABLE[level + 1] || SKILL_EXP_TABLE[10];
        const currentLevelExp = SKILL_EXP_TABLE[level] || 0;
        const expInLevel = exp - currentLevelExp;
        const expNeeded = nextLevelExp - currentLevelExp;
        const progress = Math.min(100, (expInLevel / expNeeded) * 100);
        
        html += `
            <div class="shop-item">
                <div class="shop-item-info" style="width: 100%;">
                    <div style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 15px; width: 100%;">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${skillInfo.emoji}</div>
                        <div style="flex: 1;">
                            <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center;">
                                <div class="shop-item-name">${skillInfo.name} <span style="color: #e67e22;">Lv.${level}</span></div>
                                <div style="font-size: 12px; color: #999;">${exp}/${nextLevelExp} EXP</div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc" style="margin-top: 4px;">${skillInfo.desc}</div>
                            <div style="margin-top: 6px; font-size: 13px; color: #27ae60; font-weight: bold;">
                                ✨ ${currentEffect || '暂无效果'}
                            </div>
                            <div class="field-progress" style="margin-top: 8px;">
                                <div class="field-progress-bar" style="width: ${progress}%; background: #e67e22;"></div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div style="margin-top: 12px; padding-top: 12px; border-top: 1px solid #f0f0f0;">
                        <div style="font-size: 13px; color: #666; margin-bottom: 8px;">技能效果：</div>
                        <div style="font-size: 12px; color: #888; line-height: 1.8;">
        `;
        
        skillInfo.effects.forEach(effect => {
            // 检查是否已解锁
            const effectLevel = parseInt((effect.match(/Lv(\d+)/) && effect.match(/Lv(\d+)/)[1]) || 0);
            const unlocked = level >= effectLevel;
            html += `<div style="color: ${unlocked ? '#4a7c59' : '#ccc'};">${unlocked ? '✅' : '🔒'} ${effect}</div>`;
        });
        
        html += `
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    });
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

// 根据经验计算技能等级

// ===== 农技研究面板 =====
function renderTechPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🔬 农技研究</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">研究农业技术，提高产量、节省体力。收获作物可以获得农技经验。</p>';
    
    // 农技经验显示
    html += '<div class="research-points-display">';
    html += `<span class="rp-label">📚 农技经验</span>`;
    html += `<span class="rp-value">${game.researchPoints || 0}</span>`;
    html += '</div>';
    
    // 按分类显示
    for (const [catKey, cat] of Object.entries(TECH_CATEGORIES)) {
        html += `<div class="section-title">${cat.emoji} ${cat.name}</div>`;
        html += `<p class="section-desc">${cat.desc}</p>`;
        html += '<div class="tech-list">';
        
        // 找出这个分类的所有科技
        const techsInCat = Object.values(TECH_DATA).filter(t => t.category === catKey);
        
        for (const tech of techsInCat) {
            const unlocked = isTechUnlocked(tech.id);
            const canResearch = !unlocked && 
                tech.requires.every(req => isTechUnlocked(req)) &&
                game.researchPoints >= tech.cost;
            const locked = !unlocked && tech.requires.some(req => !isTechUnlocked(req));
            
            html += `
                <div class="tech-card ${unlocked ? 'unlocked' : ''} ${locked ? 'locked' : ''}">
                    <div class="tech-header">
                        <span class="tech-emoji">${tech.emoji}</span>
                        <span class="tech-name">${tech.name}</span>
                        <span class="tech-cost">${tech.cost}点</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="tech-desc">${tech.desc}</div>
                    <div class="tech-effect">✨ ${tech.effectDesc}</div>
                    ${unlocked ? `
                        <div class="tech-status unlocked">✅ 已研究</div>
                    ` : locked ? `
                        <div class="tech-status locked">🔒 需要先研究前置</div>
                    ` : `
                        <button class="btn ${canResearch ? 'btn-primary' : 'btn-disabled'}" 
                                onclick="researchTech('${tech.id}')"
                                ${canResearch ? '' : 'disabled'}>
                            研究
                        </button>
                    `}
                </div>
            `;
        }
        
        html += '</div>';
    }
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

// 重新渲染科技面板
function rerenderTech() {
    if (currentMainTab === 'tech') {
        renderTechPanel();
    }
}


// ===== 农家建筑面板 =====
function renderBuildingPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🏡 农家设施</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">置办各种农家设施，提升生产效率。每个设施都可以加固升级。</p>';
    
    // 储存上限显示 + 扩建按钮
    html += '<div class="storage-display">';
    html += `<span class="storage-label">📦 粮食储存上限</span>`;
    html += `<span class="storage-value">${game.storageCapacity || 1000}斤</span>`;
    html += '</div>';
    html += '<div style="margin-bottom: 15px; text-align: right;">';
    const expandCost = 500;
    const canExpand = game.money >= expandCost;
    html += `<button class="action-btn" onclick="expandStorage()" ${canExpand ? '' : 'disabled'} title="花费${expandCost}元扩建仓库">🔨 扩建仓库 (+1000斤 / ${expandCost}元)</button>`;
    if (!canExpand) {
        html += `<div style="color: #e74c3c; font-size: 12px; margin-top: 4px;">还差${expandCost - game.money}元</div>`;
    }
    html += '</div>';
    
    // 按分类显示
    for (const [catKey, cat] of Object.entries(BUILDING_CATEGORIES)) {
        html += `<div class="section-title">${cat.emoji} ${cat.name}</div>`;
        html += `<p class="section-desc">${cat.desc}</p>`;
        html += '<div class="building-list">';
        
        // 找出这个分类的所有建筑
        const buildingsInCat = Object.values(BUILDING_DATA).filter(b => b.category === catKey);
        
        for (const building of buildingsInCat) {
            if (!building || !building.id) continue;
            const currentLevel = game.buildings[building.id] || 0;
            const isBuilt = currentLevel > 0;
            const isMaxLevel = currentLevel >= building.maxLevel;
            const nextCost = isBuilt ? building.upgradeCost[currentLevel - 1] || 0 : building.cost;
            const canAfford = game.money >= nextCost;
            
            html += `
                <div class="building-card ${isBuilt ? 'built' : ''}">
                    <div class="building-header">
                        <span class="building-emoji">${building.emoji || '🏠'}</span>
                        <span class="building-name">${building.name || '未知建筑'}</span>
                        ${isBuilt ? `<span class="building-level">Lv.${currentLevel}</span>` : ''}
                    </div>
                    <div class="building-desc">${building.desc}</div>
                    <div class="building-effect">✨ ${building.effectDesc}</div>
                    ${isBuilt ? `
                        ${isMaxLevel ? `
                            <div class="building-status max-level">🏆 最高等级</div>
                        ` : `
                            <button class="btn ${canAfford ? 'btn-primary' : 'btn-disabled'}" 
                                    onclick="upgradeBuilding('${building.id}')"
                                    ${canAfford ? '' : 'disabled'}>
                                加固（${nextCost}元）
                            </button>
                        `}
                    ` : `
                        <button class="btn ${canAfford ? 'btn-primary' : 'btn-disabled'}" 
                                onclick="buildBuilding('${building.id}')"
                                ${canAfford ? '' : 'disabled'}>
                            置办（${building.cost}元）
                        </button>
                    `}
                </div>
            `;
        }
        
        html += '</div>';
    }
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

// 重新渲染建筑面板
function rerenderBuilding() {
    if (currentMainTab === 'buildings') {
        renderBuildingPanel();
    }
}

function getSkillLevel(exp) {
    for (let i = 10; i >= 0; i--) {
        if (exp >= SKILL_EXP_TABLE[i]) {
            return i;
        }
    }
    return 0;
}

// 增加技能经验
function addSkillExp(skillKey, amount) {
    const skill = game.skills[skillKey];
    if (!skill) return;
    
    const oldLevel = skill.level;
    skill.exp += amount;
    const newLevel = getSkillLevel(skill.exp);
    
    if (newLevel > oldLevel) {
        skill.level = newLevel;
        const skillInfo = SKILL_EFFECTS[skillKey];
        addLog(`🎉 ${skillInfo.name}升级到 Lv.${newLevel}！`, 'good');
        showToast(`${skillInfo.name}升级！Lv.${newLevel}`, 'good');
        playBonusSound();
        
        // 里程碑奖励
        const milestoneRewards = {
            3: { money: 100, name: '小有所成' },
            5: { money: 300, name: '渐入佳境' },
            7: { money: 500, name: '炉火纯青' },
            10: { money: 1000, name: '登峰造极' }
        };
        
        for (let lv = oldLevel + 1; lv <= newLevel; lv++) {
            if (milestoneRewards[lv]) {
                const reward = milestoneRewards[lv];
                game.money += reward.money;
                addLog(`🏆 里程碑达成：${reward.name}！奖励${reward.money}元`, 'good');
                showToast(`🏆 ${reward.name}！+${reward.money}元`, 'good');
            }
        }
        
        // 技能升级解锁内容提示
        const unlockMessages = {
            cropFamiliarity: {
                2: '⭐ 解锁进阶档田地！产量+15%',
                3: '⭐ 红薯甜度提升，病害减少10%',
                4: '⭐ 翻藤操作效率提升，红薯产量+15%',
                5: '⭐ 解锁精英档田地！产量+35%',
                8: '⭐ 解锁终极档田地！产量+60%',
                10: '⭐ 改良品种！产量+30%，售价+20%'
            },
            fieldManagement: {
                1: '⭐ 偷采、小孩破坏损失-10%',
                3: '⭐ 解锁灾害预警！排水体力-20%',
                5: '⭐ 全自然灾害提前1天预警，损失-30%',
                7: '⭐ 人为事件损失-50%',
                10: '⭐ 台风暴雨无减产，人为破坏零损失'
            },
            toolMastery: {
                1: '⭐ 所有农具体力消耗-5%',
                3: '⭐ 解锁进阶农具，购买成本-10%',
                5: '⭐ 可自制简易农具，维修成本-30%',
                6: '⭐ 解锁高级农具（水车、秧马）',
                10: '⭐ 高级农具免费租赁，效果+20%'
            },
            composting: {
                1: '⭐ 堆肥成功率+10%，周期-1天',
                3: '⭐ 有机肥增产效果+2%',
                5: '⭐ 解锁热堆肥，成功率大幅提升',
                7: '⭐ 材料种类增加，肥效+5%',
                10: '⭐ 最大增产+8%，成功率100%'
            }
        };
        
        const skillUnlocks = unlockMessages[skillKey];
        if (skillUnlocks) {
            for (let lv = oldLevel + 1; lv <= newLevel; lv++) {
                if (skillUnlocks[lv]) {
                    addLog(`🔓 ${skillUnlocks[lv]}`, 'good');
                }
            }
        }
        
        // 任务检查：作物熟悉度达到2级
        if (skillKey === 'cropFamiliarity' && newLevel >= 2 && !game.quests.q12) {
            game.quests.q12 = true;
            queueQuestReward('q12', 200, '✅ 任务完成：熟能生巧，奖励200元');
        }
        // 任务检查：作物熟悉度达到5级
        if (skillKey === 'cropFamiliarity' && newLevel >= 5 && !game.quests.q37) {
            game.quests.q37 = true;
            queueQuestReward('q37', 500, '✅ 任务完成：农学专家，奖励500元');
        }
        
        // 任务检查：田间管理达到3级
        if (skillKey === 'fieldManagement' && newLevel >= 3 && !game.quests.q14) {
            game.quests.q14 = true;
            queueQuestReward('q14', 300, '✅ 任务完成：田间老手，奖励300元');
        }
        // 任务检查：田间管理达到5级
        if (skillKey === 'fieldManagement' && newLevel >= 5 && !game.quests.q38) {
            game.quests.q38 = true;
            queueQuestReward('q38', 500, '✅ 任务完成：管理达人，奖励500元');
        }
        
        // 任务检查：农具精通达到5级
        if (skillKey === 'toolMastery' && newLevel >= 5 && !game.quests.q39) {
            game.quests.q39 = true;
            queueQuestReward('q39', 500, '✅ 任务完成：工具大师，奖励500元');
        }
        // 任务检查：堆肥技能达到5级
        if (skillKey === 'composting' && newLevel >= 5 && !game.quests.q40) {
            game.quests.q40 = true;
            queueQuestReward('q40', 500, '✅ 任务完成：堆肥专家，奖励500元');
        }
    }
}


// ==================== 里程碑成就系统 ====================
function checkMilestones() {
    if (!MILESTONE_DATA) return;
    
    for (const key in MILESTONE_DATA) {
        const milestone = MILESTONE_DATA[key];
        // 已经达成的跳过
        if (game.milestones && game.milestones[key]) continue;
        
        // 检查是否达成
        try {
            if (milestone.check && milestone.check()) {
                // 达成里程碑
                game.milestones[key] = true;
                
                // 给奖励
                if (milestone.reward) {
                    game.money += milestone.reward;
                }
                
                // 提示
                addLog(`🏆 里程碑达成：${milestone.name}！奖励${milestone.reward}元`, 'good');
                showToast(`🏆 里程碑达成！${milestone.name}`, 'good');
                if (typeof playBonusSound === 'function') {
                    playBonusSound();
                }
            }
        } catch (e) {
            // 忽略错误
        }
    }
}

function isNpcKnown(npcKey) {
    // 初始5个NPC默认已认识
    const defaultKnown = ['wangcunzhang', 'lilaonong', 'zhangshen', 'wangerdan', 'zhaolaoban'];
    if (defaultKnown.includes(npcKey)) return true;
    
    // 其他NPC根据met标志或已有好感度判断
    const metFlags = {
        chenyang: 'metChenyang',
        linxiaoyu: 'metLinxiaoyu',
        sunmiaoqing: 'metSunmiaoqing'
    };
    if (metFlags[npcKey] && game[metFlags[npcKey]]) return true;
    
    // 如果已经有好感度，也算认识
    if (((game.npcs && game.npcs[npcKey]) || 0) > 0) return true;
    if (((game.friendship && game.friendship[npcKey]) || 0) > 0) return true;
    
    return false;
}

function renderNpcsPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">👥 村民</div>';
    
    // 所有NPC，按是否认识分组
    const knownNpcs = [];
    const unknownNpcs = [];
    
    for (const npcKey of Object.keys(NPC_DATA)) {
        if (isNpcKnown(npcKey)) {
            knownNpcs.push(npcKey);
        } else {
            unknownNpcs.push(npcKey);
        }
    }
    
    // 已认识的NPC
    if (knownNpcs.length > 0) {
        html += '<div class="section-title" style="margin-top:0;">👋 已认识的村民</div>';
        for (const npcKey of knownNpcs) {
            const npc = NPC_DATA[npcKey];
            const friendship = Math.max((game.npcs && game.npcs[npcKey]) || 0,(game.friendship && game.friendship[npcKey]) || 0);
            
            let level = FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[0];
            for (let i = FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                if (friendship >= FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[i].min) {
                    level = FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[i];
                    break;
                }
            }
            
            const nextLevelIndex = FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS.findIndex(l => l.min > friendship);
            const nextLevel = nextLevelIndex > 0 ? FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[nextLevelIndex] : null;
            const currentLevelMin = level.min;
            const nextLevelMin = nextLevel ? nextLevel.min : 100;
            const progress = Math.min(100, ((friendship - currentLevelMin) / (nextLevelMin - currentLevelMin)) * 100);
            
            html += `
                <div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info" style="width: 100%;">
                        <div style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 15px; width: 100%;">
                            <div style="font-size: 40px;">${npc.emoji}</div>
                            <div style="flex: 1;">
                                <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center;">
                                    <div>
                                        <span style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 16px; color: #5d4e37;">${npc.name}</span>
                                        <span style="font-size: 13px; color: #999; margin-left: 8px;">${npc.title}</span>
                                    </div>
                                    <span style="font-size: 13px; color: ${level.color}; font-weight: bold;">${level.name} (${friendship}/100)</span>
                                </div>
                                <div style="font-size: 13px; color: #666; margin-top: 4px;">${npc.desc}</div>
                                <div class="field-progress" style="margin-top: 8px;">
                                    <div class="field-progress-bar" style="width: ${progress}%; background: ${level.color};"></div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div style="margin-top: 12px; display: flex; gap: 10px; justify-content: flex-end; flex-wrap: wrap;">
                            <button class="action-btn" onclick="chatWithNpc('${npcKey}')">💬 聊天</button>
                            <button class="action-btn" onclick="showGiftModal('${npcKey}')">🎁 送礼</button>
                            ${npc.canHire ? getHireButton(npcKey, npc) : ''}
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        }
    }
    
    // 未认识的NPC
    if (unknownNpcs.length > 0) {
        html += '<div class="section-title">🔒 还没认识的村民</div>';
        for (const npcKey of unknownNpcs) {
            const npc = NPC_DATA[npcKey];
            html += `
                <div class="shop-item" style="opacity: 0.5; cursor: not-allowed;" onclick="playErrorSound(); showToast('现在还不认识这个村民，多出去走走，说不定能遇到...', 'warn');">
                    <div class="shop-item-info" style="width: 100%;">
                        <div style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 15px; width: 100%;">
                            <div style="font-size: 40px; filter: grayscale(100%);">${npc.emoji}</div>
                            <div style="flex: 1;">
                                <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center;">
                                    <div>
                                        <span style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 16px; color: #999;">???</span>
                                        <span style="font-size: 13px; color: #bbb; margin-left: 8px;">陌生人</span>
                                    </div>
                                    <span style="font-size: 13px; color: #bbb; font-weight: bold;">不认识</span>
                                </div>
                                <div style="font-size: 13px; color: #999; margin-top: 4px; font-style: italic;">现在还不认识这个村民，多出去走走，说不定能遇到...</div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div style="margin-top: 12px; display: flex; gap: 10px; justify-content: flex-end; flex-wrap: wrap;">
                            <button class="action-btn" disabled style="opacity: 0.3;">💬 聊天</button>
                            <button class="action-btn" disabled style="opacity: 0.3;">🎁 送礼</button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        }
    }
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}


// ==================== 雇佣村民系统 ====================
function getHireButton(npcKey, npc) {
    const friendship = game.npcs[npcKey] || 0;
    const isHired = game.hiredWorker === npcKey;
    
    // 已经雇佣了
    if (isHired) {
        return `<button class="action-btn" style="background: #e74c3c;" onclick="fireWorker('${npcKey}')">🔥 解雇</button>`;
    }
    
    // 已经雇佣了其他人
    if (game.hiredWorker) {
        return `<button class="action-btn" style="opacity: 0.5;" disabled>🧑‍🌾 已雇他人</button>`;
    }
    
    // 好感度不够
    if (friendship < npc.hireFriendship) {
        return `<button class="action-btn" style="opacity: 0.5;" title="好感度达到${npc.hireFriendship}才能雇佣" disabled>🔒 需好感${npc.hireFriendship}</button>`;
    }
    
    // 可以雇佣
    const skillText = npc.skills.map(s => s === 'water' ? '💧浇水' : '🌿除草').join('+');
    return `<button class="action-btn" style="background: #27ae60;" onclick="hireWorker('${npcKey}')" title="${npc.hireDesc}">🧑‍🌾 雇佣 (${npc.hireFee}元介绍费 + ${npc.dailyWage}元/天)</button>`;
}

function hireWorker(npcKey) {
    const npc = NPC_DATA[npcKey];
    if (!npc || !npc.canHire) return;
    
    const friendship = game.npcs[npcKey] || 0;
    if (friendship < npc.hireFriendship) {
        showToast('关系还没好到那个份上，再多聊聊吧', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.hiredWorker) {
        showToast('你已经雇佣了一个村民了', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.money < npc.hireFee) {
        showToast(`钱不够，雇佣费需要${npc.hireFee}元`, 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    // 扣除雇佣费
    game.money -= npc.hireFee;
    game.hiredWorker = npcKey;
    game.hireStartDay = game.day;
    game.lastWorkerWaterDay = game.day - 1; // 明天就可以浇水
    game.lastWorkerWeedDay = game.day - 3; // 3天后可以除草
    
    playClickSound();
    showToast(`✅ 雇佣了${npc.name}！一次性介绍费${npc.hireFee}元，每天工资${npc.dailyWage}元`, 'good');
    addLog(`🧑‍🌾 雇佣了${npc.name}帮忙干活，一次性介绍费${npc.hireFee}元，每天工资${npc.dailyWage}元`, 'info');
    
    // 任务检查：雇佣第一个村民
    if (!game.quests.q36) {
        game.quests.q36 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q36', 300, '✅ 任务完成：雇佣帮手，奖励300元');
    }
    
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
}

function fireWorker(npcKey) {
    const npc = NPC_DATA[npcKey];
    if (!npc) return;
    
    if (game.hiredWorker !== npcKey) {
        showToast('你没有雇佣这个人', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    game.hiredWorker = null;
    game.hireStartDay = 0;
    game.lastWorkerWaterDay = 0;
    game.lastWorkerWeedDay = 0;
    
    playClickSound();
    showToast(`已解雇${npc.name}`, 'info');
    addLog(`🔥 解雇了${npc.name}`, 'info');
    
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
}

function processWorkerDaily() {
    if (!game.hiredWorker) return;
    
    const npc = NPC_DATA[game.hiredWorker];
    if (!npc) return;
    
    // 扣日薪
    // 雇佣村民工资折扣（科技）
    const workerDiscount = getTechBonus('workerDiscount');
    let actualWage = npc.dailyWage;
    if (workerDiscount > 0) {
        actualWage = Math.floor(npc.dailyWage * (1 - workerDiscount));
    }
    
    if (game.money >= actualWage) {
        game.money -= actualWage;
        addLog(`💰 支付${npc.name}今日工资${actualWage}元`, 'info');
    } else {
        // 钱不够，自动解雇
        addLog(`💸 钱不够发工资，${npc.name}走了...`, 'bad');
        game.hiredWorker = null;
        game.hireStartDay = 0;
        game.lastWorkerWaterDay = 0;
        game.lastWorkerWeedDay = 0;
        return;
    }
    
    // 雇佣的村民干活
    const daysSinceWater = game.day - game.lastWorkerWaterDay;
    const daysSinceWeed = game.day - game.lastWorkerWeedDay;
    let workedToday = false;
    
    // 浇水（每天一次）
    if (npc.skills.includes('water') && daysSinceWater >= 1) {
        let wateredCount = 0;
        game.fields.forEach(field => {
            if (field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle' && field.stage !== 'mature') {
                field.lastWaterDay = game.day;
                wateredCount++;
            }
        });
        if (wateredCount > 0) {
            game.lastWorkerWaterDay = game.day;
            workedToday = true;
            addLog(`💧 ${npc.name}帮你浇了${wateredCount}块地`, 'info');
            if (typeof playWaterSound === 'function') {
                playWaterSound();
            }
        }
    }
    
    // 除草（每3天一次）
    if (npc.skills.includes('weed') && daysSinceWeed >= 3) {
        let weededCount = 0;
        game.fields.forEach(field => {
            if (field.crop && field.stage !== 'idle' && field.stage !== 'mature') {
                field.lastWeedDay = game.day;
                weededCount++;
            }
        });
        if (weededCount > 0) {
            game.lastWorkerWeedDay = game.day;
            workedToday = true;
            addLog(`🌿 ${npc.name}帮你除了${weededCount}块地的草`, 'info');
            if (typeof playWeedSound === 'function') {
                playWeedSound();
            }
        }
    }
    
    if (!workedToday) {
        addLog(`😴 ${npc.name}今天没什么活干，四处溜达了一圈`, 'info');
    }
}


// 和NPC聊天

// 每日自动加工
function processDailyProcessing() {
    if (!game.builtProcessing) game.builtProcessing = {};
    if (!game.dailyProcessed) game.dailyProcessed = {};
    
    // 重置每日已加工量
    game.dailyProcessed = {};
    
    for (const [key, building] of Object.entries(PROCESSING_DATA)) {
        if (!game.builtProcessing[key] || game.builtProcessing[key] <= 0) continue;
        
        // === 获取原料来源 ===
        let inputAmount = 0;
        let inputName = '';
        
        if (building.inputType === 'fish') {
            // 从鱼塘取鱼：优先大鱼，不够时小鱼凑
            let fishCount = 0;
            if (game.fishInventory) {
                for (const [fishKey, count] of Object.entries(game.fishInventory)) {
                    fishCount += count || 0;
                }
            }
            inputAmount = fishCount;
            inputName = '鱼';
        } else if (building.inputType === 'processed') {
            // 从加工品取原料（多级加工）
            inputAmount =(game.processedItems && game.processedItems[building.inputItem]) || 0;
            inputName =(PROCESSED_ITEMS[building.inputItem] && PROCESSED_ITEMS[building.inputItem].name) || building.inputItem;
        } else {
            // 从作物取原料
            const cropKey = building.inputCrop === 'rice' ? 'rice' : (building.inputCrop === 'sweet' ? 'sweet' : (building.inputCrop === 'wheat' ? 'wheat' : building.inputCrop));
            inputAmount = game.crops[cropKey] || 0;
            const cropNameMap = { rice: '稻谷', sweet: '红薯', wheat: '小麦', corn: '玉米', soybean: '大豆' };
            inputName = cropNameMap[cropKey] || cropKey;
        }
        
        // 获取加工坊等级对应的容量和体力消耗
        const buildingLevel = game.builtProcessing[key] || 1;
        const dailyCapacity = building.levelCapacity ? building.levelCapacity[buildingLevel - 1] : building.dailyCapacity;
        const levelStaminaCost = building.levelStaminaCost ? building.levelStaminaCost[buildingLevel - 1] : building.staminaCost;
        
        // 能加工的批次数
        const processingSpeedBonus = getTechBonus('processingSpeed');
        const buildingProcessingBonus = getBuildingBonus('processingSpeed');
        let effectiveCapacity = dailyCapacity;
        if (processingSpeedBonus > 0 || buildingProcessingBonus > 0) {
            effectiveCapacity = Math.floor(dailyCapacity * (1 + processingSpeedBonus + buildingProcessingBonus));
        }
        const maxBatches = Math.floor(effectiveCapacity / building.inputAmount);
        const availableBatches = Math.floor(inputAmount / building.inputAmount);
        const batches = Math.min(maxBatches, availableBatches);
        
        if (batches <= 0) continue;
        
        // === 体力消耗检查 ===
        const staminaCost = levelStaminaCost || 5;
        if (game.stamina < staminaCost) {
            addLog(`😓 ${building.name}想做活，但体力不够了（需要${staminaCost}点）`, 'bad');
            continue;
        }
        game.stamina -= staminaCost;
        
        // === 概率事件（副业更有趣）===
        const eventRoll = Math.random();
        let qualityBonus = 1.0;
        let eventText = '';
        let staminaRefund = 0;
        let extraExp = 0;
        
        if (eventRoll < 0.08) {
            // 8% 质量特别好
            qualityBonus = 1.2;
            eventText = '，这批货质量特别好';
            addLog(`✨ ${building.name}灵感来了，这批货质量特别好！产出+20%`, 'good');
        } else if (eventRoll < 0.15) {
            // 7% 小失误
            qualityBonus = 0.9;
            eventText = '，不过不小心出了点小差错';
            addLog(`⚠️ ${building.name}出了点小失误，产出少了10%`, 'bad');
        } else if (eventRoll < 0.22) {
            // 7% 省时省力
            staminaRefund = Math.floor(staminaCost * 0.3);
            game.stamina = Math.min(game.maxStamina, game.stamina + staminaRefund);
            eventText = '，今天手脚特别麻利';
            addLog(`💪 ${building.name}今天手脚麻利，省了${staminaRefund}点体力`, 'good');
        } else if (eventRoll < 0.28) {
            // 6% 悟出新技巧
            extraExp = 5;
            const skillName = building.inputCrop === 'rice' || building.inputType === 'processed' && building.inputItem === 'riceGrain' ? 'cropFamiliarity' : 'fishingMastery';
            if (game.skills[skillName]) {
                addSkillExp(skillName, extraExp);
            }
            eventText = '，干活的时候悟出了新技巧';
            addLog(`💡 ${building.name}干活的时候悟出了新技巧，${getSkillName(skillName)}经验+${extraExp}`, 'good');
        } else if (eventRoll < 0.33) {
            // 5% 设备故障
            const extraStamina = Math.floor(staminaCost * 0.2);
            game.stamina = Math.max(0, game.stamina - extraStamina);
            eventText = '，设备出了点毛病，多费了点儿劲';
            addLog(`🔧 ${building.name}设备出了点毛病，多花了${extraStamina}点体力`, 'bad');
        }
        
        // === 消耗原料 ===
        if (building.inputType === 'fish') {
            // 消耗鱼：优先大鱼
            let needFish = batches * building.inputAmount;
            const fishTypes = ['carp', 'eel', 'crab', 'shrimp', 'silverfish'];
            for (const fishType of fishTypes) {
                if (needFish <= 0) break;
                const available =(game.fishInventory && game.fishInventory[fishType]) || 0;
                if (available > 0) {
                    const consume = Math.min(available, needFish);
                    game.fishInventory[fishType] -= consume;
                    needFish -= consume;
                }
            }
        } else if (building.inputType === 'processed') {
            game.processedItems[building.inputItem] -= batches * building.inputAmount;
        } else {
            const cropKey = building.inputCrop === 'rice' ? 'rice' : (building.inputCrop === 'sweet' ? 'sweet' : (building.inputCrop === 'wheat' ? 'wheat' : building.inputCrop));
            game.crops[cropKey] -= batches * building.inputAmount;
        }
        
        // === 产出产品 ===
        let outputAmount = batches * building.outputAmount * qualityBonus;
        
        // 红薯干有科技加成
        if (building.outputItem === 'driedSweetPotato') {
            const dryYieldBonus = getTechBonus('dryYield');
            const buildingDryBonus = getBuildingBonus('dryYield');
            if (dryYieldBonus > 0 || buildingDryBonus > 0) {
                outputAmount = Math.floor(outputAmount * (1 + dryYieldBonus + buildingDryBonus));
            }
        }
        outputAmount = Math.floor(outputAmount);
        
        if (!game.processedItems) game.processedItems = {};
        game.processedItems[building.outputItem] = (game.processedItems[building.outputItem] || 0) + outputAmount;
        
        // 记录今日加工量
        game.dailyProcessed[key] = batches * building.inputAmount;
        
        addLog(`🏭 ${building.name}加工了${batches * building.inputAmount}斤${inputName}，产出${outputAmount}斤${PROCESSED_ITEMS[building.outputItem].name}${eventText}`, 'info');
    }
}

// 建造加工坊
function buildProcessing(key) {
    const building = PROCESSING_DATA[key];
    if (!building) return;
    
    // 检查是否已经建造
    if (game.builtProcessing && game.builtProcessing[key] > 0) {
        showToast('已经建造过了');
        return;
    }
    
    // 检查解锁条件
    if (!isProcessingUnlocked(key)) {
        showToast('还未解锁');
        return;
    }
    
    // 检查金钱
    if (game.money < building.buildCost) {
        showToast('钱包里钱不够，先去卖点东西换点钱', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    // 建造
    game.money -= building.buildCost;
    if (!game.builtProcessing) game.builtProcessing = {};
    game.builtProcessing[key] = 1;
    
    // 任务检查
    if (key === 'riceMill' && !game.quests.q21) { game.quests.q21 = true; queueQuestReward('q21', 200, '✅ 任务完成：石磨初启，奖励200元'); }
    if (key === 'sweetPotatoDry' && !game.quests.q22) { game.quests.q22 = true; queueQuestReward('q22', 200, '✅ 任务完成：红薯飘香，奖励200元'); }
    if (key === 'ricePolishing' && !game.quests.q25) { game.quests.q25 = true; queueQuestReward('q25', 300, '✅ 任务完成：精米坊开业，奖励300元'); }
    if (key === 'fishDrying' && !game.quests.q26) { game.quests.q26 = true; queueQuestReward('q26', 200, '✅ 任务完成：鱼塘初钓，奖励200元'); }
    if (key === 'fishBallWorkshop' && !game.quests.q28) { game.quests.q28 = true; queueQuestReward('q28', 300, '✅ 任务完成：鱼丸师傅，奖励300元'); }
    const builtCount = Object.values(game.builtProcessing).filter(v => v > 0).length;
    if (builtCount >= 3 && !game.quests.q49) { game.quests.q49 = true; queueQuestReward('q49', 400, '✅ 任务完成：农商一体，奖励400元'); }
    
    addLog(`🛠️ 置办好了${building.name}的家伙事儿！`, 'success');
    playSound('build');
    
    renderProcessingPanel();
    updateTopBar();
    saveGame();
}

// 升级加工坊
function upgradeProcessing(buildingKey) {
    const building = PROCESSING_DATA[buildingKey];
    if (!building) return;
    const currentLevel = game.builtProcessing[buildingKey] || 1;
    if (currentLevel >= 3) { showToast('已满级', 'warn'); return; }
    const cost = building.upgradeCost[currentLevel - 1];
    if (game.money < cost) { showToast('资金不足', 'bad'); return; }
    
    game.money -= cost;
    game.builtProcessing[buildingKey] = currentLevel + 1;
    
    addLog(`🎉 ${building.name}升级到了Lv${currentLevel + 1}！日产能提升至${building.levelCapacity[currentLevel]}斤`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderProcessingPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

// 手动加工（玩家点击按钮触发）
function manualProcess(buildingKey) {
    const building = PROCESSING_DATA[buildingKey];
    if (!building) {
        showToast('加工建筑不存在', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    // 获取加工坊等级
    const buildingLevel = game.builtProcessing[buildingKey] || 1;
    const dailyCapacity = building.levelCapacity ? building.levelCapacity[buildingLevel - 1] : building.dailyCapacity;
    const staminaCost = building.levelStaminaCost ? building.levelStaminaCost[buildingLevel - 1] : building.staminaCost;
    
    // 检查今天是否已达上限（dailyProcessed 已包含进行中的任务）
    const dailyDone =(game.dailyProcessed && game.dailyProcessed[buildingKey]) || 0;
    if (dailyDone >= dailyCapacity) {
        showToast('今天已经花费太多力气在这上面了，手臂都酸了，明天再来吧', 'warn');
        return;
    }
    // 检查这次加工是否会超过上限
    if (dailyDone + building.inputAmount > dailyCapacity) {
        showToast(`今天还能做${dailyCapacity - dailyDone}斤，这批会超量`, 'warn');
        return;
    }
    
    // 检查原料
    let inputAmount = 0;
    if (building.inputType === 'fish') {
        let fishCount = 0;
        if (game.fishInventory) {
            for (const [fishKey, count] of Object.entries(game.fishInventory)) {
                fishCount += count || 0;
            }
        }
        inputAmount = fishCount;
    } else if (building.inputType === 'processed') {
        inputAmount =(game.processedItems && game.processedItems[building.inputItem]) || 0;
    } else {
        const cropKey = building.inputCrop === 'rice' ? 'rice' : (building.inputCrop === 'sweet' ? 'sweet' : (building.inputCrop === 'wheat' ? 'wheat' : building.inputCrop));
        inputAmount = game.crops[cropKey] || 0;
    }
    
    if (inputAmount < building.inputAmount) {
        showToast('手头上的原料不够，先去搞点原料再来', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    // 检查体力
    if (game.stamina < staminaCost) {
        showToast(`累得不行了，需要${staminaCost}点体力...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西再来吧`, 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    // 消耗体力
    game.stamina -= staminaCost;
    
    // 消耗原料
    if (building.inputType === 'fish') {
        // 从鱼塘取鱼
        let remaining = building.inputAmount;
        if (game.fishInventory) {
            for (const fishKey of Object.keys(game.fishInventory)) {
                if (remaining <= 0) break;
                const take = Math.min(remaining, game.fishInventory[fishKey] || 0);
                game.fishInventory[fishKey] -= take;
                remaining -= take;
            }
        }
    } else if (building.inputType === 'processed') {
