        game.processedItems[building.inputItem] -= building.inputAmount;
    } else {
        const cropKey = building.inputCrop === 'rice' ? 'rice' : (building.inputCrop === 'sweet' ? 'sweet' : (building.inputCrop === 'wheat' ? 'wheat' : building.inputCrop));
        game.crops[cropKey] -= building.inputAmount;
    }
    
    // 创建加工任务（需要加工时间完成）
    // 根据加工类型设置不同加工时长（小时）
    let duration = 24; // 默认初级加工24小时
    if (['ricePolishing', 'fishBallWorkshop', 'sweetPotatoStarchMill', 'flourMill', 'tofuWorkshop', 'soyMilkKitchen', 'potatoChips', 'potatoStarch', 'peanutCandy', 'chiliSauce', 'pickleJar'].includes(buildingKey)) {
        duration = 48; // 中级加工48小时
    } else if (['riceWineBrew', 'fishSoupKitchen', 'sweetPotatoNoodlePress', 'noodleWorkshop', 'cornOilPress', 'peanutOil', 'chiliOil'].includes(buildingKey)) {
        duration = 72; // 高级加工72小时
    }
    const job = {
        buildingKey: buildingKey,
        buildingName: building.name,
        inputType: building.inputType,
        inputItem: building.inputItem,
        inputCrop: building.inputCrop,
        startDay: game.day,
        startTotalDay: game.totalDay || game.day,
        startTime: game.time,
        duration: duration,
        progress: 0,
        inputAmount: building.inputAmount,
        outputAmount: building.outputAmount,
        outputItem: building.outputItem,
        staminaCost: staminaCost,
        completed: false
    };
    
    if (!game.processingJobs) game.processingJobs = [];
    game.processingJobs.push(job);
    
    addLog(`🏡 ${building.name}开始加工，预计${duration}小时后完成（体力-${staminaCost}）`, 'good');
    
    // 记录今日已加工量
    if (!game.dailyProcessed) game.dailyProcessed = {};
    game.dailyProcessed[buildingKey] = (game.dailyProcessed[buildingKey] || 0) + building.inputAmount;
    
    // 任务检查：初次加工
    if (!game.quests.q23) {
        game.quests.q23 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q23', 150, '✅ 任务完成：初次加工，奖励150元');
    }
    
    saveGame();
    renderProcessingPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

// 检查加工坊是否解锁
function isProcessingUnlocked(key) {
    const building = PROCESSING_DATA[key];
    if (!building) return false;
    
    // 作物熟悉度Lv2 或 总资产2000金
    const cropSkillLevel = (game.skills && game.skills.cropFamiliarity && game.skills.cropFamiliarity.level) || 0;
    const totalAssets = game.money + calculateCropValue();
    
    return cropSkillLevel >= 2 || totalAssets >= 2000;
}

// 计算粮食总价值
function calculateCropValue() {
    let total = 0;
    for (const [key, amount] of Object.entries(game.crops || {})) {
        total += amount * getSeasonPrice(key);
    }
    return total;
}

// 售卖加工产品
function sellProcessedItem(itemKey, amount) {
    const item = PROCESSED_ITEMS[itemKey];
    if (!item) return;
    
    const have =(game.processedItems && game.processedItems[itemKey]) || 0;
    if (have < amount) {
        showToast('库存不足');
        return;
    }
    
    // 计算价格（使用统一的定价函数，确保显示价格和实际售价一致）
    const price = getProcessedItemPrice(itemKey);
    const money = Math.floor(price * amount);
    game.processedItems[itemKey] -= amount;
    game.money += money;
    
    // 累计售卖统计
    if (game.stats) {
        game.stats.totalSell = (game.stats.totalSell || 0) + money;
    }
    
    addLog(`💰 卖掉了${amount}斤${item.name}，获得${money}元`, 'success');
    playSound('coin');
    
    // 只刷新当前面板，不跳转
    if (currentMainTab === 'processing') {
        renderProcessingPanel();
    } else if (currentMainTab) {
        renderPanel(currentMainTab);
    }
    updateTopBar();
    saveGame();
}


// 研究科技
function researchTech(techId) {
    const tech = TECH_DATA[techId];
    if (!tech) return;
    
    // 检查是否已经研究过
    if (game.unlockedTechs && game.unlockedTechs[techId]) {
        showToast('已经研究过了');
        return;
    }
    
    // 检查前置科技
    if (tech.requires && tech.requires.length > 0) {
        for (const req of tech.requires) {
            if (!game.unlockedTechs || !game.unlockedTechs[req]) {
                showToast('需要先研究前置科技');
                return;
            }
        }
    }
    
    // 检查研究点
    if (game.researchPoints < tech.cost) {
        showToast('农技经验不足');
        return;
    }
    
    // 研究
    game.researchPoints -= tech.cost;
    if (!game.unlockedTechs) game.unlockedTechs = {};
    game.unlockedTechs[techId] = true;
    
    // 任务检查：研究任意一项科技
    if (!game.quests.q45) {
        game.quests.q45 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q45', 200, '✅ 任务完成：科技兴农，奖励200元');
    }
    
    // 应用效果（需要立即生效的）
    if (tech.effect.healthMax) {
        game.maxHealth += tech.effect.healthMax;
        game.health = Math.min(game.health + tech.effect.healthMax, game.maxHealth);
    }
    if (tech.effect.staminaMax) {
        game.maxStamina += tech.effect.staminaMax;
        game.stamina = Math.min(game.stamina + tech.effect.staminaMax, game.maxStamina);
    }
    
    addLog(`📚 研究完成：${tech.name}！${tech.effectDesc}`, 'success');
    playSound('levelup');
    
    renderTechPanel();
    updateTopBar();
    saveGame();
}

// 检查科技是否解锁
function isTechUnlocked(techId) {
    return game.unlockedTechs && game.unlockedTechs[techId];
}

// 获取科技加成总和
function getTechBonus(effectType) {
    let total = 0;
    if (!game.unlockedTechs) return total;
    
    for (const [techId, unlocked] of Object.entries(game.unlockedTechs)) {
        if (!unlocked) continue;
        const tech = TECH_DATA[techId];
        if (tech && tech.effect && tech.effect[effectType] !== undefined) {
            total += tech.effect[effectType];
        }
    }
    
    return total;
}

// 增加NPC好感度
function addNpcFavor(npcId, val) {
    if (!game.npcs) game.npcs = {};
    if (!game.friendship) game.friendship = {};
    const oldFavor = game.npcs[npcId] || 0;
    const newFavor = Math.min(100, Math.max(0, oldFavor + val));
    game.npcs[npcId] = newFavor;
    // 同步更新 friendship（确保里程碑和加成效果正确读取）
    game.friendship[npcId] = newFavor;
    // 触发里程碑检查
    if (typeof checkNpcMilestones === 'function') {
        checkNpcMilestones(npcId);
    }
    // 触发成就检查（社交类成就）
    checkAchievements();
    // 如果当前正在查看NPC页面，实时刷新
    if (currentMainTab === 'npcs' && typeof renderNpcsPanel === 'function') {
        renderNpcsPanel();
    }
}

// 获取种子实际价格（应用商店折扣）

// 获取NPC好感度加成总和
function getNpcBonus(effectType) {
    let total = 0;
    if (!game.npcMilestones) return total;
    
    for (const [npcKey, milestones] of Object.entries(game.npcMilestones)) {
        const npcData = NPC_MILESTONES[npcKey];
        if (!npcData) continue;
        
        for (const ms of npcData.milestones) {
            if (milestones.includes(ms.level) && ms.effect[effectType]) {
                total += ms.effect[effectType];
            }
        }
    }
    
    return total;
}

// 检查NPC里程碑
function checkNpcMilestones(npcKey) {
    const npcData = NPC_MILESTONES[npcKey];
    if (!npcData) return;
    
    const friendship = game.friendship[npcKey] || 0;
    if (!game.npcMilestones) game.npcMilestones = {};
    if (!game.npcMilestones[npcKey]) game.npcMilestones[npcKey] = [];
    
    const achieved = game.npcMilestones[npcKey];
    
    for (const ms of npcData.milestones) {
        if (friendship >= ms.friendship && !achieved.includes(ms.level)) {
            achieved.push(ms.level);
            addLog(`🌟 和${npcData.name}的关系达到【${ms.name}】！${ms.desc}`, 'success');
            playSound('levelup');
        }
    }
}


// 获取NPC里程碑进度文本
function getNpcMilestoneText(npcKey) {
    const npcData = NPC_MILESTONES[npcKey];
    if (!npcData) return '';
    
    const friendship = game.friendship[npcKey] || 0;
    if (!game.npcMilestones) game.npcMilestones = {};
    if (!game.npcMilestones[npcKey]) game.npcMilestones[npcKey] = [];
    
    const achieved = game.npcMilestones[npcKey];
    const total = npcData.milestones.length;
    
    // 找下一个未达成的里程碑
    let nextMs = null;
    for (const ms of npcData.milestones) {
        if (!achieved.includes(ms.level)) {
            nextMs = ms;
            break;
        }
    }
    
    if (nextMs) {
        const progress = Math.min(100, (friendship / nextMs.friendship) * 100);
        return `🌟 里程碑 ${achieved.length}/${total} | 下一个：${nextMs.name}（${nextMs.desc}）- ${friendship}/${nextMs.friendship}`;
    } else {
        return `🌟 里程碑 ${achieved.length}/${total} | 全部达成！`;
    }
}


// 获取建筑加成总和
function getBuildingBonus(effectType) {
    let total = 0;
    if (!game.buildings) return total;
    
    for (const [buildingId, level] of Object.entries(game.buildings)) {
        const building = BUILDING_DATA[buildingId];
        if (!building || !building.effect[effectType]) continue;
        
        // 如果是数值型效果（比如storageBonus），直接加
        if (effectType === 'storageBonus') {
            // 每级的效果
            for (let i = 0; i < level; i++) {
                total += building.upgradeEffect[i] || building.effect[effectType];
            }
        } else {
            // 如果是百分比型效果，取最高级的效果
            if (level > 0) {
                const effectIndex = Math.min(level - 1, building.upgradeEffect.length - 1);
                total += building.upgradeEffect[effectIndex] || building.effect[effectType];
            }
        }
    }
    
    return total;
}

// 建造建筑
function buildBuilding(buildingId) {
    const building = BUILDING_DATA[buildingId];
    if (!building) return;
    
    // 检查是否已经建造
    const currentLevel = game.buildings[buildingId] || 0;
    if (currentLevel > 0) {
        showToast('已经建造过了');
        return;
    }
    
    // 检查金钱
    if (game.money < building.cost) {
        showToast('钱包里钱不够，先去卖点东西换点钱', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    // 建造
    game.money -= building.cost;
    game.buildings[buildingId] = 1;
    
    // 应用效果（储存上限等需要立即更新的）
    if (building.effect.storageBonus) {
        const bonus = building.effect.storageBonus;
        game.storageCapacity = (game.storageCapacity || 3000) + bonus;
    }
    
    addLog(`🏗️ 建造了${building.name}！${building.effectDesc}`, 'success');
    playSound('levelup');
    
    checkAchievements();
    
    renderBuildingPanel();
    updateTopBar();
    saveGame();
}

// 升级建筑
function upgradeBuilding(buildingId) {
    const building = BUILDING_DATA[buildingId];
    if (!building) return;
    
    const currentLevel = game.buildings[buildingId] || 0;
    if (currentLevel >= building.maxLevel) {
        showToast('已达最高等级');
        return;
    }
    
    const upgradeCost = building.upgradeCost[currentLevel];
    if (game.money < upgradeCost) {
        showToast('钱包里钱不够，先去卖点东西换点钱', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    // 升级
    game.money -= upgradeCost;
    game.buildings[buildingId] = currentLevel + 1;
    
    // 应用效果
    if (building.effect.storageBonus) {
        const oldBonus = building.upgradeEffect[currentLevel - 1] || building.effect.storageBonus;
        const newBonus = building.upgradeEffect[currentLevel] || building.effect.storageBonus;
        const diff = newBonus - oldBonus;
        game.storageCapacity = (game.storageCapacity || 3000) + diff;
    }
    
    addLog(`⬆️ ${building.name}升级到${currentLevel + 1}级！`, 'success');
    playSound('levelup');
    
    renderBuildingPanel();
    updateTopBar();
    saveGame();
}

// 更新储存上限（保留作为兼容函数，实际增量在建造/升级时直接应用）
function updateStorageCapacity() {
    const storageBonus = getBuildingBonus('storageBonus');
    const base = 3000;
    const target = base + storageBonus;
    // 只提升，不降低（避免覆盖扩地/扩建的增量）
    if (target > (game.storageCapacity || 0)) {
        game.storageCapacity = target;
    }
}

function getSeedPrice(basePrice) {
    const discount = getTechBonus('shopDiscount');
    if (discount > 0) {
        return Math.floor(basePrice * (1 - discount));
    }
    return basePrice;
}

function chatWithNpc(npcKey) {
    const npc = NPC_DATA[npcKey];
    const today = game.day;
    
    // 检查今天是否已经聊过天
    if (game.lastChatDay && game.lastChatDay[npcKey] === today) {
        showToast('今天已经聊过啦~明天再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.stamina < 5) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playClickSound();
    playNpcChatter(npcKey, 1.5); // 播放NPC呢喃声
    game.stamina -= 5;
    
    // 增加好感度 1~3点
        // 计算好感度增加（科技 + NPC加成）
    let baseGain = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 1;
    let friendshipMultiplier = 1 + getTechBonus('friendshipGain');
    
    // 王二蛋的好感度加成（和其他NPC聊天时生效，和二蛋自己聊天不生效）
    if (npcKey !== 'wangerdan') {
        const npcFriendshipBonus = getNpcBonus('friendshipGain');
        if (npcFriendshipBonus > 0) {
            friendshipMultiplier += npcFriendshipBonus;
        }
    }
    
    const gain = Math.floor(baseGain * friendshipMultiplier);
    const oldFriendship = game.npcs[npcKey] || 0;
    game.npcs[npcKey] = Math.min(100, oldFriendship + gain);
    if (!game.friendship[npcKey]) game.friendship[npcKey] = 0;
    game.friendship[npcKey] = Math.min(100, game.friendship[npcKey] + gain);
    const friendship = game.npcs[npcKey];
    
    // 任务检查：第一次和村民聊天
    if (!game.quests.q9) {
        game.quests.q9 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q9', 50, '✅ 任务完成：初次交流，奖励50元');
    }
    
    // 任务检查：和任意村民达到友好（40好感）
    if (!game.quests.q15 && friendship >= 40) {
        game.quests.q15 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q15', 300, '✅ 任务完成：打成一片，奖励300元');
    }
    
    // 记录今天已经聊过天
    if (!game.lastChatDay) game.lastChatDay = {};
    game.lastChatDay[npcKey] = today;
    
    // 根据好感度等级选择对话
    let level = 0;
    for (let i = FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        if (friendship >= FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[i].min) {
            level = i;
            break;
        }
    }
    
    // 检查是否升级了好感度等级
    let oldLevel = 0;
    for (let i = FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        if (oldFriendship >= FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[i].min) {
            oldLevel = i;
            break;
        }
    }
    const levelUp = level > oldLevel;
    
    // 随机选一条对话，避免重复
    const npcDialogue = NPC_DIALOGUE[npcKey];
    let dialogues;
    if (npcDialogue) {
        dialogues = npcDialogue[level] || npcDialogue[0] || ['...'];
    } else {
        dialogues = ['（对方看起来有话想说，但不知如何开口）'];
    }
    let dialogueIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * dialogues.length);
    
    // 避免和上次对话重复
    if (!game.lastDialogue) game.lastDialogue = {};
    if (game.lastDialogue[npcKey] !== undefined && dialogues.length > 1) {
        while (dialogueIndex === game.lastDialogue[npcKey]) {
            dialogueIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * dialogues.length);
        }
    }
    game.lastDialogue[npcKey] = dialogueIndex;
    const dialogue = dialogues[dialogueIndex];
    
    // 构建弹窗内容
    let modalContent = `"${dialogue}"`;
    
    // 如果升级了好感度等级，显示特殊提示
    if (levelUp) {
        const levelName =(FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[level] && FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[level].name) || '新等级';
        modalContent += `\n\n🎉 关系提升！现在是【${levelName}】`;
    }
    
    modalContent += `\n\n好感度 +${gain}`;
    
    // 显示对话弹窗
    showModal(
        `${npc.emoji} ${npc.name}`,
        modalContent,
        null
    );
    
    addLog(`💬 和${npc.name}聊了会儿天，好感度+${gain}`, 'info');
    // 检查NPC里程碑
    checkNpcMilestones(npcKey);
    
    saveGame();
    if (currentMainTab === 'npcs') {
        renderNpcsPanel();
    renderBackpack();
    updateDailyButtons();
    }
    updateTopBar();
}

// 显示送礼弹窗（先做个简单版本，后面再完善）
function showGiftModal(npcKey) {
    const npc = NPC_DATA[npcKey];
    const today = game.day;
    
    // 检查今天是否已经送过礼
    if (game.lastGiftDay && game.lastGiftDay[npcKey] === today) {
        showToast('今天已经送过礼啦~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    // 所有送礼道具
    const gifts = [
        { key: 'snack', name: '粗点心', emoji: '🍬' },
        { key: 'liquor', name: '散装白酒', emoji: '🍶' },
        { key: 'cloth', name: '花布头', emoji: '🧵' },
        { key: 'sugar', name: '红糖', emoji: '🍯' },
        { key: 'cigarette', name: '香烟', emoji: '🚬' }
    ];
    
    let html = '<div style="max-height: 300px; overflow-y: auto;">';
    html += `<p style="margin-bottom: 10px; color: #5d4e37; font-style: italic;">"哎呀，来就来嘛，还带什么东西。"</p>`;
    html += `<p style="margin-bottom: 15px; color: #666;">选择要送给${npc.name}的礼物：</p>`;
    
    gifts.forEach(gift => {
        const owned = game.items[gift.key] || 0;
        const likeLevel = npc.likes[gift.key] || 1;
        const likeDesc = likeLevel >= 8 ? '❤️ 非常喜欢' : likeLevel >= 5 ? '💛 喜欢' : likeLevel >= 3 ? '💚 一般' : '💔 不喜欢';
        const canGive = owned > 0;
        
        html += `
            <div class="shop-item" style="margin-bottom: 8px;">
                <div class="shop-item-info">
                    <div class="shop-item-icon">${gift.emoji}</div>
                    <div>
                        <div class="shop-item-name">${gift.name}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${likeDesc} | 拥有：${owned}个</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div>
                    <button class="buy-btn" onclick="giveGift('${npcKey}', '${gift.key}')" ${!canGive ? 'disabled' : ''}>
                        赠送
                    </button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    });
    
    html += '</div>';
    
    // 显示弹窗
    document.getElementById('modal-title').textContent = `🎁 给${npc.name}送礼`;
    document.getElementById('modal-content').innerHTML = html;
    document.querySelector('.modal-buttons').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('modal-confirm').style.display = 'none';
    document.querySelector('.modal-btn.secondary').textContent = '关闭';
    document.getElementById('modal-overlay').style.display = 'flex';
}

// 送礼
function giveGift(npcKey, giftKey) {
    const npc = NPC_DATA[npcKey];
    const today = game.day;
    
    // 检查今天是否已经送过礼
    if (game.lastGiftDay && game.lastGiftDay[npcKey] === today) {
        showToast('今天已经送过礼啦~明天再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    const owned = game.items[giftKey] || 0;
    if (owned < 1) {
        showToast('礼物不足！', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playCoinSound();
    game.items[giftKey] = owned - 1;
    
    // 计算好感度加成
    const likeLevel = npc.likes[giftKey] || 1;
    const gain = likeLevel; // 喜欢等级就是好感度加成
    
    const oldFriendship = game.npcs[npcKey] || 0;
    game.npcs[npcKey] = Math.min(100, oldFriendship + gain);
    if (!game.friendship[npcKey]) game.friendship[npcKey] = 0;
    game.friendship[npcKey] = Math.min(100, game.friendship[npcKey] + gain);
    const friendship = game.npcs[npcKey];
    
    // 任务检查：第一次送礼
    if (!game.quests.q10) {
        game.quests.q10 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q10', 100, '✅ 任务完成：礼轻情意重，奖励100元');
    }
    
    // 任务检查：和任意村民达到友好（40好感）
    if (!game.quests.q15 && friendship >= 40) {
        game.quests.q15 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q15', 300, '✅ 任务完成：打成一片，奖励300元');
    }
    
    // 记录今天已经送过礼
    if (!game.lastGiftDay) game.lastGiftDay = {};
    game.lastGiftDay[npcKey] = today;
    
    // 检查是否升级了好感度等级
    let oldLevel = 0;
    for (let i = FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        if (oldFriendship >= FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[i].min) {
            oldLevel = i;
            break;
        }
    }
    let newLevel = 0;
    for (let i = FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        if (friendship >= FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[i].min) {
            newLevel = i;
            break;
        }
    }
    const levelUp = newLevel > oldLevel;
    
    // 根据NPC和喜欢程度生成个性化反应
    let reaction = '';
    const giftName =(ITEM_DATA[giftKey] && ITEM_DATA[giftKey].name) || '礼物';
    
    // NPC特殊反应（覆盖默认反应）
    const specialReactions = {
        wangcunzhang: {
            high: [`哎呀，这${giftName}好啊！我就好这口。`, `你小子有心啊，知道我喜欢${giftName}。`, `来就来嘛，还带这么合心意的东西。`],
            mid: [`嗯，${giftName}，不错。`, `谢谢你想着我。`],
            low: [`哦，${giftName}啊...行吧。`]
        },
        lilaonong: {
            high: [`嘿嘿，这${giftName}我喜欢！`, `你咋知道我爱这口？`, `好，好，有孝心。`],
            mid: [`${giftName}啊，还行。`, `有心了。`],
            low: [`...放那儿吧。`]
        },
        zhangshen: {
            high: [`哎哟，这${giftName}太合我心意了！`, `你就像我自家孩子一样懂事。`, `婶儿高兴！`],
            mid: [`${giftName}啊，谢谢啦。`, `哎呀，客气啥。`],
            low: [`...哦，谢谢。`]
        },
        wangerdan: {
            high: [`哇！${giftName}！我最爱这个！`, `你怎么知道我喜欢${giftName}？太棒了！`, `耶！有${giftName}吃！`],
            mid: [`${giftName}啊，还行吧。`, `谢谢...`],
            low: [`...这不是我喜欢的。`]
        },
        zhaolaoban: {
            high: [`这${giftName}品质不错，你有心了。`, `哈哈，会做人！`, `以后来卖粮，我给你多算点。`],
            mid: [`${giftName}啊，谢谢。`, `有心了。`],
            low: [`...嗯，放着吧。`]
        }
    };
    
    const npcReactions = specialReactions[npcKey];
    if (npcReactions) {
        if (likeLevel >= 7) {
            reaction = npcReactions.high[Math.floor(Math.random() * npcReactions.high.length)];
        } else if (likeLevel >= 4) {
            reaction = npcReactions.mid[Math.floor(Math.random() * npcReactions.mid.length)];
        } else {
            reaction = npcReactions.low[Math.floor(Math.random() * npcReactions.low.length)];
        }
    } else {
        // 默认反应
        if (likeLevel >= 7) {
            const reactions = [
                `哇！这是${giftName}！我太喜欢了！谢谢你！`,
                `你怎么知道我喜欢${giftName}？太懂我了！`,
                `太棒了！这正是我想要的！`,
                `嘿嘿，你真好~`,
                `哇，这份礼物太合我心意了！`
            ];
            reaction = reactions[Math.floor(Math.random() * reactions.length)];
        } else if (likeLevel >= 4) {
            const reactions = [
                `嗯，${giftName}，不错不错。`,
                `谢谢你的${giftName}，我收下了。`,
                `哎呀，还带礼物来，太客气了。`,
                `这份${giftName}，我很喜欢。`,
                `有心了，谢谢你的${giftName}。`
            ];
            reaction = reactions[Math.floor(Math.random() * reactions.length)];
        } else {
            const reactions = [
                `哦，${giftName}啊...谢谢你。`,
                `嗯...这份礼物，我收下了。`,
                `哎呀，你太客气了。`,
                `谢谢你的心意。`,
                `嗯，有心了。`
            ];
            reaction = reactions[Math.floor(Math.random() * reactions.length)];
        }
    }
    
    // 构建弹窗内容
    let modalContent = `<div style="font-size: 16px; color: #5d4e37; margin-bottom: 15px; font-style: italic;">"${reaction}"</div>`;
    
    // 如果升级了好感度等级，显示特殊提示
    if (levelUp) {
        const levelName =(FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[newLevel] && FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[newLevel].name) || '新等级';
        modalContent += `<div style="color: #e67e22; font-weight: bold; margin: 10px 0;">🎉 关系提升！现在是【${levelName}】</div>`;
    }
    
    modalContent += `<div style="color: #27ae60; margin-top: 10px;">好感度 +${gain}</div>`;
    
    // 关闭送礼弹窗，显示反应弹窗
    closeModal();
    
    setTimeout(() => {
        showModal(
            `${npc.emoji} ${npc.name}`,
            modalContent,
            null
        );
    }, 200);
    
    addLog(`🎁 送给${npc.name}一份${giftName}，好感度+${gain}`, 'good');
    // 检查NPC里程碑
    checkNpcMilestones(npcKey);
    
    saveGame();
    if (currentMainTab === 'npcs') {
        renderNpcsPanel();
    renderBackpack();
    updateDailyButtons();
    }
    updateTopBar();
}

// 宠物数据
const PET_DATA = {
    ahua: {
        name: '阿花',
        type: 'cat',
        emoji: '🐱',
        breed: '三花猫',
        desc: '高冷傲娇的三花猫，嘴硬心软。',
        unlockDay: 5,
        effectType: 'pestReduction',  // 虫害减少
        baseEffect: 0.10,  // 基础10%
        maxEffect: 0.30,   // 最大30%
        favoriteFood: '鱼干',
        dailyFoodCost: 20
    },
    dahuang: {
        name: '大黄',
        type: 'dog',
        emoji: '🐶',
        breed: '中华田园犬',
        desc: '忠诚憨厚的大黄狗，胆子有点小。',
        unlockDay: 7,
        effectType: 'theftReduction',  // 偷菜减少
        baseEffect: 0.20,  // 基础20%
        maxEffect: 0.50,   // 最大50%
        favoriteFood: '骨头',
        dailyFoodCost: 30
    }
};

// 宠物好感度等级
const PET_FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS = [
    { name: '陌生', min: 0, color: '#999' },
    { name: '熟悉', min: 20, color: '#3498db' },
    { name: '友好', min: 40, color: '#2ecc71' },
    { name: '亲密', min: 60, color: '#e67e22' },
    { name: '挚友', min: 90, color: '#e74c3c' }
];


// 获取宠物效果加成
function getPetEffect(effectType) {
    let total = 0;
    if (!game.pets) return total;
    
    for (const [petKey, petData] of Object.entries(game.pets)) {
        const pet = PET_DATA[petKey];
        if (!pet || pet.effectType !== effectType) continue;
        
        const friendship = petData.affection || petData.friendship || 0;
        // 根据好感度计算效果：0好感度=基础效果，90好感度=最大效果
        const ratio = Math.min(1, friendship / 90);
        const effect = pet.baseEffect + (pet.maxEffect - pet.baseEffect) * ratio;
        
        total += effect;
    }
    
    return total;
}

// 获取宠物好感度等级
function getPetFriendshipLevel(friendship) {
    let level = PET_FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[0];
    for (let i = PET_FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        if (friendship >= PET_FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[i].min) {
            level = PET_FRIENDSHIP_LEVELS[i];
            break;
        }
    }
    return level;
}

// 获取宠物效果文本
function getPetEffectText(petKey) {
    const pet = PET_DATA[petKey];
    if (!pet) return '';
    
    const petData =(game.pets && game.pets[petKey]);
    if (!petData) return '';
    
    const friendship = petData.affection || petData.friendship || 0;
    const ratio = Math.min(1, friendship / 90);
    const effect = pet.baseEffect + (pet.maxEffect - pet.baseEffect) * ratio;
    const effectPercent = Math.round(effect * 100);
    
    if (pet.effectType === 'pestReduction') {
        return `虫害减少 ${effectPercent}%`;
    } else if (pet.effectType === 'theftReduction') {
        return `偷菜事件减少 ${effectPercent}%`;
    }
    
    return '';
}

function renderPetsPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🐱 宠物</div>';
    
    const petKeys = ['ahua', 'dahuang'];
    
    petKeys.forEach(petKey => {
        const pet = PET_DATA[petKey];
        const owned = game.pets && game.pets[petKey];
        
        if (!owned) {
            // 未解锁 - 需要触发前置事件
            let unlockText = '';
            let canUnlock = false;
            if (petKey === 'ahua') {
                // 阿花（猫）：需要触发流浪猫事件并喂食3次
                const visits =(game.petEvents && game.petEvents.strayCatVisits) || 0;
                canUnlock = visits >= 3;
                unlockText = canUnlock ? '阿花决定留下来了！' : `需要在门口遇到流浪猫并喂食 (${visits}/3)`;
            } else if (petKey === 'dahuang') {
                // 大黄（狗）：使用PET_DATA中的unlockDay
                const unlockDay = pet.unlockDay || 7;
                canUnlock = (game.totalDay || game.day) >= unlockDay;
                unlockText = canUnlock ? '一只流浪狗来到了村口' : `第${unlockDay}天才会出现 (${game.totalDay || game.day}/${unlockDay})`;
            }
            html += `
                <div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon" style="opacity: 0.3;">${pet.emoji}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${pet.name} 🔒</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">${pet.breed} · ${pet.desc}</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc" style="color: #999; margin-top: 4px;">
                                ${unlockText}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        ${canUnlock ? 
                            `<button class="buy-btn" onclick="adoptPet('${petKey}')">领养</button>` :
                            `<button class="buy-btn disabled" disabled>未解锁</button>`
                        }
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        } else {
            // 已拥有
            const petData = game.pets[petKey];
            const friendship = petData.affection || petData.friendship || 0;
            const today = game.day;
            const fedToday = petData.lastFedDay === today;
            const pettedToday = petData.lastPettedDay === today;
            const playedToday = petData.lastPlayedDay === today;
            
            html += `
                <div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info" style="width: 100%;">
                        <div style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 15px; width: 100%;">
                            <div style="font-size: 50px;">${pet.emoji}</div>
                            <div style="flex: 1;">
                                <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center;">
                                    <div>
                                        <span style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 16px; color: #5d4e37;">${pet.name}</span>
                                        <span style="font-size: 13px; color: #999; margin-left: 8px;">${pet.breed}</span>
                                    </div>
                                    <span style="font-size: 13px; color: #e67e22; font-weight: bold;">好感度 ${friendship}/100</span>
                                </div>
                                <div style="font-size: 13px; color: #666; margin-top: 4px;">${pet.desc}</div>
                                <div style="font-size: 13px; color: #27ae60; margin-top: 4px; font-weight: bold;">
                                    ✨ 当前效果：${typeof getPetEffectText === 'function' ? getPetEffectText(petKey) : ''}
                                </div>
                                <div class="field-progress" style="margin-top: 8px;">
                                    <div class="field-progress-bar" style="width: ${friendship}%; background: #e67e22;"></div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div style="margin-top: 12px; display: flex; gap: 10px; flex-wrap: wrap;">
                            <button class="action-btn" onclick="feedPet('${petKey}')" ${fedToday ? 'disabled' : ''}>
                                🍖 喂食 ${fedToday ? '(已喂)' : ''}
                            </button>
                            <button class="action-btn" onclick="petPet('${petKey}')" ${pettedToday ? 'disabled' : ''}>
                                🤚 抚摸 ${pettedToday ? '(已摸)' : ''}
                            </button>
                            <button class="action-btn" onclick="playWithPet('${petKey}')" ${playedToday ? 'disabled' : ''}>
                                🎾 玩耍 ${playedToday ? '(已玩)' : ''}
                            </button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        }
    });
    
    // 宠物粪便
    if (game.petPoop && game.petPoop > 0) {
        html += '<div class="shop-category">宠物粪便</div>';
        html += `
            <div class="shop-item">
                <div class="shop-item-info">
                    <div class="shop-item-icon">💩</div>
                    <div>
                        <div class="shop-item-name">宠物粪便</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">可以用来堆肥，肥效更好</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc" style="color: #4a7c59; margin-top: 4px;">
                            当前拥有：${game.petPoop} 份
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div>
                    <button class="buy-btn" onclick="collectPoop()">收集堆肥</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

// 领养宠物
function adoptPet(petKey) {
    const pet = PET_DATA[petKey];
    
    if (game.totalDay < pet.unlockDay) {
        showToast('还没到解锁时间呢~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    // 阿花需要先喂过流浪猫3次才能领养
    if (petKey === 'ahua' && ((game.petEvents && game.petEvents.strayCatVisits) || 0) < 3) {
        showToast('还需要多喂几次流浪猫才能领养~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    if (!game.pets) game.pets = {};
    if (game.pets[petKey]) {
        showToast('已经领养过啦~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playBonusSound();
    game.pets[petKey] = {
        affection: 10,
        friendship: 10,
        lastFedDay: 0,
        lastPettedDay: 0,
        lastPlayedDay: 0
    };
    
    // 任务检查：领养第一只宠物
    if (!game.quests.q11) {
        game.quests.q11 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q11', 200, '✅ 任务完成：新的家人，奖励200元');
    }
    // 任务检查：领养第二只宠物
    const petCount = Object.keys(game.pets).filter(k => game.pets[k]).length;
    if (petCount >= 2 && !game.quests.q44) {
        game.quests.q44 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q44', 300, '✅ 任务完成：双宠之家，奖励300元');
    }
    
    addLog(`🎉 ${pet.name}来到了你家！以后就是一家人啦~`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderPetsPanel();
    if (typeof updateUI === 'function') {
        updateUI();
    }
    showToast(`${pet.name}来啦！`, 'good');
}

// 喂食宠物
function feedPet(petKey) {
    const pet = PET_DATA[petKey];
    if (!pet) return;
    
    const petData =(game.pets && game.pets[petKey]);
    if (!petData) {
        showToast('请先领养宠物~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    const today = game.day;
    
    if (petData.lastFedDay === today) {
        showToast('今天已经喂过啦~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.money < pet.dailyFoodCost) {
        showToast('钱包里钱不够，连宠物都快养不起了，先去卖点东西换点钱', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playClickSound();
    game.money -= pet.dailyFoodCost;
    petData.lastFedDay = today;
    petData.affection = Math.min(100, (petData.affection || petData.friendship || 0) + 3);
    
    // 产生粪便
    if (!game.petPoop) game.petPoop = 0;
    game.petPoop += 1;
    
    addLog(`🍖 给${pet.name}喂了饭，花费${pet.dailyFoodCost}金币，它吃得很开心，好感度+3`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderPetsPanel();
    updateTopBar();
    showToast('好感度+3！', 'good');
}

// 抚摸宠物
function petPet(petKey) {
    const pet = PET_DATA[petKey];
    if (!pet) return;
    
    const petData =(game.pets && game.pets[petKey]);
    if (!petData) {
        showToast('请先领养宠物~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    const today = game.day;
    
    if (petData.lastPettedDay === today) {
        showToast('今天已经摸过啦~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playClickSound();
    petData.lastPettedDay = today;
    petData.affection = Math.min(100, (petData.affection || petData.friendship || 0) + 1);
    
    addLog(`🤚 摸了摸${pet.name}，它舒服地眯起了眼睛，好感度+1`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderPetsPanel();
    showToast('好感度+1！', 'good');
}

// 和宠物玩耍
function playWithPet(petKey) {
    const pet = PET_DATA[petKey];
    if (!pet) return;
    
    const petData =(game.pets && game.pets[petKey]);
    if (!petData) {
        showToast('请先领养宠物~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    const today = game.day;
    
    if (petData.lastPlayedDay === today) {
        showToast('今天已经玩过啦~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.stamina < 10) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playClickSound();
    game.stamina -= 10;
    petData.lastPlayedDay = today;
    petData.affection = Math.min(100, (petData.affection || petData.friendship || 0) + 5);
    
    addLog(`🎾 和${pet.name}玩了一会儿，它特别开心，好感度+5`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderPetsPanel();
    updateTopBar();
    showToast('好感度+5！', 'good');
}

// 收集宠物粪便用于堆肥
function collectPoop() {
    if (!game.petPoop || game.petPoop < 1) {
        showToast('没有粪便可以收集~', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playDirtSound();
    const amount = game.petPoop;
    game.items.organicFertilizer = (game.items.organicFertilizer || 0) + amount;
    game.petPoop = 0;
    
    addLog(`💩 收集了${amount}份宠物粪便，做成了有机肥~`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderPetsPanel();
    updateTopBar();
    showToast(`获得${amount}份有机肥！`, 'good');
}

function renderAutomationPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🤖 自动化设备</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">花钱买个省心，设备自动干活，你只管数钱。</p>';
    
    // 已购买的设备
    const ownedDevices = Object.entries(game.automation || {}).filter(([k, v]) => v > 0);
    if (ownedDevices.length > 0) {
        html += '<div class="shop-category">✅ 已购买的设备</div>';
        ownedDevices.forEach(([deviceId, level]) => {
            const device = AUTOMATION_DATA[deviceId];
            if (!device) return;
            html += `
                <div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${device.emoji}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${device.name}（Lv${level}/${device.maxLevel}）</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">${device.levelDesc[level - 1] || device.desc}</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">${device.effectDesc}</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="shop-item-price">
                        ${level < device.maxLevel ? `<button class="buy-btn" onclick="upgradeAutomation('${deviceId}')" ${game.money < device.levelUpCost[level] ? 'disabled' : ''}>⬆️ 升级（${device.levelUpCost[level]}元）</button>` : '<span style="color:#27ae60;">✅ 已满级</span>'}
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        });
    }
    
    // 可购买的设备
    html += '<div class="shop-category">🛒 可购买的设备</div>';
    for (const [deviceId, device] of Object.entries(AUTOMATION_DATA)) {
        const currentLevel =(game.automation && game.automation[deviceId]) || 0;
        if (currentLevel > 0) continue; // 已拥有的不显示
        
        html += `
            <div class="shop-item">
                <div class="shop-item-info">
                    <div class="shop-item-icon">${device.emoji}</div>
                    <div>
                        <div class="shop-item-name">${device.name}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${device.desc}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${device.effectDesc}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">Lv1：${device.levelDesc[0]}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="shop-item-price">
                    <button class="buy-btn" onclick="buyAutomation('${deviceId}')" ${game.money < device.cost ? 'disabled' : ''}>💰 ${device.cost}元购买</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

function buyAutomation(deviceId) {
    const device = AUTOMATION_DATA[deviceId];
    if (!device) return;
    if (game.money < device.cost) { showToast('资金不足', 'bad'); return; }
    
    game.money -= device.cost;
    if (!game.automation) game.automation = {};
    game.automation[deviceId] = 1;
    
    addLog(`🎉 购买了${device.emoji}${device.name}！`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderAutomationPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function upgradeAutomation(deviceId) {
    const device = AUTOMATION_DATA[deviceId];
    if (!device) return;
    const currentLevel =(game.automation && game.automation[deviceId]) || 0;
    if (currentLevel >= device.maxLevel) return;
    
    const cost = device.levelUpCost[currentLevel];
    if (game.money < cost) { showToast('资金不足', 'bad'); return; }
    
    game.money -= cost;
    game.automation[deviceId] = currentLevel + 1;
    
    addLog(`🎉 ${device.emoji}${device.name}升级到了Lv${currentLevel + 1}！`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderAutomationPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function renderBankPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🏦 农村信用社</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">钱多了放银行，利滚利。日利率0.5%，利滚利。</p>';
    
    // 当前存款
    html += `<div class="shop-item"><div class="shop-item-info"><div class="shop-item-icon">🏦</div><div><div class="shop-item-name">当前存款</div><div class="shop-item-desc">${game.bankDeposit || 0} 元</div></div></div></div>`;
    
    // 存取款
    html += '<div class="shop-category">💰 存取款</div>';
    html += `
        <div class="shop-item">
            <div class="shop-item-info">
                <div class="shop-item-icon">💵</div>
                <div>
                    <div class="shop-item-name">存入全部现金</div>
                    <div class="shop-item-desc">当前现金：${game.money}元</div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="shop-item-price">
                <button class="buy-btn" onclick="bankDepositAll()" ${game.money <= 0 ? 'disabled' : ''}>存入</button>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="shop-item">
            <div class="shop-item-info">
                <div class="shop-item-icon">💴</div>
                <div>
                    <div class="shop-item-name">取出全部存款</div>
                    <div class="shop-item-desc">当前存款：${game.bankDeposit || 0}元</div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="shop-item-price">
                <button class="buy-btn" onclick="bankWithdrawAll()" ${(game.bankDeposit || 0) <= 0 ? 'disabled' : ''}>取出</button>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

function bankDepositAll() {
    if (game.money <= 0) { showToast('没有现金可存入', 'bad'); return; }
    if (!game.bankDeposit) game.bankDeposit = 0;
    game.bankDeposit += game.money;
    addLog(`🏦 存入${game.money}元到银行`, 'good');
    game.money = 0;
    saveGame();
    renderBankPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function bankWithdrawAll() {
    if (!game.bankDeposit || game.bankDeposit <= 0) { showToast('没有存款可取出', 'bad'); return; }
    game.money += game.bankDeposit;
    addLog(`🏦 从银行取出${game.bankDeposit}元`, 'good');
    game.bankDeposit = 0;
    saveGame();
    renderBankPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function renderNeighborPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🤝 邻里互助</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">远亲不如近邻。跟村里人处好了，农忙时邻居都会来搭把手。</p>';
    
    // 当前总好感度
    const totalFriendship = Object.values(game.friendship || {}).reduce((sum, v) => sum + (v || 0), 0);
    html += `<div class="shop-item"><div class="shop-item-info"><div class="shop-item-icon">❤️</div><div><div class="shop-item-name">全村好感度</div><div class="shop-item-desc">${totalFriendship} 点</div></div></div></div>`;
    
    // 已激活的互助
    const activeHelps = Object.entries(game.neighborHelp || {}).filter(([k, v]) => v);
    if (activeHelps.length > 0) {
        html += '<div class="shop-category">✅ 已激活的互助</div>';
        activeHelps.forEach(([helpId, active]) => {
            const help = NEIGHBOR_HELP_DATA[helpId];
            if (!help) return;
            html += `
                <div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${help.emoji}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${help.name}</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">${help.effectDesc}</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        });
    }
    
    // 可解锁的互助
    html += '<div class="shop-category">🔓 可解锁的互助</div>';
    for (const [helpId, help] of Object.entries(NEIGHBOR_HELP_DATA)) {
        if (game.neighborHelp && game.neighborHelp[helpId]) continue; // 已激活
        const canUnlock = totalFriendship >= help.requireFriendship;
        html += `
            <div class="shop-item ${canUnlock ? '' : 'locked'}">
                <div class="shop-item-info">
                    <div class="shop-item-icon">${help.emoji}</div>
                    <div>
                        <div class="shop-item-name">${help.name}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${help.desc}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${help.effectDesc}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${canUnlock ? '✅ 全村好感度达标' : `❌ 需要全村好感度${help.requireFriendship}（当前${totalFriendship}）`}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="shop-item-price">
                    <button class="buy-btn" onclick="unlockNeighborHelp('${helpId}')" ${!canUnlock ? 'disabled' : ''}>🔓 解锁</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

function unlockNeighborHelp(helpId) {
    const help = NEIGHBOR_HELP_DATA[helpId];
    if (!help) return;
    const totalFriendship = Object.values(game.friendship || {}).reduce((sum, v) => sum + (v || 0), 0);
    if (totalFriendship < help.requireFriendship) { showToast('全村好感度不足', 'bad'); return; }
    
    if (!game.neighborHelp) game.neighborHelp = {};
    game.neighborHelp[helpId] = true;
    
    addLog(`🎉 解锁了${help.emoji}${help.name}！${help.npcText}`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderNeighborPanel();
}

function renderMarketPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    const isMarketDay = MARKET_DATA.openDay.includes(game.day);
    
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🏪 集市</div>';
    
    if (!isMarketDay) {
        html += '<p class="panel-desc">今天不是赶集日。集市每月7、14、21、28日开放。</p>';
        html += '<div class="empty-state">📅 下次赶集日是第' + MARKET_DATA.openDay.find(d => d > game.day) + '天</div>';
        panel.innerHTML = html;
        return;
    }
    
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">赶集啦！十里八乡的人都来了，东西比村里便宜。</p>';
    
    // 特殊商品
    html += '<div class="shop-category">🛒 今日特供</div>';
    MARKET_DATA.specialItems.forEach(item => {
        html += `
            <div class="shop-item">
                <div class="shop-item-info">
                    <div class="shop-item-icon">${item.emoji}</div>
                    <div>
                        <div class="shop-item-name">${item.name}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${item.desc}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="shop-item-price">
                    <button class="buy-btn" onclick="buyMarketItem('${item.id}', ${item.price})" ${game.money < item.price ? 'disabled' : ''}>💰 ${item.price}元购买</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    });
    
    // 作物交易
    html += '<div class="shop-category">🌾 作物交易</div>';
    MARKET_DATA.specialCrops.forEach(crop => {
        const have = game.crops[crop.id] || 0;
        html += `
            <div class="shop-item">
                <div class="shop-item-info">
                    <div class="shop-item-icon">${crop.emoji}</div>
                    <div>
                        <div class="shop-item-name">${crop.name}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">库存：${have}斤</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="shop-item-price" style="display:flex;gap:6px;">
                    <button class="buy-btn" onclick="buyCrop('${crop.id}', ${crop.buyPrice})">💰 ${crop.buyPrice}元/斤买</button>
                    <button class="buy-btn" onclick="sellMarketCrop('${crop.id}', ${crop.sellPrice})" ${have <= 0 ? 'disabled' : ''}>💰 ${crop.sellPrice}元/斤卖</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    });
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

function buyMarketItem(itemId, price) {
    if (game.money < price) { showToast('钱不够', 'bad'); return; }
    game.money -= price;
    if (!game.items) game.items = {};
    game.items[itemId] = (game.items[itemId] || 0) + 1;
    addLog(`🛒 集市买了${(ITEM_DATA[itemId] && ITEM_DATA[itemId].name) || itemId}`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderMarketPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function buyCrop(cropId, price) {
    if (game.money < price) { showToast('钱不够', 'bad'); return; }
    game.money -= price;
    game.crops[cropId] = (game.crops[cropId] || 0) + 1;
    addLog(`🛒 集市买了1斤${cropId}`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderMarketPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function sellMarketCrop(cropId, price) {
    if (!game.crops[cropId] || game.crops[cropId] <= 0) { showToast('没有库存', 'bad'); return; }
    game.crops[cropId]--;
    game.money += price;
    addLog(`💰 集市卖了1斤${cropId}，获得${price}元`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderMarketPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function renderAgriTechPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🔬 农业科技</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">科技是第一生产力。投资农业科技，一次投入永久受益。</p>';
    
    // 当前等级
    html += `<div class="shop-item"><div class="shop-item-info"><div class="shop-item-icon">🔬</div><div><div class="shop-item-name">当前科技等级</div><div class="shop-item-desc">Lv${game.agriTechLevel || 0} / ${AGRI_TECH_DATA.levels.length}</div></div></div></div>`;
    
    // 已激活的效果
    if (game.agriTechEffects && Object.keys(game.agriTechEffects).length > 0) {
        html += '<div class="shop-category">✅ 已激活效果</div>';
        for (const [effect, value] of Object.entries(game.agriTechEffects)) {
            const level = AGRI_TECH_DATA.levels.find(l => l.effect === effect);
            if (level) {
                html += `<div class="shop-item"><div class="shop-item-info"><div class="shop-item-icon">🔬</div><div><div class="shop-item-name">${level.name}</div><div class="shop-item-desc">${level.desc}</div></div></div></div>`;
            }
        }
    }
    
    // 可升级
    const nextLevel = AGRI_TECH_DATA.levels[game.agriTechLevel || 0];
    if (nextLevel) {
        html += '<div class="shop-category">⬆️ 下一级科技</div>';
        html += `
            <div class="shop-item">
                <div class="shop-item-info">
                    <div class="shop-item-icon">🔬</div>
                    <div>
                        <div class="shop-item-name">${nextLevel.name}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${nextLevel.desc}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">研发费用：${nextLevel.cost}元</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="shop-item-price">
                    <button class="buy-btn" onclick="upgradeAgriTech()" ${game.money < nextLevel.cost ? 'disabled' : ''}>💰 ${nextLevel.cost}元研发</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    } else {
        html += '<div class="shop-category">🏆 农业科技已满级</div>';
        html += '<div class="shop-item"><div class="shop-item-info"><div class="shop-item-icon">🏆</div><div><div class="shop-item-name">恭喜！</div><div class="shop-item-desc">你已经掌握了所有农业科技，成为农业专家！</div></div></div></div>';
    }
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

function upgradeAgriTech() {
    const nextLevel = AGRI_TECH_DATA.levels[game.agriTechLevel || 0];
    if (!nextLevel) return;
    if (game.money < nextLevel.cost) { showToast('资金不足', 'bad'); return; }
    
    game.money -= nextLevel.cost;
    if (!game.agriTechLevel) game.agriTechLevel = 0;
    if (!game.agriTechEffects) game.agriTechEffects = {};
    game.agriTechLevel++;
    
    // 激活效果（同名效果叠加）
    if (game.agriTechEffects[nextLevel.effect]) {
        game.agriTechEffects[nextLevel.effect] += nextLevel.value;
    } else {
        game.agriTechEffects[nextLevel.effect] = nextLevel.value;
    }
    
    addLog(`🎉 研发了${nextLevel.name}！${nextLevel.desc}`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderAgriTechPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function renderAnimalsPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🐷 畜牧养殖</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">养点畜生，积少成多。猪牛羊鸡鸭鹅，想养什么养什么。</p>';
    
    // 已养的动物
    for (const [animalKey, animals] of Object.entries(game.animals || {})) {
        if (animals.length === 0) continue;
        const data = ANIMAL_DATA[animalKey];
        if (!data) continue;
        
        html += `<div class="shop-category">${data.emoji} ${data.name}（${animals.length}只）</div>`;
        animals.forEach((animal, idx) => {
            const mature = animal.age >= data.growthDays;
            const ready = data.product && mature && animal.daysSinceProduct >= data.productDays;
            html += `
                <div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${data.emoji}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${animal.name}（${animal.age}天）</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">体重：${animal.weight}斤 ${mature ? '✅成年' : '成长中'}</div>
                            ${ready ? `<div style="color:#e67e22;">✅ 可收获${data.productName}</div>` : ''}
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="shop-item-price" style="display:flex;gap:6px;">
                        ${ready ? `<button class="buy-btn" onclick="harvestAnimalProduct('${animalKey}', ${idx})">收获${data.productEmoji}</button>` : ''}
                        <button class="buy-btn" onclick="sellAnimal('${animalKey}', ${idx})" ${!mature ? 'disabled' : ''}>出售</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        });
    }
    
    // 购买幼崽
    html += '<div class="shop-category">🛒 购买幼崽</div>';
    for (const [key, data] of Object.entries(ANIMAL_DATA)) {
        html += `
            <div class="shop-item">
                <div class="shop-item-info">
                    <div class="shop-item-icon">${data.emoji}</div>
                    <div>
                        <div class="shop-item-name">${data.name}幼崽</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">日耗粮：${Object.entries(data.dailyFeed).map(([k,v]) => v + '斤' + ({rice:'稻谷',wheat:'小麦',corn:'玉米',sweet:'红薯',potato:'土豆',peanut:'花生',pepper:'辣椒',cabbage:'白菜',radish:'萝卜',eggplant:'茄子',garlic:'大蒜'}[k]||k)).join('、')}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${data.growthDays}天成年，${data.sellPrice}元出售</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="shop-item-price">
                    <button class="buy-btn" onclick="buyAnimal('${key}')" ${game.money < data.buyCost ? 'disabled' : ''}>💰 ${data.buyCost}元购买</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }
    
    // 动物产品库存
    if (game.animalProducts && Object.keys(game.animalProducts).length > 0) {
        html += '<div class="shop-category">📦 动物产品</div>';
        const productNames = { milk: '牛奶', egg: '鸡蛋', duck_egg: '鸭蛋', goose_egg: '鹅蛋', wool: '羊毛' };
        const productEmojis = { milk: '🥛', egg: '🥚', duck_egg: '🥚', goose_egg: '🥚', wool: '🧶' };
        for (const [key, count] of Object.entries(game.animalProducts)) {
            if (count <= 0) continue;
            const price = key === 'milk' ? 8 : key === 'egg' ? 3 : key === 'duck_egg' ? 4 : key === 'goose_egg' ? 8 : 25;
            html += `
                <div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${productEmojis[key] || '📦'}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${productNames[key] || key}</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">库存：${count}个</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="shop-item-price">
                        <button class="buy-btn" onclick="sellAnimalProduct('${key}', ${count})">💰 全卖（${price}元/个）</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        }
    }
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderOrchardPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🌳 果园种植</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">果树种下去，年年有收成。一次种植，多年收获。</p>';
    
    // 已种植的果树
    if (game.orchard && game.orchard.length > 0) {
        html += '<div class="shop-category">🌳 已种植的果树</div>';
        game.orchard.forEach((tree, idx) => {
            const data = ORCHARD_DATA[tree.type];
            if (!data) return;
            html += `
                <div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${tree.mature ? data.emoji : '🌱'}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${data.name}（已种${tree.growDays}天）</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">${tree.mature ? (tree.ready ? '✅ 果实已成熟，可采摘' : '生长中，过几天可采摘') : '幼苗期，还需' + (data.growDays - tree.growDays) + '天成熟'}</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="shop-item-price">
                        ${tree.ready ? `<button class="buy-btn" onclick="harvestFruit(${idx})">🍎 采摘</button>` : ''}
                        <button class="buy-btn" onclick="removeTree(${idx})" style="background:#e74c3c;">🪓 砍伐</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        });
    }
    
    // 购买果树
    html += '<div class="shop-category">🌱 购买果树苗</div>';
    for (const [key, data] of Object.entries(ORCHARD_DATA)) {
        const seasonMatch = data.season === game.season;
        html += `
            <div class="shop-item">
                <div class="shop-item-info">
                    <div class="shop-item-icon">${data.emoji}</div>
                    <div>
                        <div class="shop-item-name">${data.name}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${data.desc}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${data.growDays}天成熟，每季${data.yield}斤果子</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${seasonMatch ? '✅ 当前季节适合种植' : '⚠️ 建议' + SEASON_NAMES[data.season] + '种植'}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="shop-item-price">
                    <button class="buy-btn" onclick="buyTree('${key}')" ${game.money < data.buyCost ? 'disabled' : ''}>💰 ${data.buyCost}元购买</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }
    
    // 水果库存
    if (game.fruits && Object.keys(game.fruits).length > 0) {
        html += '<div class="shop-category">🍎 水果库存</div>';
        for (const [key, count] of Object.entries(game.fruits)) {
            if (count <= 0) continue;
            const data = ORCHARD_DATA[key];
            if (!data) continue;
            html += `
                <div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${data.emoji}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${data.name}</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">库存：${count}斤</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="shop-item-price">
                        <button class="buy-btn" onclick="sellFruit('${key}', ${count})">💰 全卖（${data.fruitPrice}元/斤）</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        }
    }
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderVillagePanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🤝 村长合作</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">跟村长搞好关系，一起干大事。声望越高，能做的事越大。</p>';
    
    // 当前声望
    html += `<div class="shop-item"><div class="shop-item-info"><div class="shop-item-icon">⭐</div><div><div class="shop-item-name">当前声望</div><div class="shop-item-desc">${game.reputation} 点</div></div></div></div>`;
    
    // 已合作项目
    const activeProjects = Object.entries(game.villageProjects || {}).filter(([k, v]) => v > 0);
    if (activeProjects.length > 0) {
        html += '<div class="shop-category">✅ 已合作项目</div>';
        activeProjects.forEach(([key, level]) => {
            const project = VILLAGE_PROJECTS[key];
            if (!project) return;
            html += `
                <div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${project.emoji}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${project.name}（Lv${level}/${project.maxLevel}）</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">${project.levelDesc[level - 1] || project.desc}</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        });
    }
    
    // 可合作项目
    html += '<div class="shop-category">🏗️ 可合作项目</div>';
    for (const [key, project] of Object.entries(VILLAGE_PROJECTS)) {
        const currentLevel =(game.villageProjects && game.villageProjects[key]) || 0;
        if (currentLevel >= project.maxLevel) continue;
        
        const canAfford = game.money >= project.cost;
        const canReputation = game.reputation >= project.requireReputation;
        
        html += `
            <div class="shop-item ${canAfford && canReputation ? '' : 'locked'}">
                <div class="shop-item-info">
                    <div class="shop-item-icon">${project.emoji}</div>
                    <div>
                        <div class="shop-item-name">${project.name}（Lv${currentLevel + 1}/${project.maxLevel}）</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${project.desc}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">下一级：${project.levelDesc[currentLevel] || '完成'}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${!canAfford ? '❌ 资金不足' : ''} ${!canReputation ? '❌ 声望不足（需' + project.requireReputation + '）' : ''}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="shop-item-price">
                    <button class="buy-btn" onclick="investVillageProject('${key}')" ${!canAfford || !canReputation ? 'disabled' : ''}>💰 ${project.cost}元投资</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderFarmStayPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🏡 农家乐</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">利用自家产的食材招待客人，城里人就爱这一口农家味儿。</p>';
    
    const currentLevel =(game.farmStay && game.farmStay.level) || 0;
    
    // 当前等级
    if (currentLevel > 0) {
        const levelData = FARM_STAY_DATA.level[currentLevel - 1];
        html += `<div class="shop-category">🏡 当前：${levelData.emoji} ${levelData.name}</div>`;
        html += `<div class="shop-item"><div class="shop-item-info"><div class="shop-item-icon">${levelData.emoji}</div><div><div class="shop-item-name">${levelData.name}</div><div class="shop-item-desc">日收入：${levelData.dailyIncome}元/人，最多${levelData.maxGuests}人</div><div class="shop-item-desc">昨日接待：${(game.farmStay && game.farmStay.guests) || 0}人</div></div></div></div>`;
    } else {
        html += '<div class="shop-category">🏡 尚未开业</div>';
        html += '<div class="shop-item" style="opacity:0.6;"><div class="shop-item-info"><div class="shop-item-icon">🛖</div><div><div class="shop-item-name">茅草棚</div><div class="shop-item-desc">先从最简单的茅草棚开始</div></div></div></div>';
    }
    
    // 升级
    if (currentLevel < FARM_STAY_DATA.level.length) {
        const nextLevel = FARM_STAY_DATA.level[currentLevel];
        html += '<div class="shop-category">⬆️ 升级农家乐</div>';
        html += `
            <div class="shop-item">
                <div class="shop-item-info">
                    <div class="shop-item-icon">${nextLevel.emoji}</div>
                    <div>
                        <div class="shop-item-name">${nextLevel.name}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">${nextLevel.desc}</div>
                        <div class="shop-item-desc">日收入：${nextLevel.dailyIncome}元/人，最多${nextLevel.maxGuests}人</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="shop-item-price">
                    <button class="buy-btn" onclick="upgradeFarmStay()" ${game.money < nextLevel.cost ? 'disabled' : ''}>💰 ${nextLevel.cost}元升级</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }
    
    // 招牌菜
    if (currentLevel > 0) {
        html += '<div class="shop-category">🍽️ 招牌菜</div>';
        for (const [key, dish] of Object.entries(FARM_STAY_DATA.dishes)) {
            const made =(game.farmStayDishes && game.farmStayDishes[key]) || 0;
            // 检查原料是否充足
            let hasIngredients = true;
            for (const [ingredient, amount] of Object.entries(dish.cost)) {
                let have = 0;
                if (ingredient === 'fish') have =(game.items && game.items.fish) || 0;
                else if (ingredient === 'fruit') {
                    have = Object.values(game.fruits || {}).reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0);
                }
                else if (ingredient === 'riceWine') have =(game.processedItems && game.processedItems.riceWine) || 0;
                else if (ingredient === 'chicken') have = (game.animals && game.animals.chicken && game.animals.chicken.length) || 0;
                else if (ingredient === 'lamb') have = (game.animals && game.animals.sheep && game.animals.sheep.length) || 0;
                else have =(game.crops && game.crops[ingredient]) || 0;
                
                if (have < amount) { hasIngredients = false; break; }
            }
            
            html += `
                <div class="shop-item">
                    <div class="shop-item-info">
                        <div class="shop-item-icon">${dish.emoji}</div>
                        <div>
                            <div class="shop-item-name">${dish.name}（已做${made}份）</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">${dish.desc}</div>
                            <div class="shop-item-desc">原料：${Object.entries(dish.cost).map(([k,v]) => v + ({rice:'斤稻谷',fish:'条鱼',fruit:'斤水果',riceWine:'斤米酒',chicken:'只鸡',lamb:'只羊',vegetable:'斤蔬菜'}[k]||k)).join('、')}</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="shop-item-price">
                        <button class="buy-btn" onclick="makeDish('${key}')" ${!hasIngredients ? 'disabled' : ''}>🍳 制作（收入${dish.income}元）</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        }
    }
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

function investVillageProject(projectKey) {
    const project = VILLAGE_PROJECTS[projectKey];
    if (!project) return;
    if (game.money < project.cost) { showToast('资金不足', 'bad'); return; }
    if (game.reputation < project.requireReputation) { showToast('声望不足', 'bad'); return; }
    
    game.money -= project.cost;
    if (!game.villageProjects) game.villageProjects = {};
    game.villageProjects[projectKey] = (game.villageProjects[projectKey] || 0) + 1;
    
    // 某些项目有即时效果
    if (project.effect === 'fields' && projectKey === 'newLand') {
        const newFieldId = game.fields.length + 1;
        const levels = ['新手档', '进阶档', '精英档', '终极档'];
        const newLevel = levels[Math.min(newFieldId - 1, levels.length - 1)];
        game.fields.push({ id: newFieldId, level: newLevel, type: 'paddy', crop: null, stage: 'idle', step: 0, growProgress: 0, plantedDay: 0, lastWaterDay: 0, lastWeedDay: 0, fertilized: false, fertilizerType: null, turnedVine1: false, turnedVine2: false, prepared: false, yieldLoss: 0, yieldBonus: 0 });
        addLog(`🌾 开辟了新田地！现在有 ${game.fields.length} 块田了`, 'good');
    }
    if (project.effect === 'storageBonus') {
        game.storageCapacity = (game.storageCapacity || 2000) + (projectKey === 'idleWarehouse' ? 2000 : 0);
    }
    
    addLog(`🎉 投资了${project.emoji}${project.name}！声望+5`, 'good');
    game.reputation += 5;
    saveGame();
    renderVillagePanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function upgradeFarmStay() {
    const currentLevel =(game.farmStay && game.farmStay.level) || 0;
    if (currentLevel >= FARM_STAY_DATA.level.length) return;
    const nextLevel = FARM_STAY_DATA.level[currentLevel];
    if (game.money < nextLevel.cost) { showToast('资金不足', 'bad'); return; }
    
    game.money -= nextLevel.cost;
    if (!game.farmStay) game.farmStay = { level: 0, guests: 0, reputation: 0 };
    game.farmStay.level++;
    
    addLog(`🎉 农家乐升级到了${nextLevel.emoji}${nextLevel.name}！`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderFarmStayPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function makeDish(dishKey) {
    const dish = FARM_STAY_DATA.dishes[dishKey];
    if (!dish) return;
    
    // 检查并消耗原料
    for (const [ingredient, amount] of Object.entries(dish.cost)) {
        let have = 0;
        if (ingredient === 'fish') have =(game.items && game.items.fish) || 0;
        else if (ingredient === 'fruit') have = Object.values(game.fruits || {}).reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0);
        else if (ingredient === 'riceWine') have =(game.processedItems && game.processedItems.riceWine) || 0;
        else if (ingredient === 'chicken') have = (game.animals && game.animals.chicken && game.animals.chicken.length) || 0;
        else if (ingredient === 'lamb') have = (game.animals && game.animals.sheep && game.animals.sheep.length) || 0;
        else have =(game.crops && game.crops[ingredient]) || 0;
        
        if (have < amount) { showToast('原料不足', 'bad'); return; }
    }
    
    // 消耗原料
    for (const [ingredient, amount] of Object.entries(dish.cost)) {
        if (ingredient === 'fish') game.items.fish -= amount;
        else if (ingredient === 'fruit') {
            // 从库存中减去水果
            let remaining = amount;
            for (const [fType, fCount] of Object.entries(game.fruits || {})) {
                if (remaining <= 0) break;
                const take = Math.min(remaining, fCount);
                game.fruits[fType] -= take;
                remaining -= take;
            }
        }
        else if (ingredient === 'riceWine') game.processedItems.riceWine -= amount;
        else if (ingredient === 'chicken' && game.animals.chicken) game.animals.chicken.splice(0, amount);
        else if (ingredient === 'lamb' && game.animals.sheep) game.animals.sheep.splice(0, amount);
        else if (game.crops[ingredient]) game.crops[ingredient] -= amount;
    }
    
    if (!game.farmStayDishes) game.farmStayDishes = {};
    game.farmStayDishes[dishKey] = (game.farmStayDishes[dishKey] || 0) + 1;
    game.money += dish.income;
    
    addLog(`🍽️ 制作了${dish.emoji}${dish.name}，收入${dish.income}元！`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderFarmStayPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function buyAnimal(animalKey) {
    const data = ANIMAL_DATA[animalKey];
    if (!data) return;
    if (game.money < data.buyCost) { showToast('资金不足', 'bad'); return; }
    
    game.money -= data.buyCost;
    if (!game.animals) game.animals = {};
    if (!game.animals[animalKey]) game.animals[animalKey] = [];
    
    const animalName = data.name + (game.animals[animalKey].length + 1) + '号';
    game.animals[animalKey].push({ name: animalName, age: 0, weight: 5, daysSinceProduct: 0 });
    
    addLog(`🎉 买了${data.emoji}${animalName}，花了${data.buyCost}元`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderAnimalsPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function sellAnimal(animalKey, idx) {
    const data = ANIMAL_DATA[animalKey];
    if (!data || !game.animals[animalKey]) return;
    const animal = game.animals[animalKey][idx];
    if (!animal) return;
    
    const weightFactor = (animal.weight || 50) / 100;
    const price = Math.floor(data.sellPrice * weightFactor);
    game.money += price;
    game.animals[animalKey].splice(idx, 1);
    
    addLog(`💰 卖掉${data.emoji}${animal.name}，获得${price}元`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderAnimalsPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function harvestAnimalProduct(animalKey, idx) {
    const data = ANIMAL_DATA[animalKey];
    if (!data || !data.product) return;
    if (!game.animals[animalKey]) return;
    const animal = game.animals[animalKey][idx];
    if (!animal) return;
    
    animal.daysSinceProduct = 0;
    const amount = Math.floor(data.productPrice / 5) + 1;
    if (!game.animalProducts) game.animalProducts = {};
    game.animalProducts[data.product] = (game.animalProducts[data.product] || 0) + amount;
    
    addLog(`🎉 ${data.emoji}${animal.name} 产出${data.productName} ${amount}个`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderAnimalsPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function sellAnimalProduct(productKey, amount) {
    const prices = { milk: 8, egg: 3, duck_egg: 4, goose_egg: 8, wool: 25 };
    const names = { milk: '牛奶', egg: '鸡蛋', duck_egg: '鸭蛋', goose_egg: '鹅蛋', wool: '羊毛' };
    const emojis = { milk: '🥛', egg: '🥚', duck_egg: '🥚', goose_egg: '🥚', wool: '🧶' };
    
    if (!game.animalProducts || !game.animalProducts[productKey] || game.animalProducts[productKey] < amount) return;
    
    const price = prices[productKey] || 5;
    const money = price * amount;
    game.animalProducts[productKey] -= amount;
    game.money += money;
    
    addLog(`💰 卖掉${emojis[productKey] || '📦'}${amount}个${names[productKey] || productKey}，获得${money}元`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderAnimalsPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function buyTree(treeKey) {
    const data = ORCHARD_DATA[treeKey];
    if (!data) return;
    if (game.money < data.buyCost) { showToast('资金不足', 'bad'); return; }
    
    game.money -= data.buyCost;
    if (!game.orchard) game.orchard = [];
    game.orchard.push({ type: treeKey, growDays: 0, mature: false, ready: false, daysSinceHarvest: 0 });
    
    addLog(`🌱 买了${data.emoji}${data.name}，花了${data.buyCost}元`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderOrchardPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function harvestFruit(treeIdx) {
    if (!game.orchard || !game.orchard[treeIdx]) return;
    const tree = game.orchard[treeIdx];
    const data = ORCHARD_DATA[tree.type];
    if (!data || !tree.ready) return;
    
    tree.ready = false;
    tree.daysSinceHarvest = 0;
    if (!game.fruits) game.fruits = {};
    game.fruits[tree.type] = (game.fruits[tree.type] || 0) + data.yield;
    
    addLog(`🍎 ${data.name}收获了${data.yield}斤${data.emoji}，存入库中`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderOrchardPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function sellFruit(fruitKey, amount) {
    const data = ORCHARD_DATA[fruitKey];
    if (!data || !game.fruits || !game.fruits[fruitKey] || game.fruits[fruitKey] < amount) return;
    
    const money = data.fruitPrice * amount;
    game.fruits[fruitKey] -= amount;
    game.money += money;
    
    addLog(`💰 卖掉${data.emoji}${amount}斤${data.name}，获得${money}元`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    renderOrchardPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function removeTree(treeIdx) {
    if (!game.orchard || !game.orchard[treeIdx]) return;
    const tree = game.orchard[treeIdx];
    const data = ORCHARD_DATA[tree.type];
    if (!confirm(`确定要砍伐${data ? data.name : '这棵'}树吗？`)) return;
    game.orchard.splice(treeIdx, 1);
    addLog(`🪓 砍伐了${data ? data.emoji + data.name : '果树'}`, 'info');
    saveGame();
    renderOrchardPanel();
}

function renderLogPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    panel.innerHTML = `
        <div class="panel-title">📜 事件日志</div>
        <p style="color: #999; text-align: center; padding: 40px;">完整日志请查看底部滚动栏</p>
    `;
}

// ==================== 游戏操作 ====================

// 种植作物
// 整地
function prepareField(fieldIdx) {
    if (!game.fields || fieldIdx < 0 || fieldIdx >= game.fields.length) { showToast('操作失败', 'bad'); return; }
    const field = game.fields[fieldIdx];
    
    let staminaCost = 15;
    if (game.tools.includes('hoe')) {
        staminaCost *= 0.9; // 锄头：翻地体力-10%
    }
    if (game.neighborHelp && game.neighborHelp.toolShare) {
        staminaCost *= 0.85;
    }
    staminaCost = Math.floor(staminaCost);
    
    if (game.stamina < staminaCost) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playDirtSound();
    game.stamina -= staminaCost;
    field.prepared = true;
    
    // 增加田间管理经验
    addSkillExp('fieldManagement', 2);
    
    addLog(`⛏️ 给第${field.id}块田整了地。你弯着腰，一锄头一锄头地翻着地。泥土翻过来，带着潮湿的腥气。嗯，这块地肥得很。`, 'good');
    
    // 检查任务
    if (!game.quests.q0) {
        game.quests.q0 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q0', 0, '✅ 任务完成：整地');
    }
    
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    showToast('整地完成！', 'good');
}

// 种植（播种/育苗）
function plantCrop(fieldIdx, cropKey) {
    if (!game.fields || fieldIdx < 0 || fieldIdx >= game.fields.length) { showToast('操作失败', 'bad'); return; }
    const field = game.fields[fieldIdx];
    const cropData = CROP_DATA[cropKey];
    
    if (!field.prepared) {
        showToast('需要先整地！', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.seeds[cropKey] < 1) {
        showToast('种子不足！', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.stamina < 12) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playDirtSound();
    // 消耗种子和体力
    game.seeds[cropKey]--;
    game.stamina -= 12;
    field.crop = cropKey;
    field.stage = 'seedling';
    field.step = 1;
    field.growProgress = 0;
    field.plantedDay = game.day;
    field.lastWaterDay = game.day;
    field.lastWeedDay = game.day;
    
    // 增加作物熟悉度经验
    addSkillExp('cropFamiliarity', 3);  // 从5减到3，保持比例
    field.fertilized = false;
    field.turnedVine1 = false;
    field.turnedVine2 = false;
    field.yieldBonus = 0;
    field.yieldLoss = 0;
    
    // 随机种植文案
    const plantFlavors = cropData.type === 'rice'
        ? [
            '你把种子均匀撒在秧田里，盖上一层薄土。再过几天，就能看到嫩绿的小苗了。',
            '一粒粒稻种埋进土里，等待它们发芽的那一天。',
            '播下种子，也播下了这一季的期盼。',
            '秧田整理好了，种子也种下了，接下来就是等待。',
            '看着整齐的田垄，想象着丰收的样子。',
            '春天播下一粒种，秋天收获万颗粮。'
          ]
        : [
            '你把薯块埋进土里，浇了点水。希望它们能顺利发芽。',
            '一个个薯块躺进土里，就像睡着了一样。',
            '种下红薯，也种下了甜甜的希望。',
            '土地翻好了，薯块也种下了，等着它们生根发芽。',
            '红薯的生命力很强，一定能长得很好。',
            '看着整齐的田垄，想象着红薯丰收的样子。'
          ];
    const flavorText = plantFlavors[Math.floor(Math.random() * plantFlavors.length)];
    
    addLog(`🌱 在第${field.id}块田种下了${cropData.name}。${flavorText}`, 'good');
    
    // 检查任务
    if (cropKey === 'rice_spring' && !game.quests.q2) {
        game.quests.q2 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q2', 50, '✅ 任务完成：育苗，奖励50元');
    }
    
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    showToast(`种下了${cropData.name}！`, 'good');
}

// 移栽
function transplantCrop(fieldIdx) {
    if (!game.fields || fieldIdx < 0 || fieldIdx >= game.fields.length) { showToast('操作失败', 'bad'); return; }
    const field = game.fields[fieldIdx];
    const cropData = CROP_DATA[field.crop];
    
    let staminaCost = 18;
    if (game.tools.includes('seedlingRider')) {
        staminaCost *= 0.4; // 秧马：移栽体力-60%
    }
    staminaCost = Math.floor(staminaCost);
    
    if (game.stamina < staminaCost) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playDirtSound();
    game.stamina -= staminaCost;
    field.stage = 'transplanting';
    field.step = 2;
    field.growProgress = 20;
    
    const flavorText = cropData.type === 'rice'
        ? '你弓着腰，把秧苗一棵一棵插进水里。腰酸背痛，但看着整整齐齐的秧苗，心里很踏实。'
        : '小苗已经站稳了脚跟，开始长出新的叶子。';
    
    addLog(`🌱 完成了${cropData.name}的移栽。${flavorText}`, 'good');
    
    // 检查任务
    if (!game.quests.q3) {
        game.quests.q3 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q3', 50, '✅ 任务完成：移栽，奖励50元');
    }
    
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    showToast('移栽完成！', 'good');
}

// 浇水
function waterField(fieldIdx) {
    if (!game.fields || fieldIdx < 0 || fieldIdx >= game.fields.length) { showToast('操作失败', 'bad'); return; }
    const field = game.fields[fieldIdx];
    // 每天只能浇一次水
    if (field.lastWaterDay === game.day) {
        showToast('今天已经浇过水了！', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    // 农具精通减少体力消耗（每级-3%）
    const toolSkillLevel =(game.skills.toolMastery && game.skills.toolMastery.level) || 0;
    let waterCost = Math.floor(8 * (1 - toolSkillLevel * 0.03));
    
    // 大柱NPC好感度减少浇水体力消耗
    const npcWaterBonus = (typeof getNpcBonus === 'function') ? getNpcBonus('waterStaminaReduce') : 0;
    if (npcWaterBonus > 0) {
