        waterCost = Math.floor(waterCost * (1 - npcWaterBonus));
    }
    
    if (game.stamina < waterCost) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    playWaterSound();
    game.stamina -= waterCost;
    field.lastWaterDay = game.day;
    
    // 浇水增加微量产量，科技加成
    const waterBaseBonus = 0.01; // 基础浇水增产1%
    const waterTechBonus = getTechBonus('waterBonus');
    field.yieldBonus = (field.yieldBonus || 0) + waterBaseBonus + waterTechBonus;
    
    // 增加田间管理经验
    addSkillExp('fieldManagement', 2);
    
    addLog(`💧 给第${field.id}块田浇了水。禾苗喝饱了水，看起来更精神了。`, 'info');
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    showToast('浇水完成！', 'good');
}

// 除草
function weedField(fieldIdx) {
    if (!game.fields || fieldIdx < 0 || fieldIdx >= game.fields.length) { showToast('操作失败', 'bad'); return; }
    const field = game.fields[fieldIdx];
    // 每3天才能除一次草
    const daysSinceWeed = game.day - field.lastWeedDay;
    if (daysSinceWeed < 3) {
        showToast(`还要${3 - daysSinceWeed}天才能再除草！`, 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    // 农具精通减少体力消耗（每级-3%）
    const toolSkillLevelWeed =(game.skills.toolMastery && game.skills.toolMastery.level) || 0;
    const weedCost = Math.floor(15 * (1 - toolSkillLevelWeed * 0.03));
    
    if (game.stamina < weedCost) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    playWeedSound();
    game.stamina -= weedCost;
    field.lastWeedDay = game.day;
    
    // 增加田间管理经验
    addSkillExp('fieldManagement', 3);
    
    addLog(`🌿 给第${field.id}块田除了草。${getRandomFlavor('weed')}`, 'info');
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    showToast('除草完成！', 'good');
}

// 施肥
function fertilizeField(fieldIdx, type = 'normal') {
    if (!game.fields || fieldIdx < 0 || fieldIdx >= game.fields.length) { showToast('操作失败', 'bad'); return; }
    const field = game.fields[fieldIdx];
    
    if (field.fertilized) {
        showToast('已经施过肥了！', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    let staminaCost = 10;
    if (game.tools.includes('fertilizerCart')) {
        staminaCost *= 0.6; // 施肥车：施肥体力-40%
    }
    
    // 陈阳NPC好感度减少施肥体力消耗
    const npcFertilizeBonus = (typeof getNpcBonus === 'function') ? getNpcBonus('fertilizeStaminaReduce') : 0;
    if (npcFertilizeBonus > 0) {
        staminaCost = Math.floor(staminaCost * (1 - npcFertilizeBonus));
    }
    
    staminaCost = Math.floor(staminaCost);
    
    if (game.stamina < staminaCost) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    if (type === 'organic') {
        // 有机肥
        if ((game.items.organicFertilizer || 0) < 1) {
            showToast('有机肥不足！', 'bad');
            playErrorSound();
            return;
        }
        playFertilizerSound();
        game.stamina -= staminaCost;
        game.items.organicFertilizer--;
        field.fertilized = true;
        field.fertilizerType = 'organic';
        addLog(`💩 给第${field.id}块田施了有机肥。纯天然的肥料，庄稼肯定能长得更好。`, 'good');
    } else {
        // 普通化肥
        if (game.items.fertilizer < 1) {
            showToast('化肥不足！', 'bad');
            playErrorSound();
            return;
        }
        playFertilizerSound();
        game.stamina -= staminaCost;
        game.items.fertilizer--;
        field.fertilized = true;
        field.fertilizerType = 'normal';
        addLog(`🧪 给第${field.id}块田施了肥。有了肥料，庄稼肯定能长得更好。`, 'info');
    }
    
    // 增加田间管理经验
    addSkillExp('fieldManagement', 2);
    
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    showToast('施肥完成！', 'good');
}

// 翻藤（红薯专属）
function turnVine(fieldIdx, turnNum) {
    if (!game.fields || fieldIdx < 0 || fieldIdx >= game.fields.length) { showToast('操作失败', 'bad'); return; }
    const field = game.fields[fieldIdx];
    if (game.stamina < 13) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    playWeedSound();
    game.stamina -= 13;
    
    if (turnNum === 1) {
        field.turnedVine1 = true;
        addLog(`🍃 给第${field.id}块田的红薯翻了第一次藤。红薯藤乱爬，翻一翻能让养分都集中到块根上。`, 'info');
    } else {
        field.turnedVine2 = true;
        addLog(`🍃 给第${field.id}块田的红薯翻了第二次藤。看着满地的藤蔓，想象着下面藏着的大红薯，心里美滋滋的。`, 'info');
    }
    
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    showToast('翻藤完成！', 'good');
}

// 收割
function harvestCrop(fieldIdx) {
    if (!game.fields || fieldIdx < 0 || fieldIdx >= game.fields.length) { showToast('操作失败', 'bad'); return; }
    const field = game.fields[fieldIdx];
    if (!field.crop) return;
    
    const cropData = CROP_DATA[field.crop];
    
    let staminaCost = 20;
    if (game.tools.includes('sickle')) {
        staminaCost *= 0.9; // 镰刀：收割体力-10%
    }
    
    // 农具精通减少体力消耗（每级-3%）
    const toolSkillLevelHarvest =(game.skills.toolMastery && game.skills.toolMastery.level) || 0;
    staminaCost *= (1 - toolSkillLevelHarvest * 0.03);
    staminaCost = Math.floor(staminaCost);
    
    if (game.stamina < staminaCost) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playHarvestSound();
    game.stamina -= staminaCost;
    
    // 计算产量
    let yield_ = cropData.baseYield;
    
    // 田地档位加成
    const levelBonus = { '新手档': 1.0, '进阶档': 1.15, '精英档': 1.35, '终极档': 1.6 };
    yield_ *= levelBonus[field.level] || 1.0;
    
    // 作物熟悉度加成（每级+3%）
    const cropSkillLevel =(game.skills.cropFamiliarity && game.skills.cropFamiliarity.level) || 0;
    if (cropSkillLevel > 0) {
        const cropBonus = 1 + cropSkillLevel * 0.03;
        yield_ *= cropBonus;
    }
    
    // 科技产量加成
    const techYieldBonus = getTechBonus('yieldBonus');
    if (techYieldBonus > 0) {
        yield_ *= (1 + techYieldBonus);
    }
    
    // 施肥加成
    if (field.fertilized) {
        if (field.fertilizerType === 'organic') {
            yield_ *= 1.08; // 有机肥+8%
        } else {
            yield_ *= 1.05; // 普通化肥+5%
        }
    }
    
    // 除草加成（如果最近除过草）
    const daysSinceWeed = game.day - field.lastWeedDay;
    if (daysSinceWeed < 7) yield_ *= 1.08;  // 从10天5%改成7天8%，更频繁更有价值
    
    // 浇水加成
    const daysSinceWater = game.day - field.lastWaterDay;
    if (daysSinceWater < 3) yield_ *= 1.05;  // 从5天3%改成3天5%，更频繁更有价值
    
    // 红薯翻藤加成
    if (cropData.type === 'sweet') {
        if (field.turnedVine1) yield_ *= 1.05;
        if (field.turnedVine2) yield_ *= 1.05;
    }
    
    // 事件增产/减产（确保减产不会超过90%）
    if (field.yieldBonus) yield_ *= (1 + field.yieldBonus);
    if (field.yieldLoss) yield_ *= Math.max(0.1, 1 - field.yieldLoss);
    
    // 下一季加成（瑞雪兆丰年）
    if (game.currentSeasonBonus) yield_ *= (1 + game.currentSeasonBonus);
    
    // 邻里互助：收获加成
    if (game.neighborHelp && game.neighborHelp.harvestHelp) {
        yield_ *= 1.1;
        addLog('🌾 邻居来帮你收庄稼，产量增加了10%', 'good');
    }
    
    // 随机波动 ±10%
    yield_ *= (0.9 + Math.random() * 0.2);
    
    yield_ = Math.max(0, Math.floor(yield_));
    
    yield_ = Math.max(0, Math.floor(yield_));
    
    // 入库（检查仓库容量限制）
    const storageCap = game.storageCapacity || 2000;
    const currentStorage = Object.values(game.crops || {}).reduce((sum, v) => sum + (v || 0), 0);
    let actualYield = yield_;
    
    if (currentStorage + yield_ > storageCap) {
        actualYield = Math.max(0, storageCap - currentStorage);
        const discarded = yield_ - actualYield;
        if (discarded > 0) {
            addLog(`📦 仓库满了！${discarded}斤${cropData.name}就地处理（喂鸡/堆肥），损失了`, 'bad');
        }
    }
    
    if (cropData.type === 'rice') {
        game.crops.rice = Math.max(0, (game.crops.rice || 0) + actualYield);
    } else if (cropData.type === 'sweet') {
        game.crops.sweet = Math.max(0, (game.crops.sweet || 0) + actualYield);
    } else if (cropData.type === 'wheat') {
        game.crops.wheat = Math.max(0, (game.crops.wheat || 0) + actualYield);
    } else if (cropData.type === 'corn') {
        game.crops.corn = Math.max(0, (game.crops.corn || 0) + actualYield);
    } else if (cropData.type === 'soybean') {
        game.crops.soybean = Math.max(0, (game.crops.soybean || 0) + actualYield);
    } else if (cropData.type === 'potato') {
        game.crops.potato = (game.crops.potato || 0) + actualYield;
    } else if (cropData.type === 'peanut') {
        game.crops.peanut = (game.crops.peanut || 0) + actualYield;
    } else if (cropData.type === 'pepper') {
        game.crops.pepper = (game.crops.pepper || 0) + actualYield;
    } else if (cropData.type === 'cabbage') {
        game.crops.cabbage = (game.crops.cabbage || 0) + actualYield;
    } else if (cropData.type === 'radish') {
        game.crops.radish = (game.crops.radish || 0) + actualYield;
    } else if (cropData.type === 'eggplant') {
        game.crops.eggplant = (game.crops.eggplant || 0) + actualYield;
    } else if (cropData.type === 'garlic') {
        game.crops.garlic = (game.crops.garlic || 0) + actualYield;
    }
    
    // 解锁图鉴
    unlockCollectionItem('crops', cropData.type);
    
    // 累计收获统计
    if (!game.stats) game.stats = {};
    game.stats.totalHarvest = (game.stats.totalHarvest || 0) + yield_;
    
    // 增加作物熟悉度经验
    // 作物熟悉度经验（加上NPC加成）
    let cropExp = 6;  // 从10减到6，因为收获更频繁了
    const npcCropExpBonus = getNpcBonus('cropExpGain');
    if (npcCropExpBonus > 0) {
        cropExp = Math.floor(cropExp * (1 + npcCropExpBonus));
    }
    addSkillExp('cropFamiliarity', cropExp);
    
    // 获得研究点（每100斤获得1点）
    const rpGain = Math.floor(yield_ / 100);
    if (rpGain > 0) {
        game.researchPoints += rpGain;
    }
    
    playHarvestSound();
    
    // 重置田地
    field.crop = null;
    field.stage = 'idle';
    field.step = 0;
    field.growProgress = 0;
    field.prepared = false;
    field.fertilized = false;
    field.fertilizerType = null;
    field.turnedVine1 = false;
    field.turnedVine2 = false;
    field.yieldLoss = 0;
    field.yieldBonus = 0;
    
    // 随机收获文案
    const harvestFlavors = cropData.type === 'rice'
        ? [
            '镰刀挥下去，稻穗刷刷地倒。阳光洒在金黄的稻穗上，这就是丰收的味道。',
            '金黄的稻穗在风中摇曳，这是最美的风景。',
            '看着满仓的粮食，所有的辛苦都值得了。',
            '今年的收成真不错，够吃好一阵子了。',
            '稻子熟了，空气里都弥漫着稻香。'
          ]
        : [
            '一锄头下去，红薯滚了出来，一个比一个大。看着堆成小山的红薯，心里满满的成就感。',
            '红薯藏在土里，就像一个个宝藏。',
            '今年的红薯长得真好，又大又甜。',
            '挖红薯的乐趣，只有挖过的人才懂。',
            '看着一筐筐的红薯，心里乐开了花。'
          ];
    const flavorText = harvestFlavors[Math.floor(Math.random() * harvestFlavors.length)];
    
    addLog(`🌾 收割了${cropData.name}，收获${yield_}斤！${flavorText}`, 'good');
    
    // 检查任务
    if (!game.quests.q4) {
        game.quests.q4 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q4', 200, '✅ 任务完成：第一次收割，奖励200元');
    }
    
    // 检查里程碑
    if (typeof checkMilestones === 'function') {
        checkMilestones();
    }
    
    checkAchievements();
    
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    showToast(`收获${yield_}斤${cropData.name}！`, 'good');
}

// 出售作物
function sellCrop(cropKey, amount) {
    const owned = game.crops[cropKey] || 0;
    if (owned < 1) {
        showToast('没有可出售的作物！', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    const price = getSeasonPrice(cropKey);
    let sellAmount = amount === 'all' ? owned : Math.min(amount, owned);
    // 应用售卖价格加成
    // 应用售卖价格加成（事件 + NPC好感度）
    let sellBonusTotal = game.sellBonus || 0;
    const npcSellBonus = getNpcBonus('sellPrice');
    if (npcSellBonus > 0) {
        sellBonusTotal += npcSellBonus;
    }
    const finalPrice = price * (1 + sellBonusTotal);
    let money = Math.floor(sellAmount * finalPrice);
    
    game.crops[cropKey] -= sellAmount;
    game.money += money;
    
    // 累计售卖统计
    if (!game.stats) game.stats = {};
    game.stats.totalSell = (game.stats.totalSell || 0) + money;
    game.stats.totalEarned = (game.stats.totalEarned || 0) + money;
    
    playCoinSound();
    
    const names = { rice: '水稻', sweet: '红薯', wheat: '小麦', corn: '玉米', soybean: '大豆', potato: '土豆', peanut: '花生', pepper: '辣椒', cabbage: '白菜', radish: '萝卜', eggplant: '茄子', garlic: '大蒜' };
    // 随机售卖文案
    const sellFlavors = [
        '把粮食拉到镇上卖了，换回了白花花的银子。',
        '粮商竖起大拇指，说今年的米质量真好。',
        '数着手里的钱，心里盘算着下次买什么种子。',
        '辛辛苦苦大半年，终于见到回头钱了。',
        '卖完粮，口袋鼓鼓的，走路都带风。',
        '今年的价钱还不错，心里乐开了花。'
    ];
    const flavorText = sellFlavors[Math.floor(Math.random() * sellFlavors.length)];
    addLog(`💰 出售了${sellAmount}kg ${names[cropKey]}，获得${money}元。${flavorText}`, 'good');
    
    // 检查任务
    if (!game.quests.q5) {
        game.quests.q5 = true;
        let repGain = 10;
        if (game.reputationBonus) {
            repGain = Math.floor(repGain * (1 + game.reputationBonus));
        }
        game.reputation += repGain;
        queueQuestReward('q5', 100, `✅ 任务完成：第一桶金，奖励100元+${repGain}声望`, repGain);
    }
    
    // 任务检查：声望达到100
    if (!game.quests.q17 && game.reputation >= 100) {
        game.quests.q17 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q17', 500, '✅ 任务完成：德高望重，奖励500元');
    }
    
    // 任务检查：总资产达到5000（粗略计算：元+库存价值）
    if (!game.quests.q16) {
        const riceValue = (game.crops.rice || 0) * 2.5;
        const sweetValue = (game.crops.sweet || 0) * 1.5;
        const totalAssets = game.money + riceValue + sweetValue;
        if (totalAssets >= 5000) {
            game.quests.q16 = true;
            queueQuestReward('q16', 500, '✅ 任务完成：小有积蓄，奖励500元');
        }
    }
    
    saveGame();
    checkAchievements();
    // 只刷新商店内容，不切换页面
    if (currentMainTab === 'shop') {
        refreshShopContent();
    }
    updateTopBar();
    showToast(`+${money}元`, 'good');
}

// 购买种子
function buySeed(seedKey) {
    const cropData = CROP_DATA[seedKey];
    const actualSeedPrice = getSeedPrice(cropData.seedPrice);
    if (game.money < actualSeedPrice) {
        showToast('钱包里钱不够，先去卖点东西换点钱', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    game.money -= actualSeedPrice;
    game.seeds[seedKey] = (game.seeds[seedKey] || 0) + 1;
    
    playCoinSound();
    
    addLog(`🌱 购买了${cropData.name}种子 1亩`, 'info');
    
    // 检查任务
    if (seedKey === 'rice_spring' && !game.quests.q1) {
        game.quests.q1 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q1', 100, '✅ 任务完成：第一粒种子，奖励100元');
    }
    
    saveGame();
    if (currentMainTab === 'shop') {
        refreshShopContent();
    }
    updateTopBar();
    showToast(`购买成功！`, 'good');
}

// 购买道具
function buyItem(itemKey) {
    const prices = {
        fertilizer: 50, pesticide: 80, bun: 20, medicine: 100,
        snack: 10, liquor: 50, cloth: 30, sugar: 40, cigarette: 60
    };
    const names = {
        fertilizer: '化肥', pesticide: '农药', bun: '肉包子', medicine: '感冒药',
        snack: '粗点心', liquor: '散装白酒', cloth: '花布头', sugar: '红糖', cigarette: '香烟'
    };
    
    const price = prices[itemKey];
    // 社区建设加成（村卫生站：药品购买半价）
    let finalPrice = price;
    if (itemKey === 'medicine' && game.medicineDiscount) {
        finalPrice = Math.floor(price * (1 - game.medicineDiscount));
    }
    if (game.money < finalPrice) {
        showToast('钱包里钱不够，先去卖点东西换点钱', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playCoinSound();
    game.money -= finalPrice;
    game.items[itemKey] = (game.items[itemKey] || 0) + 1;
    
    addLog(`🛒 购买了${names[itemKey]}`, 'info');
    saveGame();
    if (currentMainTab === 'shop') {
        refreshShopContent();
    }
    updateTopBar();
    showToast(`购买成功！`, 'good');
}

// 购买农具
function buyTool(toolKey) {
    const tool = TOOL_DATA[toolKey];
    if (!tool) return;
    
    if (game.tools.includes(toolKey)) {
        showToast('已经拥有了！', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.money < tool.price) {
        showToast('钱包里钱不够，先去卖点东西换点钱', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playCoinSound();
    game.money -= tool.price;
    game.tools.push(toolKey);
    
    // 任务检查：购买第一把农具
    if (!game.quests.q6) {
        game.quests.q6 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q6', 100, '✅ 任务完成：第一把农具，奖励100元');
    }
    
    addLog(`🔧 购买了${tool.name}！${tool.effect}`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    if (currentMainTab === 'tools') {
        renderToolsPanel();
    }
    updateTopBar();
    showToast(`购买成功！`, 'good');
}

// 开始堆肥
function startCompost() {
    if (game.composting) {
        showToast('已经有堆肥在制作了！', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    if (game.money < 100) {
        showToast('钱包里钱不够，先去卖点东西换点钱', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playDirtSound();
    game.money -= 100;
    game.composting = true;
    game.compostStartTotalDay = game.totalDay || game.day;
    game.compostStartDay = game.day; // 保留兼容旧存档
    
    // 堆肥需要花时间准备材料（1小时）
    game.time += 1;
    
    // 任务检查：制作第一份堆肥
    if (!game.quests.q8) {
        game.quests.q8 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q8', 150, '✅ 任务完成：第一份堆肥，奖励150元');
    }
    
    addLog('🌱 忙活了一个钟头，把堆肥的材料都备好了，等3天后来收。', 'info');
    checkAchievements();
    saveGame();
    if (currentMainTab === 'compost') {
        renderCompostPanel();
    }
    updateTopBar();
    showToast('开始堆肥！', 'good');
}

// 收获堆肥
function harvestCompost() {
    if (!game.composting) {
        showToast('没有堆肥可以收获！', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    const startDay = game.compostStartTotalDay || game.compostStartDay || game.day;
    const elapsed = (game.totalDay || game.day) - startDay;
    if (elapsed < 3) {
        showToast('还没做好呢！', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playHarvestSound();
    game.composting = false;
    game.items.organicFertilizer = (game.items.organicFertilizer || 0) + 3;
    
    // 增加堆肥经验
    addSkillExp('composting', 10);
    
    addLog('💩 堆肥做好了！收获了3份有机肥。', 'good');
    saveGame();
    if (currentMainTab === 'compost') {
        renderCompostPanel();
    }
    updateTopBar();
    showToast('收获有机肥！', 'good');
}

function roundGameState() {
    if (!game) return;
    // 防止浮点数累积
    game.money = Math.round(game.money * 10) / 10;
    game.stamina = Math.round(game.stamina * 10) / 10;
    game.health = Math.round(game.health * 10) / 10;
    game.reputation = Math.round(game.reputation * 10) / 10;
    if (game.crops.rice !== undefined) game.crops.rice = Math.round(game.crops.rice * 10) / 10;
    if (game.crops.sweet !== undefined) game.crops.sweet = Math.round(game.crops.sweet * 10) / 10;
    game.fields.forEach(f => {
        if (f.yieldBonus !== undefined) f.yieldBonus = Math.round(f.yieldBonus * 1000) / 1000;
        if (f.yieldLoss !== undefined) f.yieldLoss = Math.round(f.yieldLoss * 1000) / 1000;
    });
}

// 只更新顶部状态栏，不重新渲染面板
function updateTopBar() {
    if (!game) return;
    document.getElementById('stat-money').textContent = Math.floor(game.money);
    document.getElementById('stat-stamina').textContent = Math.floor(game.stamina);
    document.getElementById('stat-max-stamina').textContent = game.maxStamina;
    document.getElementById('stat-health').textContent = Math.floor(game.health);
    document.getElementById('stat-max-health').textContent = game.maxHealth;
    document.getElementById('stat-rice').textContent = Math.floor(game.crops.rice);
    document.getElementById('stat-sweet').textContent = Math.floor(game.crops.sweet);
    document.getElementById('stat-wheat').textContent = Math.floor(game.crops.wheat || 0);
    document.getElementById('stat-corn').textContent = Math.floor(game.crops.corn || 0);
    document.getElementById('stat-soybean').textContent = Math.floor(game.crops.soybean || 0);
    document.getElementById('stat-day').textContent = game.totalDay || game.day;
    document.getElementById('stat-season').textContent = SEASON_NAMES[game.season];
    document.getElementById('season-icon').textContent = SEASON_ICONS[game.season];
    const wData = WEATHER_DATA[game.weather] || WEATHER_DATA.sunny;
    document.getElementById('stat-weather').textContent = wData.name;
    document.getElementById('weather-icon').textContent = wData.emoji;
}

// 租用新田地
function rentNewField() {
    const rent = getNextFieldRent();
    if (game.money < rent) {
        showToast('钱包里钱不够，先去卖点东西换点钱', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    game.money -= rent;
    game.fields.push({
        id: game.fields.length + 1,
        level: '新手档',
        type: 'paddy',
        crop: null,
        stage: 'idle',
        step: 0,
        growProgress: 0,
        plantedDay: 0,
        lastWaterDay: 0,
        lastWeedDay: 0,
        fertilized: false,
        fertilizerType: null,
        turnedVine1: false,
        turnedVine2: false,
        prepared: false,
        yieldLoss: 0,
        yieldBonus: 0
    });
    
    // 任务检查：租下第二块田
    if (game.fields.length === 2 && !game.quests.q13) {
        game.quests.q13 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q13', 300, '✅ 任务完成：扩大生产，奖励300元');
    }
    // 任务检查：租下第三块田
    if (game.fields.length === 3 && !game.quests.q32) {
        game.quests.q32 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q32', 400, '✅ 任务完成：阡陌纵横，奖励400元');
    }
    // 任务检查：租下第四块田
    if (game.fields.length === 4 && !game.quests.q33) {
        game.quests.q33 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q33', 500, '✅ 任务完成：阡陌四野，奖励500元');
    }
    
    // 每扩一块地，仓库容量+1000斤
    const oldCap = game.storageCapacity || 2000;
    game.storageCapacity = oldCap + 1000;
    addLog(`🔓 租用了第${game.fields.length}块田！仓库容量+1000斤（${oldCap}→${game.storageCapacity}）`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    showToast('新田地已解锁！', 'good');
}

function getNextFieldRent() {
    const baseRent = 200;
    const n = game.fields.length + 1;
    return Math.floor(baseRent * Math.pow(1.18, n - 1));
}

// 扩建仓库（独立功能）
function expandStorage() {
    const cost = 500;
    if (game.money < cost) {
        showToast('钱不够，扩建需要500元', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    game.money -= cost;
    const oldCap = game.storageCapacity || 3000;
    game.storageCapacity = oldCap + 1000;
    
    // 任务检查：仓库扩建到5000斤以上
    if (game.storageCapacity >= 5000 && !game.quests.q31) {
        game.quests.q31 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q31', 300, '✅ 任务完成：仓廪充实，奖励300元');
    }
    
    addLog(`🔨 扩建了仓库！容量+1000斤（${oldCap}→${game.storageCapacity}）`, 'good');
    playSound('build');
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    if (currentMainTab === 'buildings') {
        renderBuildingPanel();
    } else if (currentMainTab === 'tech') {
        renderTechPanel();
    }
    showToast(`仓库扩建完成！当前容量${game.storageCapacity}斤`, 'good');
}

// ==================== 辅助函数 ====================

function getSeasonPrice(cropKey) {
    // 基础价格
    const basePrices = { rice: 3.0, sweet: 1.5, fish: 3.5, wheat: 2.5, corn: 2.0, soybean: 2.8, potato: 2.0, peanut: 3.0, pepper: 2.0, cabbage: 1.0, radish: 1.0, eggplant: 2.0, garlic: 2.0 };
    let price = basePrices[cropKey] || 1;
    
    // 季节波动
    const fluctuations = {
        rice: { spring: 1.1, summer: 1.0, autumn: 0.85, winter: 1.05 },
        sweet: { spring: 1.0, summer: 1.0, autumn: 0.9, winter: 1.25 },
        fish: { spring: 1.15, summer: 1.1, autumn: 0.9, winter: 0.7 },
        wheat: { spring: 1.05, summer: 0.9, autumn: 1.15, winter: 1.0 },
        corn: { spring: 1.0, summer: 1.1, autumn: 1.2, winter: 0.85 },
        soybean: { spring: 1.1, summer: 1.05, autumn: 0.95, winter: 1.15 },
        potato: { spring: 1.1, summer: 1.0, autumn: 1.0, winter: 1.0 },
        peanut: { spring: 1.0, summer: 1.1, autumn: 1.2, winter: 0.9 },
        pepper: { spring: 1.0, summer: 1.2, autumn: 1.1, winter: 0.8 },
        cabbage: { spring: 1.0, summer: 0.9, autumn: 1.1, winter: 1.2 },
        radish: { spring: 1.05, summer: 1.0, autumn: 1.15, winter: 1.1 },
        eggplant: { spring: 1.1, summer: 1.2, autumn: 0.9, winter: 0.8 },
        garlic: { spring: 1.2, summer: 0.9, autumn: 1.0, winter: 1.1 }
    };
    
    if (fluctuations[cropKey] && fluctuations[cropKey][game.season]) {
        price *= fluctuations[cropKey][game.season];
    }
    
    return Math.round(price * 100) / 100;
}

function getHouseStaminaRegen() {
    const house = HOUSE_DATA[game.house];
    return house ? house.staminaRegen : 15;
}

// 升级房屋
function upgradeHouse(targetHouse) {
    const houseOrder = ['新手房', '进阶房', '精英房', '终极房'];
    const currentIndex = houseOrder.indexOf(game.house);
    const targetIndex = houseOrder.indexOf(targetHouse);
    
    // 只能升级下一级
    if (targetIndex !== currentIndex + 1) {
        showToast('只能升级下一级房屋！', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    const houseData = HOUSE_DATA[targetHouse];
    if (game.money < houseData.upgradeCost) {
        showToast('钱包里钱不够，先去卖点东西换点钱', 'bad');
        playErrorSound();
        return;
    }
    
    playCoinSound();
    game.money -= houseData.upgradeCost;
    game.house = targetHouse;
    
    // 任务检查：升级到进阶房
    if (targetHouse === '进阶房' && !game.quests.q7) {
        game.quests.q7 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q7', 300, '✅ 任务完成：乔迁之喜，奖励300元');
    }
    // 任务检查：升级到精英房
    if (targetHouse === '精英房' && !game.quests.q29) {
        game.quests.q29 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q29', 500, '✅ 任务完成：安居乐业，奖励500元');
    }
    // 任务检查：升级到终极房
    if (targetHouse === '终极房' && !game.quests.q30) {
        game.quests.q30 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q30', 1000, '✅ 任务完成：豪宅大院，奖励1000元');
    }
    
    addLog(`🏠 升级到了${targetHouse}！住得更舒服了，体力恢复也更快了。`, 'good');
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
    showToast(`升级到${targetHouse}！`, 'good');
}

function checkQuests() {
    // 任务检查在操作时触发，这里可以加一些时间相关的任务
    
    // q50: 年过半百（游戏时间超过50天）
    if (game.totalDay > 50 && !game.quests.q50) {
        game.quests.q50 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q50', 500, '✅ 任务完成：年过半百，奖励500元');
    }
    
    // q34: 村中知己（2个村民达到友好40+）
    const friendlyNpcs = Object.keys(game.npcs).filter(k => (game.npcs[k] || 0) >= 40).length;
    if (friendlyNpcs >= 2 && !game.quests.q34) {
        game.quests.q34 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q34', 300, '✅ 任务完成：村中知己，奖励300元');
    }
    
    // q35: 莫逆之交（1个村民达到亲密60+）
    const intimateNpcs = Object.keys(game.npcs).filter(k => (game.npcs[k] || 0) >= 60).length;
    if (intimateNpcs >= 1 && !game.quests.q35) {
        game.quests.q35 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q35', 500, '✅ 任务完成：莫逆之交，奖励500元');
    }
    
    // q48: 世家大族（4个村民达到友好40+）
    if (friendlyNpcs >= 4 && !game.quests.q48) {
        game.quests.q48 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q48', 600, '✅ 任务完成：世家大族，奖励600元');
    }
    
    // q47: 声名远播（声望达到200）
    if (game.reputation >= 200 && !game.quests.q47) {
        game.quests.q47 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q47', 800, '✅ 任务完成：声名远播，奖励800元');
    }
    
    // q46: 全面丰收（同时拥有早稻和红薯的成熟作物）
    const hasRiceMature = game.fields.some(f => f.crop === 'rice' && f.stage === 'mature');
    const hasSweetMature = game.fields.some(f => f.crop === 'sweet' && f.stage === 'mature');
    if (hasRiceMature && hasSweetMature && !game.quests.q46) {
        game.quests.q46 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q46', 200, '✅ 任务完成：全面丰收，奖励200元');
    }
    
    // 财富任务
    const riceValue = game.crops.rice * 2;
    const sweetValue = game.crops.sweet * 0.5;
    const totalAssets = game.money + riceValue + sweetValue;
    if (totalAssets >= 10000 && !game.quests.q41) {
        game.quests.q41 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q41', 1000, '✅ 任务完成：万元户，奖励1000元');
    }
    if (totalAssets >= 20000 && !game.quests.q42) {
        game.quests.q42 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q42', 2000, '✅ 任务完成：腰缠万贯，奖励2000元');
    }
    if (totalAssets >= 50000 && !game.quests.q43) {
        game.quests.q43 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q43', 5000, '✅ 任务完成：富甲一方，奖励5000元');
    }
    
    // 技能任务
    if ((game.skills.cropFamiliarity && game.skills.cropFamiliarity.level) >= 5 && !game.quests.q37) {
        game.quests.q37 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q37', 500, '✅ 任务完成：农学专家，奖励500元');
    }
    if ((game.skills.fieldManagement && game.skills.fieldManagement.level) >= 5 && !game.quests.q38) {
        game.quests.q38 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q38', 500, '✅ 任务完成：管理达人，奖励500元');
    }
    if ((game.skills.toolMastery && game.skills.toolMastery.level) >= 5 && !game.quests.q39) {
        game.quests.q39 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q39', 500, '✅ 任务完成：工具大师，奖励500元');
    }
    if ((game.skills.composting && game.skills.composting.level) >= 5 && !game.quests.q40) {
        game.quests.q40 = true;
        queueQuestReward('q40', 500, '✅ 任务完成：堆肥专家，奖励500元');
    }
    
    // 更新左侧任务追踪器
    if (typeof renderSidebarQuests === 'function') {
        renderSidebarQuests();
    }
}

// ==================== 日志系统 ====================
function addLog(text, type = 'normal') {
    const logEl = document.getElementById('event-log');
    const item = document.createElement('div');
    item.className = 'log-item new';
    
    // 3秒后移除new高亮
    setTimeout(() => {
        item.classList.remove('new');
    }, 3000);
    
    let timeStr = `[第${game.totalDay || game.day}天]`;
    let icon = '';
    
    switch(type) {
        case 'good':
            icon = '✨';
            item.innerHTML = `<span class="log-time">${timeStr}</span><span class="log-icon">${icon}</span><span class="log-good">${text}</span>`;
            break;
        case 'bad':
            icon = '⚠️';
            item.innerHTML = `<span class="log-time">${timeStr}</span><span class="log-icon">${icon}</span><span class="log-bad">${text}</span>`;
            break;
        case 'info':
            icon = '💡';
            item.innerHTML = `<span class="log-time">${timeStr}</span><span class="log-icon">${icon}</span><span class="log-info">${text}</span>`;
            break;
        case 'crop':
            icon = '🌾';
            item.innerHTML = `<span class="log-time">${timeStr}</span><span class="log-icon">${icon}</span><span class="log-crop">${text}</span>`;
            break;
        case 'npc':
            icon = '👤';
            item.innerHTML = `<span class="log-time">${timeStr}</span><span class="log-icon">${icon}</span><span class="log-npc">${text}</span>`;
            break;
        case 'pet':
            icon = '🐾';
            item.innerHTML = `<span class="log-time">${timeStr}</span><span class="log-icon">${icon}</span><span class="log-pet">${text}</span>`;
            break;
        default:
            icon = '📝';
            item.innerHTML = `<span class="log-time">${timeStr}</span><span class="log-icon">${icon}</span><span>${text}</span>`;
    }
    
    logEl.appendChild(item);
    logEl.scrollTop = logEl.scrollHeight;
    
    // 限制日志数量，最多保留200条
    const logItems = logEl.querySelectorAll('.log-item');
    if (logItems.length > 200) {
        logItems[0].remove();
    }
}

// ==================== 玩家反馈系统 ====================
function openFeedbackModal() {
    const html = `
        <div style="text-align:center;padding:10px;">
            <div style="font-size:36px;margin-bottom:8px;">🐛</div>
            <div style="font-size:16px;font-weight:bold;color:#e74c3c;margin-bottom:10px;">遇到 Bug 了吗？</div>
            <div style="font-size:13px;color:#666;margin-bottom:15px;line-height:1.6;">
                如果你在游戏中遇到了问题，<br>
                可以在这里提交反馈，我们会尽快处理！
            </div>
            <div style="margin-bottom:12px;">
                <label style="display:block;font-size:12px;color:#888;margin-bottom:4px;text-align:left;">问题描述（必填）</label>
                <textarea id="feedback-text" style="width:100%;height:80px;padding:8px;border:1px solid #d4b896;border-radius:6px;font-size:13px;resize:none;box-sizing:border-box;" placeholder="请描述你遇到的问题..."></textarea>
            </div>
            <div style="margin-bottom:12px;">
                <label style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;font-size:12px;color:#555;cursor:pointer;">
                    <input type="checkbox" id="feedback-include-log" checked style="width:14px;height:14px;">
                    同时提交当前游戏日志（帮助更快定位问题）
                </label>
            </div>
            <div style="font-size:11px;color:#999;margin-bottom:12px;text-align:left;background:#f5f0e6;padding:8px;border-radius:4px;">
                📊 当前游戏状态：第${(game && game.day) || '?'}天 | ${(game && game.money) || 0}元 | ${(game && game.season) || '?'} | ${(game && game.mode) || 'normal'}模式
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
    showModal('提交反馈', html, submitFeedback, '取消');
    setTimeout(() => {
        const primaryBtn = document.querySelector('.modal-btn.primary');
        if (primaryBtn) primaryBtn.textContent = '📤 提交反馈';
    }, 50);
}

function submitFeedback() {
    const text = (document.getElementById('feedback-text') && document.getElementById('feedback-text').value && document.getElementById('feedback-text').value.trim)();
    const includeLog =(document.getElementById('feedback-include-log') && document.getElementById('feedback-include-log').checked);
    
    if (!text) {
        showToast('请填写问题描述', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    let feedback = `===== 李家村 - 农耕模拟器 玩家反馈 =====
`;
    feedback += `提交时间: ${new Date().toLocaleString()}
`;
    feedback += `=======================================

`;
    feedback += `【问题描述】
${text}

`;
    feedback += `【游戏状态】
`;
    feedback += `天数: 第${(game && game.day) || '?'}天
`;
    feedback += `季节: ${(game && game.season) || '?'}
`;
    feedback += `金钱: ${(game && game.money) || 0}元
`;
    feedback += `体力: ${(game && game.stamina) || 0}/${(game && game.maxStamina) || 0}
`;
    feedback += `健康: ${(game && game.health) || 0}/${(game && game.maxHealth) || 0}
`;
    feedback += `模式: ${(game && game.mode) || 'normal'}
`;
    feedback += `=======================================

`;
    
    if (includeLog) {
        feedback += `【事件日志】
`;
        const logEl = document.getElementById('event-log');
        if (logEl) {
            const logItems = logEl.querySelectorAll('.log-item');
            logItems.forEach(item => {
                feedback += item.textContent + '\n';
            });
        }
        feedback += '\n';
    }
    
    try {
        const blob = new Blob([feedback], { type: 'text/plain;charset=utf-8' });
        const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = url;
        a.download = `farm_feedback_${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,19).replace(/:/g,'-')}.txt`;
        document.body.appendChild(a);
        a.click();
        document.body.removeChild(a);
        URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
        
        // 同时存入localStorage供开发者后台查看
        const FEEDBACK_KEY = 'farm_game_feedback_v1';
        const LOG_KEY = 'farm_game_system_log';
        const stored = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(FEEDBACK_KEY) || '[]');
        stored.push({
            time: new Date().toLocaleString(),
            text: text,
            day:(game && game.day) || 0,
            season:(game && game.season) || '?',
            money:(game && game.money) || 0,
            stamina:(game && game.stamina) || 0,
            health:(game && game.health) || 0,
            mode:(game && game.mode) || 'normal'
        });
        localStorage.setItem(FEEDBACK_KEY, JSON.stringify(stored));
        
        // 记录系统日志
        const logs = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(LOG_KEY) || '[]');
        logs.push(`[${new Date().toLocaleString()}] 新反馈: ${text.substring(0, 50)}...`);
        if (logs.length > 100) logs.shift();
        localStorage.setItem(LOG_KEY, JSON.stringify(logs));
        
        showToast('📤 反馈已保存到下载文件夹', 'good');
        addLog('📤 玩家提交了bug反馈', 'info');
        closeModal();
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('保存反馈失败:', e);
        showToast('保存反馈失败: ' + e.message, 'bad');
    }
}

function saveFeedbackLog() {
    openFeedbackModal();
}

// 展开/收起日志
let logExpanded = false;
function toggleLogExpand() {
    playClickSound();
    const logEl = document.getElementById('event-log');
    const btn = document.querySelector('.event-log-expand-btn');
    
    if (logExpanded) {
        logEl.style.height = '200px';
        btn.textContent = '🔍 展开查看';
        logExpanded = false;
    } else {
        logEl.style.height = '500px';
        btn.textContent = '📉 收起';
        logExpanded = true;
    }
}

// ==================== 弹窗系统 ====================
function showModal(title, content, onConfirm) {
    document.getElementById('modal-title').textContent = title;
    modalCallback = onConfirm;
    if (!onConfirm) {
        // 被动事件：内容末尾添加"知道了"按钮
        document.querySelector('.modal-buttons').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('modal-content').innerHTML = content + 
            '<div style="text-align:center;margin-top:20px;"><button class="modal-btn" onclick="closeModal()">知道了</button></div>';
    } else {
        document.querySelector('.modal-buttons').style.display = 'flex';
        document.getElementById('modal-content').innerHTML = content;
    }
    document.getElementById('modal-overlay').style.display = 'flex';
}

function closeEventModal() {
    playClickSound();
    document.getElementById('modal-overlay').style.display = 'none';
    game.currentEvent = null;
    // 重置弹窗按钮状态
    document.querySelector('.modal-buttons').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('modal-confirm').style.display = 'inline-block';
}

function closeModal() {
    playClickSound();
    document.getElementById('modal-overlay').style.display = 'none';
    modalCallback = null;
    // 重置弹窗按钮状态
    document.querySelector('.modal-buttons').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('modal-confirm').style.display = 'inline-block';
    document.querySelector('.modal-btn.secondary').textContent = '取消';
}

function confirmModal() {
    playClickSound();
    if (modalCallback) {
        modalCallback();
    }
    closeModal();
}

// ==================== 倒计时弹窗 ====================
function openCountdownModal() {
    playClickSound();
    renderCountdownContent();
    document.getElementById('countdown-overlay').style.display = 'flex';
}

function closeCountdownModal() {
    playClickSound();
    document.getElementById('countdown-overlay').style.display = 'none';
}

function renderCountdownContent() {
    const container = document.getElementById('countdown-content');
    if (!container || !game) return;
    
    let html = '';
    let activeCount = 0;
    
    // 作物倒计时
    const growingFields = game.fields.filter(f => f.crop && f.stage !== 'idle' && f.stage !== 'mature');
    if (growingFields.length > 0) {
        html += '<div class="countdown-section">';
        html += '<div class="countdown-section-title">🌾 作物生长</div>';
        growingFields.forEach(field => {
            const cropData = CROP_DATA[field.crop];
            if (!cropData) return;
            const growDays = Math.max(0, game.day - field.plantedDay);
            const totalDays = cropData.growDays || 50;
            const remaining = Math.max(0, totalDays - growDays);
            const progress = Math.min(100, Math.floor((growDays / totalDays) * 100));
            const stageNames = { seedling: '育苗期', transplanting: '返青期', growing: '生长期', mature: '成熟期' };
            activeCount++;
            html += `
                <div class="countdown-item">
                    <div class="countdown-item-info">
                        <div class="countdown-item-name">${cropData.emoji || '🌱'} ${cropData.name} (田${field.id})</div>
                        <div class="countdown-item-desc">${stageNames[field.stage] || '生长中'} · 已种${growDays}天</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="countdown-item-time">${remaining}天</div>
                    <div class="countdown-item-progress">
                        <div class="countdown-item-progress-bar" style="width: ${progress}%"></div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        });
        html += '</div>';
    }
    
    // 成熟待收割
    const matureFields = game.fields.filter(f => f.crop && f.stage === 'mature');
    if (matureFields.length > 0) {
        html += '<div class="countdown-section">';
        html += '<div class="countdown-section-title">✅ 可收割</div>';
        matureFields.forEach(field => {
            const cropData = CROP_DATA[field.crop];
            if (!cropData) return;
            activeCount++;
            html += `
                <div class="countdown-item mature">
                    <div class="countdown-item-info">
                        <div class="countdown-item-name">${cropData.emoji || '🌱'} ${cropData.name} (田${field.id})</div>
                        <div class="countdown-item-desc">已经成熟，可以收割了！</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="countdown-item-time" style="color: #27ae60;">✅ 就绪</div>
                    <div class="countdown-item-progress">
                        <div class="countdown-item-progress-bar" style="width: 100%"></div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        });
        html += '</div>';
    }
    
    // 副业加工倒计时
    const activeJobs = (game.processingJobs || []).filter(j => !j.completed);
    if (activeJobs.length > 0) {
        html += '<div class="countdown-section">';
        html += '<div class="countdown-section-title">🏡 副业加工</div>';
        const currentTotalTime = (game.totalDay || game.day) * 24 + game.time;
        activeJobs.forEach(job => {
            const jobTotalTime = (job.startTotalDay || job.startDay) * 24 + job.startTime;
            const elapsed = currentTotalTime - jobTotalTime;
            const remaining = Math.max(0, job.duration - elapsed);
            const progress = Math.min(100, Math.floor((elapsed / job.duration) * 100));
            activeCount++;
            
            // 获取原料名称
            let inputName = '原料';
            if (job.inputCrop === 'rice') inputName = '稻谷';
            else if (job.inputCrop === 'sweet') inputName = '红薯';
            else if (job.inputCrop === 'wheat') inputName = '小麦';
            else if (job.inputCrop === 'corn') inputName = '玉米';
            else if (job.inputCrop === 'soybean') inputName = '大豆';
            else if (job.inputType === 'fish') inputName = '鲜鱼';
            else if (job.inputType === 'processed' && job.inputItem) {
                const pItem = PROCESSED_ITEMS[job.inputItem];
                inputName = pItem ? pItem.name : '原料';
            }
            
            html += `
                <div class="countdown-item">
                    <div class="countdown-item-info">
                        <div class="countdown-item-name">🏡 ${job.buildingName}</div>
                        <div class="countdown-item-desc">${job.inputAmount}斤${inputName} → ${job.outputAmount}斤${(PROCESSED_ITEMS[job.outputItem] && PROCESSED_ITEMS[job.outputItem].name) || ''}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="countdown-item-time">${remaining}时</div>
                    <div class="countdown-item-progress">
                        <div class="countdown-item-progress-bar" style="width: ${progress}%"></div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        });
        html += '</div>';
    }
    
    // 每日活动剩余次数
    html += '<div class="countdown-section">';
    html += '<div class="countdown-section-title">📅 今日活动</div>';
    
    // 锻炼
    const exerciseCount = ((game.exerciseToday && game.exerciseToday.day) === game.day) ? game.exerciseToday.count : 0;
    html += `
        <div class="countdown-item">
            <div class="countdown-item-info">
                <div class="countdown-item-name">🏃 锻炼身体</div>
                <div class="countdown-item-desc">消耗25体力，健康+1</div>
            </div>
            <div class="countdown-item-time">${Math.max(0, 3 - exerciseCount)}/3</div>
            <div class="countdown-item-progress">
                <div class="countdown-item-progress-bar" style="width: ${(exerciseCount / 3) * 100}%"></div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
    
    // 串门
    const visitCount = ((game.visitToday && game.visitToday.day) === game.day) ? game.visitToday.count : 0;
    html += `
        <div class="countdown-item">
            <div class="countdown-item-info">
                <div class="countdown-item-name">👋 串门聊天</div>
                <div class="countdown-item-desc">消耗10体力，提升好感</div>
            </div>
            <div class="countdown-item-time">${Math.max(0, 3 - visitCount)}/3</div>
            <div class="countdown-item-progress">
                <div class="countdown-item-progress-bar" style="width: ${(visitCount / 3) * 100}%"></div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
    
    // 钓鱼
    const fishCount = ((game.fishToday && game.fishToday.day) === game.day) ? game.fishToday.count : 0;
    html += `
        <div class="countdown-item">
            <div class="countdown-item-info">
                <div class="countdown-item-name">🎣 河边钓鱼</div>
                <div class="countdown-item-desc">消耗25体力，卖鱼赚钱</div>
            </div>
            <div class="countdown-item-time">${Math.max(0, 2 - fishCount)}/2</div>
            <div class="countdown-item-progress">
                <div class="countdown-item-progress-bar" style="width: ${(fishCount / 2) * 100}%"></div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
    
    // 采集
    const foragingCount =(game.dailyActions && game.dailyActions.foraging) || 0;
    html += `
        <div class="countdown-item">
            <div class="countdown-item-info">
                <div class="countdown-item-name">🌿 后山采集</div>
                <div class="countdown-item-desc">消耗15体力，采集资源</div>
            </div>
            <div class="countdown-item-time">${Math.max(0, 1 - foragingCount)}/1</div>
            <div class="countdown-item-progress">
                <div class="countdown-item-progress-bar" style="width: ${(foragingCount / 1) * 100}%"></div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
    html += '</div>';
    
    if (!html) {
        html = '<div style="text-align: center; padding: 30px; color: #888;">暂无进行中的任务</div>';
    }
    
    container.innerHTML = html;
}

function updateCountdownBadge() {
    const badge = document.getElementById('countdown-badge');
    if (!badge || !game) return;
    
    let count = 0;
    // 成熟作物
    count += game.fields.filter(f => f.crop && f.stage === 'mature').length;
    // 进行中的加工
    count += (game.processingJobs || []).filter(j => !j.completed).length;
    
    if (count > 0) {
        badge.textContent = count > 9 ? '9+' : count;
        badge.style.display = 'flex';
    } else {
        badge.style.display = 'none';
    }
}

// ==================== 背包弹窗 ====================
function openBackpackModal() {
    playClickSound();
    renderBackpackModal();
    document.getElementById('backpack-overlay').style.display = 'flex';
}

function closeBackpackModal() {
    playClickSound();
    document.getElementById('backpack-overlay').style.display = 'none';
}

function renderBackpackModal() {
    const container = document.getElementById('backpack-content');
    if (!container || !game) return;
    
    let html = '';
    let hasAny = false;
    
    // 消耗品/道具
    const consumables = [];
    for (const itemId in game.items) {
        const count = game.items[itemId];
        if (count > 0) {
            // 优先查找ITEM_EFFECTS
            let item = ITEM_EFFECTS[itemId];
            let icon = item ? item.icon : '';
            let name = item ? item.name : ((ITEM_DATA[itemId] && ITEM_DATA[itemId].name) || itemId);
            let desc = item ? item.desc : '';
            
            // 处理一些特殊物品
            if (!item) {
                if (itemId === 'fertilizer') { icon = '🧪'; name = '化肥'; desc = '用于施肥'; }
                else if (itemId === 'organicFertilizer') { icon = '💩'; name = '有机肥'; desc = '天然有机肥'; }
                else if (itemId === 'pesticide') { icon = '☠️'; name = '农药'; desc = '用于除虫'; }
                else if (itemId === 'bun') { icon = '🍞'; name = '馒头'; desc = '吃了回体力'; }
                else if (itemId === 'medicine') { icon = '💊'; name = '感冒药'; desc = '恢复健康'; }
                else if (itemId === 'fish') { icon = '🐟'; name = '鱼'; desc = '新鲜河鱼'; }
            }
            
            if (item && item.use && Object.keys(item.use).length > 0) {
                consumables.push({ itemId, icon, name, count, desc, canUse: true });
            } else {
                consumables.push({ itemId, icon, name, count, desc, canUse: false });
            }
        }
    }
    
    if (consumables.length > 0) {
        hasAny = true;
        html += '<div class="backpack-category">🧰 道具</div>';
        html += '<div class="backpack-grid">';
        consumables.forEach(item => {
            html += `
                <div class="backpack-item">
                    <div class="backpack-item-icon">${item.icon || '📦'}</div>
                    <div class="backpack-item-name">${item.name}</div>
                    <div class="backpack-item-count">×${item.count}</div>
                    ${item.canUse ? `<button class="backpack-item-use-btn" onclick="useBackpackItem('${item.itemId}')">使用</button>` : ''}
                </div>
            `;
        });
        html += '</div>';
    }
    
    // 作物库存
    const cropTypes = ['rice', 'sweet', 'wheat', 'corn', 'soybean', 'potato', 'peanut', 'pepper', 'cabbage', 'radish', 'eggplant', 'garlic'];
    const cropNames = { rice: '大米', sweet: '红薯', wheat: '小麦', corn: '玉米', soybean: '大豆', potato: '土豆', peanut: '花生', pepper: '辣椒', cabbage: '白菜', radish: '萝卜', eggplant: '茄子', garlic: '大蒜' };
    const cropEmojis = { rice: '🍚', sweet: '🍠', wheat: '🌾', corn: '🌽', soybean: '🌱', potato: '🥔', peanut: '🥜', pepper: '🌶️', cabbage: '🥬', radish: '🥕', eggplant: '🍆', garlic: '🧄' };
    const crops = [];
    cropTypes.forEach(type => {
        const count = game.crops[type] || 0;
        if (count > 0) {
            crops.push({ type, name: cropNames[type], count, emoji: cropEmojis[type] });
        }
    });
    
    if (crops.length > 0) {
        hasAny = true;
        html += '<div class="backpack-category">🌾 作物</div>';
        html += '<div class="backpack-grid">';
        crops.forEach(crop => {
            html += `
                <div class="backpack-item">
                    <div class="backpack-item-icon">${crop.emoji}</div>
                    <div class="backpack-item-name">${crop.name}</div>
                    <div class="backpack-item-count">${Math.floor(crop.count)}斤</div>
                </div>
            `;
        });
        html += '</div>';
    }
    
    // 加工品
    if (game.processedItems && Object.keys(game.processedItems).length > 0) {
        const processed = Object.entries(game.processedItems).filter(([_, count]) => count > 0);
        if (processed.length > 0) {
            hasAny = true;
            html += '<div class="backpack-category">🏡 加工品</div>';
            html += '<div class="backpack-grid">';
            processed.forEach(([key, count]) => {
                const pItem = PROCESSED_ITEMS[key];
                if (pItem) {
                    html += `
                        <div class="backpack-item">
                            <div class="backpack-item-icon">${pItem.emoji || '📦'}</div>
                            <div class="backpack-item-name">${pItem.name}</div>
                            <div class="backpack-item-count">${Math.floor(count)}斤</div>
                        </div>
                    `;
                }
            });
            html += '</div>';
        }
    }
    
    // 矿石
    if (game.mineInventory && Object.keys(game.mineInventory).length > 0) {
        const ores = Object.entries(game.mineInventory).filter(([_, count]) => count > 0);
        if (ores.length > 0) {
            hasAny = true;
            html += '<div class="backpack-category">⛏️ 矿石</div>';
            html += '<div class="backpack-grid">';
            ores.forEach(([key, count]) => {
                const ore = ORE_DATA[key];
                if (ore) {
                    html += `
                        <div class="backpack-item">
                            <div class="backpack-item-icon">${ore.emoji}</div>
                            <div class="backpack-item-name">${ore.name}</div>
                            <div class="backpack-item-count">${Math.floor(count)}块</div>
                        </div>
                    `;
                }
            });
            html += '</div>';
        }
    }
    
    if (!hasAny) {
        html = '<div class="backpack-empty">🎒 背包空空如也，去商店买点东西吧！</div>';
    }
    
    container.innerHTML = html;
}

function useBackpackItem(itemId) {
    if (!game || !game.items[itemId] || game.items[itemId] <= 0) {
        showToast('道具不足', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    const item = ITEM_EFFECTS[itemId];
    if (!item || !item.use || Object.keys(item.use).length === 0) {
        showToast('该道具无法直接使用', 'warn');
        return;
    }
    
    // 应用效果
    if (item.use.stamina) game.stamina = Math.min(game.maxStamina, game.stamina + item.use.stamina);
    if (item.use.health) game.health = Math.min(game.maxHealth, game.health + item.use.health);
    if (item.use.mood) game.mood = Math.min(100, (game.mood === undefined ? 50 : game.mood) + item.use.mood);
    
    game.items[itemId]--;
    addLog(`使用了${item.icon}${item.name}`, 'item');
    showToast(`使用了${item.icon}${item.name}！${item.desc}`, 'good');
    
    renderBackpackModal();
    updateUI();
}

// ==================== 飘字提示 ====================
function showToast(text, type = 'normal') {
    const toast = document.getElementById('toast');
    toast.textContent = text;
    toast.className = 'toast';
    if (type === 'good') toast.classList.add('good');
    if (type === 'bad') toast.classList.add('bad');
    
    toast.classList.add('show');
    
    setTimeout(() => {
        toast.classList.remove('show');
    }, 2000);
}

// ==================== 错误日志 ====================
function showErrorLogs() {
    const overlay = document.getElementById('error-log-overlay');
    const content = document.getElementById('error-log-content');
    if (!overlay || !content) return;
    
    let logs = [];
    try {
        logs = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(ERROR_LOG_KEY) || '[]');
    } catch(e) {
        logs = [];
    }
    
    if (logs.length === 0) {
        content.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align: center; padding: 30px; color: #888;">暂无错误日志 🎉</div>';
    } else {
        let html = `<div style="margin-bottom: 10px; color: #666;">共 ${logs.length} 条记录（最多保留50条）</div>`;
        logs.forEach((log, i) => {
            html += `<div style="margin-bottom: 12px; padding: 10px; background: #f8f8f8; border-radius: 6px; border-left: 3px solid #e74c3c;">`;
            html += `<div style="color: #999; font-size: 11px; margin-bottom: 4px;">${log.time || '未知时间'}</div>`;
            html += `<div style="color: #c0392b; font-weight: bold;">${log.message || '未知错误'}</div>`;
            if (log.file) {
                html += `<div style="color: #666; font-size: 11px; margin-top: 2px;">${log.file}:${log.line || '?'}</div>`;
            }
            html += `</div>`;
        });
        content.innerHTML = html;
    }
    
    overlay.style.display = 'flex';
    closeSettings();
}

function closeErrorLogModal() {
    document.getElementById('error-log-overlay').style.display = 'none';
}

function copyErrorLogs() {
    let logs = [];
    try {
        logs = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(ERROR_LOG_KEY) || '[]');
    } catch(e) {
        logs = [];
    }
    
    const text = logs.map(log => {
        return `[${log.time || '未知'}] ${log.message || '未知错误'} ${log.file ? `at ${log.file}:${log.line || '?'}` : ''}`;
    }).join('\n');
    
    if (navigator.clipboard) {
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(text || '暂无错误日志').then(() => {
            showToast('已复制到剪贴板', 'good');
        }).catch(() => {
            showToast('复制失败', 'bad');
        });
    } else {
        // 降级方案
        const textarea = document.createElement('textarea');
        textarea.value = text || '暂无错误日志';
        document.body.appendChild(textarea);
        textarea.select();
        document.execCommand('copy');
        document.body.removeChild(textarea);
        showToast('已复制到剪贴板', 'good');
    }
}

// ==================== 键盘支持 ====================
document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
    if (e.key === ' ' || e.key === 'Enter') {
        // 故事页面按空格/回车翻页
        const storyContainer = document.getElementById('story-container');
        if (storyContainer.style.display !== 'none') {
            nextStoryPage();
        }
    }
    if (e.key === 'Escape') {
        closeModal();
    }
});

// ====== 自动种田模式（放置挂机核心）======
// ==================== 任务奖励弹窗系统 ====================
// 任务完成时奖励不立即发放，而是加入队列，玩家手动点击领取
function queueQuestReward(questId, money, text, reputation) {
    if (!game || !game.pendingQuestRewards) game.pendingQuestRewards = [];
    const quest = QUEST_DATA[questId];
    if (!quest) return;
    
    game.pendingQuestRewards.push({
        questId: questId,
        name: quest.name,
        desc: quest.desc,
        reward: text || quest.reward,
        money: money || 0,
        reputation: reputation || 0
    });
    addLog(`📋 任务完成：${quest.name}，奖励已发放！去【任务追踪】领取`, 'good');
    
    // 不再自动弹出奖励弹窗，玩家需手动去任务页面领取
    // 显示一个小提示通知
    showToast(`🎁 任务「${quest.name}」完成！奖励待领取`, 'good');
}

function showQuestRewardModal() {
    if (!game || !game.pendingQuestRewards || game.pendingQuestRewards.length === 0) return;
    
    const reward = game.pendingQuestRewards[0];
    const quest = QUEST_DATA[reward.questId];
    
    let html = `<div style="text-align: center; margin-bottom: 20px;">`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 50px; margin-bottom: 10px;">🎁</div>`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px; color: #27ae60;">任务完成！</div>`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 16px; color: #5d4e37; margin-bottom: 5px;">${reward.name}</div>`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #666; margin-bottom: 15px;">${reward.desc}</div>`;
    html += `<div style="background: #f8f9e8; border-radius: 8px; padding: 12px; margin-bottom: 15px;">`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 14px; color: #8b7355;">奖励</div>`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: #e67e22;">${reward.reward}</div>`;
    html += `</div>`;
    html += `</div>`;
    html += `<div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 10px;">`;
    html += `<button class="modal-btn primary" onclick="claimQuestReward()">🎁 领取奖励</button>`;
    html += `<button class="modal-btn" onclick="closeModal()">稍后再领</button>`;
    html += `</div>`;
    
    document.getElementById('modal-title').textContent = '任务奖励';
    document.getElementById('modal-content').innerHTML = html;
    document.getElementById('modal-overlay').style.display = 'flex';
}

function claimQuestReward() {
    if (!game || !game.pendingQuestRewards || game.pendingQuestRewards.length === 0) {
        closeModal();
        return;
    }
    
    const reward = game.pendingQuestRewards.shift();
    if (reward.money > 0) {
        game.money += reward.money;
    }
    if (reward.reputation > 0) {
        let repGain = reward.reputation;
        if (game.reputationBonus) {
            repGain = Math.floor(repGain * (1 + game.reputationBonus));
        }
        game.reputation += repGain;
    }
    
    addLog(`🎁 领取了「${reward.name}」奖励：${reward.reward}`, 'good');
    playSound('coin');
    
    // 如果还有下一个，继续显示
    if (game.pendingQuestRewards.length > 0) {
        showQuestRewardModal();
    } else {
        closeModal();
    }
    
    saveGame();
    updateUI();
}

// ==================== 探索/矿洞系统 ====================
function renderExplorePanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">⛏️ 后山矿洞</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">后山上有矿洞，挖点石头、煤炭、矿石回来，能卖钱也能做农具。</p>';
    
    // 矿洞层数
    const layers = ['layer1', 'layer2', 'layer3'];
    const layerNames = { layer1: '浅层', layer2: '中层', layer3: '深层' };
    
    html += '<div class="explore-layers">';
    
    layers.forEach((layerKey, idx) => {
        const layer = MINE_DATA[layerKey];
        const isUnlocked = isMineLayerUnlocked(layerKey);
        const isDeepest = game.mineStats.deepestLayer >= idx;
        
        html += `<div class="explore-layer-card" style="background: ${isUnlocked ? '#f8f9fa' : '#e9ecef'}; border-radius: 12px; padding: 16px; margin-bottom: 12px; opacity: ${isUnlocked ? 1 : 0.6};">`;
        html += `<div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; margin-bottom: 8px;">`;
        html += `<div style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 16px;">${layer.emoji} ${layer.name}</div>`;
        html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #666;">${isUnlocked ? '已解锁' : '🔒 ' + layer.unlockCondition}</div>`;
        html += `</div>`;
        html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #666; margin-bottom: 8px;">${layer.desc}</div>`;
        html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #e67e22; margin-bottom: 8px;">💪 消耗体力：${layer.staminaCost}</div>`;
        
        // 可挖掘按钮
        if (isUnlocked) {
            html += `<div style="display: flex; gap: 8px;">`;
            html += `<button class="action-btn" onclick="mineLayer('${layerKey}')" ${game.stamina < layer.staminaCost ? 'disabled' : ''}>`;
            html += `⛏️ 挖矿（-${layer.staminaCost}体力）</button>`;
            html += `</div>`;
        }
        
        html += `</div>`;
    });
    
    html += '</div>';
    
    // 矿石库存
    html += '<div class="section-title" style="margin-top: 20px;">📦 矿石库存</div>';
    html += '<div class="ore-inventory">';
    
    for (const [oreKey, amount] of Object.entries(game.mineInventory || {})) {
        if (amount > 0) {
            const ore = ORE_DATA[oreKey];
            html += `<div class="ore-item" style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; padding: 8px; background: white; border-radius: 8px; margin-bottom: 6px;">`;
            html += `<span>${ore.emoji} ${ore.name}：${amount}个</span>`;
            html += `<span style="color: #27ae60;">${ore.basePrice}元/个</span>`;
            html += `</div>`;
        }
    }
    
    // 出售按钮
    const hasOre = Object.values(game.mineInventory || {}).some(v => v > 0);
    if (hasOre) {
        html += `<button class="action-btn" style="margin-top: 10px; width: 100%;" onclick="sellOres()">💰 出售所有矿石</button>`;
    } else {
        html += `<div style="text-align: center; color: #999; padding: 20px;">还没有矿石呢，去挖矿吧~</div>`;
    }
    
    html += '</div>';
    
    // 统计
    html += `<div style="margin-top: 16px; padding: 12px; background: #e8f4fd; border-radius: 8px; font-size: 13px; color: #2c3e50;">`;
    html += `⛏️ 累计挖矿次数：${game.mineStats.totalDigs || 0}次<br>`;
    html += `🏔️ 已探索最深：${layerNames['layer' + (game.mineStats.deepestLayer + 1)] || '未探索'}`;
    html += `</div>`;
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

function isMineLayerUnlocked(layerKey) {
    if (layerKey === 'layer1') {
        return (game.totalDay || game.day) >= 10;
    } else if (layerKey === 'layer2') {
        return ((game.skills.toolMastery && game.skills.toolMastery.level) || 0) >= 2 && game.tools.includes('pickaxe');
    } else if (layerKey === 'layer3') {
        return ((game.skills.toolMastery && game.skills.toolMastery.level) || 0) >= 5 && game.money >= 5000;
    }
    return false;
}

function mineLayer(layerKey) {
    const layer = MINE_DATA[layerKey];
    if (!layer) return;
    
    if (game.stamina < layer.staminaCost) {
        showToast('累得不行了...先回家睡一觉或吃点东西恢复体力再来吧', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    game.stamina -= layer.staminaCost;
    
    // 挖掘结果
    let totalOres = [];
    let totalValue = 0;
    
    for (const yieldData of layer.yields) {
        if (Math.random() < yieldData.probability) {
            const amount = Math.floor(Math.random() * (yieldData.max - yieldData.min + 1)) + yieldData.min;
            if (amount > 0) {
                game.mineInventory[yieldData.ore] = (game.mineInventory[yieldData.ore] || 0) + amount;
                totalOres.push({ ore: yieldData.ore, amount });
                totalValue += amount * ORE_DATA[yieldData.ore].basePrice;
                // 解锁图鉴
                unlockCollectionItem('ores', yieldData.ore);
            }
        }
    }
    
    // 更新统计
    game.mineStats.totalDigs = (game.mineStats.totalDigs || 0) + 1;
    if (!game.stats) game.stats = {};
    game.stats.totalDigs = game.mineStats.totalDigs;
    const layerIndex = parseInt(layerKey.replace('layer', '')) - 1;
    if (layerIndex > (game.mineStats.deepestLayer || 0)) {
        game.mineStats.deepestLayer = layerIndex;
    }
    
    // 增加工具精通经验
    addSkillExp('toolMastery', 3);
    
    if (totalOres.length > 0) {
        const oreText = totalOres.map(o => `${ORE_DATA[o.ore].emoji}${o.amount}个${ORE_DATA[o.ore].name}`).join('、');
        addLog(`⛏️ 在${layer.name}挖到了：${oreText}，总价值约${totalValue}元`, 'good');
        showToast(`挖到矿了！${totalOres.length}种矿石`, 'good');
    } else {
        addLog(`⛏️ 在${layer.name}挖了半天，只挖到些碎石...`, 'info');
        showToast('运气不好，没挖到什么...', 'bad');
    }
    
    saveGame();
    renderExplorePanel();
    updateTopBar();
    checkAchievements();
}

function sellOres() {
    let totalMoney = 0;
    let totalCount = 0;
    
    for (const [oreKey, amount] of Object.entries(game.mineInventory || {})) {
        if (amount > 0) {
            const ore = ORE_DATA[oreKey];
            totalMoney += amount * ore.basePrice;
            totalCount += amount;
            game.mineInventory[oreKey] = 0;
        }
    }
    
    if (totalCount === 0) {
        showToast('没有矿石可卖', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    game.money += totalMoney;
    addLog(`💰 出售了${totalCount}个矿石，获得${totalMoney}元`, 'good');
    showToast(`+${totalMoney}元`, 'good');
    playCoinSound();
    
    saveGame();
    renderExplorePanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

// ==================== 烹饪系统 ====================
function renderCookingPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🍳 农家烹饪</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">用自家种的菜、钓的鱼、采的野菜做顿饭，吃饱了才有力气干活。</p>';
    
    // 可制作的食谱
    html += '<div class="section-title">📖 食谱</div>';
    html += '<div class="cooking-list">';
    
    for (const [foodKey, food] of Object.entries(COOKING_DATA)) {
        const canCook = canCookFood(foodKey);
        const have = game.cookedFoods[foodKey] || 0;
        
        html += `<div class="cooking-card" style="background: ${canCook ? '#f8f9fa' : '#e9ecef'}; border-radius: 12px; padding: 16px; margin-bottom: 12px; opacity: ${canCook ? 1 : 0.7};">`;
        html += `<div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; margin-bottom: 8px;">`;
        html += `<div style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 16px;">${food.emoji} ${food.name}</div>`;
        html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #666;">已有：${have}份</div>`;
        html += `</div>`;
        html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #666; margin-bottom: 8px;">${food.desc}</div>`;
        
        // 材料需求
        html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; margin-bottom: 8px;">`;
        html += `<span style="color: #e67e22;">📋 需要材料：</span>`;
        const ingTexts = [];
        if (food.ingredients.fishInventory) ingTexts.push(`🐟 鱼×${food.ingredients.fishInventory}`);
        if (food.ingredients.crops) {
            for (const [ck, amt] of Object.entries(food.ingredients.crops)) {
                const cnames = { rice: '水稻', sweet: '红薯', wheat: '小麦', corn: '玉米', soybean: '大豆', potato: '土豆', peanut: '花生', pepper: '辣椒', cabbage: '白菜', radish: '萝卜', eggplant: '茄子', garlic: '大蒜' };
                ingTexts.push(`${cnames[ck] || ck}×${amt}`);
            }
        }
        if (food.ingredients.processedItems) {
            for (const [pk, amt] of Object.entries(food.ingredients.processedItems)) {
                const pitem = PROCESSED_ITEMS[pk];
                ingTexts.push(`${(pitem && pitem.emoji) || ''}${(pitem && pitem.name) || pk}×${amt}`);
            }
        }
        if (food.ingredients.foragingItems) {
            for (const [fk, amt] of Object.entries(food.ingredients.foragingItems)) {
                let fnName = fk;
                for (const season of Object.values(FORAGING_DATA)) {
                    const found = season.items.find(i => i.id === fk);
                    if (found) { fnName = found.name; break; }
                }
                ingTexts.push(`${fnName}×${amt}`);
            }
        }
        html += ingTexts.join('、');
        html += `</div>`;
        
        // 效果
        html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #27ae60; margin-bottom: 8px;">`;
        const effects = [];
        if (food.stamina) effects.push(`💪 +${food.stamina}体力`);
        if (food.health) effects.push(`❤️ +${food.health}健康`);
        if (food.mood) effects.push(`😊 +${food.mood}心情`);
        html += effects.join('、');
        html += `</div>`;
        
        // 按钮
        html += `<div style="display: flex; gap: 8px;">`;
        if (canCook) {
            html += `<button class="action-btn" onclick="cookFood('${foodKey}')">🍳 烹饪（-${food.staminaCost}体力）</button>`;
        } else {
            html += `<button class="action-btn" disabled>🔒 材料不足</button>`;
        }
        if (have > 0) {
            html += `<button class="action-btn" onclick="eatFood('${foodKey}')">🍽️ 吃一份</button>`;
            html += `<button class="action-btn" onclick="sellFood('${foodKey}')">💰 卖一份（${food.sellPrice}元）</button>`;
        }
        html += `</div>`;
        html += `</div>`;
    }
    
    html += '</div>';
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

function canCookFood(foodKey) {
    const food = COOKING_DATA[foodKey];
    if (!food) return false;
    
    if (game.stamina < food.staminaCost) return false;
    
    const ing = food.ingredients;
    
    if (ing.fishInventory) {
        let fishCount = 0;
        if (game.fishInventory) {
            for (const count of Object.values(game.fishInventory)) {
                fishCount += count || 0;
            }
        }
        if (fishCount < ing.fishInventory) return false;
    }
    
    if (ing.crops) {
        for (const [cropKey, amount] of Object.entries(ing.crops)) {
            if ((game.crops[cropKey] || 0) < amount) return false;
        }
    }
    
    if (ing.processedItems) {
        for (const [itemKey, amount] of Object.entries(ing.processedItems)) {
            if ((game.processedItems[itemKey] || 0) < amount) return false;
        }
    }
    
    if (ing.foragingItems) {
        for (const [itemKey, amount] of Object.entries(ing.foragingItems)) {
            if ((game.foragingItems[itemKey] || 0) < amount) return false;
        }
    }
    
    return true;
}

function cookFood(foodKey) {
    const food = COOKING_DATA[foodKey];
    if (!food) return;
    
    if (!canCookFood(foodKey)) {
        showToast('材料不够，做不了这道菜', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    game.stamina -= food.staminaCost;
    
    const ing = food.ingredients;
    
    if (ing.fishInventory) {
        let remaining = ing.fishInventory;
        for (const fishKey of Object.keys(game.fishInventory || {})) {
            if (remaining <= 0) break;
            const take = Math.min(remaining, game.fishInventory[fishKey] || 0);
            game.fishInventory[fishKey] -= take;
            remaining -= take;
        }
    }
    
    if (ing.crops) {
        for (const [cropKey, amount] of Object.entries(ing.crops)) {
            game.crops[cropKey] -= amount;
        }
    }
    
    if (ing.processedItems) {
        for (const [itemKey, amount] of Object.entries(ing.processedItems)) {
            game.processedItems[itemKey] -= amount;
        }
    }
    
    if (ing.foragingItems) {
        for (const [itemKey, amount] of Object.entries(ing.foragingItems)) {
            game.foragingItems[itemKey] -= amount;
        }
    }
    
    game.cookedFoods[foodKey] = (game.cookedFoods[foodKey] || 0) + 1;
    
    // 统计
    if (!game.stats) game.stats = {};
    game.stats.totalCooked = (game.stats.totalCooked || 0) + 1;
    
    // 解锁图鉴
    unlockCollectionItem('foods', foodKey);
    
    addLog(`🍳 做了一份${food.name}！${food.desc}`, 'good');
    showToast(`做好了${food.name}！`, 'good');
    
    saveGame();
    checkAchievements();
    renderCookingPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function eatFood(foodKey) {
    const food = COOKING_DATA[foodKey];
    if (!food) return;
    
    const have = game.cookedFoods[foodKey] || 0;
    if (have < 1) {
        showToast('没存货了', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    game.cookedFoods[foodKey] = have - 1;
    
    if (food.stamina) {
        game.stamina = Math.min(game.maxStamina, game.stamina + food.stamina);
    }
    if (food.health) {
        game.health = Math.min(game.maxHealth, game.health + food.health);
    }
    if (food.mood) {
        game.mood = Math.min(100, (game.mood === undefined ? 50 : game.mood) + food.mood);
    }
    
    addLog(`🍽️ 吃了一份${food.name}，${food.desc} 感觉浑身都有劲了！`, 'good');
    showToast(`吃了${food.name}！体力+${food.stamina || 0}`, 'good');
    
    saveGame();
    renderCookingPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

function sellFood(foodKey) {
    const food = COOKING_DATA[foodKey];
    if (!food) return;
    
    const have = game.cookedFoods[foodKey] || 0;
    if (have < 1) {
        showToast('没存货了', 'bad');
        return;
    }
    
    game.cookedFoods[foodKey] = have - 1;
    game.money += food.sellPrice;
    
    addLog(`💰 卖了一份${food.name}，赚了${food.sellPrice}元`, 'good');
    showToast(`+${food.sellPrice}元`, 'good');
    playCoinSound();
    
    saveGame();
    renderCookingPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

// ==================== 社区建设系统 ====================
function renderCommunityPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🏛️ 村公共建设</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">村里的大事，大家出力。捐点材料、出点钱，把村子建设得更好。</p>';
    
    html += '<div class="section-title">🔨 建设项目</div>';
    html += '<div class="community-list">';
    
    for (const [projKey, proj] of Object.entries(COMMUNITY_PROJECTS)) {
        const projData = game.communityProjects[projKey] || { progress: 0, completed: false };
        const isUnlocked = isCommunityProjectUnlocked(projKey);
        const isCompleted = projData.completed;
        const progressPercent = Math.min(100, Math.floor((projData.progress / proj.totalProgress) * 100));
        
        html += `<div class="community-card" style="background: ${isCompleted ? '#d4edda' : (isUnlocked ? '#f8f9fa' : '#e9ecef')}; border-radius: 12px; padding: 16px; margin-bottom: 12px; opacity: ${isUnlocked ? 1 : 0.6};">`;
        html += `<div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; margin-bottom: 8px;">`;
        html += `<div style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 16px;">${proj.emoji} ${proj.name}</div>`;
        html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: ${isCompleted ? '#28a745' : '#666'};">${isCompleted ? '✅ 已完成' : (isUnlocked ? `${progressPercent}%` : '🔒 ' + proj.unlockCondition)}</div>`;
        html += `</div>`;
        
        if (!isCompleted && isUnlocked) {
            html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #666; margin-bottom: 8px;">${proj.desc}</div>`;
            
            // 进度条
            html += `<div style="width:100%;background:#e0e0e0;border-radius:4px;height:12px;margin-bottom:8px;">`;
            html += `<div style="width:${progressPercent}%;background:#27ae60;height:12px;border-radius:4px;transition:width 0.5s;"></div>`;
            html += `</div>`;
            html += `<div style="font-size: 12px; color: #666; margin-bottom: 8px;">${projData.progress}/${proj.totalProgress} 进度</div>`;
            
            // 所需材料
            html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; margin-bottom: 8px;">`;
            html += `<span style="color: #e67e22;">📋 还需要：</span>`;
            const needTexts = [];
            if (proj.materials.stone) {
                const haveStone =(game.mineInventory && game.mineInventory.stone) || 0;
                needTexts.push(`🪨 石块 ${proj.materials.stone}个（你有${haveStone}）`);
            }
            if (proj.materials.money) {
                needTexts.push(`💰 ${proj.materials.money}元`);
            }
            html += needTexts.join('、');
            html += `</div>`;
            
            // 奖励
            html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #27ae60; margin-bottom: 8px;">🎁 完成后：${proj.rewardDesc}</div>`;
            
            // 贡献按钮
            html += `<div style="display: flex; gap: 8px;">`;
            if (proj.materials.stone && ((game.mineInventory && game.mineInventory.stone) || 0) > 0) {
                html += `<button class="action-btn" onclick="contributeToProject('${projKey}', 'stone')">🪨 捐石块</button>`;
            }
            if (proj.materials.money && game.money >= 10) {
                html += `<button class="action-btn" onclick="contributeToProject('${projKey}', 'money')">💰 捐钱</button>`;
            }
            html += `</div>`;
        } else if (isCompleted) {
            html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; color: #28a745; font-weight: bold;">✅ 已完成！${proj.rewardDesc}</div>`;
        }
        
        html += `</div>`;
    }
    
    html += '</div>';
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}

function isCommunityProjectUnlocked(projKey) {
    if (projKey === 'village_well') {
        return game.day >= 5;
    } else if (projKey === 'stone_bridge') {
        const wellData =(game.communityProjects && game.communityProjects.village_well);
        return wellData && wellData.completed;
    } else if (projKey === 'village_school') {
        const totalAssets = game.money + calculateCropValue();
        return totalAssets >= 3000;
    } else if (projKey === 'ancestral_hall') {
        return game.reputation >= 100;
    } else if (projKey === 'health_station') {
        const totalAssets = game.money + calculateCropValue();
        return game.metSunmiaoqing && totalAssets >= 5000;
    }
    return false;
}

function contributeToProject(projKey, type) {
    const proj = COMMUNITY_PROJECTS[projKey];
    if (!proj) return;
    
    if (!game.communityProjects[projKey]) {
        game.communityProjects[projKey] = { progress: 0, completed: false };
    }
    
    const projData = game.communityProjects[projKey];
    if (projData.completed) {
        showToast('这个项目已经完成了！', 'good');
        return;
    }
    
    let contributed = 0;
    
    if (type === 'stone') {
        const haveStone =(game.mineInventory && game.mineInventory.stone) || 0;
        if (haveStone < 1) {
            showToast('没有石块了，去矿洞挖点吧', 'bad');
            return;
        }
        const needStone = proj.materials.stone || 0;
        const remainingNeed = Math.ceil((proj.totalProgress - projData.progress) / (proj.totalProgress / needStone));
        const useStone = Math.min(haveStone, remainingNeed, 5); // 一次最多捐5个
        game.mineInventory.stone -= useStone;
        contributed = useStone * Math.floor(proj.totalProgress / needStone);
        addLog(`🪨 给${proj.name}捐了${useStone}个石块`, 'good');
    } else if (type === 'money') {
        const needMoney = proj.materials.money || 0;
        if (game.money < 10) {
            showToast('钱不够，先赚点钱再来', 'bad');
            return;
        }
        const remainingNeed = Math.ceil((proj.totalProgress - projData.progress) / (proj.totalProgress / needMoney));
        const useMoney = Math.min(game.money, remainingNeed, 50); // 一次最多捐50
        game.money -= useMoney;
        contributed = useMoney * Math.floor(proj.totalProgress / needMoney);
        addLog(`💰 给${proj.name}捐了${useMoney}元`, 'good');
    }
    
    projData.progress += contributed;
    
    // 检查是否完成
    if (projData.progress >= proj.totalProgress) {
        projData.progress = proj.totalProgress;
        projData.completed = true;
        addLog(`🎉 ${proj.name}建设完成！${proj.rewardDesc}`, 'good');
        showToast(`🎉 ${proj.name}建设完成！`, 'good');
        playBonusSound();
        
        // 应用项目奖励
        if (proj.rewards) {
            if (proj.rewards.staminaRegen) {
