                game.staminaRegenBonus = (game.staminaRegenBonus || 0) + proj.rewards.staminaRegen;
            }
            if (proj.rewards.foragingBonus) {
                game.foragingBonus = (game.foragingBonus || 0) + proj.rewards.foragingBonus;
            }
            if (proj.rewards.researchPointBonus) {
                game.researchPointBonus = (game.researchPointBonus || 0) + proj.rewards.researchPointBonus;
            }
            if (proj.rewards.reputationBonus) {
                game.reputationBonus = (game.reputationBonus || 0) + proj.rewards.reputationBonus;
            }
            if (proj.rewards.healthRegen) {
                game.healthRegenBonus = (game.healthRegenBonus || 0) + proj.rewards.healthRegen;
            }
            if (proj.rewards.medicineDiscount) {
                game.medicineDiscount = (game.medicineDiscount || 0) + proj.rewards.medicineDiscount;
            }
        }
        
        // 村小学扩建完成后自动解锁林老师
        if (projKey === 'village_school' && !game.metLinxiaoyu) {
            game.metLinxiaoyu = true;
            if (!game.npcs.linxiaoyu) game.npcs.linxiaoyu = 0;
            if (!game.friendship.linxiaoyu) game.friendship.linxiaoyu = 0;
            game.npcs.linxiaoyu = Math.max(game.npcs.linxiaoyu, 10);
            game.friendship.linxiaoyu = Math.max(game.friendship.linxiaoyu, 10);
            addLog('🎉 村小学扩建完成！林老师来村里教书了，去和她打个招呼吧！', 'good');
            showToast('🎉 林老师来村里了！', 'good');
        }
    } else {
        const percent = Math.floor((projData.progress / proj.totalProgress) * 100);
        showToast(`贡献成功！当前进度 ${percent}%`, 'good');
    }
    
    // 增加声望
    let repGain = 2;
    if (game.reputationBonus) {
        repGain = Math.floor(repGain * (1 + game.reputationBonus));
    }
    game.reputation += repGain;
    
    saveGame();
    renderCommunityPanel();
    updateTopBar();
}

// ==================== 图鉴系统 ====================
function getFishName(fishKey) {
    const names = {
        'carp': '鲤鱼',
        'catfish': '鲶鱼',
        'crucian': '鲫鱼',
        'grass_carp': '草鱼'
    };
    return names[fishKey] || fishKey;
}

function unlockCollectionItem(category, itemId) {
    if (!game.collection) game.collection = {};
    if (!game.collection[category]) game.collection[category] = {};
    if (game.collection[category][itemId]) return; // 已解锁
    
    game.collection[category][itemId] = true;
    
    // 查找物品名称
    let itemName = itemId;
    const catData = COLLECTION_DATA[category];
    if (catData && catData.items) {
        const item = catData.items.find(i => i.id === itemId);
        if (item) itemName = item.name;
    }
    
    addLog(`📖 图鉴新发现！解锁【${itemName}】`, 'good');
    showToast(`🎉 图鉴解锁：${itemName}`, 'good');
    playBonusSound();
}

function renderCollectionPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    
    if (!game.collection) game.collection = {};
    
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">📖 农家图鉴</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">记录你在乡下的点点滴滴，每一份收获都值得被铭记。</p>';
    
    // 统计总进度
    let totalItems = 0;
    let unlockedItems = 0;
    for (const catKey of Object.keys(COLLECTION_DATA)) {
        const catData = COLLECTION_DATA[catKey];
        totalItems += catData.items.length;
        const unlocked = game.collection[catKey] ? Object.keys(game.collection[catKey]).length : 0;
        unlockedItems += unlocked;
    }
    const totalPercent = totalItems > 0 ? Math.floor((unlockedItems / totalItems) * 100) : 0;
    
    html += `<div style="margin-bottom: 20px; padding: 15px; background: linear-gradient(135deg, #667eea 0%, #764ba2 100%); border-radius: 12px; color: white; text-align: center;">`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 28px; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 5px;">${unlockedItems}/${totalItems}</div>`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 14px; opacity: 0.9;">图鉴收集进度</div>`;
    html += `<div style="margin-top: 10px; height: 8px; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.3); border-radius: 4px; overflow: hidden;">`;
    html += `<div style="height: 100%; width: ${totalPercent}%; background: #4ade80; border-radius: 4px; transition: width 0.5s;"></div>`;
    html += `</div>`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 12px; margin-top: 5px; opacity: 0.8;">${totalPercent}% 已解锁</div>`;
    html += `</div>`;
    
    // 按类别渲染
    for (const [catKey, catData] of Object.entries(COLLECTION_DATA)) {
        const unlockedMap = game.collection[catKey] || {};
        const unlockedCount = Object.keys(unlockedMap).length;
        const catPercent = catData.items.length > 0 ? Math.floor((unlockedCount / catData.items.length) * 100) : 0;
        
        html += `<div style="margin-bottom: 20px;">`;
        html += `<div style="display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: space-between; margin-bottom: 10px; padding: 10px 15px; background: #f0f4f8; border-radius: 10px;">`;
        html += `<div style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 10px;">`;
        html += `<span style="font-size: 24px;">${catData.emoji}</span>`;
        html += `<div>`;
        html += `<div style="font-weight: bold; color: #2c3e50;">${catData.name}</div>`;
        html += `<div style="font-size: 12px; color: #7f8c8d;">${catData.desc}</div>`;
        html += `</div>`;
        html += `</div>`;
        html += `<div style="text-align: right;">`;
        html += `<div style="font-weight: bold; color: #667eea;">${unlockedCount}/${catData.items.length}</div>`;
        html += `<div style="font-size: 12px; color: #95a5a6;">${catPercent}%</div>`;
        html += `</div>`;
        html += `</div>`;
        
        html += `<div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fill, minmax(100px, 1fr)); gap: 10px;">`;
        for (const item of catData.items) {
            const isUnlocked = unlockedMap[item.id];
            html += `<div style="`;
            if (isUnlocked) {
                html += `background: white; border: 2px solid #4ade80;`;
            } else {
                html += `background: #e9ecef; border: 2px solid #dee2e6; opacity: 0.6;`;
            }
            html += ` border-radius: 10px; padding: 12px 8px; text-align: center; transition: transform 0.2s;`;
            html += ` cursor: ${isUnlocked ? 'default' : 'not-allowed'};`;
            html += `" title="${isUnlocked ? item.name : '???'}">`;
            html += `<div style="font-size: 28px; margin-bottom: 5px;">${isUnlocked ? item.emoji : '❓'}</div>`;
            html += `<div style="font-size: 13px; font-weight: bold; color: ${isUnlocked ? '#2c3e50' : '#adb5bd'};">${isUnlocked ? item.name : '???'}</div>`;
            if (isUnlocked) {
                html += `<div style="font-size: 10px; color: #4ade80; margin-top: 3px;">✓ 已解锁</div>`;
            }
            html += `</div>`;
        }
        html += `</div>`;
        html += `</div>`;
    }
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}


// ==================== 成就系统 ====================
function getCollectionCount() {
    if (!game.collection) return 0;
    let count = 0;
    for (const cat of Object.values(game.collection)) {
        count += Object.keys(cat).length;
    }
    return count;
}

function getNpcMetCount() {
    let count = 0;
    if (game.npcs) {
        for (const [key, val] of Object.entries(game.npcs)) {
            if (val > 0 || (typeof val === 'object' && val.favor > 0)) count++;
        }
    }
    return count;
}

function checkAchievements() {
    if (!game.achievements) game.achievements = {};
    
    const conditions = {
        totalHarvest:(game.stats && game.stats.totalHarvest) || 0,
        totalSell:(game.stats && game.stats.totalSell) || 0,
        totalEarned:(game.stats && game.stats.totalEarned) || 0,
        totalFish:(game.stats && game.stats.totalFish) || 0,
        totalForage:(game.stats && game.stats.totalForage) || 0,
        totalProcessed:(game.stats && game.stats.totalProcessed) || 0,
        totalCooked:(game.stats && game.stats.totalCooked) || 0,
        totalDigs:(game.stats && game.stats.totalDigs) || 0,
        day: game.day || 1,
        money: game.money || 0,
        reputation: game.reputation || 0,
        collectionCount: getCollectionCount(),
        npcMetCount: getNpcMetCount(),
        hasCompost: game.composting || false,
        hasWell:(game.buildings && game.buildings.well) >= 1 || false
    };
    
    for (const [key, ach] of Object.entries(ACHIEVEMENT_DATA)) {
        if (game.achievements[key]) continue; // 已解锁
        
        // 解析条件
        const parts = ach.condition.split('>=');
        if (parts.length === 2) {
            const condKey = parts[0].trim();
            const condVal = parseInt(parts[1].trim());
            if (conditions[condKey] !== undefined && conditions[condKey] >= condVal) {
                unlockAchievement(key);
            }
        } else {
            // 布尔条件检查（如 hasCompost, hasWell）
            if (ach.condition === 'hasCompost' && conditions.hasCompost) {
                unlockAchievement(key);
            }
            if (ach.condition === 'hasWell' && conditions.hasWell) {
                unlockAchievement(key);
            }
        }
    }
}

function unlockAchievement(achKey) {
    const ach = ACHIEVEMENT_DATA[achKey];
    if (!ach || game.achievements[achKey]) return;
    
    game.achievements[achKey] = {
        unlocked: true,
        unlockDay: game.day || 1
    };
    
    // 发放奖励
    let rewardText = '';
    if (ach.reward.money) {
        game.money += ach.reward.money;
        rewardText += `+${ach.reward.money}元 `;
    }
    if (ach.reward.reputation) {
        let repGain = ach.reward.reputation;
        if (game.reputationBonus) {
            repGain = Math.floor(repGain * (1 + game.reputationBonus));
        }
        game.reputation += repGain;
        rewardText += `+${repGain}声望 `;
    }
    
    addLog(`🏆 成就解锁【${ach.name}】！${ach.desc} ${rewardText ? '奖励：' + rewardText : ''}`, 'good');
    showToast(`🏆 成就解锁：${ach.name}！`, 'good');
    playBonusSound();
    
    // 如果当前在看成就面板，刷新它
    if (currentMainTab === 'achievements') {
        renderAchievementsPanel();
    }
}

function renderAchievementsPanel() {
    const panel = document.getElementById('content-panel');
    if (!game.achievements) game.achievements = {};
    
    let html = '<div class="panel-title">🏆 成就殿堂</div>';
    html += '<p class="panel-desc">每一步脚印都值得被铭记。完成成就，领取属于你的荣耀。</p>';
    
    // 统计
    const totalAch = Object.keys(ACHIEVEMENT_DATA).length;
    const unlockedCount = Object.keys(game.achievements).length;
    const percent = Math.floor((unlockedCount / totalAch) * 100);
    
    html += `<div style="margin-bottom: 20px; padding: 15px; background: linear-gradient(135deg, #f5af19 0%, #f12711 100%); border-radius: 12px; color: white; text-align: center;">`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 28px; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 5px;">${unlockedCount}/${totalAch}</div>`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 14px; opacity: 0.9;">成就完成度</div>`;
    html += `<div style="margin-top: 10px; height: 8px; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.3); border-radius: 4px; overflow: hidden;">`;
    html += `<div style="height: 100%; width: ${percent}%; background: #4ade80; border-radius: 4px; transition: width 0.5s;"></div>`;
    html += `</div>`;
    html += `<div style="font-size: 12px; margin-top: 5px; opacity: 0.8;">${percent}% 已完成</div>`;
    html += `</div>`;
    
    // 按类别分组
    const categories = {
        farming: { name: '🌾 农耕', emoji: '🌾' },
        economy: { name: '💰 经济', emoji: '💰' },
        fishing: { name: '🎣 钓鱼', emoji: '🎣' },
        foraging: { name: '🌿 采集', emoji: '🌿' },
        processing: { name: '🏡 加工', emoji: '🏡' },
        cooking: { name: '🍳 烹饪', emoji: '🍳' },
        mining: { name: '⛏️ 矿洞', emoji: '⛏️' },
        social: { name: '👥 社交', emoji: '👥' },
        collection: { name: '📖 图鉴', emoji: '📖' },
        general: { name: '📅 综合', emoji: '📅' },
        building: { name: '🏗️ 建设', emoji: '🏗️' }
    };
    
    for (const [catKey, catInfo] of Object.entries(categories)) {
        const catAchs = Object.values(ACHIEVEMENT_DATA).filter(a => a.category === catKey);
        if (catAchs.length === 0) continue;
        
        const catUnlocked = catAchs.filter(a => game.achievements[a.id]).length;
        
        html += `<div style="margin-bottom: 20px;">`;
        html += `<div style="display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: space-between; margin-bottom: 10px; padding: 10px 15px; background: #f0f4f8; border-radius: 10px;">`;
        html += `<span style="font-weight: bold; color: #2c3e50;">${catInfo.name}</span>`;
        html += `<span style="color: #667eea; font-weight: bold;">${catUnlocked}/${catAchs.length}</span>`;
        html += `</div>`;
        
        html += `<div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fill, minmax(220px, 1fr)); gap: 10px;">`;
        for (const ach of catAchs) {
            const isUnlocked = game.achievements[ach.id];
            html += `<div style="padding: 12px; border-radius: 10px; border: 2px solid ${isUnlocked ? '#4ade80' : '#e0e0e0'}; background: ${isUnlocked ? '#f0fdf4' : '#f9f9f9'}; opacity: ${isUnlocked ? 1 : 0.7};">`;
            html += `<div style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 8px; margin-bottom: 6px;">`;
            html += `<span style="font-size: 22px;">${isUnlocked ? ach.emoji : '🔒'}</span>`;
            html += `<span style="font-weight: bold; color: ${isUnlocked ? '#2c3e50' : '#999'};">${ach.name}</span>`;
            if (isUnlocked) {
                html += `<span style="font-size: 12px; color: #4ade80; margin-left: auto;">✓ 第${game.achievements[ach.id].unlockDay}天</span>`;
            }
            html += `</div>`;
            html += `<div style="font-size: 12px; color: #666; margin-bottom: 4px;">${ach.desc}</div>`;
            if (ach.reward && (ach.reward.money || ach.reward.reputation)) {
                html += `<div style="font-size: 11px; color: #f39c12;">奖励: ${ach.reward.money ? ach.reward.money + '元' : ''}${ach.reward.reputation ? ' +' + ach.reward.reputation + '声望' : ''}</div>`;
            }
            html += `</div>`;
        }
        html += `</div>`;
        html += `</div>`;
    }
    
    panel.innerHTML = html;
}
